            ♦ _*SURAH NISA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (472)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمُ ....*

_"Logo! Apne Parwardegar se darte raho."_ (Taqwa Ikhtiyar karo.)
(Surah Nisa: 1)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Surah Ale Imraan khatm hua jo ke pura Surah Madhe Ahle Bait (as) se pur tha. Ale Imran mean Janabe Abu Talib (as) ki aulad jo ke Ahle Bait (as) hain.
Aaj se ham Surah Nisa ki Tafseer shuru karenge. Iski pahli ayat Taqwa ka hukm de rahi hai, jis ke bare mein kai bar ham explain kar chuke hain. Is surah ki kuchh khusoosiyat hain jo ahadis mein mulaheza farmayen:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📖
Amirul Momenin Ali (as):
_"Jo shakhs har Jumah ke Din Sura Nisa padhega fishare Qabr se mehfooz rahega."_
(Kitab Sawabul Aamaal)
📖
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo Surah Nisa padhe to goya usne har Meeras hasil karne par Sadqa kiya hai aur Khuda use us shakhs jaisa ajr dega jisne koi ghulam kharid kar azad kiya ho aur Surah Nisa padhne wala shakhs Shirk se mehfooz rahega aur woh un logon mein se qarar payega jinki Khuda maghferat karega."_
(Misbah Kaf'ami, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*21st Mahe Safar 1438*
22nd November 2016, Tuesday,

          ♦ _*NASL-E-ADAM (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (473)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ نَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ وَخَلَقَ مِنْهَا زَوْجَهَا وَبَثَّ مِنْهُمَا رِجَالًا كَثِيرًا وَنِسَاءً ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ الَّذِي تَسَاءَلُونَ بِهِ وَالْأَرْحَامَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلَيْكُمْ رَقِيبًا*

_"Logo! Apne Parwardegar se darte raho Jisne tumhe ek Nafs se paida kiya aur uska joda bhi usi ki jins se paida kiya aur in dono se bakasrat Mard o Aurat Duniya mein phaila diye hain."_
_"Us Khuda se darte raho jiska wasta de kar tum ek doosre se sawal karte ho aur rishta o Talluqat ko bigadne se darte raho. Yaqeenan Allah tumhara Nigeban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 1)

📚📖 💏
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Bahut sare alag alag nazaryat hain lekin jo Imam (as) ki zabani ho wohi zyada Mohkam aur qawee hoga.

*Nasle Adam (as):*
Imam Sadiq (as) se Zurarah ne sawal kiya ke log kahte hain:
Allah ne Adam (as) ne apne do beton ka nikah do betiyon se kiya aur yun nasl chali.
Doosri baat jo log kahte hain ke Hazrat Hawwa ko Adam (as) ki bayen (left rib) pasli se paida kiya.??
Imam Sadiq (as) ne jawab diya:
"Allah ki Shaan isse kahen buland o bala hai ke apne Auliya, Asfiya, Anbiya (as), Rusul, Momenin o Momenat ko Haram milap se paida kare, kiya Khuda ko ye Qudrat nahi thi ke woh kisi Halal tareeqe se nasle Insaan ko jari kare?."
"Khuda is se bhi buland o bartar hai aur Aajiz nahi hai ke Woh Adam (as) ki zauja ko uski pasli se paida kare aur phir log Etraz karen ke Adam (as) ne apne hi ek hi hisse se nikah kiya tha!!!!!.

Baat ye hai ke Allah Ta'ala ne Adam (as) ko mitti se paida kiya. Phir un mein Rooh phoonki aur Malaika se unka Sajda karaya. Iske baad Adam (as) par neend tari ki aur doosra insaan paida kiya aur ise paida karke Adam ke raano ke qareeb litaya aur Khuda ne ye isliye kiya taake Aurat mard ke taabe rahe. Hawwa harkat karne lagi. Iski harkat se Adam ki aankh khul gayi aur aap ne bedar hokar apni jins ka joda dekha to Aap ye dekh kar hairan rah gaye ke woh unki ham shakl thi magar sinf (gender) ka farq tha. Hazrat Adam (as) ne guftugu ki to usne unki zaban nein jawab diya. Jab usse poochha tu kaun hai usne kaha mein bhi Khuda ki makhlooq hun. Adam (as) ne arz kiya: 'Khudaya ye haseen makhlooq kaun hain iska qurb achha lagta hai aur meri nigahen use dekhkar thakti nahi.' Allah ne farmaya ye Meri Kaneez hai, kiya tum chahte ho ke ye tumhare sath rahe aur tum se ins o muhabbat kare aur tum se baten kare aur tere Ahkam ki farma bardari kare? Adam (as) razi ho gaye. Allah ne farmaya tum Mujh se rishta talab karo. Ye Meri Kaneez hai aur tumhari shahwani zarooriyat ki takmeel ka zariya hai.' Phir Adam (as) mein jinsi shahwat (sexual desire) paida ki. Adam (as) ne arz kiya rishta talab karta hun, Teri Raza kiya hai?
Allah ne farmaya is Rishte ke evaz tumhe iska Haqqe Meher ada karna hoga aur Meher ye hai ke tum ise Mere Deen ke Usool o Qawaid ki Ta'leem doge."
Adam (as) ne farmaya manzoor hai. Adam (as) aur Bibi Hawwa ka Nikah ho gaya. Jab Adam (as) ne Hawwa ko bulaya ke mere pas aao Allah ne Adam (as) se kaha tum unke pas jao. Isliye Nikah ki darkhast mard karte hain na ke Aurat.
Phir Hazrat Adam (as) ko do bete hue Habil aur Qabil. Qabil ne Habil ko qatl kiya..Habil ki Shahadat par Hazrat Adam (as) ne 500 saal gham manaya, girya kiya aur biwi se maqarebat nahi ki. Phir Hazrat Sheesh paida hue. Kuchh arse baad Yafis paida hue. Jab dono jawan hue to Aap ne Khuda se unki Shaadi ki darkhast ki. Chunanche Allah ne Jumerat ke Din Asr ke baad Jannat se ek Hoor nazil ki jiska naam tha "Nazalah" jo Sheesh ki zauja huin. Doosri Hoor nazil hui jiska naam "Manzalah" tha Yafis ki zauja hui. Iske baad Shees ko beta aur Yafis ko beti hui aur jawan hone par in dono cousin ki shaadi hui. Aur is tarah Nasl e Insaani Duniya mein chali aur phali phooli."
(Noorus Saqlain, Kitab Ilalus Sharaye)
(Isi Ayat ka doosra hissa Silah Rahem kal jari rahega)
To be Cont'd....
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Nisa "نسآء" (Aurto) ko 'Nisa' kahne ki wajah ye hai ke Adam (as) ke Ins (attachment) ke markaz unki biwi Hawwa thi."_
(Kitab Ilalush sharay)
💏
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Ek Yahudi H. Ali (as) ki khidmat mein haazir huwa aur arz ki, "Khuda ne Farishto'n ko hukm diya ke Adam (as) ko Sajda karo to kya H. Muhammad (saww) ke liye bhi koi aisi fazilat hai?" Aap ne farmaya, "Khuda ne Farishto'n ko jo Adam (as) ke Sajde ka hukm diya tha wo oosi wajah se tha ke Muhammad (saww) aur unke Awsiya ke Noor ko uski aulaad se qaraar diya tha. Farishto'n ka Sajda Adam (as) ki parastish aur Ibadat ke liye nahi tha balke Khuda ke hukm ki ita'at aur oos baat ka eteraaf tha ke H. Muhammad (saww) Adam (as) se afzal hain. Agar Adam (as) ko ye fazilat ataa ki to Paigambar e Akram (saww) ko oos se bar-tar fazilat ataa farmayi kyun ki KHUD Khuda ne H. Muhammad (saww) par Salwaat bheji aur tamaam Farishto'n aur makhluqaat ko aap par Salwaat bhejne ka hukm diya. Pus jo shakhs bhi aap par har haal hayaat o mamaat (life and death) mein Salwaat bhejega, Khuda Wande Mut'aal usay 10 guna (10 times) Ajr ataa farmata hai, har Salwaat ke badle mein 10 nekiyaa'n ataa farmata hai. Jo shakhs Rasule Khuda (saww) ki wafaat ke baad unpar Salwaat bheje to wo usay sunte hain aur Salaam ka jawaab dete hain kyun ki Khuda ne har haajat-mand ki Dua ki qubooliyyat ko Paigambar e Akram (saww) par Salwaat bhejne par mauqoof kiya hai."_
(Durood O Salaam Ki Barkatein, p44)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*22nd Mahe Safar 1438*
23rd November 2016, Wednesday,

          ♦ _*SILAH-E-REHM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (474)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ اتَّقُوا رَبَّكُمُ الَّذِي خَلَقَكُمْ مِنْ نَفْسٍ وَاحِدَةٍ وَخَلَقَ مِنْهَا زَوْجَهَا وَبَثَّ مِنْهُمَا رِجَالًا كَثِيرًا وَنِسَاءً ۚ وَاتَّقُوا اللَّهَ الَّذِي تَسَاءَلُونَ بِهِ وَالْأَرْحَامَ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلَيْكُمْ رَقِيبًا*

_"Logo! Apne Parwardegar se darte raho Jisne tumhe ek Nafs se paida kiya aur uska joda bhi usi ki jins se paida kiya aur in dono se bakasrat Mard o Aurat Duniya mein phaila diye hain."_
_"Us Khuda se darte raho jiska wasta de kar tum ek doosre se sawal karte ho aur rishta o Talluqat ko bigadne se darte raho. Yaqeenan Allah tumhara Nigeban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 1)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_ (Cont'd)
Is ayat ka doosra hissa Silah Reham ke bare mein hai. Means apne Rishtedaron se talluqat rakhna. Ahadis ke zariye is ki ahmiyat mulaheza ho:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Sadiq (as):
Is Ayat (4:01) ke bare mein farmate hain:
_"Isse logon ki Rishtedariyon ke Talluqat murad hain. Allah ne unke jodne aur qaem rakhne ka hukm diya hai. Kiya tum nahi dekhte ke Allah ne apne Taqwe ke sath sath Rishtedariyon ke talluqat qaem rakhne ka hukm diya hai."_
(Usoole Kafi, Raavi: Jameel bin Daraj)
👥
Amirul Momenin Ali (as):
_"Tum mein se baaz log gusse mein aate hain to woh raazi hone mein nahi aate. Tum mein se jab kisi shakhs ko apne Rishtedar par ghussa aaye to uske qareeb ho jao aur uske jism se apna jism mas (touch) kare. (Gale mile) kiyonki jab ek Rishta doosre Rishte se milta hai to use sukoon aa hata hai. Rehm Arsh se muallaq (latka) hai aur woh hamesha kahta rahta hai: "Khudaya! Jo mujhe milaye Tu bhi use mila aur jo mujhe qata kare Tu bhi usko Qata kar aur isi haqeeqat ki taraf Allah Ta'ala ne is Ayat (4:1) mein ishara kiya hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Raavi: Asbagh bin Nabata)
👥
Imam Ali (as):
_"Silah Rehmi karo agarche Salam ke zariye se hi kiyon na ho kiyonki Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai: (4:1)."_
👥
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Aimma e Ale Muhammad (as) ka Rehm Arsh se muallaq hai aur woh Allah se darkhwast karta rahta hai. "Khudaya! Jo mujhe jode Tu bhi use jod aur jo mujhe qata kare Tu bhi usko Qata kar"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👥
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Sil e Rahem karega 4 inaam Allah se paayega:_
_- *Allah ki Muhabbat,*_
_- *Wus'at e Rizq,*_
_- *Umr mein izafa,*_
_- *Jannat mein daakhil hoga.*_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p117)
👥
Imam Ali (as):
_"Qaribi Rishtedaaro'n ki Dushmani bichchu ke dank se zyada dard-naak hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)
👥
Janabe Fatima Zahra (sa):
_"Allah ne Waaledain ke saath neki karne ko Apni naraazgi ke liye dhaal banaya hai…aur Sil e Rahem ko bulandi ka aur lambi Umr ka sabab qaraar diya hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
👥
Imam Reza (as):
_"Kabhi kabhi wo shakhs jo Sil e Rahem kare agar uski umr 3 saal tak baaqi hai to Khuda uski umr 30 saal kar deta hai aur Khuda jo chahta hai anjaam deta hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p117)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*YATEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (475)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَآتُوا الْيَتَامَىٰ أَمْوَالَهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَتَبَدَّلُوا الْخَبِيثَ بِالطَّيِّبِ ۖ وَلَا تَأْكُلُوا أَمْوَالَهُمْ إِلَىٰ أَمْوَالِكُمْ ۚ إِنَّهُ كَانَ حُوبًا كَبِيرًا*

_"Yateemon ko unka Maal de do aur unke achhe Maal ko apne bure Maal se mat badlo aur unke Maal apne Maal ke sath milakar mat khao. Ye bahut bada Gunah hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 2)

📚📖 😔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 3 sakht hukm hain:
1. Yateen jab baligh ho jaye to uska Maal de den. Amanat mein khayanat na karen. Uske Maal ko apna Maal na samjhen.
2. Na hi Yateem ke qeemti Maal ko apne kam qeemat wale Maal se badlen.
3. Yateem ke Maal ko apne Maal mein mix na karen.
Yateemo ke sath is tarah ki hera pheri bahut bada Gunah hai.
Iski detail Ayat Baqarah: 220 mein mulaheza farmayen.

Imam Sadiq (as) & Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
" _*إِنَّهُ كَانَ حُوبًا كَبِيرًا*_
_Means zamin se baramad hone wali bhari cheez ko kaha jata hai."_
(Yani itna bada Gunah hai.)
(Tafseer Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😔
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jab koi Momin kisi Yateem ke sar par hamdardi se haath pherta hai to Allah uske haath ke niche aaye har baal ke badle Neki likhta hai."_
(Tauba Aagosh e Rehmat)
😔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Baghair maa-baap ke Yateem se bada Yateem wo hai jo apne Imam e Zamana tak na pahu'ch sake aur ahkaam e Deen (rules of religion) aur wazaaif e Ilaahi ke jaan'ne mein hairaan o pareshaan ho. (Hamari Ummat ke Ulema mein se) jo unki hidayat aur taalim o tarbiyat kare, wo roz e Qayamat hamare saath mehshoor honge aur ek khaas buland darje ke maalik honge."_
(Ehtejaaj e Tabrisi, v1, p15)
😔
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne apne Nabi (saww) ko Yateem is liye banaya taaki unpar kisi ki Ita'at (Obedience) farz na rahe."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p99)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*24th Mahe Safar 1438*
25th November 2016, Friday,

              ♦ _*4 BIWIYAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (476)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ خِفْتُمْ أَلَّا تُقْسِطُوا فِي الْيَتَامَىٰ فَانْكِحُوا مَا طَابَ لَكُمْ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ مَثْنَىٰ وَثُلَاثَ وَرُبَاعَ ۖ فَإِنْ خِفْتُمْ أَلَّا تَعْدِلُوا فَوَاحِدَةً أَوْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ أَدْنَىٰ أَلَّا تَعُولُوا*

_"Agar tumko andesha ho ke Yateemon ke sath insaaf na kar sakoge to jo Aurten tum ko pasand aayen to un mein se do do, teen teen, char char se Nikah kar lo. Lekin agar tumhe khauf ho ke Biwiyon ke darmiyan Adl na kar sakoge to phir ek hi Biwi par iktefa karo, ya un aurton ko Biwi bana lo jo tumhare qabze mein aayi ho (Kaneez). Ye baat be insaafi se bachne ke liye zyada qareen e sawab hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 3)

📚📖 👩‍❤‍👩👩‍❤‍👩
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Mard ko ek hi waqt mein 4 Biwiyan rakhne ki ijazat di hai bashart ke sab ke sath insaaf ho.
West aur doosre log Deen e Islam ke is qawaneen par etraaz karte hain: Musalman zyada biwiyan rakhte hain, Polygamy ke qael hain. Polygamy ya zyada Aurten rakhna Islam ne shuru nahi kiya balke isne limit kiya. Arabon ka zamana Jahiliyat mein dastoor tha ke kai kai Aurten apne sath rakhte the. Islam ne kaha bas sirf 4 woh bhi agar hasiyat ho ya charon ke sath Adl se pesh aye tab.
Islam Deen e Fitrat hai. Is ka har qanoon Fitrat ke mutabiq hai. Hota ye hai ke Duniya mein Aurton ki abadi Mardon se zyada hoti hai. Pahle zamane mein aur aaj bhi jab jange hoti hain to kafi Mard mare jate hain. Baad mein kuchh bewa aur kuchh kunwari Aurten bachti hain. Ab agar ek se zyada ka jayz na hoti to unhe baqi ki zindagi ghair shadishuda basar karna padta.
Mard mein shahwat zyada hoti hai, fitratan aisa hota hai ko woh ek par iktefa nahi kar pata. Lehaza woh gunah ka murtakib hoga. Jawan ladki ka ghair shaadi shuda rahne mein bhi khatra hai. Ghair shaadi shuda Aurat ki zindagi mahfooz nahi hoti. Wohi bewa ke liye bhi. Agar jinsi maqsad na bhi ho phir bhi ek aurat financially ekele ke bajay kisi Mard ke nikah mein rahegi to zyada safe hogi. Doosri taraf aisa hota ke kisi wajah se ek Biwi se koi aulad nahi hoti. Mard doosri Biwi se ye khwahish puri kar sakta hai, doosri nahi to teesri...etc. Lekin Shart ye hai ke sab ke sath Adl se pesh aana hoga. Halanke biwi apne Shauhar ke sath akele hi rahna pasand karti  hai, woh sauton bardasht nahi karegi. Yahan Mard ko munsefana roll ada karna hoga warna uska ghar aman ke bajae jahannam ban jayga. Isliye Mard ko doosri shaadi karne se pahle sare pahluwon ko madde nazar rakhna hoga.
Jab ham doosre mazhib dekhte hain ke ek Biwi ke hote hue Mard doosri aurton ke sath najaez talluqat rakhta hai. West mein ye fuhush sex pornography jo common hai uski wajah yehi hai. Woh illegal tariqe istemal karta hai. Dekha jaye to West ne Aurat ki izzat ko bech diya hai. Islam Aurat ko izzat deta hai. Isliye Islam ne shart rakh kar ise regularise kar diya.
4 sab ke liye zaroori nahi kiya balke jo ba hasiyat hain aur Adl kar sakte hain.
Ek Mard jo ek Aurat se Nikah karta hai aur ek Shakhs aise hi rakhel rakhta hai - dono mein farq hai. Shadi shuda ko sare qanoon ki pabandi karni padti hai aur Mard Aurat ki zindagi ki guarantee leta hai jabke ghair shaadi shuda baghair license ke kisi qanoon ki paband nahi hote aur us mein Mard Aurat ko sirf dhoka deta hai.
Ek Mard ki 4 biwiyan to ek biwi ke 4 mard kiyon nahi. Hindu Mythology mein Durupati ke 5 Shauhar the jo Pando kahlate the. Kauro aur Pando mein jab juwe ki baazi lagi to us mein unhone Aurat ko laga diya. Dono mein jhadap hui to Mahabharat shuru hui.
Ab dekhiye Islam kiya kahta hai.
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Mard ke liye basharte Adl 4 Biwiyan ek hi waqt mein Halal hain jabke Aurat ke liye ek waqt mein sirf ek hi Shauhar Halal hai. Iski wajah ye hai ke jab Mard ke pas 4 Aurten hon to un Aurton se jitne bhi bachche honge woh usi Mard ki taraf mansoob honge. Agar bilfarz kisi Aurat ke ek hi waqt mein do ya zyada Shauhar hon to phir pata na chalega ke paida hone wala bachcha kis ka hai. Is se Nasab, Meeras aur Qaumiyat ki pahchan khatm ho jayegi."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)
👩‍❤‍👩👩‍❤‍👩
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ghairat mardon mein payi jati hai jabke Auton mein Hasad (Jealousy) paya jata hai. Isi liye Aurat ke liye sirf ek shauhar halal kiya gaya jabke Mard ke liye char Biwiyan halal ki gayin. Agar Khuda ne Aurat ka ghairat ka jazba rakha hota to uski maujoodgi mein baqi teen Aurten Mard ke liye jayz qarar na deta."_
(Al Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👩‍❤‍👩
H. Isa (as):
_"Duniya aur Akherat ki misaal (ek shakhs ki) 2 biwi jaisi hai. Wo agar ek ko raazi karega to dusri uspe gussa ho jayegi."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar)

*25th Mahe Safar 1438*

             ♦ _*MEHER*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (477)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَآتُوا النِّسَاءَ صَدُقَاتِهِنَّ نِحْلَةً ۚ فَإِنْ طِبْنَ لَكُمْ عَنْ شَيْءٍ مِنْهُ نَفْسًا فَكُلُوهُ هَنِيئًا مَرِيئًا*

_"Aur Aurton ke MEHER khush dili ke sath ada karo. Albatta agar woh khud apni khushi se tumhe Meher ka kuchh hissa maaf kar den to tum ise khushgawar samajh kar khao."_
(Surah Nisa: 4)

📚📖 💑
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Hamare Samaj mein dastoor ye hai ke baap apni beti ke liye shaadi se pahle saari umr Jahez (Dowry) ki tayyari karta hai tab kahi shaadi ki naubat aati hai. Samaj ne Shaadi ko ek mushkil kar bana diya hai jabke Islam mein Shaadi ko bahut asaan banaya hai. Mard ko uski biwi ko Meher dena hota hai. Ladki ke baap par koi aisi cheez zaroori nahi. Balke mutalba ladki ki taraf se hona chahiye. Meher Aurat ka Haq hai.
Yahan Ayat mein صدق means Meher aur نحله means Qarz ya Tohfa. Means Mard Aurat Meher is tarah ada kare jaise us par uska qarz hai ya jaise Tohfa diya jata hai. Meher ki koi raqam fix nahi hai. Jaise Nikah apas mein ek agreement hai waise hi jo bhi Meher apas mein tay ho jay de. Agar Mard Shaadi ke pahle dede to isse ladki wale Jahez ka intezam kar sakte hain, kiyonki ye fitrat hain ke baaq apni beti ko kuchh gift deta hai. Agar usko Meher ki raqam mil jaye to us par bojh nahi padega.
Jo log ba haisiyat hai unko koi problem nahi aati lekin ghareeb gharane mushkilat mein rahte hain. Bahaisiyat log bhi koshish karen ke zyada show bazi na karen ke ye riwaj ban jay. Islam ne saadi shaadi ki takeed ki hai.
Islam ne Aurat ko usko Meher jaisa gift de kar uski Izzat ko dobala kiya hai. Balke Meher Aurat ka insurance aur safety hai. Meher Talaaq ko rokta hai.
💑
Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Haq e Meher Mard par wajib hai. Allah ne Aurat par Haq e Meher wajib nahi kiya. Iski wajah ye hai Aurat ka Naan o Nafqa Mard par wajib wajib hai aur Nikah ke zariye se Aurat goya apne aap ko furukht kar rahi hoti hai aur Mard kharid raha hota hai aur bay o shara (transaction) mein raqam ki adaygi zaroori hoti hai. Alawa az een Auraten Tijarat (Business) ke liye bhi bahar aa ja nahi sakti."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)
💑
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Haq e MEHER sirf Mard par farz hai Aurat par nahi. Agarche Nikah se dono ko hi jinsi taskeen (sexual affair) faraham hoti hai. Iski wajah ye hai ke jab Haq e Zaujiyat ki adaygi ke dauran Mard ko inzaal ho jaye to woh khada ho jata hai aur biwi ke inzaal ka intezar nahi karta. Jabke Aurat aisa nahi karti. Isi wajah se Haq e Meher bhi Mard par wajib kiya gaya hai."_
(Ilalus Sharay)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💑
Imam Kazim (as)
se puchha gaya ke Meher e Sunnat 500 Dirham kyun hai to aap ne farmaya,
_"Allah Rabbul Aalameen ne Apne upar waajib kiya hai ke jo bhi Momin 100 martaba ALLAHU AKBAR aur 100 martaba SUBHAN ALLAH aur 100 martaba AL HAMDU LILLAH aur 100 martaba LA ILAHA ILLALLAH aur 100 martaba Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (saww) par DUROOD padhh kar Hoor e Ein se shaadi ki darkhwast karega to Allah Ta'ala uski shaadi Hoor se zaroor karega aur ye uska mehr hoga. Phir Allah ne Apne Nabi (saww) ko Wahi farmaayi ke Mominaat ke haqq Mehr 500 Dirham muqarrar kare"._
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p580)
💑
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Choro'n ki 3 qismein hain: Zakaat na dene wala, Aurato'n ka Meher hazam kar jaane wala aur Qarz lekar adaaygi ki niyyat na rakhne wala."_
(Khisaal, ch3)

        ♦ _*NADAANO SE BACHO*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (478)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تُؤْتُوا السُّفَهَاءَ أَمْوَالَكُمُ الَّتِي جَعَلَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ قِيَامًا وَارْزُقُوهُمْ فِيهَا وَاكْسُوهُمْ وَقُولُوا لَهُمْ قَوْلًا مَعْرُوفًا*

_"Aur apne wo Maal jinhe Khuda ne tumhare liye zindagi ke qaem rakhne ka zariya banaya hai, Nadaan (Foolish) logon ke hawale na karo. Usi Maal mein se khana khao aur unhe is mein se libas pahnao aur achhe tareeqe se baat karo."_
(Surah Nisa: 5)

📚📖 💴💴
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Demonetization kar daur hai apne Maal ko sanbhal kar rakhen. Paper Currency ki koi value nahi hoti. Ye is tarah hai ke kisi ne mujh se Maal udhar liya aur ek paper par likh kar dede lekin ho sakta hai woh apne likhe ko jhotla de aur dhoka dede. Bewaqoofon ko apna qeemti Maal na sonpe.
Ayat mein سفهاء means Nadaan, bewaqoof logon ke liye aya hai. Raghib ne Mufradat mein سفه means ek tarah ki kam wazani aur badan ka halka hona jis mein ye haalat ho ke chalte waqt balance barabar na rahe. Imam Sadiq (as) farmate hain Sufaha means Sharabi aur jo us jaisa ho. Woh log jin par bharosa nahi kar sakte. Imam Baqir (as) ke mutabiq Aurten, bachche aur Sharaabi murad hain.
Ayaten jabke Yateemon ki kifalat ke bare mein hain lekin ye rule general hai. Jo bhi shakhs kama raha hai aur apne ahlo ayal ki kifalat kar raha hai us apni economic condition ka bhi dhyan rakhna chahiye. Isliye apni mehnat ka paisa kisi ko baghair check kare na den.
Ajkal bahut se log chande ki raseed ya dabba liye ghoote rahte hain. Chanda dete waqt bhi verify karna chahiye ke chanda lene wala genuine hai. Ya agar aap koi investment kar rahe hon tab bhi ye dekhna zaroori hai kahi koi fraud to nahi. Ya kuchh log kisi ke zariye paisa transfer karte hai. Har shakhs ko careful aur mohtaat rahna zaroori hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💴💴
Riwayat:
_"Allah ne bewaqoofo'n ko Rizq is liye ataa kiya taaki Aqalmand samajh le ke Rozi haasil karne ka taalluk chhal, kapat, saazish, daga-baazi se nahi hai."_
(Rizq)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*27th Mahe Safar 1438*
28th November 2016, Monday,

          ♦ _*FAHESHA AURAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (489)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاللَّذَانِ يَأْتِيَانِهَا مِنْكُمْ فَآذُوهُمَا ۖ فَإِنْ تَابَا وَأَصْلَحَا فَأَعْرِضُوا عَنْهُمَا ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ تَوَّابًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Aur woh Mard aur Aurten (jo Shadi shuda na hon) aur bura kam kar baithen inhe takleef pahunchao (un par Hadd jari karo) aur such much Tauba kare aur apni Islah kar len (aur guzishta harkaat ki talafi karen) to unhe Maaf kar do kiyonki Khuda wande Alam Tauba Qubool karne wala aur Meherban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 16)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal ki jo Ayat thi woh Shadi Shuda Fahesha Aurat ke bare mein thi jiska hukm waqtiya tha isliye woh ayat mansookh ho gayi aur Surah Noor ki Ayat mein doosra final hukm aya.
Aaj ki Ayat kunwari Fahsha Aurton ke liye hai. Unko bhi saza ka hum hai lekin usse halka hai, yahan Tauba ki bhi gunjayish rakhi gayi hai.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat se murad Ghair Shadi Shuda Mard aur Aurat hain agar woh ye bura kam karen to unhe saza di jaye."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Tafseer e Namoona)

Ghair Muslim ye eiteraz karte hain ke Islami Qawanin bahut sakht hain jo ke zulm hai. Ji haan sakht hain Mujrim ke liye taake Society mein jurm kam hon. Lekin jurm sabit hone ki bhi bahut se sharait hain woh pore honge tabhi mujrim mana jayga. Fahesha ke liye 4 witness (gawah) ki zaroorat hai jo ke bahut mushkil kaam hai. 4 gawaho gawahi den ke unhone dekha hai tab. Is tarah kisi ko bhi saza dena itna asaan nahi.
Lekin agar woh Tauba kar le to Maafi ki jagah bhi hai. Mashoor waqea hai: Imam Moosa Kazim (as) jinki aksar zindagi qaed khane mein guzri. Khalifa e waqt ne ek Fahesha ko Imam ki khidmat ke liye bhej diya. Fahesha Aurat Qaed Khane mein ayi aur isi intezar mein baithi rah gayi ke kab Imam Sajde se uthe aur woh unko apni tarah attract kare. Imam ke amal ka us Aurat par aisa asar hua ke woh jisne apni sari umr fuhush o badkari mein guzari aaj woh bhi ibadat guzar bab gayi. Jab Khalifa ne ye dekha to bola ke tujhe saza milegi to usne kaha mujhe teri saza ki parwa nahi mujhe Allah ki saza se dar lagne laga hai.
Ye the silsila e Ahle Bait (as) ki ek kadi.
Is silsile ki 11vi kadi Imam Hasan Askari (as) ki aaj Shahadat ka din hai. Ahle Bait (as) ki Dushmani aaj bhi parwan par hai. Samarrah mein unke Mazar ko Bom se udana is baat ki gawahi deta hai. Baqi ki mismari bhi gawah hai. Jinho ne hame itne achhe talimat di, hame Hywan se Insaan banaya unke sath aisa sulook. Ye lamhe fikriya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___ Syed Shoeb Raza
----------------------------------------------

_- aur Deen ki hifazat karne wala ho,
_- khwaishaat e nafs ki mukhalefat karne wala ho,_
_- apne Aqaa ke hukm ki ita'at karne wala ho,_

(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p227)

se sawaal kiya gaya ke

In dono mein kaun afzal hai?"_
Aap ne farmaya,:
_"Hamari Ahadees bayaan karne wala aur hamare Shiyo'n ke dilo'n ki islaah karne wala 1000 Aabido'n se behtar hai."_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p73)

                 ♦ _*TAUBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (491)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّمَا التَّوْبَةُ عَلَى اللَّهِ لِلَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ السُّوءَ بِجَهَالَةٍ ثُمَّ يَتُوبُونَ مِنْ قَرِيبٍ فَأُولَٰئِكَ يَتُوبُ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا*
_"Allah par Tauba ki qubooliyat ka Haq sirf unke liye hai jo Nadani ki wajah se koi bura fe'l kar guzarte hain. Iske baad jaldi hi Tauba karte hain. Aise logon ki Allah Tauba qubool karta hai aur Allah Sahib e Hikmat aur Sahib e Ilm hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 17)

📚📖  🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ameerul Momenin Imam Ali (as):
_"Jise Tauba naseeb hoti hai woh qubooliyat se mehroom na raha kiyonki Allah ka farman hai: (4:17)."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🙏🏻
Ek qaul ye hai ke har Fe'le Ma'siyat (Sinful act) agarche jan boojh kar bhi kiyon na ho jaye woh "Jihalat" mein shamil hai. Kiyonki har fe'l ki muharrik Jihalat hi hoti hai aur Jihalat hi fe'l e qabeeh ko aaraasta karke pesh karti hai. Yahi mafhoom Imam Sadiq (as) se manqool hai:
_"Har gunah jiska irtekab insaan karta hai agarche woh Aalim bhi kiyon na ho phir bhi irtekab e Gunah ke waqt Jahil hota hai kiyonki Khuda ki Na-Farmani Jihalat ki hi paidawar hoti hai. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Yusuf (as) ka woh qaul naql kiya hai jo unhone apne bhaiyon se kaha tha: "Kiya tumhe maloom hai ke tum ne Jahil ban kar Yusuf (as) aur uske bhai se kiya sulook kiya tha?" (Yusuf:89)_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Tum mein behtareen wo log hain jo khata ke baad Tauba karein."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p41)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab banda e Momin khaalis dil ke saath Tauba karta hai to Khuda us se mohabbat karta hai aur uske aibo'n ko duniya aur Akherat mein chhupa deta hai."_
Raawi ne sawaal kiya,
_"Uske aibo'n ko kyun kar chhupaye jaate hain?"_
Imam (as) ne farmaya,
_"Dono Farishto'n ne uske gunah qalam-bund kiye (likhe) hote hain, Wo unhe faramosh kar deta hai…aur jab wo Khuda ke huzoor pahu'nchta hai, uske khilaaf uske gunaho'n ki gawaahi dene waali koi cheez nahi hoti"._
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p808)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Momin ko uske kiye huwe gunah ki Tauba karne ke liye 7 ghante deta hai. Agar wo itne waqt mein Tauba kar leta hai to uske Naama e Amal mein kuchh nahi likkha jaata. Magar jo wo Tauba nahi karta, to phir wo gunah likha jaata hai."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar, Hadees 541)
🙏🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Gunaho'n ka tark (avoid) karna Tauba karne se zyada behtar hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p807)
🙏🏻
Imam e Shafaee
(Ahle Sunnat ke Imam)
ne ailaan kiya hai ke,
_“Agar Aal e Muhammad (as) ki mohabbat gunah hai to ye ek aisa gunah hai ke jis se main kabhi Tauba nahi kar sakta aur agar Aal e Muhammad (as) ki mohabbat ka naam hi Rafz hai to tamaam duniya ke logo’n mein sabse bada Raafizi main hoon.”_
(Haqeeqat e Tabarra by Allamah Farogh Kazmi, p41)

                ♦ _*TAUBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (492)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَيْسَتِ التَّوْبَةُ لِلَّذِينَ يَعْمَلُونَ السَّيِّئَاتِ حَتَّىٰ إِذَا حَضَرَ أَحَدَهُمُ الْمَوْتُ قَالَ إِنِّي تُبْتُ الْآنَ وَلَا الَّذِينَ يَمُوتُونَ وَهُمْ كُفَّارٌ ۚ أُولَٰئِكَ أَعْتَدْنَا لَهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*

_"Tauba un logon ke liye nahi jo buraiyan karte rahte hain yahan tak ke jab un mein se kisi ki Maut ka waqt aa jata hai to us waqt kahta hai ke ab Tauba kar raha hun. Isi tarah Tauba un logon ke liye bhi nahi hai jo Kafir ho kar maren. Aise logon ke liye hamne dardnak Azaab tayyar rakha hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 18)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal ki Ayat mein zikre hua tha ke Tauba wa Isteghfar turant kar len to qubool ho sakti hai. Kiyonki woh Gunah Jihaliyat ki bina par hue the.
Aaj ki Aayat mein Tauba concept ke misuse ke bare mein zikr kiya hai. Jo shakhs jan boojh kar gunah karta rahe ye soch kar ke marne se pahle Tauba kar lenge. Ya woh log jo aisi umr mein pahunch jate hain ke kabhi kabhi bhi is Duniya se rukhsat ho sakte hain Tauba Tauba karne lagte hain. Aksar ye trend dekha gaya hai ke puri umr to Dunyadari mein busy rahe kabhi Masjid ka rukh nahi kiya Akheri waqt retired hone par Masjid ke paband ho jate hain.
Jabke rivayaton mein milta hai ke Akheri waqt tak bhi Tauba qubool ho sakti hai. Tauba tab qubool nahi hoti jab woh sakarat ki manzil mein pahunch jata hai. Jankani ke Alam mein jab Maut samne dikhai deti hai aur insaani aankh ke parde uth jate hain aur ek khas binai paida hoti hai aur kuchh haqaeq jinka talluq doosri Duniya se hai aur apne is Duniya ke kiye hue Aamaal dekhta hai. Aise waqt mein woh pachhtawa karta hai phir Tauba karta hai to woh waqt nikal chuka hota hai kiyonki ab woh Alam e Barzakh mein dakhil ho chuka hota hai.
Aise waqt mein Tauba ki qubooliyat ka daromadar us ki Niyyat par hai.
Quran mein (Yunus:90-91) Firon ka zikr hai ke jab woh doob raha tha us waqt woh Khuda par Imaan laya jabke puri umr apne aap ko Khudai ka dawa karta raha. Uski is waqt Tauba qubool nahi hui. Rivayat ke mutabiq jab poochha gaya ki uski laash kiyonkar abhi tak baqi hai, bataya gaya woh is wajah se hai ke usne akheri waqt Allah ka iqrar kiya.
Woh Mujrim jo sooli par chadha diya gaya hai tab woh maafi mage to kiya usko maaf kar diya jayega? Nahi, kiyonki woh samajh raha hai ab to mein marne wala hai to kiyo na maafi mang le.
Allah sab Niyyaton se waqif hai uske mutabiq woh Tauba qubool karta hai.
*استغفر الله ربي واتوب اليه*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻____Syed Shoeb Raza

     ♦ _*AURAT KA MISUSE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (493) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا يَحِلُّ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَرِثُوا النِّسَاءَ كَرْهًا ۖ وَلَا تَعْضُلُوهُنَّ لِتَذْهَبُوا بِبَعْضِ مَا آتَيْتُمُوهُنَّ إِلَّا أَنْ يَأْتِينَ بِفَاحِشَةٍ مُبَيِّنَةٍ ۚ وَعَاشِرُوهُنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ ۚ فَإِنْ كَرِهْتُمُوهُنَّ فَعَسَىٰ أَنْ تَكْرَهُوا شَيْئًا وَيَجْعَلَ اللَّهُ فِيهِ خَيْرًا كَثِيرًا*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Tumhare liye Aurton ka zabardasti waris banna Halal nahi hai aur na ye Halal hai ke unhe majboor karke unke Haq e Meher ka kuchh hissa uda lene ki koshish karo jo tum inhe de chuke ho. Albatta agar woh badchalani ka irtakab karen to doosri baat hai. Unke sath achchhe se zindagi basar karo. Aur agar woh tumhe napasand hon to ye bhi ho sakta hai ke tumhe ek cheez napasand ho magar Allah is mein bahut si bhalai rakh de."_
(Surah Nisa: 19)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein kuchh buraiyan jo zamana jahiliyat mein payi jati thi us ka zikr jai. Us zamana mein aisa hota tha ke ek Aurat ka Shauhar ka jab inteqal hota to uska beta us Aurat par kapda dal kar kahta tha ke ye meri miraas hai. Lekin is Ayat mein bahut si nasihaten hain. Kuchh ye hain:
1. Aurat ko unke Maal ki lalach mein qaedi na banao.
2. Auraton se Meher ka Haq zabardasti bakhshwane ki koshish na karo.
3. Siwai us Aurat ke jo khule aam Fahesha ho. Rivayat ke mutabiq Fahesha means (a) Zinakar (b) Shauhar ki nafarman.
4. Apni Aurton ke sath shaista nek zindagi guzaren.
5. Kabhi aisa hota hai ke biwi ko pasand nahi karte lekin uske Maal ki wajah se rakhte hain. Zahir hai to phir unhe sataenge. Ye ghalat hai.
6. Bahut bar aisa hota hai ke jo hamko pasand nahi Allah usi mein behtari rakhta hai.
Tafseel mein jane gunjayish nahi hai.
Tarikh mein hamne dekha ke Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) jo ke Rasool (saww) ki waris thi aur Fadak jo ke Rasool (saww) ne tohfe ke taur par diya tha hakim ne hadap liya aur apne liye Halal kar liya. Jo Fahesha thi woh to is ayat ke mutabiq haqdar hai hi nahi. Shauhar ki nafarman ko Fahesha kaha gaya hai. Unke sath waisa hi bartao hoga jaisa Jamal mein hua. Ho sakta hai Rasool (saww) bhi is Fahesha ko na pasand karte hon lekin is ayat ki pairavi karte hue ke ho sakta hai Allah ki kuchh achhi maslehat ho.
Allah chahta hai ke ham Halal zindagi basar karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Choro'n ki 3 qismein hain:_
_- Zakaat na dene wala,_
_- *Aurato'n ka Meher hazam kar jaane wala* aur_
_- Qarz lekar adaaygi ki niyyat na rakhne wala._
(Khisaal, ch3)

       ♦ _*AURAT PAR ZULM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (494) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ أَرَدْتُمُ اسْتِبْدَالَ زَوْجٍ مَكَانَ زَوْجٍ وَآتَيْتُمْ إِحْدَاهُنَّ قِنْطَارًا فَلَا تَأْخُذُوا مِنْهُ شَيْئًا ۚ أَتَأْخُذُونَهُ بُهْتَانًا وَإِثْمًا مُبِينًا*

_"Aur agar tum ek Biwi ki jagah doosri Biwi laane ka iraada kar hi lo to khwah tumne use dher sara Maal hi kiyon na diya ho, us mein se kuchh wapas na lo. Kiya tum bohtan aur sareeh (clear) zulm se wapas lo ge?"_
(Surah Nisa: 20)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal ki ayat ke zel mein bataya tha ke ho sakta hai Mard kabhi apni Biwi se na khush rahte huwe bhi unko Maal ki lalach ki bina par zabarsasti rakhte hain aur un par zulm kare aur usko sataye. Isse uske ghar ka mahaul kharab hota hai aur bahut sare nuqsanat ho sakte hain.
Aaj ke Ayat ke mutabiq agar nahi jam raha hai to Talaq de do. Lekin zamana jahiliyat mein agar Mard ko koi doosri Aurat pasand aa gayi to pichhli Biwi se peechha chhodane ke liye woh us par tohmat lagate aur us par sakhti karte taake Aurat apni taraf se Talaq le aur Meher bhi maaf kar de. Allah ne is bure fe'l ki mazzamat ki aur Aurton par zulm se bachaya.
Allah ne Hukm diya aur farmaya ke agar doosri karne ka faisla kar hi liya hai to Mard Aurat se Meher aur uska koi bhi Maal wapas nahi le sakta aur agar Meher nahi diya hai to Talaq ke waqt Meher dena hoga aur uska Maal liya hai to woh bhi wapas karna hoga. Ayat ne insaan ki aql ko jinjhoda hai ke jiske sath tumne itni raazdar zindagi guzari aur itne fida the aaj itne dushman kiyon ho gaye aur uspar tohmat lagane lage!!
Islam ne Aurat ke Huqooq ka zyada khayal rakha hai aur Aurat ko ek khas izzat o azmat di hai
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_'Agar koi shakhs kisi aurat se Nikah uske maal ki wajah se ya uske jamaal (khubsoorati) ki wajah se karega to kabhi Rozi nahi payega. Aur agar wo uske Deen ki wajah se Nikah karega to Allah Ta'ala usko maal aur jamaal dono ki Rozi dega."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p241)
👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi Shaadi kare aur uski Niyyat ye ho ke Meher nahi dega to Allah ke nazdeek wo Zina karne waale ke barabar hai."_
(Namaz ki Tafseer, p93)
👰🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs apni beti ka rishta faasiq (immoral / charitraheen) insaan ko de to goya usne Qat e Rahem kiya aur apni beti ko khandaan se juda kiya."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v1, p92)
👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as)
ki khidmat mein ek aurat haazir huwi aur kaha ke main Shaadi nahi karna chaahti.
Imam (as) ne puchha, _"kyun?"_
Usne kaha, _"Fazilat haasil karne ke liye."_
Imam (as) ne farmaya, _"Laut ja. Agar aisa karne mein (Shaadi na karne mein) fazilat hoti to Hazrat Fatima (sa) tujh se zyada uski haq-daar thi. Koi aurat unpar sabqat (pahel / precedence) na le jaati."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v14, p131)

🕌 *TA'MIR MASJID E QUBA* 🕌
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
♦ _*BETE KA MAA SE NIKAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (496)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَنْكِحُوا مَا نَكَحَ آبَاؤُكُمْ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ إِلَّا مَا قَدْ سَلَفَ ۚ إِنَّهُ كَانَ فَاحِشَةً وَمَقْتًا وَسَاءَ سَبِيلًا*

_"Jin Aurton se tumhare Baap Nikah kar chuke hain unse Nikah na karo magar jo pahle ho chuka wo ho chuka. Ye ek be hayai Fuhush aur Khuda ke Ghazab ka zariya aur badtareen raasta hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 22)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Is ayat ke zel us Arab Jahilayat ka daur ham batate hain jahan haiwaniyat ke alawa kuchh na tha, Quran ne usi ki taraf ishaara kiya hai aur ise behayai aur Fuhush bataya hai. Aur unke raaste ko badtareen raasta bataya hai, Khuda Ghazab hai un par. Ab jo log aise logon ki pairavi karte hain to woh kis rah par ja rahe hain aap samajh sakte hain.
Is Ayat ke zel mein misal ke taur par ye Shajra peshe Khidmat hai jisse Ayat ki aur wazahat ho jayegi:

Khandaane Quraish mein se ek shakhs Nufail ghulam tha Janab Abdul Muttalib ka. Unhi ke yahan ek Kaneez bhi thi jiska naam Sahaak tha jo Sheeps ki dekhbhal karti thi. Dono ka illegal chakkar chala aur unse nikal pada Khattab jisko Janabe Abdul Muttalib ke dar ki wajah se dust bin mein phek diya. Usko ek Yahoodi Aurat ne uthaya aur parvarish kar jawan kiya. Phir kisi tarah Haseen o Jameel Sahaak aur Khattab mein chakkar chal pada (Saahak ko nahi maloom tha ke ye mera hi beta hai.) aur unse nikli Hantama. Usko bhi unhone dar kar kachre mein pheka. Us ladki ko Hisham ibne Mughira ne uthaya aur apni kaneezi mein rakha aur jawan kiya. Khattab ne us ladki ko dekha to uska aashiq ho gaye aur uske Malik Hisham se Nikah ke liye propose kiya. Hantama aur Khattab ki Shaadi hui phir unse paida hua UMAR.
Summary:
- Sahaak +Nufail = Khattab.
- Sahaak +Khattab= Hantama.
- Khattab+Hantama=Umar.

Doosri Sunni rivayat is tarah bhi hai.
"Khattab bin Nufail Quraish mein se tha aur unki Maa Qabila e Fahem ki ek Aurat thi jis nasm Zahaka tha, woh Aurat Nufail ki Biwi thi, jab Nufail mar gaya to us ke baad unke bete Umar bin Nufail ne apni Maa se Shaadi ki. Pas us se Zaid paida hua. Zaid ki Maa aur Khattab ki Maa ek hi hai, ye Zaid us Saeed ka Baap hai jo un mein se hai jinhe (baqaul Ahle Sunnat) Nabi (saww) ne Jannat ki Basharat di."
(Sunni Ref: Al Ma'arif ibne Qateeba, Vol 104, Beirut print,
Shia Ref: Mustadrakat Ilm Rijal Al Hadis by Namazi Shahroodi, Vol 8, P-585.)
(Note:
Ab isko Muajeza ya coincidence kahiye ke hamari Ayat ki sequence mein is Hafta e Bara'at mein wohi Ayat ayi jo Umar ke Shajre ki taraf ishaara kar rahi hai.)
Al Hamdo lillah ke ba taufeeq e Ilahi ham aiso ki pairavi se bach gaye.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Reza (as):
_"Janabe Abdul Muttalib ne 5 Sunnate aisi jari ki thi jinhe Islam aane ke baad Khuda ne bhi jaari rakha. Un mein se ek baat ye thi ke unhone Baap ki Mankooha (Biwi) ko bete par haram qaraar diya tha aur Allah Ta'ala ne bhi uski taeed ki aur farmaya: Ayat (4:22)."_
(Uyoonul Akhbaar, Noorus Saqlain).

           ♦ _*HARAM AURTEN*_ ♦
          *(Jinse Nikah Haram hai)*

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (497) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*حُرِّمَتْ عَلَيْكُمْ أُمَّهَاتُكُمْ وَبَنَاتُكُمْ وَأَخَوَاتُكُمْ وَعَمَّاتُكُمْ وَخَالَاتُكُمْ وَبَنَاتُ الْأَخِ وَبَنَاتُ الْأُخْتِ وَأُمَّهَاتُكُمُ اللَّاتِي أَرْضَعْنَكُمْ وَأَخَوَاتُكُمْ مِنَ الرَّضَاعَةِ وَأُمَّهَاتُ نِسَائِكُمْ وَرَبَائِبُكُمُ اللَّاتِي فِي حُجُورِكُمْ مِنْ نِسَائِكُمُ اللَّاتِي دَخَلْتُمْ بِهِنَّ فَإِنْ لَمْ تَكُونُوا دَخَلْتُمْ بِهِنَّ فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَحَلَائِلُ أَبْنَائِكُمُ الَّذِينَ مِنْ أَصْلَابِكُمْ وَأَنْ تَجْمَعُوا بَيْنَ الْأُخْتَيْنِ إِلَّا مَا قَدْ سَلَفَ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Tum par Haram ki gayi tumhari *Maayen, Behne, Phoophiyan, Khalayen, Bhatijyan, Bhanjiyan* aur tumhari *woh Maayen jinhone ne tumko doodh pilaya* aur tumhari *doodh sharik Behne aur tumhari Biwiyon ki Maayen* aur tumhari un Biwiyon ki ladkiyan jinhone tumhari tumhari god mein parvarish payi hai, jinse tumhare jinsi talluqat (sex) qaem hue hon aur agar tumne unse jinsi talluqat qaem na kiya ho to (inhe chhod kar unki ladkiyon se Nikah kar lene mein) tum par koi harj nahi hai. Tumhari *Sulbi beton ki Biwiyan aur do Behno ka rk sath jama karna* sab Haram hai. Magar jo pahle ho gaya so ho gaya. Yaqeenan Allah Bakhshnewala Rahemkarnewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 23)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Kal Quran ki Ayat ke ek Nikah ke Ahkam ka zikr hua.
Aaj ki Ayat mein un Auraton ki list hai jin se na Nikah kar sakte hain aur na Sexual relation rakh sakte hain.
Iski wazahat following rivayat mein ki gayi hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mere walid ne 34 qism ki sharamgahen (Sex) Haram hain, unmein se kuchh permanent aur kucch temporary Haram hain, 18 Qur'an mein, 16 Sunnat mein:_
_*In Quran:*_
1. Zina (Adultery)
2. Baap ki Biwi se bete ka Nikah.
3. Maayrn (Mothers)
4. Betiyan (Daughters)
5. Behne (Sisters)
6. Phoophiyan (Father's Sisters)
7. Khalayen (Mother's Sisters)
8. Bhatijiyan (Brother's Daughter)
9. Bhanjiyan (Sister's Daughters)
10. Razai Maayen (Suckling Mother)
11. Razai Behne (Suckling Sisters)
12. Saas (Mother in Laws)
13. Jin Biwiyon se jinsi talluq (sex) hua ho uski rahbiya Betiyan.
14. Sulbi Beton ki Biwyan.
15. Ek hi time Do Behno ka jama karna.
16. Shadi Shuda Aurat jo kisi ke Aqd mein ho.
17. Hayez se sex Haram hai.
18. E'tekaaf mein Sex Haram hai.
*In Sunnat:*
1. Mahe Ramzan mein Din mein.
2. La'an لعان ke baad La'an wali Aurat.
3. Iddat mein.
4. Ehram mein karna ya karana.
5. Zahar ظهار ke kaffara se qabl.
6. Mushrekah se.
7. Jis Aurat ko 9 Talaqen de chuka ho.
8. Azad Aurat ku maujoodgi mein Kaneez se.
9. Muslim Aurat ki maujoodgi mein Zimmi Aurat se.
10. Phoophi ki maujoodgi mein Bhatiji se aur Khala ki maujoodgi mein Bhanji.
11. Kaneez ke sarparast ki ijazat ke baghair.
12. Jo Azad Aurat se Shaadi ki qudrat rakhta ho uska Kaneez se Nikah.
13. Maale Ghanimat (War Booty) ki taqseem ke pahle ghanimat mein aane wali Aurat se.
14. Mushrik Kaneez.
15. Zar khaiz Kaneez se istebrai rehm se qabl Nikah.
16. Jis Aurat ne Makatebat ka muaeda kiya ho aur kuchh hissa ada bhi kar chuki ho to usse bhi."
In sab se Sexual relation nahi rakh sakte.
(Kitabul Khisal, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
             ♦ _*MUTAA'*_ ♦
      ( *Temporary Marriage*)
As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (498) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالْمُحْصَنَاتُ مِنَ النِّسَاءِ إِلَّا مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ ۖ كِتَابَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ ۚ وَأُحِلَّ لَكُمْ مَا وَرَاءَ ذَٰلِكُمْ أَنْ تَبْتَغُوا بِأَمْوَالِكُمْ مُحْصِنِينَ غَيْرَ مُسَافِحِينَ ۚ فَمَا اسْتَمْتَعْتُمْ بِهِ مِنْهُنَّ فَآتُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ فَرِيضَةً ۚ وَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِيمَا تَرَاضَيْتُمْ بِهِ مِنْ بَعْدِ الْفَرِيضَةِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aur Shaadi shuda Aurten bhi tum par Haram hain alawa unke jo tumhari Kaneezi mein aa jayen. Yeh Allah ka Qanoon hai jiski pabandi tumhare liye lazim kar di gayi hai. Unke ma siwa jitni Aurten hain unhe apne Amwal ke zariye se hasil karna tumhare liye Halal kar diya gaya hai basharteke unhe hisaar e Nikah (bounding) mein Mehfooz karo. Sirf Shehwat rani (Sexual Desire) maqsood na ho. Pas un mein se jin Aurton se tum ne Mutaa' kiya hai unki ujrat bataur farz unko ada karo. Meher ki qarardad (Marriage Certificate) ke baad bahami razamandi (Mutual Consent) se tumhare darmiyan samjhota ho jaye to us mein tumhare liye koi harj nahi hai. Beshak Allah Aleem o Hakim hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 24)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein jin baton ka tazkara hua hai woh yeh hai:
- Shaadi Shuda Aurat se Nikah Haraam hai except Kaneez.
- Jin Aurton se Allah ne Nikah Haraam kiya hai unhe chhod kar baqi sab Aurton se Nikah jaez hai. Condition ye hai ke baqaeda Nikah aur likha padhi ho Meher sath. (Aise hi na le ke bhage)
- Ek Temporary Marriage (Mutaa') ka zikr hai.
_*MUTAA' (Temporary Marriage):*_
Insaan max. 4 Aurten rakh sakta hai kuchh sharat ke sath. Lekin iske alawa Mard ek Temporary Marriage bhi kar sakta hai kuchh sharaet ke sath. At present is par sirf Shia amal karte hain. Ahle Sunnat is se inkar karte hai.
Kuchh mutarjameen Qur'an mein is Ayat mein word استمتعتم ka lafzi tarjuma karte hain: 'Aurat se fayda uthane aur unke Meher dene ki baat'. Jabke ye word hai متع se drive hua hai.
Tafseer par tawajjoh de to ye baten samne aati hain:
1. Ye Ayat Temporary Marriage (Mutaa') ki takeed karti hai.
2. Is qism ki Shaadiya Rasool (saww) ke zamaane mein hoti thi jisko Allah ne sahi qarar diya.
3. Is qism ki Shaadi ki Society mein Ijtemai Zaroorat bhi hai.
4. Mutaa' se bahut se buriyon ke problem solve ho jate hain.
Tarikh mein milta hai buzurg Ashab aur Tabaeen maslan Abdullah ibne Abbas, Ubai ibne Ka'ab, Jabir bin Abdullah, Imran bin Haseen, Saeed bin Jubair, Mujahid, Qatada, Sadi - in sab ne is Ayat se Nikah e Mutaa' se murad liya hai. Mufassarin Ahle Sunnat aur Mufasserin Ahle Bait (as) ne bhi yehi meaning liya. Yahan tak ke Imam Fakhre Raazi ne iski tafseeli bahes ki hai aur isko Mutaa' ke baare mein hi bataya lekin kaha ke ye Ayat mansookh ho gayi.
Lekin tamam ka ye ittefaq hai ke ye Ayat Mutaa' ke baare mein hai lekin Ahle Sunnat hazrat isliye isko amal mein nahi laate wo is rivayat ki wajah se:
Umar ne kaha:
*متعتان كانتا على عهد رسول الله و انا محرمها و معاقب عليها متعة النساء و متعة الحج.*
_"Mutaa' Paighambar (saww) ke ahde Mubarak mein the, inhe mein (Umar) Haraam karta hun aur un par Saza bhi dunga Aurton se Mutaa' aur Hajje Tamatto"_
(Kanzul Irfan, Vol 2, P-158, Tafseer e Qartabi, Tabari, Sunan e Kubra, Behqi in Kitabun Nikah)
Is quote se zahir hai jis cheez ko Rasool (saww) aur Qur'an ne Halaal kiya tha usko baad mein Haraam kar diya gaye.
Mutaa' sexual crime ko khatm karta hai. Zina nahi hote. Isse Mard ke fitri taqaze poore hote hain.   Illegal sexual crime mein kami hoti hain. Aurat ki safety hai. Ye legal tareeqa hai.
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Ye Ayat Mutaa' ke mutalliq nazil hui aur is mein Allah Ta'ala ne Musalmano ko hukm diya ke unhone jin Aurton se Mutaa' kiya hai Woh unhe unka Haq e Meher farz samajh kar ada karen aur agar Mutaa' ki miaad (time) puri ho jaye to zaujain ko ikhtiyar hai ke woh bahami razamandi se muddat mein tausee' (extension) kar sakte hain aur jab Mutaa' ka time mukammal ho jaye to Mamtuaa' Aurat us waqt tak doosre ke liye Halal nahi hogi jab tak woh do baar Mahwari (Mensuration) na dekh le."_
Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya kiya is mein bhi 4 ki limit hai? Aap (as) ne farmaya: _"Nahi, ye to ek tarah ka ijarah hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
Detail Ahkam Tauzeeh  mein refer kar sakte hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
*المتعة نزل به القران و جرت بها السنة من رسول الله.*
_"Mutaa' ka hukm Qur'an mein nazil hua hai. Aur Sunnat e Rasool iske mutabiq jari hui."_
👰🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
Abdullah bin Umairishi ke jawab mein farmaya:
*احلها الله فى كتابه و على لسان نبيه فهى حلال الى يوم القيامة.*
_"Khuda wanda Alam ne ise Qur'an mein apne Paighambar (saww) ki zaban par Halaal kiya aur woh Qayamat tak Halaal hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-467, Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-360)

       ♦ _*KANEEZ SE NIKAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (499) 💏

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ لَمْ يَسْتَطِعْ مِنْكُمْ طَوْلًا أَنْ يَنْكِحَ الْمُحْصَنَاتِ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ فَمِنْ مَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ مِنْ فَتَيَاتِكُمُ الْمُؤْمِنَاتِ ۚ وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِإِيمَانِكُمْ ۚ بَعْضُكُمْ مِنْ بَعْضٍ ۚ فَانْكِحُوهُنَّ بِإِذْنِ أَهْلِهِنَّ وَآتُوهُنَّ أُجُورَهُنَّ بِالْمَعْرُوفِ مُحْصَنَاتٍ غَيْرَ مُسَافِحَاتٍ وَلَا مُتَّخِذَاتِ أَخْدَانٍ ۚ فَإِذَا أُحْصِنَّ فَإِنْ أَتَيْنَ بِفَاحِشَةٍ فَعَلَيْهِنَّ نِصْفُ مَا عَلَى الْمُحْصَنَاتِ مِنَ الْعَذَابِ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ لِمَنْ خَشِيَ الْعَنَتَ مِنْكُمْ ۚ وَأَنْ تَصْبِرُوا خَيْرٌ لَكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ غَفُورٌ رَحِيمٌ*

_"Jiske paas Azaad Mo'min Aurton se Nikah karne ki Maali wus'at (Financial capacity) na ho to woh Mo'mina Kaneez Aurat se Nikah kar le. Khuda tumhare Imaan se bakhabar hai. Tum sab ek hi giroh se talluq rakhte ho. Lehaza unke sarparaston ki ijazat se unke sath Nikah karlo aur Ma'aroof tareeqe se unka Mehr ada karo taake woh hisaare Nikah mein mehfooz ho kar rahen. Azad Shehwat rani na karti phiren aur na chori chhupe Aashnaiyan (love affair) karen. Phir jab woh hisaar e Nikah mein mehfooz ho jayen aur uske baad badchalani (fuhush) karen to un par us saza ki ba nisbat aadhi saza hai jo azad Aurton ke liye muqarrar hai. Ye ijazat un logon ke liye hai jinhen ye khadsha ho ke Shaadi ne hone se unki iffat (Modesty) ka band toot jayega. Agar tum Sabr karo to ye tumhare liye behtar hai aur Allah Bakhnewala, Meherban hai"_
(Surah Nisa: 25)

📚📖 👰🏻💏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ab jo logo ka joda kahin nahi lag pata, status nahi milta, khaandan alag hain, Maal nahi hain etc.. to Allah ne Kaneezon se bhi Nikah jayez kiya hai. Kaneez means female ghulam, permanent naukaraniyan jaise ke pahle dastoor tha. Lekin ye riwaaj aaj ke zamane mein nahi hai. Kaneez ka status low nicha mana jata tha.
Lekin jaisa ke ham Buzurgane Deen ke baare mein padhte hain ke unki biwi Kaneez thi, ya unki maa kaneez thi. To ye kaneezen doosri aam kaneezon se alag hasiyat rakhti thi, woh alag Imaan ke darje par faez thi, Janabe Fatema (sa) ki Kaneez Janab e Fizza (sa) iski Aala misal hain. Unka ek Exceptional Status tha.
Is Ayat mein Shaadi karni ki zyada takeed ki hai, karo kaise bhi karo, chahe Kaneez se hi karo. Kiyonki ek Naujawan ki agar Shaadi karne mein deri ki to woh jaisa ke khud Qur'an ishaara kar raha hai ke woh kahin bhi illegal love affair mein phans sakta hai, us waqt parent ka hath malne ke siwa koi chara na hoga.  
Baqi Shaadi ke Ahkam Tauzeehul Masael mein bayan kiye gaye hain refer kar sakte hain. Ham bhi Ahkam Section mein kuchh waqt pahle English mein part by part post kar chuke hain.
Is baat par mutawajjah hon ke Insaan ki har aadaton ko Qur'an ne ujagar kar diya. Isliye Qur'an hamre liye rahe hidayat hai.
Inshallah aap hamari is series ko lagatar padhte rahenge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💏
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs ghurbat (gareebi) ke darr se shaadi nahi karta ho aisa shakhs Khuda se Su e Zann (negative opinion) rakhta hai, kyun ki Khuda ne farmaya, "Nikah karo, ke Khuda Wande Aalam tumhe Apne fazl o karam se Rozi ataa kare aur tumhe Gani kare"._
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v1, p91)
👰🏻 💏
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Nek aur paak-daaman qabile (khandaan) mein Shaadi karo, kyun ki maa-baap ke akhlaaq aulaad mein muntaqil (transfer) hote hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p493)
👰🏻 💏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi shakhs kisi aurat se Nikah uske maal ki wajah se ya uske jamaal (khubsoorati) ki wajah se karega to kabhi Rozi nahi payega. Aur agar wo uske Deen ki wajah se Nikah karega to Allah Ta'ala usko maal aur jamaal dono ki Rozi dega."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p241)

        ♦ _*AHKAM E KHUDA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (500) 📜

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ لِيُبَيِّنَ لَكُمْ وَيَهْدِيَكُمْ سُنَنَ الَّذِينَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ وَيَتُوبَ عَلَيْكُمْ ۗ وَاللَّهُ عَلِيمٌ حَكِيمٌ*

_"Khuda chahta hai ke tumhare liye wazeh Ahkam bayan karde aur tumhe tumse pahle walon ki rah dikhlaye aur tumhari Toba qubool kare. Allah khoob janne wala aur Hikmat wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 26)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Abhi tak Nikah aur Aurton ke Ahkam ki Ayaton ka Qur'an mein zikr ho raha tha, jabke Quran ka one third hissa Fiqhi Ahkam bhi hai.
Insaan ye sochta hai ke kiyon ye sab Islami Qanooni pabandiya lagayi jati hain. Allah ko hame Azad chhod dena chahiye, ham jaise chahe kuchh bhi karen. Jaise Western System mein sab Azaad, Aurten Azaad ghoomti hain, kisi ki koi rok tok nahi. Aur Islam ne to Aurat ko qaidi bana diya hai. In sab sawalon se Islam ko ek ghulami ka mazhab qarar dete hain, ye daqyanoosi mazhab hai, is modern aur Advanced zamane mein iski koi jagah nahi.
Allah ne in sab sawalon ka jawab is Ayat mein de diya. Means jo bhi Ahkam Allah ne bayan kiye hamare fayde ke liye. Agar traffic ka koi rules na ho aur sab ko Azad kar diya jaye ke kaise bhi drive karen, natija kiya niklega na to koi apni manzil tak pahunch payega, accident betahasha honge, afra tafri ka mahaul ho jayega. To aap batayi dono mein se kiya behtar hai strict rules ya freedom.
Isiliye Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai ke ye System pahli bhi tha, tumhare liye koi naya nahi. Nahi to Duniya kab ki khatm ho gayi hoti. Lekin agar koi anjane mein gunah kar baithta hai to Woh Tauba Qubool bhi kar sakta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕯📚
Baqirul Uloom Imam Mohd Baqir (as)
_"Mujhe logon ke haal par tajjub hai ke woh chand qatarat par guzar rahe hain aur Azeem Nehr ko chhode hue hain!!_
Sawal kiya 'Nehr' kiya hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Rasoole Khuda (saww) Ilm ki Azeem Nehr hain. Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Adam (as) se lekar Hazrat Esa (as) tak unke liye tamam Anbiya ke Sunan jama kiye the."_
Sawal kiya 'Sunan' kiya hai?
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tamam Anbiya (as) ka unhe Ilm (Knowledge) diya gaya. Rasoole Akram (saww) ne woh sara Ilm Ameerul Mo'menin Ali (as) ke sipurd kiya tha."_
Phir sawal kiya ke kis ke pas zyada Ilm tha Rasoole Khuda (saww) ya Ali (as).
Imam (as) ne jawab diya jab tamam Anbiya (as) ka Ilm Rasoole Khuda (saww) mein aa gaya aur Rasool (saww) ne woh Ilm Ali (as) ke hawale kar diya to khud hi samajh lena chahiye."
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

                ♦ _*TAUBA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (501) 🙏🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاللَّهُ يُرِيدُ أَنْ يَتُوبَ عَلَيْكُمْ وَيُرِيدُ الَّذِينَ يَتَّبِعُونَ الشَّهَوَاتِ أَنْ تَمِيلُوا مَيْلًا عَظِيمًا * يُرِيدُ اللَّهُ أَنْ يُخَفِّفَ عَنْكُمْ ۚ وَخُلِقَ الْإِنْسَانُ ضَعِيفًا*
[Surat An-Nisa' 27 - 28]

_"Aur Allah chahta hai ke tumhari Tauba qubool kare aur khwahishat ke pairokar chahte hain ke tum rahe rast se hat kar door nikal jao. Allah to chahta hai ke tumhare liye takhfeef (light-halka) ka samaan kare kiyonki Insaan kamzor paida kiya gaya hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 27-28)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Mandarja bala Ayat mein ye bayan ho raha hai ke Allah to chahta ke jab ham Tauba karen to hamari Tauba qubool kare. Lekin Tauba ki shart ye hai ke jo bhi hamne gunah kiya hai us par pasheman hon aur ainda bhi koi gunah ka irada na ho. Agar is khuloos se ham Dua karenge to Allah kiyon nahi qubool karega.
Aaj Jumeraat hai, Due e Kumail ki bahut zyada fazilat hai. Ye Dua jo Hazrat Ali (as) ne apne sahabi Kumail bin Ziyad ko ta'leem farmayi. Iske tarjuma par dhiyan den.
Allah ke banda jab Huzoor e Ilahi mein pesh hota hai, kis tarah ye apne Parwardegar se samne gidgidata hai, kis tarah bayan karta hai. Is Dua ke har fiqre mein gahre matalib chhupe hain.
Aaj ki Ayat se related Dua ke kuchh fiqro par dhiyan den:

*اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَهتِكُ الْعِصَمَ*
_"Khudaya! Mere un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo NAMOOS ko batta laga dete hain."_

*اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ النِّقَمَ*
_"Khudaya! Un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo NUZOOL E AZAAB ka baes (cause) hain."_

*اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُغيِّرُ النِّعَمَ*
_"Khudaya! Un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo NE'MATON KO MUTAGAYYIR (Change) kar diya karte hai."_

*اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَحْبِسُ الدُّعَاءَ*
_"Khudaya! U  Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo DUA'ON ko Teri Bargah tak pahunchne se rok dete hain."_

*اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَقْطَعُ الرََّّجَاءَ*
_"Khudaya! Un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo UMEEDON ko muqata (cut) kar dete hain."_

*اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ البَلاءَ*
_"Khudaya! Un Gunahon ko bakhsh de jo NUZOOL E BALA ka sabab (cause) hote hain."_

*اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي كُلَّ ذَنْبٍ أَذْنَبْتُهُ وَكُلَّ خَطِيئَةٍ أَخْطَأْتُهَا*
_"Khudaya! Mere tamam Gunahon aur Khataon * bakhsh de."_

Is mein woh Gunahon ke asarat (effects) bayan kar diye jo insaan ki zindagi mein asar andaz hote hain.

Phir banda wohi dohrata jo Allah ne zikr kiye ke insaan to zaeef hai. Kaise woh itne Gunahon ka Azaab bardasht kar sakta hai.
Shahwat zada Duniya is bande ko gande rah par khechti rahti hai. Mushkil hai Aisi quwwat se is zaeef insaan ka muqabala karna, isliya anjane mein khata kar baithta hai. Isliye Allah ne Tauba ka darwaza khol rakha.
Isi baat ko isi Dua mein is tarah bayan karta hai:

*يَا رَبِّ ارْحَمْ ضَعْفَ بَدَنِي وَرِقَّةَ جِلْدِي وَدِقَّةَ عَظْمِي*
_"Parwardegar! Mere badan ki kamzori, mere jild (skin) ki narmi, aur mere haddiyon ki barikiyon par Rahem farma."_

Phir aage bayan karta hai:
*يَا كَرِيمُ، يَا رَبِّ*

*وَأَنتَ تَعْلَمُ ضَعْفِي عَن قَلِيلٍ مِّن بَلاءِ الدُّنْيَا وَعُقُوبَاتِهَا،*

_" Aye Karim, Parwardegar! Tu jaanta hai ke mein Duniya ki mamooli Bala aur adna si sakhti ko bardasht nahi kar sakta..."_
*يَا سَيِّدِي فَكَيْفَ بِي*
*وَأَنَا عَبْدُكَ الضَّعِيفُ الذَّلِيلُ الْحَقِيرُ الْمِسْكِينُ الْمُسْتَكِينُ*

_"Ay mere Malik, mein kaisi bardasht kar sakta hun..._
_Mein ek Banda e Zaeef (Weak), Zaleel (lowly), Haqeer (wretched), Miskeen o bechara (miser) ki hasiyat rakhta hun."_
(Dua-e-Kumail)

Is tarah banda Dua mangta hai. Zyada tafseel ki yahan gunjaish nahi. Readers se guzarish hai is Dua ke tarjume ko padhen aur kuchh sabaq hasil karke us par Amal karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Aye Maabud! Jab bhi main kehta hoo'n ke main aamada aur taiyar hoo'n aur Tere huzoor mein Namaz padhne ko khada hota hoo'n aur Tujh se munajaat karta hoo'n, to mujhe oo'ngh aane lagti hai. Jab ke main Namaz mein hota hoo'n aur jab main Tujh se raaz o niyaaz karne lagu'n to oos haal mein bar-qaraar nahi rehta. Mujhe kya ho gaya? Main kehta hoo'n ke mera baatil saaf hai. Main Tauba karne waalo'n ki sohbat mein baithh-ta hoo'n aise mein koi aafat aa padd-ti hai jis se mere qadam dagmaga jaate hain aur mere Teri huzoor ke darmiyaan koi cheez aadd ban jaati hai. Mere Sardaar! Shayad ke Tu ne mujhe Apni bargaah se hata diya aur Apni khidmat se door kar diya hai. Ya shayad Tu ne dekha ke maine Tujh se mu'nh pher liya hai to mujhe bura samajh liya. Shayad Tu ne dekha ke main jhooto'n mein se hoo'n, to mujhe mere haal par chhor diya. Ya shayad, Tu dekhta hai ke main Teri ne'mato'n ka shukr adaa nahi karta to mujhe mehroom kar diya hai. Ya shayad Tu ne mujhe Ulema ki majlis (gathering) mein nahi paaya to oos bina par Tu ne mujhe zaleel kar diya hai. Ya shayad Tu ne mujhe gaafil dekha to uspar mujhe Apni Rehmat se maayus kar diya hai. Ya shayad Tu ne mujhe bekaar ki baatein karne waalo'n mein dekh to mujhe unhi mein rehne diya. Ya shayad, Tu meri Dua ko sun'na pasand nahi karta to mujhe parey kar diya. Shayad Tu ne mujhe mere jurm o gunah ka badla diya hai. Ya shayad maine Tujh se hayaa karne mein kami ki, to mujhe ye sazaa mili.
(Dua e Abu Hamza Sumaali)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*21st Rabiul Awwl 1438*
22nd December 2016, Thursday,

               ♦ _*MAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (502) 💰

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَأْكُلُوا أَمْوَالَكُمْ بَيْنَكُمْ بِالْبَاطِلِ إِلَّا أَنْ تَكُونَ تِجَارَةً عَنْ تَرَاضٍ مِنْكُمْ ۚ وَلَا تَقْتُلُوا أَنْفُسَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِكُمْ رَحِيمًا*

_"Aye Imaan walo! Apas mein ek doosre ke Maal batil tareeqon se na khao. Magar ye ke bahami (mutual) razamandi se len den ho aur apne aap ko qatl na karo. Yaqeenan Allah tum par Meherban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 29)

📚📖 💰
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tijarat (Business) ke len den (transactions) se jo nafa (profit) hasil hota hai wo Halal hai. Lekin kisi Maal ghasb karna Haram hai. Isi ke sath Allah Ta'ala ne ye bhi farmaya ke apne aap ko qatl na karo. Is hukm ka maqsad ye hai ke ek doosre ko qatl na karo kiyonki Islam mein poori Ummat ko Nafs e Waheda tasawwur kiya jata hai. Apne kisi Musalman bhai ko na-haq qatl na karo.
Doosra mafhoom hai Khud Kashi na karo. Khud Kashi ek Zahiri hoti hai aur doosre Batini. Zahiri jo sab ko pata hai, Haram hai. Lekin Batini jaise Drug ka istemal jiska result Maut hota hai. Har slow poison wali cheezen. Koi kisi ke qatl ka badla le raha hai jisme wo khud mar jai. Shadi shuda shakhs agar badkari kare to rajm (kode) ka mustaheq ho jata hai. Ye sab Haram hai.
Is Ayat ki taujeeh aise bhi hoti hai ke apne Ahle Ma'ashre (Society) ki loot khasot karke inhe Ma'ashi (Financially) taur par qatl na karo.
Isi tarah kisi ka qarz wapas na dena, woh bhi Harram hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Sama'aa bin Mehran ne Imam Sadiq (as) se arz kiya:
Ek Shakh maqrooz ho aur uske pas thodi si daulat ho jis se basad mushkil apni guzar basar kar raha ho, kiya wo apne bachcho ko khana khilaye ya Qarz ada kare? Agar woh Qarz wapas karta hai to use logon se mazeed Qarz lena padta hai ya phir use majbooran Sadaqa qubool karna padta hai. Aise shakhs ke liye kiya hukm hai?
Imam (as) ne jawab mein farmaya:
_"Use chahiye ke woh Qarz ada kare aur logon ka Maal na khai ya uske pas itna sarmaya ho jisse logo ke huqooq ada kar sakta ho. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ka farman hai: (4:29)."_
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo apne bhai ka Maal khayega aur wapas nahi karega wo Qayamat ke din Aag ke bhadakte huwe angaare kha raha hoga."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)

               ♦ _*ZULM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (503)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَٰلِكَ عُدْوَانًا وَظُلْمًا فَسَوْفَ نُصْلِيهِ نَارًا ۚ وَكَانَ ذَٰلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Zulm o ziyadti se aisa iqdam karega to ham usko zaroor aag mein jhonkenge aur ye Allah ke liye ye kaam bada asaan hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 30)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal jo Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke apne Muslim Society mein loot khasot kar ke unka Maal na khao, aisa karna apne aap ko qatl karna hai. Is baat ko jari rakhte hue Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai jo aisa zulm karega usko Jahannam ki Aag mein jhonk diya jayega. Allah Zulm ko pasand nahi karta.

     ♦ _*GUNAH-E-KABEERA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (504)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنْ تَجْتَنِبُوا كَبَائِرَ مَا تُنْهَوْنَ عَنْهُ نُكَفِّرْ عَنْكُمْ سَيِّئَاتِكُمْ وَنُدْخِلْكُمْ مُدْخَلًا كَرِيمًا*

_"Agar tum un Gunahane Kabeera (Bade Gunah) se bachte rahe jin se tumhe roka ja raha hai to ham tumhari chhoti moti khataon ko tumhare hisab se saqit (ignore) kar denge aur tum ko izzat ke maqam mein dakhil karenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 31)

📚📖 🎄
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Islam ka concept Christianity ke barkhilaf hai. Christian aisa mante hain ke ham kitne bhi Gunah karen, Hazrat Esa (as) hamari taraf se qurban ho gaye aur poori ummat ke gunah maaf kar diye aur ab wo azaad hain. Is concept ka wo zyada prachar kar ke gairon ko apni taraf ghaseette hain, attract karte hain, means Christianity apna ke ab kitne bhi Gunah karo!!!!
Allah is ayat mein bhi farma raha hai ke Insaan Gunahe Kabeera ko agar tark kar de to ho sakta hai Allah chhote mote gunahon ko maaf kar de aur baizzat use Jannat mein dakhil kar de.
🎄 _*Gunahan-e-Kabeera:*_ 🎄
-----------------------------------
Alqama Hazrami, Abu Hisan Al Ajali, Abdullah bin Ajalan ne Imam Mohd Baqir (as) ki Ziyarat ki tab Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Apne Nufoos ko munawwar karo. Agar tum Gunahane Kabeera ka irtekab nahi kiya hai to mein tumhe Jannat ki zamanat deta hun."_
Gunahe Kabeera kiya hain.
Imam (as) ne farmaya Allah ki Kitab mein 7 hain:
"(1) Allah ke sath Shirk.
(2) Yateem ka Maal khaana.
(3) Sood (Interest) khana.
(4) Waledain ki nafarmani.
(5) Jihad se farar.
(6) Momin ka Qatl.
(7) Shareef Aurat par Ilzam tarashi.
_Agar ham in Gunahon se azad hain to phir Jannati hain."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Ye 7 main hain aur iske alawa ye bhi hain:
🎄
Imam e Sadiq (as):
_"Qur'an mein Gunahe Kabeera:_
(1) Shirk (Maeda: 72)
(2) Allah ki tadbeer se be Khauf. (Aaraf:99)
(3) Khuda ki Rehmat se Mayoosi. (Yusuf: 87)
(4) Waledain ki nafarmani. (Maryam: 32)
(5) Qatle Na Haq. (Nisa: 94)
(6) Sharif Aurat par Ilzam tarashi. (Noor: 23)
(7) Yateem ka Maal khana. (Nisa: 10)
(8) Jihad se farar. (Anfal: 16)
(9) Sood khana. (Baqarah: 275)
(10) Jadoo karna. (Baqarah: 102)
(11) Zina. (Furqaan: 68-69)
(12) Jhooti Qasam khana. (Ale Imraan: 77)
(13) Khayanat Karna. (Ale Imraan: 161)
(14) Wajib Zakat Ada na karna. (Tauba: 35)
(15, 16) Jhooti Gawahi dena. sachchi gawahi ko chhupana. (Baqarah: 283)
Isi tarah Sharab Noshi, Juwa bazi jo fele Shaitan hain, Tarke Namaz aur tarke deegar faraiz bhi Gunahe Kabeera hain."
(Uyoonul Akhbar from Imam Reza (as) Raavi: Mutakallim Amr bin Abeed Basari)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🎄
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar Gunahaan e Kabeera se insaan parhez karta ho to ek Namaz se doosri Namaz tak jitne gunah e sagheerah honge to Namaz unka kaffara ho jaayegi."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p16)
🎄
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Astagfaar ke saath Kabeera Gunah kabeera nahi aur israar (persistence) ke saath Sagheera (chhote) Gunah sagheera nahi hai (takraar [repetition / dohraana] Sagheera ko Kabeera bana deti hai)."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p131)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*TAMANNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (505) 😱

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَتَمَنَّوْا مَا فَضَّلَ اللَّهُ بِهِ بَعْضَكُمْ عَلَىٰ بَعْضٍ ۚ لِلرِّجَالِ نَصِيبٌ مِمَّا اكْتَسَبُوا ۖ وَلِلنِّسَاءِ نَصِيبٌ مِمَّا اكْتَسَبْنَ ۚ وَاسْأَلُوا اللَّهَ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمًا*

_"Aur Khuda ne jo baaz ko baaz se kuchh zyada diya hai, uski Tamanna aur Aarzoo na karo. Jo kuchh Mardon ne kamaya hai uske mutabiq unka hissa hai aur jo kuchh Aurton ne kamaya hai uske mutabiq unka hissa hai. Haan Allah se Uske Fazl ki darkhwast karte raho. Yaqeenan Allah har cheez ka janne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 32)

📚📖 😱
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke kisi ko ye nahi kahna chahiye ke Aye Kaash!!! Mujhe bhi falan ki tarah se Daulat, Nemat aur Haseen Biwi mili hoti. Kiyonki ye Hasad (Jealousy) hai, iske bajai Khuda se ye request karni chahiye ke: Parwardigar! Jaisa Toone use Nemat ata ki hai waisi Nemat mujhe ata kar. Yehi Imam Sadiq (as) ki hadis bhi hai. Mazeed mein rivayaten mulaheza farmayen:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😱
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Jab koi kisi cheez ki Tamanna kare aur us mein Allah ki Raza bhi muzmir ho to woh Duniya se us waqt tak rehlat nahi karega jab tak us Nemat ko hasil na kar le."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
(e.g. jaise Ziyarate qabre Imam Husain (as) ki Tamanna karna.)
😱
Imam Ali (as):
_"Jo zyada aarzu rakhta ho usay zyada mushkilaat ka saamna karna padta hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p234)
😱
Imam Ali (as):
_"Aqalmand apni koshish par bharosa karta hai aur Jaahil apni aarzu'on aur tamannao'n par bharosa karta hai."_
(Nahjul Balagah)
🙌🏻 👏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Raavi Maisar bin Abdul Aziz)
_"Maisar! Khuda se mangte raho. Ye na kahna ke Taqdeer ke tahet Ma'amelat ka faisla ho chuka hai. Aur ab Dua be sood (not useful) hai. Yad rakho! Allah ke pas ek Manzelat hai jise Sawal kiye baghair hasil nahi kiya ja sakta. Agar Aadmi apna moo band rakhe aur Sawal hi na kare to use kuchh bhi nahi milega. Lehaza Sawal karo, Muraad pao."_
_"Maisar! Yad rakho, jab koi Darwaza bar bar khatkhataya jaega, to Akhirkar khul hi jayega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
😱

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)

              ♦ _*WIRASAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (506) 📜

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِكُلٍّ جَعَلْنَا مَوَالِيَ مِمَّا تَرَكَ الْوَالِدَانِ وَالْأَقْرَبُونَ ۚ وَالَّذِينَ عَقَدَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ فَآتُوهُمْ نَصِيبَهُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ شَهِيدًا*

_"Hamne har us Tarke ke Haqdar muqarrar kiye hain jo Waledain aur Qareebi Rishtedar chhod jayen aur jinse tumne Ahd o Paiman kiya hai, unka hissa bhi inhe de do. Beshak Allah har cheez par Nigran hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 33)

📚📖 📜
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya ke Waledain ki Aulad aur Qareebi Rishtedar Waaris hote hain. Iske baad Khuda ne farmaya jinse tumne Ahd liya hai unhe bhi meeras mein hissa do.
Kuchh mufasserin ke mutabiq Ayat ka doosra hissa mansookh hai lekin kuchh ke nazdeek mansookh nahi hai. Ayat ka doosra hissa Ahd o Paiman ka talluq zamana jahiliyyat se hai. Jisko log palak karte the usko apne waarison mein dakhil samajhte the. Iski Khuda ne is Ayat se mumane'at (Stop) kar di aur ek rivayat mein hai ke ibteda Islam mein aksar log  Rasool e Khuda (sa) par akele Imaan laate the aur baqi aqroba (relatives) unke Kafir rahte to Rasoolullah (saww) ne tamam musalmano mein jo jis ke jod ka tha baham ek doosre ka bhai bana diya. Chunanche khud ne Hazrat Ali (as) se bhai chara kiya. Magar jab unke aqroba bhi Musalman ho gaye to ye ayat nazil hui.
Jab Allah ka farman hai ke waris ko unka Haq do. To phir kiyon Hazrat Ali (as) aur Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke waris the unko unka Haq nahi diya gaya? Ye sawal ta qayamat baqi rahega.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Musa Kazim (as)
(Raavi: Hasan bin Mehboob)
*وَالَّذِينَ عَقَدَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ فَآتُوهُمْ نَصِيبَهُم*
Ayat ke is part ke bare mein poochhne par farmaya:
_"Is se Aimma (as) muraad hain. Allah ne unse tumhara Ahd o Paiman kiya hai."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
📜
Ayesha:
_"Janabe Fatima (sa) binte Rasul (saww) ne Abu Bakr ke paas kisi ko bheja aur apni miraas ka mutaleba kiya Rasul (saww) ke oos maal se jo aap ko Allah Ta'ala Madina aur Fadak mein inayat farmaya tha aur Khaibar ka jo paanchwa hissa reh gaya tha. Abu Bakr ne ye jawaab diya ke Rasul (saww) ne khud hi irshaad farmaya tha ke 'Hum Paigambaro'n ka koi waaris nahi hota'…Abu Bakr ne Fatima (sa) ko kuchh bhi dena manzoor na kiya. Is par Fatima (sa) Abu Bakr se khafa / na-raaz ho gayi'n aur unse milna tark kar liya aur uske baad wafaat tak unse koi guftagu nahi ki…"_
(Sahih Bukhari, v5, ch 59, h4240)
📜
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
(Raavi: Miswaar bin Makhrana)
_"Fatema (sa) mera tukda hai, jisne ise naraz kiya usne mujhe naraz kiya."_
(Sahih Bukhari, Book 57, Hadia 61)

              ♦ _*MARD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (507) 👱🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الرِّجَالُ قَوَّامُونَ عَلَى النِّسَاءِ بِمَا فَضَّلَ اللَّهُ بَعْضَهُمْ عَلَىٰ بَعْضٍ وَبِمَا أَنْفَقُوا مِنْ أَمْوَالِهِمْ ۚ فَالصَّالِحَاتُ قَانِتَاتٌ حَافِظَاتٌ لِلْغَيْبِ بِمَا حَفِظَ اللَّهُ ۚ وَاللَّاتِي تَخَافُونَ نُشُوزَهُنَّ فَعِظُوهُنَّ وَاهْجُرُوهُنَّ فِي الْمَضَاجِعِ وَاضْرِبُوهُنَّ ۖ فَإِنْ أَطَعْنَكُمْ فَلَا تَبْغُوا عَلَيْهِنَّ سَبِيلًا ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلِيًّا كَبِيرًا*

_"Mard Aurton ke Hakim aur Nigran hain. In fazilatonnki bina par jo Khuda ne kuchh ko kuchh par di hain aur is bina par ke unhone Aurton par apna Maal kharch kiya hai pas jo Nek Aurten hain woh ita'at shua'ar (obedient) hoti hain aur unki ghaibat (absence) mein un cheezon ki hifazat karti hain jinki Khuda ne hifazat chahi hai. Aur jin Aurton se tumhe Nafarmani ka andesha ho unhe nasihat karo aur khwab gahon mein un se alaihda raho aur maro. Iske baad agar woh tumhari ita'at (obedience) karne lagen to ziyadti ki koi rah talash na karo. Yaqeenan Khuda bahut Buland o Bala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 34)

📚📖 👱🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah Ta'ala ne Mardon ko Aurton ka Hakim qarar diya hai. Iski do wujuhat hain:
(1) Khuda ne unko Fazilat di hai. In mein se kuchh _Haqeeqi Sifat_ hain aur kuchh _Ahkam e Sharaii_ hain. Haqeeqi Fazail ka daromadar Ilm o Qudrat se hai. Mardon ko ye Aurton se zyada rahti hai. Isi liye sare Anbiya wa Imam Mard hi the. Yahan tak ke Pesh Imam bhi, Qazi bhi Mard hi hota hai.
(2) Mard Auton ka kharch uthata hai. Meher deta hai. Naan o Nafqa uske zimme hai.
Imam Reza (as):
_"Meeras mein Aurat ko Mard ki ba nisbat aadha hissa diya gaya hai to iski wajah ye hai ke jab Aurat ki Shaadi ho jati hai to uske Naan o Nafqa ki zimmedari uske Shauhar par aaid ho jati hai. Mard ne chunke Biwi ko Naan o Nafqa faraham karna hota isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne use Meeras mein zyada hissa ata kiya. Aur uski wajah ye hai ke Aurat ki kifalat Mard ki zimmedari hoti hai jabke Aurat par Mard ki kifalat farz nahi hai aur bawaqte zaroorat Aurat par wajib nahi hai ke woh Mard ki kifalat kare. Isi haqeeqat ko is ayat mein bayan kiya hai. (4:34)"_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
👱🏻
Hazrat Ali (as) se manqool hai ke Yahoodi ke ek giroh ko unke sawal par jawab dete hue
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne farmaya:

_"Mard ko Aurton par itni Fazilat hai jitni Aasman ko Zameen par hai, pani Zamern ko zindagi deta hai usi tarah Mard bhi Aurton ko zindagi dete hain. Agar Duniya mein Mard na hote to Allah Auton ko paida hi nahi karta. (4:34)_
_Allah ne Adam ko Mitti se paida kiya aur uski bachi hui mitti se Hawwa ko paida kiya. Aurton ki ita'at (follow) sab se pahle Adam ne ki thi, isi liye Allah ne unhe Jannat se bahar nikal diya tha. Allah ne Duniya mein Aurton par Mardon ki Fazilat ko wazeh kiya hai. Kiya tum nahi dekhte ke Aurat ko Mahwari (Mensuration) aati hai jiski wajah se woh Ibaadat se qasir reh jati hai jabke Mard is tarah ki Nijasat se mehfooz hain."_
(Kitab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

🙇 👱🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Mard ka apni Family ke saath baithna Allah ko oos ke Etekaaf se zyada pasand hai jo Masjid e Nabawi mein bajaa laya jaaye."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p509)

    ♦ _*MIYA BIWI MEIN SULAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (508) 💔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ خِفْتُمْ شِقَاقَ بَيْنِهِمَا فَابْعَثُوا حَكَمًا مِنْ أَهْلِهِ وَحَكَمًا مِنْ أَهْلِهَا إِنْ يُرِيدَا إِصْلَاحًا يُوَفِّقِ اللَّهُ بَيْنَهُمَا ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلِيمًا خَبِيرًا*

_"Agar tumhe Miya Biwi ke talluqat mein talkhi (kadwahat) ka khauf ho to ek hakam (Munsif - Arbitrator) Mard ke Rishtedaron mein se ek aur ek Aurat ke Rishtedaron mein se muqarrar karo. Wo dono Islah karna chahenge to Khuda unke darmiyan muwafeqat ki rah nikal dega. Allah Aleem aur Khabeer hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 35)

📚📖 💔
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Kal ki Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke Aurat Shauhar ki ita'at kare aur nafarmani par Mard Aurat ko mamooli saza de sakta hai taake woh rahe rast par aa jaye. Lekin baat itni bigad jati hai ke dono ko sath rahna mushkil ho jata hai. Agar Miya Biwi ka jhagda akhari nobat par aa jaye to Allah ka farman hai ke dono ke Maike ke taraf se Hakam (arbitrator) (Musleh) select karen taake woh dono ke darmiyan faisla kar saken. Allah farma raha ke Woh is mein koi Rah nikalega. Ya to rishta judega ya tootega. Unka faisla dono ko manna hoga.
Allah ne is Ayat mein Sulah ka tareeqa bataya hai aur iski takeed ki hai.
💔
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Q: Agar Hakamain Judai ka faisla karen tab?)
A: _"Lekin zaroori hai ke Aurat Paak haalat mein ho aur Shauhar ne us se Jama (sex) na kiya ho."_
(Q: Agar ek Hakam ka faisla Judai ka ho lekin doosre ka nahi tab?)
A: _"Jab tak dono Hakam Judai ka faisla na den us waqt tak Judai waqe nahi hogi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
💔
Hazrat Ali (as) ke pas Shauhar Biwi aye aur apna jhagda pesh kiya to aap ne dono ki taraf se Hakam muqarrar kiye aur Hakamain se farmaya tumhe ikhtiyar hai chahe inka milap karo, ya Judai.
Shauhar na Judai par razi tha aur na Talaq par.
Hazrat Ali (as) ne Shauhar par Aurat ka Naan o Nafqa (Kharcha) wajib kiya aur use mujame'at (sex) se rok diya.
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
💔 *HAKAMIYYAT:*
Hazrat Ali (as):
Khawarij, jinhone Hazrat Ali (as) ke liye jani qurbaniya di, ne kiyon Imam ko chhodna pasand kiya? Uski wajah ye thi ke unhone Hakamain (Arbitrators) muqarrar kiye. Agar Arbitration ka tareeqa ghalat hota to kiya Allah is Ayat mein Miya Biwi ke jhagde mein Hakam muqarrar karne ki takeed kar raha hai.
(Kitab Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Do logo'n mein sulah karwaana (oo shakhs ki) tamaam Namazo'n aur Rozo'n se afzal hai."_
(A Bundle Of Flowers)
💔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Behtareen Sadqa logo'n mein sulah karvana hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p41)
💔
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mal'oon hai, mal'oon hai wo shakhs jiski taraf uska bhai (dost) sulah ka haath badhaaye aur wo usay jhattak de."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p105)
