             ♦ _*NEK SULOOK*_ ♦
*Waledain, Rishtedar, Yateem, Miskeen, Colleagues, Musafir, Kaneez se*

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (509) ☘

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاعْبُدُوا اللَّهَ وَلَا تُشْرِكُوا بِهِ شَيْئًا ۖ وَبِالْوَالِدَيْنِ إِحْسَانًا وَبِذِي الْقُرْبَىٰ وَالْيَتَامَىٰ وَالْمَسَاكِينِ وَالْجَارِ ذِي الْقُرْبَىٰ وَالْجَارِ الْجُنُبِ وَالصَّاحِبِ بِالْجَنْبِ وَابْنِ السَّبِيلِ وَمَا مَلَكَتْ أَيْمَانُكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ مَنْ كَانَ مُخْتَالًا فَخُورًا*

_"Allah ki Ibaadat karo, aur Uske sath kisi cheez ko Sharik na karo aur Maa Baap ke sath Nek Sulook karo aur Qarabatdaron ke sath aur Yateemo, Miskeeno je sath Nek Sulook karo aur Padosi Rishtedar, Ajnabi Hamsaya (Neighbours), Pehlu ke sath (colleague), Musafir se aur un laundi ghulamo se jo tumhare qabze mein hon, se Ehsan ka ma'amla rakho. Allah Maghroor aur Mutakabbir logon ko pasand nahi karta."_
(Surah Nisa: 36)

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚📖
_*Waledain (Parents):*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Rasool e Khuda (saww) sur Hazrat Ali (as) dono (Roohani) Waledain hain.Qur'an mein hai (4:36), is Ayat mein jahan Jismani Waledain murad hain wahan Roohani Waledain yani Rasool e Akram (saww) aur Ali (as) murad hain."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

👨‍👩‍👧‍👧👨‍👩‍👧‍👧
_*Qareebi Rishtedar:*_
Imam Ali (as):
_"Qaribi Rishtedaaro'n ki Dushmani bichchu ke dank se zyada dard-naak hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)
☘
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne jise Daulat ataa ki usay oos Daulat ke zariye rishtedaaro'n ki madad aur behtareen mehmaan-nawazi karna chaahiye."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat)
👬👭
_*Yateem (Orphan):*_
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs Yateem ko apne Ahlo Ayal mein dakhil kare aur uska kharch bardasht karta rahe yaha tak ke woh khud mustaghna (self sufficient) ho jaye to Allah Ta'ala us par Jannat Wajib kar dega."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🚌🚈
_*Safar (Journey):*_
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Duniya mein is andaaz mein zindagi basar karo goya tum musafir ho aur apne aap ko as'haab e quboor (qabr waalo'n) mein tasavvur karo."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p26)
🏡🏚🏠
*Hamsaya (Neighbour):*
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
_"Tere Hamsaya ka tujh par ye Haq hai ke jab woh ghayeb hon to uske ghar aur Maal ki nighebani karo aur jab maujood ho to uska ehteram karo. Aur jab woh mazloom hon to uski madad karo aur uski laghzishon (defects) ko talash na karo. Agar tumhe us mein koi burai maloom ho to use chhupao aur agar tum ye samjho ke woh tumhari nasihat qubool karta hai to tanhai mein usko nasihat karo. Kisi mushkil mein use tanha na chhodo aur uski laghzishon (slips) se darguzar (ignore) karo aur usse Husn e Ma'asherat (socially good) qayem karo."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Risalatul Huqooq, Noorus Saqlain)
☘
_Hamsayegi ke Hudood._ _(Neighbourhood Limits):_
Imam Baqir & Sadiq (as):
_"Har taraf se chalis hath."_
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Aage peechhe dayen aur bayen har taraf 40 Ghar."_
(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar)

Agar har fard in baton par amal kare to ghair ke darmiyan Tableegh ki zaroorat hi nahi padegi.

             ♦ _*KANJOOSI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (510)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ يَبْخَلُونَ وَيَأْمُرُونَ النَّاسَ بِالْبُخْلِ وَيَكْتُمُونَ مَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ ۗ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابًا مُهِينًا*

_"Jo KANJOOSI karen aur doosron ko bhi Bukhl (hoarding) ka hukm den aur jo kuchh Khuda ne unhe diya  hai woh use chhupayen . Hamne Kafiron ke liye Ruswa karne wala Azaab tayyar kiya hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 37)

📚📖 💰
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs apne Maal mein se Farze Zakaat ada kare aur mushkil ke waqt apni qaum ki madad kare to woh Kanjoos nahi hai. Mukammal Bakheel woh shakhs hai jo apne Maal mein se Wajib Zakaat ada na kare aur mushkil ke waqt apni qaum ki madad na kare aur baqi faltu kaamo mein daulat kharch karta phirta hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Shahih (Miser) kaun hai?)
_"Shahih  Bukhl se buland darje ko kaha jata hai. Bakheel woh hai jo apni daulat kharch karne mein bhukhl (Kanjoosi) kare. Jabke Shahih شحيح woh ke jo kisi doosre ko daulat kharch karte hue dekh le to use takleef mehsoos ho. Aur Shahih ki khwahish hoti hai ke poori Duniya ka rizq uske haath mein ho, chahe jaez tareeqe se aaye ya najaez zariye se aaye aur Allah ki ata kardah rizq par qana'at nahi karta."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hamare Shiyon mein 3 khaslaten nahi hongi:_
_1. Woh hath phaila kar kisi se Sawal nahi karenge._
_2. Wo Bakheel (Kanjoos) nahi honge._
_3. Lawatat لواطت (Homosexuality) nahi karayenge."_
(Kitabul Khisaal, Noorus Saqlain)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Khuda ko jiski zaroorat nahi hoti woh bukhl se ibteda karta hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
💰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Sakhi ka Khana Dawaa aur Kanjoos ka Khana bimari hota hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Kanjoos ka wohi dost hota hai jisne uska tajruba na kiya ho."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Kanjoosi)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Kanjoos kitna badnaseeb hai ke duniya mein faqeero'n jaisi zindagi guzarta hai aur Qayamat mein ameero'n (maaldar) jaisa hisaab deta hai."_
(Tanzeemul Makatib, Mar ’05)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

  ♦ _*SHOW OFF OF KHAIRAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (511)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالَّذِينَ يُنْفِقُونَ أَمْوَالَهُمْ رِئَاءَ النَّاسِ وَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَلَا بِالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۗ وَمَنْ يَكُنِ الشَّيْطَانُ لَهُ قَرِينًا فَسَاءَ قَرِينًا * وَمَاذَا عَلَيْهِمْ لَوْ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ وَأَنْفَقُوا مِمَّا رَزَقَهُمُ اللَّهُ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ بِهِمْ عَلِيمًا*

_"Woh log bhi Allah ko na-pasand hain jo apne Maal mahez logon ke dikhane ke liye kharch karte hai aur dar haqiqat na to unka Allah par Imaan hai aur na hi Roz e Akherat par. Jis ka hamnashin (Dost) aur sathi Shaitan ho, kiya badtareen sathi hai."_
_"Aur agar ye Allah aur Roz e Akherat par Imaan le ayen aur Khuda ke diye hue Rizq mein se Kharch karen to is mein unka kiya nuqsan hai. Allah inhe behtar Jaanta hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 38 - 39)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Insaan ko Allah ki rah mein Allah ke diye hue hi rizq mein se kharch karna hota hai. Lekin agar usne apni naam o shohrat ke liye kharch kiya to bhale hi usne Allah ke naam pe kiya lekin usne Shaitan ko apna badtareen dost bana liya. Allah sawal kar raha hai agar yehi khuloos e Niyat se Allah ki raah mein kharch karta to kiya harj tha.
Agar Insaan ko Allah wa Akherat par Imaan hota to woh har kaam Allah ke liye karta, chunke insaan mein Imaan ki kamzori payi jati hai isliye, Nek kamo mein kharch karte waqt woh Allah ke bajai logon se Ajr ka umidwar hota hai. Aise logon ke yaar dost Shaitan ke alawa aur koi nahi hota.
Logon ne Duniya ke khatir New Year ke mauqe par betahasha kharch kiya, guzishta raat Duniya mein Gunah o Badkari Shabab par thi. Ye kisi ko khabar nahi ke ham past Duniya ki or ek aur seedhi chad rahe hain. Hamara Kamal chhoot gaya hai. Ham to Duniya ke nashe mein madhosh hain. Is Duniya ki rang raliyon mein so gaye hain. Woh is baat se bekhabar ho jata hai ke kab use thokar lage aur phir sota hua ye insaan apni fitrat par pade labade ko utar kar jag khada ho, aur Allah Allah kare. Kahen ham zamane ke is darya mein na bah jayen. Is toofani Duniya mein ham ladkhada na jayen balke sabit qadam rahen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek dirham IMAM ko dena afzal hai oos Ek Laakh dirham se jo raah e Khuda mein doosre kaamo'n mein kharch kiya jaaye."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v2, p54)
🍪🍵🍶
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo logo'n ko dikhaane ke liye kisi ko khana dega to Allah usay Jahannum ka Sadid khilayega; jo pyet mein jaate hi aag ban jayega."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal)
☘🍀
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs koi nek Amal chhipa kar anjaam deta hai to usay Makhfi (hidden) Amal mein likh diya jaata hai, aur jab uska zabaan se iqraar karta hai to usay Mitaa diya jaata hai aur zaahiri Amal mein likh diya jaata hai, phir jab doosri martaba zabaan se iqraar karta hai to usay Riya (dikhawa / show off) mein likh diya jaata hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, h6818)
🍃🍂
Imam Ali (as):
_"Amal bagair kisi riyaa kaari ya dikhawe ke anjaam do, kyun ki jo Allah ke ilawa kisi aur ke liye amal karta hai, to Allah usay oosi ke sahare chhor deta hai."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, Riya-kaari)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
     ♦ _*ALLAH ZALIM NAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (512)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَظْلِمُ مِثْقَالَ ذَرَّةٍ ۖ وَإِنْ تَكُ حَسَنَةً يُضَاعِفْهَا وَيُؤْتِ مِنْ لَدُنْهُ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Allah kisi par zarrah barabar bhi zulm nahi karta. Agar koi ek Neki kare to Allah use dugni (double) kar deta hai. Phir use apni taraf se Ajre Azeem ata karta hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 40)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah kisi par Zulm nahi karta, Woh Insaafwar hai. Jisko log bala o musibat, zindagi ke utar chadao, Toofan, nagahani hadson ko dekh kar Allah ka zulm samajhte hain, aisa nahi hai. Allah kisi ko satata nahi. Jo kuchh bhi hadsat Duniya mein hote hain uski wajah khud insaan ke amaal hain. Allah ne jo instructions Insaan ko diye hain woh usne follow nahi karta to phir agar woh koi musibat mein mubtela hota hai to woh usi ki wajah se hai. Allah ne Insaan ko ikhtiyar diya hai jo chahe kare lekin uska natija usko bhugatna hoga. Isi liye jo itne Deeni Taleemat di jati hai Insaan ko khabardar karne ke liye.
Allah agar Jabbar hai to Rehman o Rahim bhi hai. Agar Insaan ek qadam Neki ki taraf badhta hai, Allah use 10 qadam khechta hai.
Jo Woh Zulm nahi karta to kisi ke zulm ko pasand bhi nahi karta. Allah zalim ko sirf mohlat deta hai lekin Mazloom ko uske Ajre se mehroom nahi rakhta.
Dushmanane Ahle Bait ne Ahle Bait (as) par shuru se hi zulm jari rakha, zulm ka shabab (climax) Karbala mein hua. Yahan tak ke Muhibbane Ahle Bait (as) ko nahi chhoda.
Aaj bhi Dushmane Ahle Bait (as) ki hukumat jari hai.
Aaj barsi hai Ayatullah Nimr ki Shahadat ki jinko Ale Saud ne Muhibbe Ahle Bait ke jurm mein Shaheed kiya. Yahan tak ke unka farzand ko bhi phansi ki saza sunai ja chuki hai. Natija ham dekh rahe hain ke Saudi ki aaj haalat kiya hai. Saddam ne bhi aise hi mazalim dhaye the, Duniya ne uska hashr dekha.
🔰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Gazab e Ilaahi oos shakhs par bahut hi sakht hota hai jo aise shakhs par zulm karta hai jis ka haami o naasir Allah ke alaawa aur koi nahi hota."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5, p865)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ek Neki ke badle Allah 10 Nekiyaa'n deta hai, lekin Neki ke liye WILAYAT E ALI (as) ZARURI HAI. Jo shakhs aqeeda e Wilayat rakh kar Neki kare to usay har Neki ke badle kam az kam 10 Nekiyo'n ka ajr milta hai. Agar aqeeda e Wilayat ke bagair koi shakhs Neki karta hai to uski Nekiyo'n ki wajah se Dunyaavi takleef khatm kar di jaati hai lekin Akherat mein uska koi hissa nahi hota."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p313)
🔰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Wo gunah jiska tumhe ranj / dukh ho, Allah ke nazdeek oos Neki se behtar hai jis se tum mein guroor (pride) paida ho jaaye."_
(Nahjul Balagah)
🔰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya, _"Qasam hai Apni Izzat o Jalaal ki, jab Main kisi bande par Rahem ka irada karta hoo'n to Main oos waqt tak Apne bande ko duniya se nahi jaane doo'nga jab tak uske gunaho'n ki talaafi na kar lunga chaahe uske jism ko bekaar kar ke, chaahe Rizq ki tangi se, chaahe dunyawi khauf se aur phir bhi agar gunah baaqi rahein to maut mein sakhti karunga. Allah Ta'ala ne qasam khaayi Apni Izzat o Jalaal ki ke jab Main kisi bande ko Azaab dene ka irada karta hoo'n to nahi jaane deta is duniya se jab tak uski har neki ka badla na de doo'n chaahe to wus'at (expansion / vriddhi) e Rizq se, ya badan ki sehat se ya duniyavi aman se aur agar phir bhi Neki rehi to maut ki sakhti uspar aasaan kar deta hoo'n aur phir Akherat mein pakadd leta hoo'n"._
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p157)

♦ _*QAYAMAT KE DIN GAWAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (513)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَكَيْفَ إِذَا جِئْنَا مِنْ كُلِّ أُمَّةٍ بِشَهِيدٍ وَجِئْنَا بِكَ عَلَىٰ هَٰؤُلَاءِ شَهِيدًا * يَوْمَئِذٍ يَوَدُّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَعَصَوُا الرَّسُولَ لَوْ تُسَوَّىٰ بِهِمُ الْأَرْضُ وَلَا يَكْتُمُونَ اللَّهَ حَدِيثًا*

_"Us waqt unki kiya haalat hogi jab Ham har ummat mein se ek Gawah (Witness) layenge aur Aap (saww) ko un sabka Gawah bana kar layenge. Us waqt woh sab log jinhone Rasool (saww) ki baat nahi maani thi aur nafarmani karte rahe the, tamanna karenge, aye kash! Unke liye zameen phat jati aur woh us mein sama jaate. Woh Khuda se koi baat na chhupa sakenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 41 - 42)

📚📖 📜
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Ali (as):
"Allah Ta'ala Ahle Mehshar ko jama karega. Us Din haalat ye hogi ke log ek doosre ka saamna karne se bhagte phir rahe honge jaisa ke us Ayat mein hai:
_"Us Din Insaan apne bhai aur apni Maa, apne Baap, apni Biwi aur Aulad se bhag raha hoga."_
(Surah Abas: 34-36)
"Allah Ta'ala us Aalam mein bolne ke liye kahega, pas wo wohi kalam karenge jiski ijazat hogi. Us waqt Rasool uth kar apni Ummaton ki Gawahi denge jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai. (4:41-42)"
(Kitabut Tawheed, Noorus Saqlain)
📜
Hazrat Ali (as):
"Anbiya wa Rusul ko utha kar poochha jayega kiya unhone paigham pahunchaya, yehi sawal Ummat se bhi hoga. Jab woh kahenge hamare pas koi Basheer o Nazir nahi aya to us waqt Anbiya Rasoole Akram (saww) se kahenge ke woh unke sadaqat ki Gawahi den. Rasool e Akram (saww) sadaqat ki Gawahi denge aur Anbiya ke inkar karne walon ki takzeeb karenge. Aanhazrat (saww) ki Gawahi ke baad Allah Ta'ala farmayega Woh har cheez par qadir hai, Woh tumhare aaza wa jawareh (body parts) se bhi Gawahi dilwa sakta hai. Ab inkar karne walon ke pas koi excuse baqi nahi rahega.
Habibe Khuda (saww) apne Ummat ke Munafeqeen o Kuffar ke khilaf bhi Gawahi denge aur Khuda ke huzoor mein unki Ahd Shikni aur Sunnat ki tabdili ka shikwa karenge aur Aap arz karenge ke Khudaya! Meri Ummat ne mere Ahle Bait (as) par Zulm kiye aur unhone pichhle Anbiya ki Ummaton ki pairavi ki."
(Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)
📜
Us waqt insaan farar ki rah doondhega, ye chahega ke use zameen nigal le. Mayoosi ka aalam ye ho jata hai ke wo sochta ke woh 'adam' عدم ho jaye. Lekin insaan kabhi adam (non-existance) na hoga. Means Insaan ye sochta hai ke khud kashi kar lun to mein khatm ho jaonga. Aisa nahi hai. Insaan bach nahi sakta. Insaan ke sirf state (halaten) badalti hain wujood nahi. Uski mahiyat badalti rahti hai. Allah ne jab paida kar diya to woh pahle Alam e Zar mein tha, phir Duniya mein aata hai, phir Aalam e Barzakh, phir Qayamat mein hisab o kitab ke baad Jannat ya Jahannam mein hamesha rahega. (فيها خالدون).
Isliye Insaan ka har amal CCTV mein qaid ho raha hai, Qayamat ke Din uski film usko dikha di jayegi. Tab pastaynge to kiya ho sakta hai, qissa to unka tamam ho hi jayga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Har Momin ke aazaa (bodyparts) uske bar-khilaaf gawaahi nahi denge, ma-siwa uske nahi ke wo sirf unhi ke khilaaf gawaahi denge jinke khilaaf azaab ka hukm mohqiq (tai / ascertain) ho chuka hoga (yaani jo mustahaq e azaab honge)"_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p103)
📜
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Qayamat ke din Momin ke a'aza (haath / paav) uske khilaaf gawaahi nahi denge. A'aza sirf uske khilaaf gawaahi denge jo Azaab ka haqdaar hoga; jab ke Momin ka Naama e Aamal uske daayein haath mein diya jayega aur wo khushi se usay padhega aur uspar zarra barabar zulm nahi kiya jayega."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p196)
📜
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar gunahgaaro'n ki shahadat (gawaahi) qubool na ki jaaye to phir Ambiya (as) aur Awsiya (as) ke alawa koi bhi shahadat (gawaahi) nahi de sakta hai. Jab tak kisi ko apni aa'nkho'n se gunah mein murtakib hote huwe na dekh lo aur aur 2 shaahido'n (gawaaho'n) ne uske baare mein gawaahi na di ho to jaan lo ke wo shakhs aadil hai."_
(Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) - Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p161)

♦ _*NEEND KI NASHE MEIN NAMAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (514)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَقْرَبُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَأَنْتُمْ سُكَارَىٰ حَتَّىٰ تَعْلَمُوا مَا تَقُولُونَ وَلَا جُنُبًا إِلَّا عَابِرِي سَبِيلٍ حَتَّىٰ تَغْتَسِلُوا ۚ وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَفُوًّا غَفُورًا*

_"Aye Sahebane Imaan! Jab tum nashe ki haalat mein ho to Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tumhe hosh na aa jaye ke tum kiya kar rahe ho._
_Aur Janabat ki haalat mein bhi Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tum Ghusl na kar lo magar ye ke raste se guzar rahe ho._
_Agar kabhi aisa ho ke tum Beemar ho ya safar mein ho ye mein se kpi shakhs rafe haajat karke aaye ya tumne Auraton se lams (Mubasherat- Intercourse) kiya ho._
_Aur tumhe Wuzu ke liye paani na mile to Paak Mitti se Tayammum kar lo aur apne hathon aur chehron par Masah kar lo._
_Beshak Khuda Bahut Ma'af karne wala aur Bahut Bakhshne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 43)

📚📖 😡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein 3 hisse hain. Ek hissa peshe khidmat hai.

Is Ayat mein rivayat ke mutabiq Nashe se murad hai, sharaab ka nasha nahi. Imaan wale Sharabi nahi hote. Imaan walon ko sabaq diya gaya hai ke woh Neend se uthne ke baad ankh malte hue turant musalleh par na chale jayen balke jab kuchh Neend ka nasha utar jay tab Namaz padhen.
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Khabardar! Susti ki haalat mein Namaz ke liye na utho aur na hi jamaiyan (yawning) lete hue aur na hi bhari ban kar Namaz ke liye aao kiyonki ye Munafeqat ki Alamat hai. Allah ne Ahle Imaan ko nashe ki haalat mein Namaz ke qareeb aane ke liye mana kiya hai ke woh Neend ke nashe mein Namaz ke qareeb na jayen."_
(Kiyltab Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

(Ayat ka doosra hissa to be cont'd.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😡
Imam Ali (as):
_*Yad rakho! Nasha 4 tarah ka hota hai:_
_(1) Sharab ka Nasha._
_(2) Daulat ka Nasha._
_(3) Neend ka Nasha._
_(4) Hukoomat ka Nasha."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🍷
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jo sharaab pikar nashe mein ho to Allah agle 40 din ki uski Namaz qubool nahi karega. Agar uski Namaz chhutegi to dohri (double) sazaa milegi."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aaamal aur Iqaabul Aaamal)
😡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Allah ko (logo'n mein) teen (3) cheezein pasand hai: -_ _Kam bolna,_
_kam sona aur_
_kam khana…"_
(Isna Ashariyyah p.92)
(A Bundle Of Flowers)
😡
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Din ke ibtedaai (shuruaat ke) hisse mein Sona (sleeping) jihaalat aur gareebi hai aur_
_dopahar ka sona aur Qailula karna ne'mat hai aur_
_baad e Asr sona bewaqoofi hai aur_
_Maghrib o Ishaa ke darmiyaan sona Rizq se mehroom kar deta hai."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p318)

          ♦ _*HALAT E JUNUB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (515)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَقْرَبُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَأَنْتُمْ سُكَارَىٰ حَتَّىٰ تَعْلَمُوا مَا تَقُولُونَ وَلَا جُنُبًا إِلَّا عَابِرِي سَبِيلٍ حَتَّىٰ تَغْتَسِلُوا ۚ وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَفُوًّا غَفُورًا*

_"Aye Sahebane Imaan! Jab tum nashe ki haalat mein ho to Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tumhe hosh na aa jaye ke tum kiya kar rahe ho._
_Aur Janabat ki haalat mein bhi Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tum Ghusl na kar lo magar ye ke raste se guzar rahe ho._
_Agar kabhi aisa ho ke tum Beemar ho ya safar mein ho ye mein se kpi shakhs rafe haajat karke aaye ya tumne Auraton se lams (Mubasherat- Intercourse) kiya ho._
_Aur tumhe Wuzu ke liye paani na mile to Paak Mitti se Tayammum kar lo aur apne hathon aur chehron par Masah kar lo._
_Beshak Khuda Bahut Ma'af karne wala aur Bahut Bakhshne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 43)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_ (Cont'd..)
Is Ayat ke zail mein kal zikr hua ke Neend ke Nashe mein Namaz ke nazdeek na jayen.
_*Halat e Janabat:*_
Janabat ki haalat mein bhi na Namaz padh sakte hai, na Masjid mein dakhil ho sakte hain.
💧
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Haez aur Munjib Masjid se guzar sakte hain. Ayat ke mutabiq"_
(Ilalush Sharaye)
💧
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"(Haez aur Munjib) Masjid mein baithne ke liye dakhil nahi ho sakte albatta Masjid mein se guzar sakte hain kiyonki Allah ka farman hai. (4:43), woh Madjid mein kuchh rakh sakte hain utha nahi sakte."_
_"Iski wajah ye hai ke kuchh rakhne ke liye unhe dakhil hona ki zaroorat nahi hai bas haath badha kar rakh sakte hain jabke kuchh uthane ke liye unko andar dakhil hone ki zaroorat hai."_
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
💧
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Janabat bhi ek tarah se Haez ki manind hai kiyonki jab insaan par Janabat tari hoti hai to insaan ke wujood se badboo aane lagti hai isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne Janabat ka Ghusl e Wajib kiya taake insaan ke wujood se badboo je bhabhooke na aayen. Alawa az ein Khuda be Ghusl ko bando ki azmaish ja bhi zariya banaya hai."_
(Kitab Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)
💧
Mazeed Ahkam e Shariyat ke liye Tauzeehul Masail Ay. Sistani (DZ)  Maslah no.351 to 526 refer karen.
Is group mein ham English Ahkam post kar chuke hain.

(Next part on Tayammum to be Cont'd ......)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_”Jo koi gusl e Janabat mein apne jism ke ek baal ko bhi jaan bujh-kar (khushk / dry) chhorega, wo Dozakh mein hoga.”_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p451)
🚿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"…Zara Allah ki is hikmat (wisdom) par ghaur karo ke Usne har Azoo (each organ of the body / jism ke har ang) ko kis qadar sahi muqaam par rakha hai aur fuzla (jism ki najis gandagi / excrements) ke liye kaise zaroof (container / paatr) khalq farmaaye hain taaki fuzlaat (gandagi) jism mein na phailein aur tamaam jism ko faasid na bana de (bigaadd na de). Agar Tilli (spleen) na hoti to zard (yellow) paani khoo'n mein daakhil ho kar mukhtalif bimariya'n paida kar deta. agar Masana (Bladder / Mutrashay) na hota to Peshaab khaarij na hoti (baahar nahi nikalti) aur Peshaab Khoon mein daakhil ho kar saare jism mein zeher phaila deta."_
(Tibb e Imam Reza (as), p66)

      ♦ _*TAYAMMUM*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu tu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (516)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَقْرَبُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَأَنْتُمْ سُكَارَىٰ حَتَّىٰ تَعْلَمُوا مَا تَقُولُونَ وَلَا جُنُبًا إِلَّا عَابِرِي سَبِيلٍ حَتَّىٰ تَغْتَسِلُوا ۚ *وَإِنْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَوْ عَلَىٰ سَفَرٍ أَوْ جَاءَ أَحَدٌ مِنْكُمْ مِنَ الْغَائِطِ أَوْ لَامَسْتُمُ النِّسَاءَ فَلَمْ تَجِدُوا مَاءً فَتَيَمَّمُوا صَعِيدًا طَيِّبًا فَامْسَحُوا بِوُجُوهِكُمْ وَأَيْدِيكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَفُوًّا غَفُورًا*

_"Aye Sahebane Imaan! Jab tum nashe ki haalat mein ho to Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tumhe hosh na aa jaye ke tum kiya kar rahe ho._
_Aur Janabat ki haalat mein bhi Namaz ke qareeb na jao jab tak tum Ghusl na kar lo magar ye ke raste se guzar rahe ho._
_Agar kabhi aisa ho ke tum Beemar ho ya safar mein ho ye mein se kpi shakhs rafe haajat karke aaye ya tumne Auraton se lams (Mubasherat- Intercourse) kiya ho._
_*Aur tumhe Wuzu ke liye paani na mile to Paak Mitti se Tayammum kar lo aur apne hathon aur chehron par Masah kar lo.*_
_Beshak Khuda Bahut Ma'af karne wala aur Bahut Bakhshne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 43)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
*Tayammum:*
Jab Bimari ya Safar mein Ghusl ya Wuzu mein paani istemal na kar sake ya na mile tab Tayammum karna chahiye.
*Method:*
Niyat, Apne dono hatheliyon ko Matti par mare, poori peshani par dono hatheliyon ko phere bal ki jagah se naak ke sire tak, phir Matti par hath mare, left hatheli ko dayen hath (right hand) ke tamam pusht (back) par, phir dayen hatheli ko bayen hath ke tamam pusht par phere (masah) kare. Ye Tarteeb se kiya jaye.

*Q:* Sawal hota hai ke Tayammum se kiya fayda, jabke isse gandgi to saf nahi hoti.

*Wujuhat (Reasons):*
*A. Akhlaqi Fayda:*
Tayammum ek Ibaadat hai. Jab insaan apne hath mitti par marta hai. Isse Khuda ki bargah mein aajezi o inkisari (humbleness) paida hoti hai, jisse woh doosri Ibaadaton ki taraf amada hota hai.
*B. Hifzane Sehet ( Health):*
Aaj ki Duniya mein ye sabit ho chuka hai ke Mitti (Mud) apne bahut se germs (Bacterias) ki wajah se gandgiyon ko door kar sakti hai. Ye germs jo kisi bhi cheez ko analyse karke tarah tarah ki badboo door karte hain, zamin ki satah (surface) par hi rahte hain jinhe sunlight milti rahti hai. Isiliye jab murde aur doosri ghalazaten zamin mein dafan ho jati hain, unko ye germs decompose kar ke sari badboo nikal dete hain. Hence Mitti (Mud, clay) Antibiotics ka kam karti hai. Isliye Matti wohi paani ka kaam karti hai. Paani (Water) Hallal (حللال) hai, means woh nuqsandeh germs ko apne aap mein dissolve kar ke baha le jata hai, jabke Mitti usko nist o nabood (destroy) kar deti hai, Maut ke ghat utar deti hai.
Lekin zaroori hai Tayammum ki Mitti Paak (Pure طيب) ho. Surface (satah) se li hoi ho jis par light padti hai.
Allah ke bataye hue sabhi Ahkam be Ma'ani nahi hoti, har fe'l mein kuchh na kuchh maslehat hoti hai, ye alag baat hai ke ham isse waqif nahi hote.

Inshallah Surah Maeda mein aur tazkara karenge.
Tayammum ke detail Fiqhi Ahkam Tauzeehul Masael Ay. Sistani Maslah no. 655 - 691 refer karen.
Ham is group mein pahle English mein pesh kar chuke hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 *JUMA MUBARAK*
Imam Reza (as)
se sawaal huwa ke Namaz e Juma 2 rak'at hai aur agar Imam na ho to 4 rak'at Namaz e Zuhr kyun padhi jaati hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya ke iski bahut si wajuhaat (reasons) hai:
_"(1) Log Namaz e Juma ke liye door daraaz se safar kar ke aate hain. Allah Ta'ala ne chaha ke log thake huwe hain is liye inhe 2 rak'at ki ri'aayat (concession) di jaaye. Is liye Namaz e Juma 2 Rak'at hai._
_(2) Imam kuchh deyr ke liye khutba deta hai aur muqtadi khutba sunte rehte hain aur unhe Namaz ka intezaar hota hai aur jo Namaz ke intezaar mein ho to wo bhi Namaz mein shumaar kiya jaata hai. Isi liye Juma ke 2 khutbe 2 Rak'at qaaem karne ke barabar hai._
_(3) Imam ke saath 2 Rak'at Namaz Khuda ki nazar mein 4 Rak'at hai kyun ki Imam ke Ilm, Fiqh, Adl aur Fazl ki wajah se 2 Rak'at Namaz ko itni bulandi naseeb hoti hai ke wo 4 Rak'at maani jaati hai._
_(4) Juma musalmano'n ki Eid hai aur Namaz e Eid 2 Rak'at hi huwa karti hai aur 2 khutbo'n ki wajah se isme qasr paida nahi hoti."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p232)

♦ _*AHLE KITAB KI ZIYADTIYAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (517)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا نَصِيبًا مِنَ الْكِتَابِ يَشْتَرُونَ الضَّلَالَةَ وَيُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَضِلُّوا السَّبِيلَ * وَاللَّهُ أَعْلَمُ بِأَعْدَائِكُمْ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَلِيًّا وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ نَصِيرًا*

_"Kiya Aap ne un logon ko nahi dekha jinhe Kitab ka Hissa diya gaya hai woh Gumrahi ka karobar kar rahe hain aur woh ye khwahish rakhte hain ke tum bhi raaste se bhatak jao."_
_"Allah tumhare Dushmano ko achchi tarah se janta hai aur tumhari sarparasti aur madad ke liye Allah hi Kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 44 - 45)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayat mein zikr ho raha hai ke Ahle Kitab ke hamil (carrier) bajai iske isse kuchh hidayat pate gumrahi ke raste par chal pade. Balke ye chahte hain ke doosre bhi unki tarah gumrah hon.
Yehi haal Ahle Kitab hamile Qur'an walon ka hai. Ahle Islam ke pass Qur'an jaisa Allah ka Kalam hote hue bhi gumrahi ke raaste par hain. Agar sabhi ne Qur'an se Hidayat li hoti to Sabhi Musalman ek hote. Ye is wajah se ke woh Vilayat e Amirul Mo'menin Ali (as) jo ke Sirat e Mustaqeem hain, se bhatak gaye hain.
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p915)
🌻
Imam Hasan Askari (as):
_"Momin ke liye kitni buri baat hai ke aisi cheez ki taraf raghbat (khwaish) rakhe jo uski zillat o ruswaayi ka sabab ho."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p237)
🌻
Imam Hasan Askari (as):
_"Taqwa e Ilahi ikhtiyaar karo aur (hamare liye) baais e zeenat bano, baais e buraayi na bano."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p243)
🌻
Imam Hasan Askari (as):
_"Har buraayi ki chaabi gussa hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p235)

               ♦ _*TEHREEF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (518)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مِنَ الَّذِينَ هَادُوا يُحَرِّفُونَ الْكَلِمَ عَنْ مَوَاضِعِهِ وَيَقُولُونَ سَمِعْنَا وَعَصَيْنَا وَاسْمَعْ غَيْرَ مُسْمَعٍ وَرَاعِنَا لَيًّا بِأَلْسِنَتِهِمْ وَطَعْنًا فِي الدِّينِ ۚ وَلَوْ أَنَّهُمْ قَالُوا سَمِعْنَا وَأَطَعْنَا وَاسْمَعْ وَانْظُرْنَا لَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُمْ وَأَقْوَمَ وَلَٰكِنْ لَعَنَهُمُ اللَّهُ بِكُفْرِهِمْ فَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا*

_"Yahoodiyon mein se kuchh log aise bhi hain jo Alfaz ko unke mahel o maqam se pher dete hain aur Deen ke khilaf taana zani ke liye apni zabano ko tod madod kar kehte hain *سَمِعْنَا وَعَصَيْنَا* (hamne suna aur nafarmani ki) aur *َاسْمَعْ غَيْرَ مُسْمَعٍ* (Aap hamari baat sunen jabke aapki baat sunne ke layeq nahi) aur *رَاعِنَا* (hamara charwaha) halanke agar wo iske bajaye *سَمِعْنَا وَأَطَعْنَا* (hamne suna aur ita'at ki) aur *َاسْمَعْ* (aap hamari baat sunen) *انْظُرْنَا* (Aap ham par nazar e karam karen) kahte to unke liye ziyada behtar aur ziyada munasib hota lekin unke Kufr ki wajah se Allah ne un par La'anat ki hai. Un mein se kam hi afraad Imaan layenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 46)

📚📖 🍂
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yahan is baat ka zikr hai ke Yahoodi kaise lafzon ko bigad kar Islam ka mazaq udate aur be-adabi karte the. Tehzeeb wa baat karne ka saleeqa tha hi nahi.
Dushman ke pas jab koi jawab nahi rehta to isi tarah se taana mezi baaten karte hain.
Islam ne is cheez ki mazammat ki hai.
Doosri baat ye ke hamse jo lafz ka istemal karne ke liya kaha gaya hai wohi istemal kare, kiyonki ham itna ilm nahi rakhte. Jo Alqab jis ke liye istemal kiye hain wohi istemal karen. Jo Duayen hame batai gayi hain wohi padhen, un mein tehreef (changes) na karen.
🍂
Imam Sadiq (as)
ne apne sahabi se kaha, _"Aye Abu Baseer! Is lafz (Raafizi) se pareshaan hone ki zarurat nahi hai kyun ki ye to Khuda Wande Aalam ki taraf se tumhe milaa hai". Bani Israil ke 70 aadmi the jin par jab Firoun aur uske logo'n ki gumraahi waazeh ho gayi to un logo'n ne unka saath chhor diya aur unse alag ho kar H. Musa (as) ke saath shaamil ho gaye kyun ki unke liye H. Musa (as) ka saaheb e hidayat hona waazeh ho chuka tha. To chunke wo log Firoun ka inkaar kar ke aaye the is liye H. Musa (as) ke lashkar mein unko Raafizi kaha gaya (Raafizi yaani inkaar karne waale). Ye log is poore lashkar mein sab se zyada sakht Ibadat-guzaar the aur H. Musa (as) aur H. Haroon (as) aur unki aulaad se bahut zyada mohabbat karte the to Khuda Wande Aalam ne H. Musa (as) ke paas Wahi bheji ke 'Taurait' mein un logo'n ka yehi naam rakh do kyun ki Hum ne unke liye yehi naam ikhtiyaar kiya hai, chunaanche H. Musa (as) ne likh liya. Phir ye naam Khuda Wande Aalam ke paas mehfooz raha aur ab tum logo'n ko milaa hai…."_
(Shiane Ahlebait (as), p44)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍂
Riwayat:
Ibrahim bin Abbas ka bayaan hai ke, _"Main ne kabhi nahi dekha ke Imam Reza (as) ne kisi shakhs se bhi ek na-munasib lafz kaha ho ya kisi ki baat kaat di ho jab tak wo apni baat tamaam na kar de, ya kisi ki haajat ko poori karne ka imkaan hote huwe uski baat ko radd kar diya ho, ya kisi ke saamne pair phaila kar baithhe ho'n, ya taik lagaa-kar baithhe ho'n, ya kisi naukar ya ghulaam ko bura bhala kaha ho, ya thook diya ho, ya sun'ne mein qehqahe lagaaye ho, balke hamesha tabassum (smile) se kaam lete the. Jab ghar mein dastarkhwaan lagta tha to tamaam naukaro'n aur ghulamo'n ko saath bithha lete the, raat ko bahut kam sotey the aur zyada hissa bedaar (jaagte) rehte the. Aksar raato'n mein to shaam se lekar fajr tak bedaar hi rehte the. Roze bahut rakhte the, har mahine 3 Roze to beher-haal rakhte the aur usay saare saal ka Roza qaraar dete the. Nekiyaa'n bahut karte the aur chhupa-kar Sadqa bahut dete the khususiyat ke saath taarik (andheri) raato'n mein…"_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p168)

  ♦ _*CHEHRO KA BIGADNA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (519) 🐵

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ آمِنُوا بِمَا نَزَّلْنَا مُصَدِّقًا لِمَا مَعَكُمْ مِنْ قَبْلِ أَنْ نَطْمِسَ وُجُوهًا فَنَرُدَّهَا عَلَىٰ أَدْبَارِهَا أَوْ نَلْعَنَهُمْ كَمَا لَعَنَّا أَصْحَابَ السَّبْتِ ۚ وَكَانَ أَمْرُ اللَّهِ مَفْعُولًا*

_"Aye woh log jinhen Kitab di gayi hai. Hamare nazil kiye hue Qur'an par Imaan lao jo us Kitab ki tasdeeq karta hai jo tumhare pas maujood hai.  Qabl iske ke Ham chehre bigad kar pusht (back) ki taraf pher den ya un par is tarah La'anat karen jis tarah se Hamne Ashaab e Sabt par La'anat ki hai aur Allah ka hukm jari ho kar hi rahta hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 47)

📚📖 🐵
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Baqir (as):
"Jabir! Sab se pahle Shaam (Syria) ke ilaaqe mein tabahi aayegi. Akheri Zamane mein yahan se 3 parcham (Flag) buland honge; " Ashab اصهب", "Abqa' ابقع "," Sufyani Flag سفيانى".
'Sufyani Ashab aur Abqa se jang karega aur un dono par fatah (Victory) karega. Phir Sufyani Iraq ki taraf kooch karega. Qarya pahunch kar ek lakh sakashon ko qatl karega. Phir woh 70,000 ka lashkar lekar Kufa ayega aur Ahle Kufa ko qatl karega. Unhe Saleeb (crucify) par chadhayega aur unhe qaid karega. Isi asna mein Khurasan se Siyah Parcham namudar honge un mein Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke Ashab honge jo tezi se safar karenge. Ghulamon mein se ek shakhs kuchh kamzor afrad ko sath milakar khurooj (attack) karega lekin Sufyani ja Sipeh Salaar use Heera aur Kufa ke darmiyan qatl kar dega. Sufyani Medina ki taraf apna lashkar ravana karega. Us waqt Hazrat Mahdi (atfs) Hazrat Moosa (as) ki tarah khamoshi se Medina chhod kar Mecca chale jayenge. Jab Sufyani ke Sipah Salar ko maloom hoga ke Imam Mahdi (atfs) Medina se Mecca chale gaye hain to woh bhi apna lashkar lekar Mecca ki janib ravana hoga. Raaste mein woh ek sehra mein padao karega ke Aasmaan se sada aayegi:
"Aye Sehra! In logon ko fana kar de."
Us waqt Sehra (plain ground) un sab ko nighal lega bas 3 aadmi bach jayege jin ke chehre pusht ki janib mude honge aur unka Bani Kalb se hoga aur inhi ke mutalliq Allah ne irshad farmaya: (4:47)
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)
🐵
Majmaul Bayan mein manqool hai:
Imam Baqir (as) ne farmaya:
"Ayat.. ان نطمس وجوها .... means unhe Hidayat se hata denge aur pase pusht kar denge. Means tumhara rukh Hidayat ke bajaye hamesha gumrahi ki taraf rahega aur tum hamesha ke liye falah o kamyabi se mehroom ho jaoge."
_"Jis Kitab ki taalimat par Ahle Kitab ko Imaan laane ki dawat di gayi hai us mein Hazrat Ali (as) ki Vilayat bhi shamil hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Askari (as)
se sawaal kiya gaya ke "Ek shakhs aap ki Ahadees logo'n mein bayaan karta hai aur usko logo'n mein mash'hoor karta hai aur logo'n ke aur aap ke Shiyo'n ke dilo'n ki islaah (sudhaar / reform) karta hai aur doosra shakhs Aabid (Ibadat-guzaar) hai magar wo aap ki Ahadees ko logo'n mein bayaan nahi karta. In dono mein kaun afzal hai?"
Aap ne farmaya:
_"Hamari Ahadees bayaan karne wala aur hamare Shiyo'n ke dilo'n ki islaah karne wala 1000 Aabido'n se behtar hai."_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p73)

                 ♦ _*SHIRK*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (520) 🌿

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يَغْفِرُ أَنْ يُشْرَكَ بِهِ وَيَغْفِرُ مَا دُونَ ذَٰلِكَ لِمَنْ يَشَاءُ ۚ وَمَنْ يُشْرِكْ بِاللَّهِ فَقَدِ افْتَرَىٰ إِثْمًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Beshak Allah is baat ko Ma'af nahi karta ke iske sath Shirk kiya jaye iske alawa jise chahe Ma'af karde aur jisne Khuda ke sath Shirk kiya to usne bahut bada jhoot tarasha hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 48)

📚📖  🌿
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
Ayat (4:48) ke padhne ke baad farmaya:
_"Shirk ke Alawa baaqi tamam Gunah qabil e Maghferat hain."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌿
Abil Abbas ne Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha: 'Mushrik  banne ki kam az kam had kiya hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Jo apni taraf se koi raye qayem kare aur isi ko me'yaar (criteria) bana kar Muhabbat o Nafrat kare."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
🌿
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Gunahan e Kabira ki ta'dad panch hai aur ye woh Gunah hain jin par Allah ne Dozakh ko Wajib kiya hai. Allah Ta'ala farmata hai: (4:48)."_
(Kitab Sawabul Aamal)
🌿
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Ta'ala tamam makhlooq se hisab lega nagar jisne Khuda ke sath Shirk kiya hoga usse hisab nahi lega aur uske liye hukm jari karega use Dozakh mein dal diya jaye."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)
🌿
Is Ayat ke zariye Mominin ko Ummeed o Khauf aur Fazlo o Adl ke darmiyan lakar khada kiya aur yehi Momin ki sifat hai.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar Momin ke Khauf aur Ummeed ka wazan kiya jaye to dono ka palda barabar hoga."_
(Majmaul Bayan)
🌿
Abil Abbas ne Imam Sadiq (as) se poochha: 'Mushrik  banne ki kam az kam had kiya hai?
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Jo apni taraf se koi raye qayem kare aur isi ko me'yaar (criteria) bana kar Muhabbat o Nafrat kare."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
🌿
To phir sawal paida hota hai ke isse Insaan ke doosre Gunahon ke liye hausla afzai hai???
Jawab: Jaisa ke pahle bhi arz kiya chuka hai ke Gunah ki Maafi Allah ke hath mein hai, jo Maafi ke layeq hoga wohi Maghferat payega. Ye sab Allah ke Hikmat ke taqazon par munhasir hai. Isliye zaroori nahi sab ke Gunah Ma'af ho jayen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌿
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Wilayat Ali (as) ka inkar na qabile Maafi jurm hai aur Muhibbane Ali (as) ke jin Gunahon ko Khuda chahe Ma'af kar dega."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)

                 ♦ _*SELFI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (521) 🍁

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ يُزَكُّونَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ ۚ بَلِ اللَّهُ يُزَكِّي مَنْ يَشَاءُ وَلَا يُظْلَمُونَ فَتِيلًا * انْظُرْ كَيْفَ يَفْتَرُونَ عَلَى اللَّهِ الْكَذِبَ ۖ وَكَفَىٰ بِهِ إِثْمًا مُبِينًا*

_"Kiya aap ne un logon ko nahi dekha jo apne Nafs ki Pakeezgi ka Ailan karte hain halanke Allah jisko chahta hai Pakeezgi ata karta hai aur bando par zarrah barabar bhi zulm nahi kiya jayega."_
_"Aap dekhen woh kis tarah se Khuda par jhoot tarash rahe hain unke Gunahgar hone ke liye yehi wazeh (clear) Gunah Kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 49 - 50)

📚📖 🍁
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Khud satai (Self Praise) ka tazkarah hai. Ayat to Yahood o Nasara ko mukhatib hai lekin ye nasihat sab ke liye hai.
Ya aam zaban mein yun kahen ke inke bol bachan zyada par kam mein zero hote hain. Sirf woh lambi lambi hankna jante hain.
Khud Satai ka source hai Khud bini, ghuroor, ghamand. Bahut si qaumo ki bad hali, ladai jhagde isi ka natija hain. Means har insaan ye samjhta hai ke mein hi Nek Pak o Pakeeza hun, baqi sab log usse kamtar hain. Lekin ye sab Fazilat Allah ata karta hai jo zara bhi zulm nahi karta, unka khud ka kuchh nahi hota. فتيلا _'Fateelah'_ Means usko kahte hain jo khajoor ki ghuthli par jo bareek si jhilli hoti hai. Means Allah itna bhi Zulm nahi karta.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍁
Imam Ali (as):
*(Ausaaf e Muttaqeen)*
_"Woh apne Aamal ki kam miqdar se mutmain nahi hote aur zyada ko zyada nahi samajhte. Woh apne hi Nafson par (kotahiyon) ka ilzam rakhte hain aur apne Aamal se khauf zada rahte hain aur jab un mein se kisi ki (Islah o Taqwa ki bina par) saraha jata hai to woh apne Haq mein kahi hui baton se laraz uthta hai aur kahta hai ke mein doosron se apne Nafs ko zyada janta hun aur mera Parwardigar mujhse bhi zyada mere Nafs ko janta hai. Khudaya! Unki baton par meri giraft na karna aur mere mutalliq ye ho Husn e Zan (+ve thinking) rakhte hain mujhe is se behtar qarar dena aur mere un Gunahon ko bakhsh dena jo unke ilm mein nahi hain."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*12th Rabius Sani 1438*
11th January 2016, Wednesday,

♦ _*ALE MOHD (AS) KA MULKE AZEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (523) 👑

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَمْ لَهُمْ نَصِيبٌ مِنَ الْمُلْكِ فَإِذًا لَا يُؤْتُونَ النَّاسَ نَقِيرًا * أَمْ يَحْسُدُونَ النَّاسَ عَلَىٰ مَا آتَاهُمُ اللَّهُ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ ۖ فَقَدْ آتَيْنَا آلَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَآتَيْنَاهُمْ مُلْكًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Kiya unka bhi Mulk o Hukumat mein koin hissa hai? Agar aisa hota to ye doosron ko phooti kodi bhi na dete. Phir kiya ye log doosre logon se Hasad karte hain ke Allah ne apne Fazl se unhe nawaza hai. (Agar unka yehi me'yar criteria hai to) hamne Ale Ibrahim ko Kitab o Hikmat ata ki hai aur hamne unko Mulke Azeem diya hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 53 - 54)

📚📖 👑
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se jab is ayat  اطيعوا الله و اطيعو االرسول و اولى الامر منكم ke bare mein sawal kiya gaya to Imam ne jawab mein ye Ayat (4:52) ka zikr kiya aur phir (4:54) ke zail mein farmaya:
"Aur yehi haal ham se munharif afraad ka hai ke woh gumrahi ke Rehbaron ki Ita'at karke us par fakhr karte hain aur kahten hain ke hamare ye Imam Ale Muhammad (as) behtar hain. To kiya unka bhi Mulk mein koi hissa hai.
Iski taaweel ye bhi hai ke kiya Ale Muhammad (as) ke siyasi hareefon ka Khilafat o Imamat e Ilahiyyah mein bhi koi hissa hai? Agar unka kuchh hissa hota to woh logon ko phooti kaudi ka mohtaj rakhte. نقير " Naqeer' dar asal darmiyani nuqte ko kaha jata hai jo khajoor ki ghuthli ke bairooni hisse par darmiyan mein hota hai. Means ye log Naqeer barabar bhi khuchh na dete.
Woh Mehsood log (jinse hasad karte hain) ham hi hain jinhe Khuda ne Imamat ke uhde se nawaza hai jiski wajah se log hamse Hasad karte hain. Allah ne Ale Ibrahim (as) par bada Fazl kiya, Allah ne is Khandan mein Anbiya o Rusul aur Aimma maboos farmaye. Tajjub hai ke log Ale Ibrahim (as) ki Imamat ko maan lete hain lekin Ale Muhammad (as) ki Imamat ko manne par amada nahi hain!!   "
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer Durrul Mansoor)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ke nazdeek logon ki manzilat (status) ka haal maalum karne ke liye ye dekho ke wo hum (Ahlebait (as) ki Ahadees bayaan karne mein kaise hain (aur apni taraf se uske maani (interpretation) to bayaan nahi karte)."_
(Al Kaafi, v1, p106)
😏
Imam Ali (as):
_”Hasad nekiyo'n ko is tarah tabaah kar deta hai jis tarah aag lakdiyo'n ko jalaa deti hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p180)
😏 👋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Musafeha karo, ke wo dil se Hasad aur Keena (nafrat) ko duur kar deta hai."_
(Al Kaafi, v4, p91)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*14th Rabius Sani 1438*
13th January 2016, Friday,

             ♦ _*DOZAKH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (524) ♨

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ آمَنَ بِهِ وَمِنْهُمْ مَنْ صَدَّ عَنْهُ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِجَهَنَّمَ سَعِيرًا * إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا بِآيَاتِنَا سَوْفَ نُصْلِيهِمْ نَارًا كُلَّمَا نَضِجَتْ جُلُودُهُمْ بَدَّلْنَاهُمْ جُلُودًا غَيْرَهَا لِيَذُوقُوا الْعَذَابَ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"In mein se kuchh us par Imaan laye hain aur kuchh ne moo moda hai. Moo modne walon ke liye Jahannam kafi hai. Beshak jin logo ne hamari Ayaat ka inkar kiya anqareeb ham unhe Dozakh mein jhonk denge. Jabke unki ek khaal pak jayegi to ham uski jagah doosri khaal tabdeel kar denge taake Azaab ka zaiqa chakhte rahen. Beshak Allah ghayeb aur Hikmat wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 55 - 56)

📚📖 ♨
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ayaat e Ilahi (Signs of Allah) ke tamam Munkarin ko Dozakh mein bheja jayega. Hazrat Ameerul Momenin aur Aimma e Huda bhi Ayaat (Allah ki Nishaniyon) mein shamil hain.
Jabke Aag unki khaal ko jala degi to uski jagah unhe doosri khaal pahna di jayegi taake unke Azaab mein tasalsul (continuity) qayem rahe.
Imam Sadiq (as) se jab khaal ki tabdeeli ke bare mein poochha gaya to Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Iski misaal yun samjho ke agar ek eint (brick) ko tum tod kar mitti mein tabdeel kar do, phir us mitti ko dye mein rakh kar naye sire se eint bana do to kiya wo wohi eint nahi hogi? Eint wohi hogi albatta wo nai sire se wujood mein layi gayi hogi."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim)
♨
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Husain bin Ali (as) ka qaatil Aag ke Sandooq mein hoga. Nisf (Half) Ahle Duniya ka Azaab uske liye makhsoos hoga. Uske haath pair Dozakh ki Aag ki Zanjeeron se bandhe honge. Uski Sadooq Dozakh mein palatte palatte Aakhirkar Dozakh ke nichle hisse mein ja giregi aur usse aisi badboo (bad smell) ke bhabhooke uthenge ke tamam Dozakhi is badboo ki Khuda ke samne shikayat karenge aur woh hamesha Azaab e Aleem mein mubtela rahega. Iske sath doosre Qatilaan e Imam Husain (as) bhi honge. Jab inki khaalen jal jayengi to unhen nahi khaalen pahna di jayegi taake Azaab ka silsila jari wa sari rahe. Unse ek lamhe ke liye bhi Azaab nahi hataya jayega aur unhe Dozakh ka ubalta hua paani pilaya jayega. Azaab e Dozakh ki wajah se un par Halakat ho."_
(Uyoonul Akhbaar, Noorus Saqlain)

Pas Ayaat o rivayaat ke mutabiq Dushmane Ahle Bait (as) ka Qayamat ke Din ye hashr hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ♨
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Dozakh walo'n mein sabse kam darje ka Azaab ye hai k Jahannumi ko aag ke 2 joote pehnaye jayenge jiski garmi se uska dimaag ubal jaayega."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*15th Rabius Sani 1438*
14th January 2016, Saturday,

               ♦ _*JANNAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (525) 🌳🌴🌾

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ سَنُدْخِلُهُمْ جَنَّاتٍ تَجْرِي مِنْ تَحْتِهَا الْأَنْهَارُ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ۖ لَهُمْ فِيهَا أَزْوَاجٌ مُطَهَّرَةٌ ۖ وَنُدْخِلُهُمْ ظِلًّا ظَلِيلًا)

_"Aur woh log jo Imaan laye aur Nek Amal kiye ham inhe aise Baghaat (Jannat) mein dakhil karenge jahan Nehren baih rahi hongi, jahan hamesha rahenge. Jannat mein unke liye Pakeeza Biwiyan hongi aur ham inhe ghani chhaon mein dakhil karenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 57)

📚📖 🌳🌴🌾🏞🏝
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Jaise ke guzishta Ayat mein zikr hua tha ke jo log Vilayat e Ahle Bait (as) ke inkar karenge unka Qayamat mein kiya hashr hoga. Kaise woh Dozakh mein jalenge. Uske baad Allah Ta'ala un logo ko Jannat ki basharat deta hai jo Vilayat ka iqraar karenge.
Ahadis mulaheza farmayen:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌳🌴🌾🏞🏝
Imam Baqir (as):
_" 'Zill' (Surah Furqaan, Surah 25, Ayat 45) tuloo e fajr aur tuloo e shams ke darmiyaan hai (between dawn and sunrise). (Ek aur riwayat mein hai ke) sab haalato'n se wo pakiza-tareen hai kyun ki andhera tabiyat mein nafrat ka baais hota hai aur aa'nkho'n ki binaayi (vision) kam hoti hai lekin suraj ki shu'a (sunrays) hawaa ko narm aur paakiza karti hai aur aa'nkho'n ki raushni ko zyada karti hai. Is liye Allah Ta'ala ne is se Jannat ki sifat ko bayaan farmaya hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p105)
🌾🌴🍃🍂
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Wilayat e Ali (as) ka itteba (follow / paalan) karna aur unki Wilayat ko tasleem karna tumhare umoor (affairs) ko pareshaan na hone dega, adl o insaaf ko tumse qaaem rakhega aur aakhir tumko Jannat mein pahu’ncha dega."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p81)
🌳🌴🍂
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Meri aur mere Ahlebait (as) ki Wilayat Jahannum se amaan ka waseela hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p232)
🏞 🌾🍂🌴
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_Jo shakhs ye chahta hai ke wo Jannat mein H. Khaleelullah (as) ke ghar ka hamsaya (padosi) ho aur Jahannum ki aag se mehfooz rahe to usko chahiye ke wo Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) se mohabbat kare aur uski Wilayat ka iqraar kare."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v2, p365)
🌾🍂🌴🍃
Imam Mehdi (atfs)
se puchha gaya ke Ahle Jannat ke yahaa'n Jannat mein bachche bhi paida honge? Aap ne farmaya: _"Jannat aurato'n ke haamela (pregnant) hone ka maqaam nahi hai aur kisi ki paidaish ka maqaam nahi hai…aur wahaa'n bachpane ki kamzoriyaa'n bhi nahi hongi. Iske bawajood Ahle Jannat ko har wo ne'mat haasil hogi jis ki dil khwaaish karenge aur jo aa'nkho'n ke liye lazzat ka sabab hogi. Albatta, jab Momin bete ki khwaaish karega to Allah usay hamal aur wiladat (pregnancy aur birth) ke bagair hi beta de dega."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p558)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

             ♦ _*AMAANAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (526) 💰👏🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ اللَّهَ يَأْمُرُكُمْ أَنْ تُؤَدُّوا الْأَمَانَاتِ إِلَىٰ أَهْلِهَا وَإِذَا حَكَمْتُمْ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ أَنْ تَحْكُمُوا بِالْعَدْلِ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ نِعِمَّا يَعِظُكُمْ بِهِ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ سَمِيعًا بَصِيرًا*

_"Beshak Allah tumhe Hukm deta hai ke Amanaten unke Malikon tak pahunchao aur jab logon ke darmiyan faisla karo to Adl se karo. Allah tumhe Behtareen Nasihat karta hai. Beshak Allah Sunnewala, Dekhnewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 58)

📚📖 💰👏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj ki Ayat mein do baton ka zikr hai:
(1) Amanat ki adaigi,
(2) logon ke darmiyan Adl se kaam lena.
Amanat ke bare mein ye milta hai bhale hi Kuffare Quraish Rasoole Khuda (saww) ke Dushman the lekin apni Amanaten unhi ke pas rakhte the kiyonki woh unko Ameen mante the. Jahan Khayanat woh kabhi soch bhi nahi sakte the. Isliye Hijrat ke waqt jab Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Makkah chhoda to unhone apne Dushmano ki Amanaton ko unke Malikon ko lautane ki zimmedari Hazrat Ali (as) sipurd ki aur Ameen banaya.
(Detail Kitabon mein darj hai.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰👏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Amaanat uske maalik ko lauta do chaahe wo Imam Husain (as) ka qaatil hi kyun na ho."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p236)
💰👏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Logo'n ki Amaanat rakhne se Rozi aati hai aur amaanat mein Khayaanat karne se Faqeeri aati hai."_
(Tuhaful Uqool)
💰👏🏻
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Namaz, Zakat, Roza, Hajj ki adaigi bhi Amanat ka hissa hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*ULIL AMR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (527)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُوا الرَّسُولَ وَأُولِي الْأَمْرِ مِنْكُمْ ۖ فَإِنْ تَنَازَعْتُمْ فِي شَيْءٍ فَرُدُّوهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ خَيْرٌ وَأَحْسَنُ تَأْوِيلًا*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Ita'at karo Allah ki aur Ita'at karo Rasool ki aur un logo ki jo tum mein Sahib e Amr hon. Phir agar tumhare darmiyan kisi maamle mein tanaza (dispute) ho jaye to use Allah aur Rasool ki taraf pher do agar waqai Allah aur Roze Akherat par Imaan rakhte ho. Yehi behtar aur anjam ke lehaz se Ahsan tariqa hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 59)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is mein discussion kafi Taveel hai, ikhtesar se kuchh points rivayaat ki roshni mein bayan kar rahe hain.
*Sawal:*
Kiya Ulil Amr ki zaroorat hai? Agar hai to kaun hona chahiye?
*Jawab:*
1. Hudood e Ilahi ke nigehbaan aur Ahkam e Ilahi ka nifaz.
2. Qaum o Milat ko uske chief ki zaroorat hoti hai taake uski hifazat kare.
3. Ummat e Islamiya ko bikharne se bachana.
4. Rehbar Masoom hona chahiye, agar Masoom nahi hoga to uske follower ko ye itemad nahi hoga, woh ghalti karega to follower bhi ghalti karenge. Natija ye agar Rehbar hi Jahannam jay to uske followers bhi Jahannam mein ja sakte hain. Agar log uski hidayat karen to phir woh Rehbar kaisa.
5. Rehbar Ale Rasool mein se hi ho kiyonki doosron ke Masoom hone ki koi guarantee nahi. Jabke ye baat musallam hai ke Ahle Bait (as) har lehaz se Afzal hain, to unhe chhod kisi aur Mafzool ko Rehbar maan len to ye bewaqoofi hogi.
6. Isliye Ulil Amr koi bhi Hakim, Muslim Badshah, desh ka sarbrah nahi ho sakta kiyonki aisi koi guarantee nahi ke woh aap par zulm kar raha hai.
7. Jaisa ke har Musalman manta hai ke Nabiyon jo ke Rehbar the, unko Allah ne muqarrar kiya, isliye Ulil Amr bhi logon ka muntakhab shuda nahi, balke Allah ki taraf se appointed hona chahiye.
(Iqtebas Uyoonul Akhbar Ar Reza)

(To be Cont'd .....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasool e Khuda (saww):
_"Jabir (ibne Abdullah Ansari)! Wo (Ulil Amr) mere Khalifa hain aur mere baad woh Musalmano ke Imam hain. Un mein se Pehle Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) hain, phir Hasan (as) hain, phir Husain (as) hain, phir Ali ibnul Husain (as) hain, phir Mohd ibne Ali (as) hain, jinka Torat mein laqab "Baqir" hai (aur Jabir tum unse mulaqat karoge. Jab tumhari unse mulaqat ho to meri taraf se unhe Salam kahna) phir Jafar Sadiq bin Mohd (as) hain, phir Moosa bin Jafar (as), phir Ali bin Moosa (as), phir Mohd bin Ali (as), phir Ali bin Mohd (as) hain, phir Hasan bin Ali (as) hain, phir woh Imam honge jo mere ham naam aur meri ham kunniyat honge. Woh zameen par Khuda ki Hujjat aur bando mein Khuda ka Baqiyyah honge. Aur woh Hasan bin Ali ke farzand honge. Allah Ta'ala uske haath par East & West ko Fatah karega. Woh apne doston aur Shiyon se Ghaibat ikhtiyar karenge. Zaman e Ghaibat mein unki Imamat ke Aqeede par wohi qaem rahega jiske dil ka Khuda ne Imtihan liya hoga....."_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Noorus Saqlain)

             ♦ _*ULIL AMR*_ ♦
( *Those who are Authority among you*)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (527) 👑

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُوا الرَّسُولَ وَأُولِي الْأَمْرِ مِنْكُمْ ۖ فَإِنْ تَنَازَعْتُمْ فِي شَيْءٍ فَرُدُّوهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ خَيْرٌ وَأَحْسَنُ تَأْوِيلًا*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Ita'at karo Allah ki aur Ita'at karo Rasool ki aur un logo ki jo tum mein Sahib e Amr hon. Phir agar tumhare darmiyan kisi maamle mein tanaza (dispute) ho jaye to use Allah aur Rasool ki taraf pher do agar waqai Allah aur Roze Akherat par Imaan rakhte ho. Yehi behtar aur anjam ke lehaz se Ahsan tariqa hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 59)

📚📖 👑
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Isse pahle hamne bataya ke Ulil Amr se murad na koi Badshah, King ya hukmuran hain, balke Ale Rasool, Ahle Bait (as) hain. Islam ke 73 firqon mein se sirf Shia firqa Ahle Bait (as) ko apna Imam wa Rehbar manta hai. Rehbar ki kiya khusisiyat honi chahiye ye hamne kal bataya.
Ayat ne ye bhi ishaara kar diya ke is matter mein tanaza (dispute) wa ikhtelaf to hoga. To Allah ne iska solution bhi isi Ayat mein bataya diya. Means matter ke solution ke liye Allah wa Rasool ki taraf rujoo wa refer karen. Kal ham ne Rasool (saww) ke ek qaul ko pesh kiya tha. Aaj kuchh aur ahadis mulaheza farmayen.
👑
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Iska mafhoom ye nahi ke agar tumhara Ulil Amr se tanaza ho jaye, balke iska mafhoom ye hai ke agar Ulil Amr ke tayyum (Choosing) mein tumhara apas mein ikhtelaf ho jaye ke kaun Ulil Amr hain? to isle liye Khuda aur Rasool (saww) ki taraf rujoo karo, jise woh Ulil Amr qarar den uski ghair mashroot (unconditional) ita'at karo. Warna ye baat na mumkin hai ke Khuda unki ita'at ka hukm bhi de aur unse jhagadne ki bhi ijazat de de."_
(Rozatul Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
👑
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Ulil Amr Masoom (Infallible) aur Mathar (Pure, Clean) hain. Woh kabhi Gunah nahi karte aur Khuda ki nafarmani nahi Karte. Wo Moayyad (Supporter), Mowaffaq aur Khuda ki taraf se musaddad (appointed) hote hain. Allah unki wajah se bando ko Rizq deta hai hai aur Shehro ko abad rakhta hai aur unki wajah se Aasman se barish hoti hai aur unki wajah se Zameen ki Barkat zahoor pazeer hoti hai aur unki wajah se nafarmano ko mohlat di jati hai aur un par jald saza nazil nahi hoti. Roohul Quds unse alaihda nahi hota aur woh Roohul Quds se alaihda nahi hote aur na woh Quran se juda hote hain aur na Qur'an unse juda hota hai."_
(Kitab Ilalus Sharay, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👑
Ameerul Momenin Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Allah ko Allah ki hasiyat se pahchano aur Rasool ko Risalat se Pahchano aur Ulil Amr ko Neki, Adl aur Ehsan se Pahchano."_
(Kitabut Tauheed)

*20th Rabius Sani 1438*
19th January 2016, Thursday,

            ♦ _*ULIL AMR*_ ♦
( *Ulema e Ahle Sunnat ki Nazar mein*)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (527) 🇵🇰

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا أَطِيعُوا اللَّهَ وَأَطِيعُوا الرَّسُولَ وَأُولِي الْأَمْرِ مِنْكُمْ ۖ فَإِنْ تَنَازَعْتُمْ فِي شَيْءٍ فَرُدُّوهُ إِلَى اللَّهِ وَالرَّسُولِ إِنْ كُنْتُمْ تُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ ۚ ذَٰلِكَ خَيْرٌ وَأَحْسَنُ تَأْوِيلًا*

_"Aye Imaanwalo! Ita'at karo Allah ki aur Ita'at karo Rasool ki aur un logo ki jo tum mein Sahib e Amr hon. Phir agar tumhare darmiyan kisi maamle mein tanaza (dispute) ho jaye to use Allah aur Rasool ki taraf pher do agar waqai Allah aur Roze Akherat par Imaan rakhte ho. Yehi behtar aur anjam ke lehaz se Ahsan tariqa hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 59)

📚📖 🇵🇰
👉 _*Tafseer:*_ (Cont'd..)
Ulema e Ahle Sunnat ke is Ayat ke zel mein mukjtalif nazaryat hain. Baaz ko ham yahan quote kar rahe hain:
🇵🇰
Mashoor Mufassir Qur'an Fakhruddin Razi is Ayat ke zel mein kahte hain ke Ulil Amr ka Masoom (معصوم عن الخطا) hona zaroori hai agar nahi to woh khata karega, jabke Khuda ne Ulil Amr ki Ita'at ko lazim qarar diya hai, to is hukm mein tazad (contradiction) paya jayega, means ek taraf khata karna ya follow karna haram hai lekin ita'at bhi wajib. Masoom ka na hona Aqle Salim ke khilaf hai.'
(Tafseer e Kabeer Razi, Vol 10, P-144)
Isse ye baat zahir hai ke Rehbar ka Masoom hona zaroori hai. Tarikh mein hamne dekha ke kisi ne bhi Ismat (infallibility) ka dawa nahi kiya siwai Ahle Bait (as) ke jo ke Ale Rasool (saww) hain.
🇵🇰
Mashoor Islami Mufassir Abu Hayyan Andalusi Maghribi (D: 756 AH) Tafseer Bahrul Muheet mein likhte hain ke ya Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) aur Aimma Ahle Bait (as) ki shaan mein nazil hui.
(Behrul Muheet, Vol 3, P-278)
🇵🇰
Alim e Ahle Sunnat Abu Bakr bin Momin Shirazi Risala e Eteqaad mein (Manaqibe Kashi) ibne Abbas se naql karte hain ke ye Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) ki shaan mein us waqt nazil hui jab Paighambar e Islam (saww) ne inhe Jang e Tubuk ke mauqe par apni jagah Medina mein chhoda tha aur Rasool e Akram (saww) ne Ali (as) se farmaya:
_*"Kiya tum pasand nahi karte ke tumhe mujh se wohi nisbat hai jo Haroon ko Moosa (as) se thi jabke Moosa (as) ne unse kaha tha ke tum Bani Israel mein mere Janasheen (Caliph) ban jao aur unki islah karo. Uske baad farmaya Khuda wande Alam ne farmaya: (4:59)*"_
(Ehqaqul Haq, Vol 3, P-478)
🇵🇰
To phir sawal yahi baqi rah jata hai ke jab Rasoole Khuda (as) ne Ahle Bait (as) ko min janibe Khuda apna Janashin bana diya to phir kisi aur ke daman ko kiyon pakde hain!!!!!!
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🇵🇰
'Ek din ek shakhs Hazrat Ali (as) ki khidmat mein hazir hua. Usne poochha kam az kam wo kaunsi cheez hai jiske zariye Insaan Momin ki saff mein shamil ho sakta hai aur kam az kam wo kaunsi cheez hai jisse Insaan Kafiron ya Gumrah logon mein shumar ho jata hai?
Hazrat Amirul Momenin (as) ne farmaya:
_"Kam az kam wo cheez jiski wajah se Insaan Gumrahon mein shamil ho jata hai ye hai ke woh Khuda ki Hujjat aur Numainde (representative) se aur uske Shahid o Gawah ko, jiski Ita'at o Vilayat zaroori hai, na pahchane."_
Poochha kaun hai woh?
Farmaya:
_"Woh wohi hain jinhe Khuda ne apne Paighambar ke barabar qarar diya hai.(4:59)"_
_"Rasoolullah (saww) ne mukhtalif mauqon par aur apne Akhiri Khutbe mein tazkarah kiya:_
_*"Mein tumhare darmiyan do cheezen bataur yadgar chhod raha hun agar tum inse tamassuk (touch) mein raho ge to mere baad hargiz Gumrah na honge: 'Khuda ki Kitab aur meri Itrat jo mere Ahle Bait hain."*_
(Kitab e Ahle Sunnat: Yanabiul Mawaddah, P-114, 116)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

            ♦ _*TAGHOOT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (528) 👺👹😈

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ يَزْعُمُونَ أَنَّهُمْ آمَنُوا بِمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ يُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَتَحَاكَمُوا إِلَى الطَّاغُوتِ وَقَدْ أُمِرُوا أَنْ يَكْفُرُوا بِهِ وَيُرِيدُ الشَّيْطَانُ أَنْ يُضِلَّهُمْ ضَلَالًا بَعِيدًا*

_"Aye Paighambar! Kiya Aap ne un logon ko nahi dekha jo ye guman karte hain ke woh us Kitab par Imaan laye hain jo Aap ki taraf nazil ki gayi hai aur woh un Kitabon par bhi Imaan rakhte hain jo Aap se pahle utari gayi hain magar chahte hain ke apne ma'amelat ka faisla Taghoot se karayen. Halanke unhe Taghoot ke inkar Hukm diya gaya hai. Shaitan to inhe bhatka kar rahe raast se door le jana chahta hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 60)

📚📖 👺👹😈
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Pichhli Ayat mein Allah ka hukm hua ke _*Ulil Amr*_(Sabane Amr) ki ita'at karo, rivayaton se ye bhi wazeh hua ke ye Ahle Bait (as) yani Rasool wa Ale Rasool (saww) hain. Aaj ki ayat usi baat ko aur takmeel kar rahi hai. Is Ayat mein un munafeqeen ki taraf ishaara hai jo Dushman e Rasool wa Ale Rasool the. Is ayat ne Taghoot ki pairavi karne ke liye mana kiya. Ye un Batil Rehbaron ki taraf bhi ishaara kar rahi hai jinhone Rasool (saww) se baghawat ki aur unke baad mein unhone ne apni taraf dawat di.
Jo Shakhs Haq ke khilaf faisla kare, aur log uske pas faisla karwane jayen, woh Taghoot hain.
Pichhli ayaat mein bhi takeed ki gayi thi ke Jibt o Taghoot ki pairavi na karen. Aur ye kaun hain ham pahle bata chuke hain. 1 2 3.
🏴
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jisne bhi Gumrahi ka parcham buland kiya to woh Taghoot hai."_
(Roza e Kafi)
👹👺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)!...Khuda ki qasam! Aap se mohabbat wo rakkhega jo Momin hoga aur bugz wo rakkhega jo Munafiq (hypocrite) hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👺👹😈
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Munafiq ki 3 nishaniyaa'n hain:_
_(1) Jab baat karta hai to jhoot bolta hai,_
_(2) Jab waada karta hai to waada khilaafi karta hai,_
_(3) Jab amaanat rakhi jaati hai to khayaanat karta hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p188)
👹👺
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Kitna bura wo shakhs hai jo 2 chehre aur 2 zabaan waala ho - yaani Munafiq ho; saamne apne biradar e Momin ki taarif kare aur peethh pichhe geebat kare."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)

            ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa    Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (512) 👹

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا قِيلَ لَهُمْ تَعَالَوْا إِلَىٰ مَا أَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ وَإِلَى الرَّسُولِ رَأَيْتَ الْمُنَافِقِينَ يَصُدُّونَ عَنْكَ صُدُودًا * فَكَيْفَ إِذَا أَصَابَتْهُمْ مُصِيبَةٌ بِمَا قَدَّمَتْ أَيْدِيهِمْ ثُمَّ جَاءُوكَ يَحْلِفُونَ بِاللَّهِ إِنْ أَرَدْنَا إِلَّا إِحْسَانًا وَتَوْفِيقًا * أُولَٰئِكَ الَّذِينَ يَعْلَمُ اللَّهُ مَا فِي قُلُوبِهِمْ فَأَعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ وَعِظْهُمْ وَقُلْ لَهُمْ فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ قَوْلًا بَلِيغًا*

_"Jab unse kaha jata hai ke aao us cheez ki taraf jo Allah ne nazil ki hai aur Rasool ki taraf aao to Aap dekhenge ke Munafiq Aap ke pas aane se katrate hain."_
_"Phir us waqt kiya hota hai jab unke haath ki layi musibat un par aan padti hai?"_
_"Us waqt ye Aap ke pas qasmen khaate hue aate hain aur kahte hain ke Khuda ki Qasam! Ham to sirf bhalai chahte the aur hamari Niyyat sirf yehi thi ke fariqain mein kisi tarah muwafeqat (accommodate) ho jaye."_
_"Allah Janta hai jo kuchh unke dilon mein hai unse ta'aruz (turn away) mat karo balke unhe samjhao aur aisi nasihat karo jo unke dilon mein utar jaye."_
(Surah Nisa: 61 - 63)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Phichhli Ayaton mein jo Munafeqeen ka zikr hua jo Taghoot ki pairavi karte hain. Ye kaun hain woh ham bata chuke hain (1 2 3).
Ab sab unko Seedhe Raaste par bulaya jata hai to aane se katrate hain. Quran, Rasool (saww), Ale Rasool (as) hi Seedha Raasta hai.
Lekin jab koi musibat aan padti to Panjatan ka wasta de kar duayen mangte hai aur kahte hain Ali ka daman nahi chhodenge.
Yahan musibat se murad pareshaniya, badbakhtiyan hain jo unhi ki wajah se aati hain. Ye unke liya Khuda ka Azaab hai.
Akheri Ayat ke mutabiq ye tanbeeh bhi ki hai ke bhale hi woh Munafiqat par utre hue hain lekin hamen unko chhodna nahi hai balke hamara farz hai ke Nasihat jari rakhen. Mean inteqami sulook se mana kiya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡
Imam Sadiq (as)
se kisi shakhs ne kaha, "Allah aap ko jazaa e khair ataa farmaye. Kya Hazrat Ali (as) Deen mein pukhta aur qawi (firm and strong) nahi the?" Aap (as) ne farmaya, "Haa'n, wo qawi the". Usne kaha, "Phir qaum kis tarah unpar ghaalib aa gayi aur unhone iska difaa (defend) nahi kiya aur na unko roka". To Aap (as) ne farmaya: _"Kitaab e Khuda mein ek Ayat hai jisne unko is baat se roka"._
Us shakhs ne kaha, "Wo kaun si Aayat hai?"
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
( *لَوْ تَزَيَّلُوا لَعَذَّبْنَا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*) [Surat Al-Fath 25]
_"'Lav Tazayyalu La'azzabnallazina Kafaru Minhum 'Azaaban Aleema'."_ _Kyun ki Allah Azza wa Jall ki Momin amaanatein Kaafiro'n aur Munafiqo'n ki sulbo'n (loins) mein maujood the to Ali (as) ke liye ye mumkin nahi tha ke unke aaba (purvaj) ko qatl kare de'n ta waqt ye ke amaanatein paida ho jaayein aur jab amaanatein nikal aayi'n to Ali (as) unpe hamlawar huwe aur unse muqabila kiya. Isi tarah hamare Ahlebait (as) ke Qaim (atfs) ka us waqt tak Zahoor na hoga jab tak Allah ki Amaanatein paida na ho jaayein phir wo apne Mukhaalifeen par ghalba Haasil kar ke unko qatl karenge"._
(Kamaluddin, v2, p608)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hargiz (munafiq) logo'n ki Masajid ki tadaad aur (Namaz e ba) jamaat se dhoka na khao; inke jism ikatthe lekin dil bikhre huwe hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*23rd Rabius Sani 1438*, 22nd January 2016, Sunday,

    ♦ _*WASILA E BAKHSHISH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (530) 🙏🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا أَرْسَلْنَا مِنْ رَسُولٍ إِلَّا لِيُطَاعَ بِإِذْنِ اللَّهِ ۚ وَلَوْ أَنَّهُمْ إِذْ ظَلَمُوا أَنْفُسَهُمْ جَاءُوكَ فَاسْتَغْفَرُوا اللَّهَ وَاسْتَغْفَرَ لَهُمُ الرَّسُولُ لَوَجَدُوا اللَّهَ تَوَّابًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Hamne koi Rasool nahi bheje magar isliye ke Hukm e Khuda se uski Ita'at ki jaye. Agar ye mukhalefat karne wale jo apne aap par zulm karte hain (Khuda ke Hukm ko pao tale rondte hain) Aapke pas aate aur Khuda se Maghferat mangte aur Paighambar bhi unke liye isteghfar karte to woh Khuda wande Alam ko Tauba Qubool karne wala aur Maherban paate."_
(Surah Nisa: 64)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Pichhli Ayaton se munsalik is ayat mein Payambare Akram (saww) ki Ita'at ka Hukm Allah de raha hai. Gunehgaron ke liye inko Shafi banaya hai. Inke wasile se agar Allah se Maghferat talab ki jaye to zaroor mustajab hogi. Allah khud kah raha hai agar Rasool e Khuda (saww) ka Wasila ikhtiyar karo. Isliye jo Rasoole Khuda ko apne jaisa samjhte hain aur Rasool ki Shafa'at ke munkir hain woh is Ayat ko jhutla rahe hain. Allah Buzurg o Bartar o Aala ke saamne ye nacheez khaati gunehgar banda kaise saamna kar sakta hai. Isliye wasile ki zaroorat hai.
Rivayat ke mutabiq agar Rasoole Khuda (saww) Shaher hain to Hazrat Ali (as) uska Darwaza hain. Isliye Rasool ke pas jane se pahle Hazrat Ali (as) ke raaste se guzarna hoga. Isliye pahle Shafa'at Ahle Bait (as) ke zariye hogi.
🙏🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
"Rasool e Akram (saww) ki hayaat mein ek gunehgar shakhs Rasool ke pas bakhshish ke liye aa raha tha. Raaste mein Imam Hasan o Husain (as) dikhai diye to unko kandho par bitha kar Rasoole Khuda (saww) ki khidmat mein hazir hua aur kaha:
_" Ya Rasoolallah! Mein in Shehzadon ke waste se Khuda se panah ka talabfar hun."_
Ye dekhkar Aanhazrat (saww) muskurai aur farmaya: "Jao tum azad ho."
Iske baad Imam Hasan o Husain (as) se farmaya:
_"Us gunehgar ke mutalliq meine tumhari Shifarish qubool ki."_ Tab ye Ayat (4:64) nazil hui.
(Kitab Al Manaqib, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Roz e Qayamat tum mein se mere nazdeek-tareen aur meri Shafa'at ka haq-daar wo hoga jo Sach bolne wala, Amaanat ka adaa karne wala aur khush-khalq (good-natured / well-mannered) hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p471)

             ♦ _*TASLEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (531) 😌😞

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلَا وَرَبِّكَ لَا يُؤْمِنُونَ حَتَّىٰ يُحَكِّمُوكَ فِيمَا شَجَرَ بَيْنَهُمْ ثُمَّ لَا يَجِدُوا فِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ حَرَجًا مِمَّا قَضَيْتَ وَيُسَلِّمُوا تَسْلِيمًا*

_"Nahi Ay Muhammad! Tumhare Rab ki Qasam! Ye kabhi Momin ho hi nahi sakte jab tak ke apne bahami ikhtelafat mein ye tumko Faisla karne wala maan len, phir jo kuchh tum faisla karo us par apne dilon mein bhi tangi mehsoos na karen, balke sar basar tasleem kar len."_
(Surah Nisa: 65)

📚📖 😌😞
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein bhi pichhle zikr ko jari rakhte hue Rasool (saww) ki ita'at ka hukm ki pairavi ki takeed ki gayi hai. Apne ikhtelafat ko Rasool (saww) ke zariye suljhayen. Rasool (saww) ke baad Ale Rasool (as) ke pas jayen. Rasool (saww) aur Ale Rasool (as) hamare liye raafe' ikhtelafat hain. Unke faisla na maanna kufr hai. Rasool wa Ale Rasool (as) ki maujoodgi mein apni raye rakhna jasarat hogi. Ye qaul ke _"Paighambar (saww) ne ye farmaya tha aur mein ye kahta hun"_ mein tazaad (contradiction) paya jayega, aur nafarmani kahlaygi, jis cheez ko Rasool (saww) halal kiya, usko agar koi haram kare, ye bhi nafarmani hai, kisi Ahkam ko badal dena ya bidat karna, jasarat hogi,  jabke hukm ye hua hai ke baghair chun o chara ke sar kham karke tasleem karna. Islam (religion) kuchh nahi bas Tasleem hai. (الاسلام هو التسليم).
😌😞
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) se Zaid Shakham ne arz kiya ke hamare pas ek shakhs rahta hai jiska naam "Kaleeb" hai. Uske saamne Aapka jab bhi koi farman pesh kiya jata hai to woh fauran kahta hai ke mein use tasleem karta hun. Isi jazba e tasleem ki wajah se woh "Kaleeb Tasleem" naam se mashoor ho gaya hai. Aap (as) ne uske liye dua e khair farmayi aur kaha:
_"Jaante ho ke Tasleem kiya hai?"_
Aap (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tasleem Khushoo (Humbleness) aur jhuk jaane ka naam hai."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😌😞
Imam Baqar (as):
_"....Wajah ye hai ke Uska har Fe'l Hikmat o Sawab par mabni hai. Woh Mutakabbir, Jabbar, Wahid o Qahaar hai. Uske Faisle ke khilaf jiske dil mein tangi mehsoos ho woh Kafir hai aur jis ne Uske kisi Fe'l ka inkar kiya to usne Haq o Sadaqat ka inkar kiya."_
(Kitabut Tawheed, Noorus Saqlain)

        ♦ _*ITA'AT E KHUDA*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (532) 😌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْ أَنَّا كَتَبْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ أَنِ اقْتُلُوا أَنْفُسَكُمْ أَوِ اخْرُجُوا مِنْ دِيَارِكُمْ مَا فَعَلُوهُ إِلَّا قَلِيلٌ مِنْهُمْ ۖ وَلَوْ أَنَّهُمْ فَعَلُوا مَا يُوعَظُونَ بِهِ لَكَانَ خَيْرًا لَهُمْ وَأَشَدَّ تَثْبِيتًا * وَإِذًا لَآتَيْنَاهُمْ مِنْ لَدُنَّا أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا * وَلَهَدَيْنَاهُمْ صِرَاطًا مُسْتَقِيمًا*

_"Agar Hamne unhe Hukm diya hota ke apne aap ko halak kar do ya apne gharon se nikal jao to un mein se kam hi aadmi is par amal karte. Halanke jo nasihat unhe ki jati hai agar ye us par amal karte to ye unke liye zyada behtari aur zyada sabit qadmi ka mojib hota."_
_"Aur jab ye aisa karte to Ham unhe Apni taraf se bahut bada Ajr dete."_
_"Aur unhe Seedha Raasta dikha dete."_
(Surah Nisa: 66 - 68)

📚📖 😌
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Allah ne ham par koi mushkil Hukm nahi diya, balke sirf wohi Hukm diya jo ham kar sakte hai. Allah ke Ahkam itne sakht nahi jitna hamko lagte hain. Yahan Allah ne misal di hai, jab Yahoodiyon ko Allah ne saza di to Hukm diya ke ek doosre ko qatl karen. Ya nikal bhagen. Unhone aisa kiya bhi. Lekin agar is tarah ke sakht hukm hame diye jate to us par amal karna dushwar hota.
Allah ka har Hukm hamare liye fayda bakhsh hota hai aur Imaan ki taqwiyat ka mojib hota hai. Jis qadr Insaan Khuda ke Hukm ki ita'at ki raah mein qadam badhaiga us qadr us mein isbaat aur isteqamat (Stability & Steadfastness) paida hogi. Khuda ke farman ki ita'at ek Roohani exercise hai jisse Roohani quwwat mein izafa hota hai. Is tarah woh slowly slowly aise maqam par pahunch jata hai jahan koi quwwat uske Imaan par ghalib (overcome) nahi aa sakti aur na dhoka de sakti hai.
Seedha Raasta, Tasleem o Raza ke bare mein ham pahle explain kar chuke hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😌😞
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aalim wo hai jo Khuda ki taraf se aql rakhta ho, Uski ita'at ke mutabiq amal karta ho aur Uski naraazgi se bachta ho."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p23)
😌😞
Imam Ali (as):
_"…Dushmano'n ke zulm par Sabr karo kyun ki jis Zaalim ne tumhare maamle mein Allah ki na-farmaani ki hai uska behtareen badla Allah ki ita'at karne mein hai. Allah khud usko Azaab e Jahannum mein giraftaar karega."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p135)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*26th Rabius Sani 1438*, 25th January 2016, Wednesday,

         ♦ _*AJRE ITA'AT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (533) 👥

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يُطِعِ اللَّهَ وَالرَّسُولَ فَأُولَٰئِكَ مَعَ الَّذِينَ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِمْ مِنَ النَّبِيِّينَ وَالصِّدِّيقِينَ وَالشُّهَدَاءِ وَالصَّالِحِينَ ۚ وَحَسُنَ أُولَٰئِكَ رَفِيقًا * ذَٰلِكَ الْفَضْلُ مِنَ اللَّهِ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ عَلِيمًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Khuda aur Rasool ki ita'at kare to woh (Qayamat ke Din) aise logon ka sathi hoga jin par Khuda ne apni Nemat tamam kar di hai aur woh Anbiya (Prophets), Siddiqeen (Truthfuls), Shohada (Martyrs), aur Sulaha (Pious) mein se hain aur woh behtareen Rafeeq (Sathi) hain."_
_"Ye Khuda wande Alam ka Fazl o Karam hai aur ye baat kafi hai ke Woh (Bando ke halaat, Niyyaton aur Aamal se) Aagah hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 69 - 70)

📚📖 👥
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj Republic Day hai. Aaj ke din India ka Aeen (constitution) amal mein aya. Ab jo is ko follow karega usko Govt appreciate karegi, ezaaz o Award se nawaza jayega. Jo nahi follow karega usko punish kiya jayega.
Is Ayat mein bhi yehi farmaya gaya hai. Agar ham Muslim hai to Islam ke  Aeen ko follow karna hoga. Farmaya gaya jo Allah aur Rasool ki ita'at karega Qayamat ke Din usko un 4 sathiyon ke sath rakha jayega jin par Allah ki Nematen nazil hui. Surah Al Hamd mein bhi ye dua mangte hain.
_"Hamen un raaste par chala jin par Allah ki Nematen nazil hui na ke Gumrah ke raaste par."_
Is ayat mein in Nemat yafta Hazrat ka zikr hai.
Riwayaton se wazahat ho jayegi ke ye kaun Hazraat hain.
(1) *Anbiya:* (1,24,000 Paighambar)
(2) *Siddiqeen:* Sachche log. Ye Amirul Momenin wa Aimma (as) hain.
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Siddiq 3 hain: (1) Hazrat Ali (as), (2) Habib Najjar (3) Momin e Ale Firon."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
_"Har Ummat mein Siddiq aur Farooq hota hai aur is ummat ka Siddiq aur Farooq Ali Ibne Abi Talib (as) hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar)
(3) *Shohada:* Imam Hasan o Husain (as).
(4) *Saleheen:* Shia:
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Juma ki Raaton mein hamari khusoosi shaan hoti hai. Aur Saleheen se woh log murad hain jo Ameerul Momin (as) aur ham par Imaan laye hain."_
👥
"Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka talluq Bazm e Anbiya se hain. Hazrat Ali (as) Bazm e Siddiqeen ke Afzal Fard hain. Hasan o Husain (as) Shuhada (Martyrs) ke Sardar hain. Aimma e Huda (Imams) ka talluq Bazm e Saleheen se hain aur Qaim e Ale Mohd (atfs) ka talluq *وَحَسُنَ أُولَٰئِكَ رَفِيقًا* se hain."
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim)

Ye followers, ita'at guzar bando ki khush bakhti hogi ke Qayamat ke Din unko aise saathi milenge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Jo khwaishaat e nafs ki pairavi karega, wo dushman ki khwaishaat poori karega."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p209)
🌻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aajiz (incapable / asamarth) wo hai jo nafsaani khwahishaat ki pairavi kare aur amal ke baghair Allah se ummeedein waabasta rakhe."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v1, p52)

            ♦ _*SELF DEFENCE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (534) 🗡⚔🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا خُذُوا حِذْرَكُمْ فَانْفِرُوا ثُبَاتٍ أَوِ انْفِرُوا جَمِيعًا*

_"Aye Ahle Imaan! Muqabile ke liye har waqt tayyar raho. Phir mauqa wa maqam ki munasib ki munasibat se alag alag daston (regiment) ki shakl mein niklo ya ikatthe (combined) ho kar."_
(Surah Nisa: 71)

📚📖 🗡⚔🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ale Imaan ke liye aam qanoon hai. Aql ka bhi yehi taqaza hai ke agar zinda rahna hai to apne difa ka khayal rakha jaye. Jo fard aur qaum apne difa se ghafil ho jaye to woh khoon Ashaam dushman ke liye tar niwala sabit hoti hai. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne Musalmano ko takeed ki ke woh har waqt difa ke liye tayyar rahen. Ye Ayat Jange Uhud ke baad nazil hui thi. Dushman ke khatrat se mehfooz rahne ke liye Musalman ko apni difa mazboot karni hogi.

Yahan حذر (Hizr) ke mukhtalif meaning hain. Ba rivayat Imam Mohd Baqir (as) ke iska meaning hai "apna aslah (weapons) hath mein pakad lo. Aur ثبات means "mushtarka fauj" hai.
(Majmaul Bayan)

Yahan ye dhiyan rahe Islam ne difa ka hukm diya hai, attack ya dushman par hamla karne ka hukm nahi diya. Apni hifazat ka hukm diya hai.
Isliye ajkal jo jihad ke nare lag rahe hain ye sab Qur'an ke khilaf kaam ho raha hai. Bomb explosion, khud kashi ki Islam ne tarbiyat nahi di. Nihatte log, civilians par hamla Islam ke khilaf hai. Islami Jang ke usool aate nahi jang karne chale. Ye log Islam ko badnam kar rahe hain.
Haan ye hain ye Musalman ko apni mazbooti rakhni chahiye. Apni difa ke liye woh apne sare hunar istemal kar sakta hai.
🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻🗡⚔🗡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Dua Momin ka hathiyaar hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p8)
🗡⚔🗡
Janabe Fatima (sa):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam ne (khandaan e Risaalat ki) ita'at ko maashre ke nizaam ki hifazat ke liye aur Imamat (Aimma e Masumeen (as)) ko ikhtelaaf se bachaane ke liye qaraar diya hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p39)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
