              ♦ _*MUNAFIQ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (535) 👹

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنَّ مِنْكُمْ لَمَنْ لَيُبَطِّئَنَّ فَإِنْ أَصَابَتْكُمْ مُصِيبَةٌ قَالَ قَدْ أَنْعَمَ اللَّهُ عَلَيَّ إِذْ لَمْ أَكُنْ مَعَهُمْ شَهِيدًا * وَلَئِنْ أَصَابَكُمْ فَضْلٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ لَيَقُولَنَّ كَأَنْ لَمْ تَكُنْ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُ مَوَدَّةٌ يَا لَيْتَنِي كُنْتُ مَعَهُمْ فَأَفُوزَ فَوْزًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Tumhare darmiyan kuchh (Munafiq) log hain ke woh khud bhi kahil hain aur doosron ko bhi sust banate hain. Agar koi musibat aa pahunche to woh kahte ke Khuda ne ham par ehsaan kiya ke ham mujahedeen ke saath nahi the ke ham (is musibat) ko dekhte."_
_"Agar koi Maal e Ghanimat (Booty) tumhe mil jaye to thik, halanke tum mein aur un mein koi mawaddat o dosti nahi. Phir bhi woh bilkul is tarah se kahte hain: "Kaash! Ham bhi unke saath hote aur nijaat aur Azeem Kamyabi se hamkinar hote."_
(Surah Nisa: 72 - 73)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as) se manqool hai ke munafeqeen ki aam ravish ye thi ke woh Jang se ji churaya karte the aur heele bahano se apne gharon mein thaher jate the. Agar kisi Jang mein Musalmano ko sadma pahunchta to ye khush ho kar kahte ke Khuda ka Shukr hai mein is Jang mein unke saath sharik na tha. Aur jab kabhi Musalmano ko fatah hasil hoti hai aur iske saath Maal e Ghanimat milta hai to woh kafe afsos mal kar kahte hain ke kaash mein bhi unke saath shamil hota aur mein bhi Kamyabi hasil karta."
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

Imam Reza (as):
_"Koi shaheed aisa nahi hai magar ye ke aarzu karta hai kaash main H. Imam Husain (as) ke saath shaheed hota aur unke humraah Behisht (Jannat) mein jaata."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v1, p131)
😏🌱🌾
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Kitna bura wo shakhs hai jo 2 chehre aur 2 zabaan waala ho - yaani Munafiq ho; saamne apne biradar e Momin ki taarif kare aur peethh pichhe geebat kare."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (536) ⚔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَلْيُقَاتِلْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ الَّذِينَ يَشْرُونَ الْحَيَاةَ الدُّنْيَا بِالْآخِرَةِ ۚ وَمَنْ يُقَاتِلْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ فَيُقْتَلْ أَوْ يَغْلِبْ فَسَوْفَ نُؤْتِيهِ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Woh log jinhone Duniya ki Zindagi Akherat ke badle bechi hai unhe chahiye ke Khuda ki raah mein Jang karen aur jo shakhs raahe Khuda mein Jang kare aur qatl ho jaye ya ghalib aa jaye to Ham use Ajr e Azeem dengen."_
(Surah Nisa: 74)

📚📖 ⚔🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yahan is ayat mein doosri Ayaton ki tarah Jihad fi Sabil lillah ka Hukm diya gaya hai. Jaisa ke ham pahle bhi bata chuke hain Jihad apni aur apne Mazhab ki difa hai, na ke hamla, ya kisi par zulm. Kisi ke bhi hukm se Jihad nahi ho sakta. Jihad ke Hukm ki authority sirf Imam ya Naeb e Imam ki hai. Imam masoom hota hai aur unka hukm khata se mubarrah (defect free) hota hai. Koi bhi khud sakhta leader agar ye ailan kare to woh legal nahi hoga. Misal: Agar koi Hindwasi leader Pakistan ke khilaf Jang ka Ailan kar de jabke Indian President ki taraf se aisa koi hukm na ho to usko khud Indian Govt arrest kar legi aur usko traitor mana jayega. Yehi system Islam mein hai.
Musalmano ki tarikh mein yehi hota chala aya hai, har kisi ne apne ko Khalifa bata kar logon par Jihad ke naam par zulm karna shuru kiya. Isse Islam badnaam hua aur Jihad ko negative way mein liya gaya. Pas jo Jihad fi Sabi lillah na ho use Antakwad, dahshatgardi, terrorism kahte hai.
Haqeeqi Jihad ka ailan sirf aur sirf Imam Mahdi (atfs) hi karenge Zahoor ke baad.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔🗡
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Afzal jihad khwaishaat ke khilaaf Nafs ki jihad hai aur Dunyavi lazzato'n ko chhorna (Jihad) hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v2)
👨‍👦‍👦
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Bachcho'n ke liye Halaal Rizq kamana Allah ki raah mein Jihad karne ke barabar hai."_
(Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p222)
📚
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jab Ilm ki baten suno to un par amal karo aur dilon kushadgi mehsoos karo. Baaz auqat yun bhi hota hai ke jab kisi ke dil mein Ilm zyada aa jaye aur woh use bardasht na kar sake to Shaitan us par qudrat pa leta hai. Dekho jab kabhi Shaitan tum se jhagda kare to uske saamne wo cheezen pesh karo jinhen tum pahchante ho. Shaitan ka makr kamzor hota hai."_
Raavi: "Ham kis pahchani hui cheez se uska muqabila karen?
Aap (as) ne Farmaya:
_"Tum us waqt Khuda ki Qudrat pesh karke apne aap ko Shaitani Khayalat o Waswaas se mehfooz rakho."_
(Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (537) ⚔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا لَكُمْ لَا تُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ وَالْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ مِنَ الرِّجَالِ وَالنِّسَاءِ وَالْوِلْدَانِ الَّذِينَ يَقُولُونَ رَبَّنَا أَخْرِجْنَا مِنْ هَٰذِهِ الْقَرْيَةِ الظَّالِمِ أَهْلُهَا وَاجْعَلْ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ وَلِيًّا وَاجْعَلْ لَنَا مِنْ لَدُنْكَ نَصِيرًا*

_"Akhir tumhe kiya ho gaya hai ke tum Allah ki raah mein un Kamzor Mardon, Aurton aur Bachchon ke liye Jihad nahi karte jinhe kamzor bana kar rakha gaya hai jo barabar dua karte hain ke Khudaya! Hamen is basti se nikal le jiske bashinde (inhabitants) Zaalim hain aur *apni taraf se hamare liye koi Sarparast (Vali) aur Madadgar muqarrar farma.*"_
(Surah Nisa: 75)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Jihad ka Haqiqee maqsad ka izhar kiya gaya hai. Jihad ka maqsad Mazloomo ki madad karna hai. Jihad ke do hadaf (purpose) hain:
(1) Khudai Hadaf (2) Insaani Hadaf.
Ye dono ek doosre se juda nahi hain.
Jihad Zalimana attack ka naam nahi, na hi apne mazhab ki badhane ke liye, kiyonke Islam mein Jabr nahi. By force kisi par apna Deen nahi thopa ja sakta. Islam Azaadi ka hami hai. Jihad difa ka naam hai.
Is Ayat mein is baat ki taraf bhi Ishaara hai ke ye ahm kaam (Jihad) ek Vali ke zere nigrani mein hoga jo Allah ki taraf se appointed hoga. Pas jin logon ka nazarya ye hai ke Rasool (saww) apne baad kisi ko Rehbar o Sarparast muqarrar nahi kar ke gaye (Sahih Muslim), is Ayat ke bar khilaf hai. Jihad jaisa ahm kaam baghair Rehbar ke ho hi nahi sakta. Rehbar Allah ki taraf se hota hai. Agar woh apna Rehbar khud chun sakte the to phir kiyon Allah se apne liye ek Vali muqarrar karne ki dua kar rahe the. Quran ke Ahkam sirf Rasool e Akram (saww) ke Zamane tak mahdood nahi balke unke baad bhi Qayamat tak ke liye hain. Isliye Rasool (saww) ke baad bhi Ahle Bait (as) ki Vilayat jari rahi jo Allah ki taraf se muqarrar kardah the. Ab aap khud faisla karen, aap kis Rehbar pasand karenge logon ka chuna hua ya Allah ka muntakhab kardah?
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Zaalim mazloom ki Duniya ko utna barbaad nahi karta jitna mazloom zaalim ke Deen ko barbaad kar deta hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5, p881)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (538) ⚔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا يُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ۖ وَالَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا يُقَاتِلُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ الطَّاغُوتِ فَقَاتِلُوا أَوْلِيَاءَ الشَّيْطَانِ ۖ إِنَّ كَيْدَ الشَّيْطَانِ كَانَ ضَعِيفًا*

_"Jin logon ne Imaan ka raasta ikhtiyar kiya hai, woh Allah ki raah mein Jihad karte hain, aur jinhone Kufr ka raasta ikhtiyar kiya hai, woh Taghoot ki raah mein ladte hain. Pas Shaitan ke sathiyon se Jihad karo aur yaqeen jano ke Shaitan ki chaalen haqiqat mein  nihayat hi kamzor hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 76)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jihad ke maqasid ham pahle bata chuke hain, ye fi Sabilillah hota hai, means ye bhi Ibaadat hai. Jo bhi kaam khushnoodiye Khuda ke liye ho woh Ibaadat hai. Asl baat ye hai ke ham kis ke liye lad rahe hain, kis ke khilaf lad rahe hain. Is Ayat mein do group bataya gaya hai ek Imaan wale aur doosre Taghoot wale. Taghoot kaun woh bhi pahle ham bata chuke hain. Ab in do raasta mein se hame ek sahih raasta chunna hai. Lekin problem ye hain ke insaan Taghoot ki Ma'arefat nahi rakhta taake usse doori ikhtiyar kare. Isliye woh Shaitani chaalon mein phans jata hai. Kiyonki woh ghaafil hai. Taghoot ki madah sarai hoti hai. Taghoot ko hi log Islam ka Rehbar maan lete hain. Taghoot bhi Imaan walon ke khilaf Islam ka parcham lahrata hai aur logon ko uksata hai Islam ke liye Jihad karo. Bichaaron ke ye pata nahi hota ke haqeeqi Islam kis taraf hai. Is tarah dono fareeq Islam ke liye jang ka rahe hote hain. Ayat ke mutabiq ye sari Taghooti chaalen zara si der mein dher ho jati hain. Momin ke liye ye Imtihan ki ghadi hoti hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Aye Rab! Tu Shaitan ki aarzu poori na hone de balke Tu uske evaz meri zabaan ko Apni Hamd mein masroof kar de."_
(Dua e Makaarimul Akhlaaq)
🍀☘
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne H. Musa (as) ko 4 baato'n ki wasiyyat ki:_
_(1) Jab tak tere gunah maaf na ho, doosro'n ke aib talaashne mein mashgool na hona,_
_(2) Jab tak Mere khazaane khatm na ho, apni Rozi ki fikr mat karna,_
_(3) Meri Haakimiyat (rule) ke hote huwe kisi gair ki haakimiyat ko tasleem na karna aur_
_(4) *Jab tak Shaitan mar na jaaye uske Makr o Fareb se ghaafil na rehna.*"_
(Khisaal, p118)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa  Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (538)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَلَمْ تَرَ إِلَى الَّذِينَ قِيلَ لَهُمْ كُفُّوا أَيْدِيَكُمْ وَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ وَآتُوا الزَّكَاةَ فَلَمَّا كُتِبَ عَلَيْهِمُ الْقِتَالُ إِذَا فَرِيقٌ مِنْهُمْ يَخْشَوْنَ النَّاسَ كَخَشْيَةِ اللَّهِ أَوْ أَشَدَّ خَشْيَةً ۚ وَقَالُوا رَبَّنَا لِمَ كَتَبْتَ عَلَيْنَا الْقِتَالَ لَوْلَا أَخَّرْتَنَا إِلَىٰ أَجَلٍ قَرِيبٍ ۗ قُلْ مَتَاعُ الدُّنْيَا قَلِيلٌ وَالْآخِرَةُ خَيْرٌ لِمَنِ اتَّقَىٰ وَلَا تُظْلَمُونَ فَتِيلًا*
(Surah Nisa: 77)

📚📖

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_

se puchha gaya ke Hazrat Ali (as) ne apne siyaasi harifo'n se jung kyun nahi ki? Aap ne farmaya:

(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p129)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (540)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَيْنَمَا تَكُونُوا يُدْرِكْكُمُ الْمَوْتُ وَلَوْ كُنْتُمْ فِي بُرُوجٍ مُشَيَّدَةٍ ۗ وَإِنْ تُصِبْهُمْ حَسَنَةٌ يَقُولُوا هَٰذِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۖ وَإِنْ تُصِبْهُمْ سَيِّئَةٌ يَقُولُوا هَٰذِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ ۚ قُلْ كُلٌّ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۖ فَمَالِ هَٰؤُلَاءِ الْقَوْمِ لَا يَكَادُونَ يَفْقَهُونَ حَدِيثًا*

_*"Tum jahan kahi bhi raho, *Maut tumhe paa legi agarche Mohkam Burjon (Strong Lofty Towers) mein ja raho."*_
_"Aur agar unhe (Munafeqeen ko) حسنه 'Hasanah' (Goodness) (aur Kamyabi) hasil ho to kahte hain ke ye Khuda ki taraf se hain. Aur 'Sayyeah' سيئه (aur Shikast) se dochar hon to kahte hain ye tumhari taraf se hai. Kah do ke sab Allah ki taraf se hain. Pas ye giroh kiyon tayyar nahi hota ke Haqaiq ka idrak kare."_
(Surah Nisa: 78)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Qur'an ki mataddid Ayaat mein Maut ka zikr hua hai. Is Ayat mein is baat ki takeed ki gayi hai ke Maut ka aana yaqeeni aur hatmi hai, isse farar na mumkin hai. Jaisa ke doosri Ayaton mein Maut ke liye Yaqeen ka lafz istemal hua hai:
*وَاعْبُدْ رَبَّكَ حَتَّىٰ يَأْتِيَكَ الْيَقِينُ*
[Surat Al-Hijr 99]
*حَتَّىٰ أَتَانَا الْيَقِينُ*
[Surat Al-Muddaththir 47]
Dua-e-Kumail ke fiqre:
*ولا يمكن الفرار من حكومتك.*
_"Teri Hukumat se Farar na mumkin hai."_
Ziyarat e Ale Yaseen mein و ان الموت حق Maut ko Haq qarar diya hai.
Koi bhi Shakhs kahin bhi rahe chahe aage pichhe daye bayen uper niche buland towers mein, use Maut pakad hi legi. Mashoor Ayat hai ke har shakhs ko Maut ka maza chakhna. Har Insaan apni Aankh se har kisi ko marte dekhta bhi hai. Isliye har insaan ko apne Amaal ka hisaab dena hoga. Ayat ka doosra part Amaal ke mutaalliq hai, .....next post mein.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Malekul Maut ki nigaah karne ki surat ye hai ke jaise log baithe ho'n aur unhe saktah (laqwah / paralysis) ho jaaye aur wo baat karne ke qaabil na rahein. Ye haalat hoti hai jab Malekul Maut unko dekhta hai."_
(Furoo e Kafi, v1, p354)
👹
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Momin ki nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna sufaid tha us se zyada sufaid aur raushan ho jaata hai, pehshani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski aa'nkho’n se aansuo’n ki tarah rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Rooh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)
👹
Imam Ali (as):
_"Mujhe Ta'jjub hai us shakhs par jo apni Maut par ikhtiyaar nahi rakhta phir apni Aarzuo'n (Ambitions) ko kaise badhata hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (541)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَيْنَمَا تَكُونُوا يُدْرِكْكُمُ الْمَوْتُ وَلَوْ كُنْتُمْ فِي بُرُوجٍ مُشَيَّدَةٍ ۗ وَإِنْ تُصِبْهُمْ حَسَنَةٌ يَقُولُوا هَٰذِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۖ وَإِنْ تُصِبْهُمْ سَيِّئَةٌ يَقُولُوا هَٰذِهِ مِنْ عِنْدِكَ ۚ قُلْ كُلٌّ مِنْ عِنْدِ اللَّهِ ۖ فَمَالِ هَٰؤُلَاءِ الْقَوْمِ لَا يَكَادُونَ يَفْقَهُونَ حَدِيثًا*
[Surat An-Nisa' 78]

_"Tum jahan kahi bhi raho, Maut tumhe paa legi agarche Mohkam Burjon (Strong Lofty Towers) mein ja raho."_
_*"Aur agar unhe (Munafeqeen ko) حسنه 'Hasanah' (Goodness) (aur Kamyabi) hasil ho to kahte hain ke ye Khuda ki taraf se hain. Aur 'Sayyeah' سيئه (aur Shikast) se dochar hon to kahte hain ye tumhari taraf se hai. Kah do ke sab Allah ki taraf se hain. Pas ye giroh kiyon tayyar nahi hota ke Haqaiq ka idrak kare."*_
(Surah Nisa: 78)

📚📖 🚶
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Maut ka tazkarah hua ke isse kisi ko farar nahi. Ayat ke doosre hisse mein Amal ka tazkarah hai ke Amal ka source kiya hai. Qur'an mein ek jagah ye hai ke jo bhi Hasana (Neki) hai woh Khuda ki taraf se jabke jitni buraiyyan hai insaano ke apne amal ka natija hai. Lekin is Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai Nek o Bad sab ka source Allah hai. Ye tazad (contradiction) nahi. Ye sochna ghalat hoga ke jitne gunah ham kar rahe hain sab Allah karwa raha hai. Ye sahi hai ke hamara Khaliq Allah hai, hame ghumane phirane wala bhi Allah hai. Woh hi Jaza deta hai to Wohi Saza bhi deta hai. Allah ne hi Nek insaano ko paida kiya to Us hi ne Khunkhar Janwaron ko jo insaan ko khaa jata hai. Us hi ne qaatil ko Us hi ne maqtool ko paida kiya. Isi tarah jaise ke ek chaaqu (knife) hai jisko ek karigar ne banaya, uska maqsad uske sahi istemal ke liye tha, taake uske zariye tarkari kati jaye. Lekin insaan usi chaaqu se kisi ko qatl kar de to is mein banane wale ka qusoor nahi balke istemal karne wale ka qusoor hai. Insaan ne kisi ko apne haath se maara, usko haath Allah ne diye. Agar uske pas hath na hote to woh nahi maar sakta tha. Allah ki qadrat ka woh ghalat fayda utha raha hai.
Is tarah insaan ke sabhi amaal ka source Allah hai kulli taur par.
Doosri baat ye ke insaan ke amaal ke mutalliq Shia na Jabr ke qael hain na Azaadi ke. Ashayra Sunni Aqeede ke mutabiq Jabr hai. Mutazela maante hain ke insaan apne amaal mein Azad hai.
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) ke mutabiq امر بين الامرين hai. Means na Jabr hai na Azaadi, balke beech ka raasta hai.
Jo Amaal insaan ke haath mein nahi hain (Takveeni) jaise Kaala paida hona. Yahan insaan majboor hai, kuchh nahi kar sakta, lekin Sharaii Ahkam jo Insaan kar sakta hai jaise Namaz, Roza etc uske ikhtiyar mein hai. Pas ek jagah insaan ko Allah ne ikhtiyar diya to doosri taraf mahdood kar diya. Means apni limit mein insaan chahe kuchh bhi kare. Lekin us limit ke bahar insaan nahi ja sakta.
Allah ne use Mukhtar banaya isliye source Allah hai. Is liye Allah ne jo kuchh hame hukm diya hai utna baja layen. Isliye saza wo jaza hai. Agar Jabr hota to ye sab be-maani ho jate. Qayamat ka koi matlab na rahta. Chunke amal mein ikhtiyar hai isliye Sawab hai. Agar 100 km hamne car se safar kiya to ye koi Kamal nahi mana jayega lekin agar ye 100 km agar aap ne paidal poora kiya to Kamal mana jayega aur aap Inaam ke haqdar honge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👥
Imam Zainul Abedin (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Anbiya (as) aur unke Abdaan (bodies) ko Teenat e Illiyeen طينت علين se paida kiya aur Momenin ke dilon ki takhleeq bhi is Teenat se ki jabke unke Abdaan ko usse kamtar darje ki Teenat se paida kiya.  Jabke Kafiron ko aur unke dilon aur unke ajsaam ko Teenat e Sijjeel طينت سجيل se paida kiya. Phir Allah ne dono Teenaton ko ek dooare se makhloot (mix) kar diya. Yehi wajah hai ke Momin ke ghar Kafir paida ho jata hai aur Kafir ke ghar Momin paida hota hai. Aur is Teenat ke ikhtelat (mixture) ki wajah se Momin se burai sarzad ho jati hai aur Kafir se Neki zahoor pazir ho jati hai. Mominin ke dil uski taraf mael rahte hain jisse unki takhleeq hui hai aur Kafiron ke dil bhi uski taraf mael rahte hain jis se woh paida hue hain."_
(Ilalus Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)

              ♦ _*AAMAAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (542)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا أَصَابَكَ مِنْ حَسَنَةٍ فَمِنَ اللَّهِ ۖ وَمَا أَصَابَكَ مِنْ سَيِّئَةٍ فَمِنْ نَفْسِكَ ۚ وَأَرْسَلْنَاكَ لِلنَّاسِ رَسُولًا ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ شَهِيدًا*

_"Jo Nekiyan tum par pahunchi hain woh Khuda ki taraf se hain aur jo Burai tumhe pahunchi wo khud tumhari taraf se hai aur Hamne tumhe logo ke liye Rasool bana kar bheja hai aur is bare mein Khuda ki Gawahi kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 79)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat pichhli ayat se muttasil hai. Jaisa ke hamne kal bataya tha pichhli Ayat ka hukm kulli tha. (In General), yani har cheez ka source Allah hai. Ab is Ayat mein Juzii Hukm hai. Sab Buraiyyan hamari taraf se hain. Qazi chor ka hath kate, ya chor apne hath kate, dono ek hi baat hain. Hukm e Sharii jis mein hame Allah ne ikhtiyar diya hai, karen ya na karen, lekin Rasool ko hamari Hidayat ke liye bhi bheja. Nabi ko bhej kar Allah ne ham par fazl kiya. In sab baton ke liye Khuda ki Gawahi kafi hai. Ye sab baten Adl e Ilahi sabit karti hai. Shiyon ke 5 Usool e Din mein 2nd Adl e Ilahi hai.
(Usool e Din: 1.Tawheed, 2.Adl, 3. Nubuwwat, 4. Imamat, 5. Qayamat.)
Jabke Ahle Sunnat mein 3 Usool hain: Tawheed, Nubuwwat, Qayamat etc.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5, p867)

              ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (543) ⚔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ يُطِعِ الرَّسُولَ فَقَدْ أَطَاعَ اللَّهَ ۖ وَمَنْ تَوَلَّىٰ فَمَا أَرْسَلْنَاكَ عَلَيْهِمْ حَفِيظًا * وَيَقُولُونَ طَاعَةٌ فَإِذَا بَرَزُوا مِنْ عِنْدِكَ بَيَّتَ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْهُمْ غَيْرَ الَّذِي تَقُولُ ۖ وَاللَّهُ يَكْتُبُ مَا يُبَيِّتُونَ ۖ فَأَعْرِضْ عَنْهُمْ وَتَوَكَّلْ عَلَى اللَّهِ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلًا*

_"Jis Shakhs ne Paighambar ki ita'at ki usne Khuda ki ita'at ki aur jo rugardani (turn away) kare to tum uske jo jawab deh nahi ho."_
_"Woh Aapke saamne kahte hain ke ham farmabardar hain lekin jab woh tumhari Bazm se bahar jate hain to un mein ek giroh tumhari guftagu ke bar khilaf raat ko khufiya (Secret) meetings tashkeel deta hai jo kuchh woh un meetings mein kahte hain Khuda use likhta hai. Unki parwa na karo (aur unke mansoobon aur sazishon se na daron) aur Khuda par tawakkal karo aur Kafi hai ke Woh tumhara Madadgar aur Hifazat Karne wala ho."_
(Surah Nisa: 80 - 81)

📚📖 ⚔
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Ita'at e Rasool ko Allah ki Ita'at qarar diya hai. Aur jo log Qur'an o Rasool ko maante hain lekin zaheran to jatate hain ke ham unki ita'at karte hain lekin Allah kah rah hai woh ita'at nahi karte. Means woh Munafeqeen hain. Tarikh mein hai logon ne Saqeefa mein Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke hukm ke khilaf khufiya meetings ki. Jabke Ahle Medina Rasool e Akram (saww) ke Dafan Kafan mein mashghool the. Udhar Ashaab Saqeefa mein mashghool the. Jabke Janasheen e Paighambar ka Ghadeer mein pahle hi Ailan ho chuka tha.
Rasool e Khuda (saww) ki mashoor hadis tamam kutube Islam mein majood hai ke Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne farmaya ke mein do Qeemti cheezen (Saqlain) chhod kar ja raha hun ek Khuda ki Kitab Qur'an aur doosre Ahle Bait (as), jo inse touch mein rahega woh gumrah na hoga. Pas jis tarah Allah wa Rasool ki ita'at wajib hai usi tarah Ahle Bait (as) ki ita'at wajib hai. Isliye Khuda ne Amro Nahy ka Haq Paighambar (saww) diya aur Paighambar (saww) ne ye Haq Ali (as) aur Aimma e Ahle Bait (as) ko diya, pas logon ka farz hai ke unke Amr o Nahy se roogardani na karen kiyonki ye Khuda ki mukhalefat hogi.
(Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-396)
Pas jo Qur'an aur Allah ke Rasool ko maanta hai woh kaise unki ita'at se inkar kar sakta hai. Isliye Ayat ka ishaara Munafeqeen par hai jo maante to hain lekin ita'at mein khalis nahi hain. Woh log Islam ke daere mein rahte hue Islam ki jade khodte hain. Lekin Allah inki sazishon ko dekhta rahta hai, inki sazishon se ghabrane ki zaroorat nahi, Allah hamara muhafiz hai.
Is Ayat mein Munafeqeen o Mukhalefin ki tarikh ka khulasa hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚔
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)!...Khuda ki qasam! Aap se mohabbat wo rakkhega jo Momin hoga aur bugz wo rakkhega jo Munafiq (hypocrite) hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Munafiq ki 3 nishaniyaa'n hain:_
_(1) Jab baat karta hai to jhoot bolta hai,_
(Jhoot bola ke Paighambar (saww) ne kisi ko apna Janashin nahi banaya)

_(2) Jab waada karta hai to waada khilaafi karta hai,_
(Wada kiya tha Rasoole ke Naqse qadam par chalenge lekin tod diya.)

_(3) Jab amaanat rakhi jaati hai to khayaanat karta hai."_
(Allah ne jo amr o nahy amanat mein diye the unki ita'at mein Khayanat ki)

(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p188)

              ♦ _*QUR'AN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (544) 📚📖

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*أَفَلَا يَتَدَبَّرُونَ الْقُرْآنَ ۚ وَلَوْ كَانَ مِنْ عِنْدِ غَيْرِ اللَّهِ لَوَجَدُوا فِيهِ اخْتِلَافًا كَثِيرًا*

_"Kiya ye log Qur'an mein fikr o tadabbur nahi karte. Agar Qur'an ghairullah (others) ki taraf se hota to wo is mein bahut zyada ikhtelaf pate."_
(Surah Nisa: 82)

📚📖
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Kitab e Khuda ka baaz hissa doosre baaz hisse ki tasdeeq karta hai aur Qur'ani Ayaat mein koi ikhtelaf nahi hai. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: (4:82)"_
(Nahjul Balagha)

Qur'an ka tazkara aur tafseel pahle ham Ramzan mein kar chuke hain. Yahan Allah Quran mein research ki dawat de raha hai. Qur'an ilm ka khazana hai aur hamare Nabi (saww) ke mojeza bhi. Lekin insaan mein ye isteta'at nahi ke Qur'an ko khud akele samajh sake. Rasool e Akram (saww) ki Rivayaat ke mutabiq Qur'an wa Ahle Bait (as) juda nahi ho sakte.
Aaj Imam Zainul Abedin (as) ke Wiladat hai. Imam Sajjad (as) usi Ahle Bait (as) ki ek kadi hain. Mulaheza farmayen:
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Agar sare Purab o Paschim ke bashinde halak ho jayen aur mein sirf Qur'an e Karim ke sath rah jaon, to mein viraniyat ka shikar nahi rahunga."_
_"Qur'an se lagao rakhoge to tum akelapan mahsoos nahi karoge."_
(Al Kaafi)

Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Sayyadus Sajedeen (as) Qur'an ki qirat mein ek dilchasp aur khoobsurat awaz ke hamil the. Jab bhi woh Qur'an ki qirat karte, udhar se guzarne wale log unke darwaze par ruk kar unki awaaz ko sunte the."_
(Al Kaafi)
Tilawat ke saath Aap Duao mein zyada mashgool rahte. Aap (as) ke Duayen logon ke ke liye ibrat ka zariya hain.
Un Dua mein se ek Sahifa Sajhadiya hai. William Chittick ke mutabiq ye sab se purani taaleef hai. Qur'an ke baad isi Kitab ka aala maqam hai, jaise Nahjul Balagha. Aap (as) ki aur bahut se Duayen hai jaise Dua e Makaremul Akhlaq, Dua Abu Hamza Sumali waghaira. Aap (as) ne Duaon ke zariye Zalim Bani Hukumat ke daur mein khamosh Tabligh ki.
Ek aur Maroof Kitab 'Risalatul Huqooq' hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

🙇 📚
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Gaur o fikr karo aur jiske liye paida kiye gaye ho uske liye amal karo kyun ki Khuda ne tumko bekaar o abas (without any reason / vyarth) nahi paida kiya hai."_
(Tehzeeb e Aal e Muhammad (as), p84)

             ♦ _*ULIL AMR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (545) 🚩

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا جَاءَهُمْ أَمْرٌ مِنَ الْأَمْنِ أَوِ الْخَوْفِ أَذَاعُوا بِهِ ۖ وَلَوْ رَدُّوهُ إِلَى الرَّسُولِ وَإِلَىٰ أُولِي الْأَمْرِ مِنْهُمْ لَعَلِمَهُ الَّذِينَ يَسْتَنْبِطُونَهُ مِنْهُمْ ۗ وَلَوْلَا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ وَرَحْمَتُهُ لَاتَّبَعْتُمُ الشَّيْطَانَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا*

_"Aur jab unke pas Amn ya Khauf ki koi khabar aati hai to woh use phaila dete hain, halanke agar woh *Rasool (saww) aur Ulil Amr (as)* ki taraf palta dete to unse istefada karne wale haqiqat e haal ka ilm paida kar lete aur agar tum par Khuda ka Fazl aur Rehmat na hoti to chand afraad ke alawa tum sab Shaitan ki pairavi karte."_
(Surah Nisa: 83)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Ayat (Sura Nisa: 59) mein Allah, Rasool (saww) aur Ulil Amr ki ita'at lazim qarar di gayi hai. Aur hamne bataya tha ke Ulil Amr kaun hain. Aaj ki is Ayat mein bhi yehi hukm hai ke kisi bhi khabar ki Ulil Amr se tasdeeq karwa len. Kiyonki unhe hi sirf istenbat (Scrutiny) ke haq hai. Ulil Amr sirf Aimma Ahle Bait (as) hain. Ab yahan Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai agar Khuda ki Rehmat na hoti: isse murad Vilayat e Aimma hain, to sab Shaitan ki pairavi karte means Vilayat e Aimma ke khilaaf sirf Shaitan hi hai.
Rivayat:
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Jisne Vilayat e Khuda aur Ilm e Ilahi ke istinbat ki ahliyat ko Anbiya ke gharano se nikal kar doosre gharano mein dakhil kiya to usne Hukm e Khuda ki mukhalefat ki aur Jahilon ko Amr e Ilahi ka Vali tasleem kiya aur Hidayat ke baghair takalluf wa tasnao karne walo ko Rehbar tasleem kiya aur unke mutalliq guman kiya ke ye log Ilm e Ilahi se istinbat karne wale hain. Un logon ne Khuda par jhoot tarasha hai aur Allah ki Wasiyyat ko fash kiya hai. Unhone Khuda ke Fazl ko wahan nahi rakha jahan Khuda ne use rakha tha. Chunanche woh khud bhi gumrah hue aur doosron ko bhi gumrah kiya. Qayamat ke Din unke pas koi Hujjat na hogi. Phir ye Ayat padhi (Anaam:89)"_
(Kamaluddin, Noorus Saqlain)
Imam Moosa Kazim(as):
_"Rehmat se Rasoole Akram (saww) aur Fazl se Ali (as) murad hain"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
Isi liye Umar har waqt Ali (as) ko refer karta rahta tha aur kahta ke agar Ali (as) na hote to mein halak ho jata.
Yani jo Ulil Amr ko jo chhodega woh halak ho jayega.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
Imam Sadiq (as)
se jab puchha gaya ke Allah ne Hazrat Ali (as) aur unki family ke naam ka Quran mein kyun zikr nahi kiya, to Imam (as) ne jawaab diya, _"Unse keh do ke Namaz ka hukm aaya magar Allah ne ye nahi kaha ke 3 rakaat ya 4 rakaat padhni hai, Rasul (saww) ne ye sab bataaya. Aur jab zakat ka hukm huwa to Allah ne nahi kaha ke 40 mein 1 dirham zakat hai, magar Rasul (saww) ne samjhaya. Aur Hajj ka hukm huwa to Allah ne nahi kaha ke tawaf 7 hai, magar Rasul (saww) ne bataaya. Aise hi Surah Nisa ki Ayat no. 59 naazil hui 'Aye Imaanwalo'n, Allah ki ita'at karo aur Rasool (saww) ki ita'at karo, aur tum mein se jo Ulil Amr hai unki ita'at karo..' aur ye Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) aur H. Hasan (as) aur H. Husain (as) ki shaan mein naazil hui."_
(Tafsir Ayyashi, v1, p, 249-250, Tafseer As Saafi, v1, p364, 'Imamat' - Allamah Syed Saeed Akhtar Rizvi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*16th Jamadi ul Awwal 1438*, 14th February 2017, Tuesday,

            ♦ _*JIHAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (546) 🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَقَاتِلْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ لَا تُكَلَّفُ إِلَّا نَفْسَكَ ۚ وَحَرِّضِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۖ عَسَى اللَّهُ أَنْ يَكُفَّ بَأْسَ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا ۚ وَاللَّهُ أَشَدُّ بَأْسًا وَأَشَدُّ تَنْكِيلًا*

_"Aye Nabi! Tum Allah ke ki raah mein lado. Tum apni zaat ke alawa aur kisi ke zimmedar nahi ho aur Momenin ko Jihad par amaada karen, baeed nahi ke Allah Kafiron ka zor tod de. Allah intihai Quwwat wala aur Sakht Saza dene wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 84)

📚📖 🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne apne Habib Karim ko bahut si khusosiyat ata farmayi. ..... Phir Allah ne unhen woh zimmedari sonpi jo Usne unse qabl kisi Nabi ko nahi sonpi thi. Allah ne Aasmaan se ek be Niyam Talwaar AnHazrat par nazil ki aur Ayat (4:84) nazil hui."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
Sulaiman bin Khalid ne sawal kiya:
"Log kahte hain ke agar Hazrat Ali (as) ke siyasi mukhalefeen Batil par hote to woh unse jang karte. Chunke unhone apne siyasi hareefon se jang nahi ki isse maloom hota hai ke woh Haq par the?"
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_"Tan tanha Jihad karne ka hukm sirf Rasool Maqbool (saww) ke sath makhsoos hai. Allah ne apne Nabi (saww) se farmaya (4:84), jabke doosre Ahle Imaan ko hukm hai ke woh Giroh aur Jamat ke sath milkar jang karen. Jaisa ke is Ayat mein hai: (Anfal:15-16). Isse maloom hua ke Jang ke liye Lashkar ki zaroorat hoti hai jabke Hazrat Ali (as) ke pas lao Lashkar maujood nahi tha. Is liye unhone Jang nahi ki thi."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi, Noorus Saqlain)

Siyasat mein jisko public support kare wohi aage badhta hai. Election ka daur hai, har leader jab ye dekhta hai ke mere saath zyada ta'dad mein voters hain tabhi woh Siyasi Jang mein utarta hai. Ab logon ka farz banta hai ke usi leader ko chune jo unke liye fayde mand ho.

Hazrat Ali (as) ko koi Siyasi dawa pesh karna nahi tha ke woh uske liye apne hareef se ladte. Woh to Allah ke appointed Imam the, log maane ya na maane. Agar log unko support karte to unhe fayda hota Imam ko nahi. 4 Saal ki Siyasi daur mein ye bhi dikha diya. Logo ne support kiya to hukumat bani, warna hukumat unka maqsad nahi tha. 11 Aimma ki zindagi se yehi lesson milta hai, jahan aksariyat batil hukumat ko support kar rahi thi, lekin Imam ne unke khilaf koi mahaz nahi khada kiya. Imam e Zamana (atfs) bhi apne isi Lashkar ke intezar mein hain, jab 313 ka Lashkar tayyar ho jayga tab Zahoor karenge aur Zalimo Kuffar ka muqabila karenge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡🐕
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Har Shakhs ke liye koi na koi Kutta (Sifat Dushman) hota hai. Tumhare aghyaar (opposites) ke zariye se Allah tumhe isse mehfooz rakhega. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala farma raha hai: "Allah intihai Quwwat wala aur Sakht Saza dene wala hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

              ♦ _*SHAFA'AT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (547) 👈🏻👉

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ يَشْفَعْ شَفَاعَةً حَسَنَةً يَكُنْ لَهُ نَصِيبٌ مِنْهَا ۖ وَمَنْ يَشْفَعْ شَفَاعَةً سَيِّئَةً يَكُنْ لَهُ كِفْلٌ مِنْهَا ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ مُقِيتًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Achhi Shifarish karega use uska hissa milega aur jo Buri Shifarish karega use us mein se hissa milega aur Allah har cheez par iqtedar rakhne wala hai. "_
(Surah Nisa: 85)

📚📖 👈🏻👉
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Shafa'at ya Shifarish yahan kai meaning mein hai:
Un mein se ek hai Amr e bil Maroof wa Nahi anil Munkar, Achhi Guidance ya Buri rahnumai. Isliye jo ye kaam kar raha hai woh bhi us kaam mein sharik hai, isliye use bhi jaza wa saza milegi.
Doosra matlab ye hai kisi ke haq mein Dua karna.
Ahadis mulaheza farmayen:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

🙇 🙌🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo Shakhs apne Musalman bhai ke liye uske pase pusht Dua kare to woh qubool hogi aur Khuda Farishta usse kahega usse dugna tumhare liye bhi hai aur Ayat mein Naseeb se murad yehi hai."_
(Tafseer e Safi, Namoona)
👈🏻👉
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jisne Neki ka hukm diya ya Burai se mana kiya ya Achhai ki Rahnumai ki ya uska ishaara kiya to woh us Neki aur bhalai mein sharik hai aur jis ne Burai ka hukm diya ya uska raasta dikhaya ya ishaara kiya to woh us Burai mein barabar ka sharik hai."_
(Kitabul Khisal, Noorus Saqlain)
👈🏻👉

(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p471)

              ♦ _*SALAAM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (548) 👋🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا حُيِّيتُمْ بِتَحِيَّةٍ فَحَيُّوا بِأَحْسَنَ مِنْهَا أَوْ رُدُّوهَا ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَلَىٰ كُلِّ شَيْءٍ حَسِيبًا*

_"Aur jab tumhe ehteram ke saath  *SALAAM* kiya jaye to usko usse behtar andaaz mein jawab do. Ya phir waisa hi lauta do. Beshak Allah har cheez ka hisab karne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 86)

📚📖 👋🏻
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Salam karna Mustahab lekin Jawab dena Wajib hai, balke isse behtar jawab dena chahiye means Imam Baqir (as) ke mutabiq aisa jawab do jis tarah Malaika Hazrat Ibrahim (as) se kahte the. و عليك السلام و رحمة الله و بركاته. Muqeem ke liye Salam ki takmeel musafeha aur musafir ke liye muaneqa (gale milna) hoti hai. Jamat mein koi ek jawab de de to kafi hai. Chhota bade ko Salam kare aur guzarne wala baithe hue ko Salam kare aur qaleel kaseer par. Salam ki pehel karne wala Khuda wa Rasool ki nazar mein zyada maqam rakhta hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) jab bhi Janabe Fatema Zahra (sa) ke ghar par jaate ya guzarte unko Salam karte. Aur bahut si fazilaten hain jiski gunjaish yahan par nahi hai.
Qur'an ne hame yehi tariqa bataya. Agar ham Musalman hain to isi ko follow karna behtar hai. Isliye jo alfaz aam logon mein istemal hote hain jaise Hii, Hello, Adaab, Ya Ali Madad, Tasleem ...... etc. chahe sahi kiyon na hon lekin Qur'an ne hamko jo hukm diya usi par amal karen. Salam chunke ek Dua hai jis mein ham ek doosre ki salamti ki dua karte hain. Isliye Ghair Muslim, badkar, ghamzada ko Salam karne se mana kiya hai. Ab agar koi jan boojh kar Salam ki jagah koi aur lafz istemal kare to woh Qur'an wa rivayat ke khilaf amal hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👋🏻
Paighambar e Islam (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs Salam se pahle guftugu shuru karde uska jawab na do."_
(Usool e Kaafi, Vol 2, Tasleem)
👋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Bakheel (Kanjoos) woh hai jo Salam mein kanjoosi se kaam le."_
(Usool e Kaafi, Vol 2, Tasleem)
👋🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
_l"افشاء السلام: Salam ko aam karne wale ko Khuda dost rakhta hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
👋🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Apne ghar waalo'n par Salaam karo, tumhare ghar mein barkat hogi."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p27)
👋🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Teen Afraad par Salaan na kiya jaye:_
_(1) Jo Janaze ke saath chal raha ho._
_(2) Jo Namaze Juma ki taraf ja raha ho._
_(3) Jo Hammam mein baitha ho."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
👋🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Ye aadmi qaabil e Salaam nahi hai:_
_Yahoodi, Nasraani, Majoosi, Baitul Khalaa ke andar (jo toilet mein ho), Sharaab ke dastar-khwaan par baithhne wala, Wo shaayar jo aurato'n par ilzaam lagata hai, wo shakhs jo mazaaq mein maa ki gaali deta hai."_
(Khisaal, ch6)

              ♦ _*QAYAMAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (549) 👆

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*اللَّهُ لَا إِلَٰهَ إِلَّا هُوَ ۚ لَيَجْمَعَنَّكُمْ إِلَىٰ يَوْمِ الْقِيَامَةِ لَا رَيْبَ فِيهِ ۗ وَمَنْ أَصْدَقُ مِنَ اللَّهِ حَدِيثًا*

_"Allah Woh hai jiske alawa koi Ma'bood nahi. Woh tum sab ko Qayamat ke Din zaroor jama karega aur Allah ki baat se badhkar Sachchi baat aur kiski ho sakti hai?"_
(Surah Nisa: 87)

📚📖 👆
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kalma e Tawheed ke baad Allah hamko remind kar raha hai ke Qayamat ke Din ham sab mahshoor honge. Allah ki ke kalam ka ham inkar nahi kar sakte kiyonki Uska Kalam sachcha hai. Isliye hame apne eteqaad o Amaal mein khabardar rahna chahiye.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👆
Imam Ali (as):
_"Yaqeenan Aaj amal hai, hisaab nahi; aur Kal (Qayamat ke din) Hisaab hoga, Amal nahi."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Amal)
👆
Imam Reza (as) ne Neshapur (Iran) mein Laa ilaaha illallah ki Tafseer mein Farmaya.:
“Mein ne apne Walid  Musa ibn Ja’ffar (as) se suna, unhone unke Walid Ja’ffar ibn Muhammad (as) unhone Muhammad ibn Ali (as) se,  unhone Ali ibn al-Husan (as) se,  unhone Husain ibn Ali (as)se, unhone Ali ibn Abi Talib (as) se Rasoole Khuda (saww) se, unhone Jibrael se,  ke Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:
_*"Kalma e Laa ilaaha illallah mera Qila (Fort) hai, jo bhi is Qile mein dakhil ho gaya woh Mere Azaab se Mehfooz ho gaya"*_
Phir Imam (as) kuchh ruke aur farmaya:
_*"Iski kuchh Sharait hain aur mein un mein se ek Shart hai."*_
(Hadis Silsalatuz Zahab, Ahsan al-Maqaal)
👆
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Qayamat ke din bando'n se sabse pehla sawaal hum Ahlebait (as) ki mohabbat ka kiya jayega."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p219)

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (550) 👹😈

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَمَا لَكُمْ فِي الْمُنَافِقِينَ فِئَتَيْنِ وَاللَّهُ أَرْكَسَهُمْ بِمَا كَسَبُوا ۚ أَتُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَهْدُوا مَنْ أَضَلَّ اللَّهُ ۖ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ سَبِيلًا*

_"Kiya wajah hai ke Munafeqeen ke mutalliq tumhari do rayen kiyon hain? Halanke jo buraiyyan unhone kamai hain unki wajah se Allah ne unhe ulta pher diya hai to kiya tum use Hidayat dena chahte ho jise Khuda ne Hidayat nahi di hai. Jise Khuda gumrahi mein chhod de uske liye tum koi raasta nahi paoge."_
(Surah Nisa: 88)

📚📖 😈👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
'Ye woh Munafeqeen hain jo Makkah se Medina aye aur unhone Musalmano ke saamne Islam ka izhaar kiya. Kuchh Din Medina mein rahe lekin woh wapas Makkah chale gaye aur wahan unhone Shirk ka izhaar kiya. Phir kuchh dino baad woh Mushrikon ka Maal le kar Yamama gaye. Raaste mein unhone Musalman mile to unhone chaha ke un par hamla kar den kiyonki woh Mushrik hai, magar kuchh ka kahna tha ke unke khilaf jang nahi karni chahiye kiyonki woh Momin hain, phir ye ayat nazil hui. (4:88)'
(Tafseer e Majmaul Bayan)
Aaj bhi aisa mahaul paida ho jata , kuchh log Munafeqeen ki taraf narm gosha rakhte hai aur unka iraada ye rahta hai ke unko rahe raast par layen lekin woh unki chaal mein dhoka kha jate hain. Jinse Allah naraaz hai unko kaise raazi karwaoge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😈👹
Imam Reza (as):
_"Khuda Wande Aalam Momin ki Dua ke shauq mein uski Dua ko der se mustajab karta hai aur kahta hai, "Mujhe ye awaaz pasand hai." Aur Munafiq ki Dua jald qubool karta hai aur farmata hai ke "Mujhe uski awaaz pasand nahi"._
(Dua aur Ahle Bait (as), p38)
😈👹
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jisne apna jismaani khushoo (humility / vinamrata) apne dil ke khushoo se zyada zaahir kiya, uska ye feyl hamare nazdeek Munafiqat (hypocrisy) hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p100)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hargiz (Munafiq) logo'n ki Masajid ki tadaad aur (Namaz e ba) Jamat se dhoka na khao; inke jism ikatthe lekin dil bikhre huwe hain."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (551) 😈👹

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَدُّوا لَوْ تَكْفُرُونَ كَمَا كَفَرُوا فَتَكُونُونَ سَوَاءً ۖ فَلَا تَتَّخِذُوا مِنْهُمْ أَوْلِيَاءَ حَتَّىٰ يُهَاجِرُوا فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ ۚ فَإِنْ تَوَلَّوْا فَخُذُوهُمْ وَاقْتُلُوهُمْ حَيْثُ وَجَدْتُمُوهُمْ ۖ وَلَا تَتَّخِذُوا مِنْهُمْ وَلِيًّا وَلَا نَصِيرًا*

_"Woh chahte hain ke jis tarah se woh khud Kafir hain tum bhi unhi ki tarah se Kafir ban jao aur tum unke barabar ho jao. Khabardar! Tum unhe apna dost na banana jab tak woh raahe Khuda mein hijrat na karen. Phir agar woh moo mod len to unhe pakad lo aur jahan tum unhe pao qatl kar do. Aur un mein se kisi ko apna dost aur Madadgar na banao."_
(Surah Nisa: 89)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein ek giroh Munafeqeen ki himayat kar raha tha. Yahan is Ayat mein jo Munafeqeen Makkah ja kar wapas Kufr ke darje par chale gaye unke liye Allah ne Sakht Hukm diya hai.
Ek Muashere, Society ki tashkeel ke liye zaroori hota hai k khatarnak Elements ko nikal bahar kiya jaye, kiyonki ye log khud Musalmano ke beech rah kar khurafat paida kar sakte hain.
Aaj ki zinda misal sab ke saamne hai *'ISIS, Daes, Taliban* jo zahir mein to apne aap ko Islam ka parcham buland kar rahe hain lekin uske saye mein khilaf e Islam kaam ka kar rahe hain aur Duniya dekh rahi hai ke ye Islam hai? Is tarah ye log Islam ko aziyyat pahunchate hain.
Ye wazeh rahe ke ye Jihad Munafeqeen ke liye hai jo Kufr ke mushabeh hain. Allah ka ye hukm Zulm ke khilaf hai aur sirf Masoom ki Rehbari mein hi ho sakta hai. Agar aam khud sakhta Rehbar ye kaam karega to khata karega aur apne mafad mein begunaho ka khoon bahaiga. Aaj jo Musalmano ki taraf se Jihad Jihad ke naare sunte hain, inka Jihad Masjidon mein dhamake karna, masoom bachcho ki jaan lena, School mein firing karna....... Ye sab isliye hain ke inka Rehbar khud Munafiq hai, aur inhone Islam ka sahi raasta jo ke Ahle Bait (as) ka raasta hai chhod diya hai.

(To be cont'd ....)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😈👹
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Insaani roop mein jo Shayateen rahte hain unke paas Makr, Heele, Waswase aur Dhoke ke bada samaan maujood hai aur unki poori koshish hoti hai ke Ahle Haq ko Khuda ki taraf se Deen ki Shakl mein jo Izzat mili hai aur jisse eoh khud tahiy daman hain, kisi na kisi tarah se Ahle Haq se Deen ki Nemat salb kar len, taake Shak, Inkaar aur Takzeeb mein Musalman aur Khuda ke Dushman yaksan (same) ho jayen. Khud to pahle hi Kafir hain aur woh Musalmano ko bhi apne jaisa Kafir banana chahte hain. Un logon ke mutalliq Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya:_
_"Woh chahte hain ke tum bhi unki tarah Kafir ban jao aur un jaise ho jao. (4:89)"_
(Roza e Kaafi)

              ♦ *SULAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (552) 🇽🇪

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِلَّا الَّذِينَ يَصِلُونَ إِلَىٰ قَوْمٍ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ مِيثَاقٌ أَوْ جَاءُوكُمْ حَصِرَتْ صُدُورُهُمْ أَنْ يُقَاتِلُوكُمْ أَوْ يُقَاتِلُوا قَوْمَهُمْ ۚ وَلَوْ شَاءَ اللَّهُ لَسَلَّطَهُمْ عَلَيْكُمْ فَلَقَاتَلُوكُمْ ۚ فَإِنِ اعْتَزَلُوكُمْ فَلَمْ يُقَاتِلُوكُمْ وَأَلْقَوْا إِلَيْكُمُ السَّلَمَ فَمَا جَعَلَ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ عَلَيْهِمْ سَبِيلًا*

_"Albatta woh Munafiq is Hukm se mustasna (exception) hain jo kisi aisi qaum se ja mile jiske sath tumhara Muaeda (Treaty) hai. Isi tarah woh Munafiq bhi mustasna hain jo tumhare pas ladai se  dil bardashta ho kar aate hain. Na tum se ladna chahte hain aur na apni qaum se ladna chahte hain aur agar Allah chahta to unhe tum par musallat (overpower) kar deta. Woh bhi tum se ladte agar woh tum se kinara kashi ikhtiyar kar len aur ladne se baaz rahen aur tumhari taraf SULAH ka haath badhain to Allah ne tumhare liye un par dast drazi ki koi Sabeel nahi rakhi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 90)

📚📖 🇽🇪
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Munafeqeen jinhone Kufr ikhtiyar kiya qatl karne ka hukm aya, to is ayat mein 2 tarah ke Munafeqeen ko chhodne ka hukm diya:
(1) Jinse Jangi Muaeda (Peace Treaty) hai.
(2) Jo Musalmano se Jang nahi karna chahte.
Ye Ayat Sulah Hudebiya ke pahle nazil hui.
Ham pahle bata chuke hain ke Islam mein Difa (defence) hai, attack nahi hai. Islam isko ghalat manta hai ke hamara Dushman agar hamse Muqabile ki himmat nahi rakhta ya kamzor hai to ham uska fayda uthayn. Balke aise logon ke sath Sulah ka darwaza khol diya hai. Islam mein Jabran kisi ko Musalman nahi banaya ja sakta. By Force ki yahan koi jagah nahi hai. Na koi yahan taqat azmai karna hai.
Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne Bani Zamrah se Musalehat kar rakhi thi aur doosra qabila Bani Ashja feminine ki wajah se kamzor tha. Aisi halat mein dono qabile ek sath rah rahe the. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne un par hamla karne se mana kiya. Phir ye Ayat nazil hui.
Jihad ke conditions mein se ye ek condition hai. Lekin Aaj kal jo ho raha hai Gulf mein ya Muslim hukumaton mein unhone ye saare usool taaq par rakh diye hain. Muslim Unity Ahle Bait (as) ki rassi ko thame rakhna thi, lekin is chhod kar saare Musalman bikhre hue hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🇽🇪
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Main Ek saal ki Namaz aur Rozo'n se badhh-kar 2 dosto'n mein Sulah (compromise) karane ko pasand karta hoo'n."_
(Sawaabul Aamal o Iqaabul Aamal)
🇽🇪
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo aage badh-kar logo'n mein Sulah karvaye to uske lautne take Farishte uspar Salaam bhejenge aur usay Shab e Qadr ka sawaab milega."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p212)

            ♦ _*JIHAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (553) 👹

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*سَتَجِدُونَ آخَرِينَ يُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَأْمَنُوكُمْ وَيَأْمَنُوا قَوْمَهُمْ كُلَّ مَا رُدُّوا إِلَى الْفِتْنَةِ أُرْكِسُوا فِيهَا ۚ فَإِنْ لَمْ يَعْتَزِلُوكُمْ وَيُلْقُوا إِلَيْكُمُ السَّلَمَ وَيَكُفُّوا أَيْدِيَهُمْ فَخُذُوهُمْ وَاقْتُلُوهُمْ حَيْثُ ثَقِفْتُمُوهُمْ ۚ وَأُولَٰئِكُمْ جَعَلْنَا لَكُمْ عَلَيْهِمْ سُلْطَانًا مُبِينًا*

_"Aur tumhe aise bhi Munafiq milege jo chahte hain ke tum se  mehfooz rahen aur apni qaum se bhi mehfooz rahen magar ye log jab bhi fitna ka mauqa payenge us mein  kood parenge. Agar woh tumhare muqabile mein baaz na rahen aur tumhare liye Sulah wa Salamti pesh na karen aur apne haath ko jang se na roke to woh jahan mile unhe pakdo aur qatl kardo. Unke khilaf Khuda ne tumhe khula ghalba ata kiya hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 91)

📚📖 👹
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein kuchh Munafeqeen ke liye Sulah ka hukm hua lekin ye Ayat aise Munafeqeen ke liye hai jo matlab parast hain. Woh dono se mile rahna bhi chahte hai taake amn o amaan mein rahen, aur khufiya tareeqe se Musalmano ke khilaf sazishen rachen. Ye ek tarah se aasteen ka saanp hain. Yahan lafz ثقفتموهم istemal hua hai means kisi cheez ka mushkil se maharat ke sath haath aana. Ye khatarnak dogle qism ke log hain mushkil se pahchan mein aate hain. Aise logon ke liye Allah ka Hukm Qatl hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👹
Imam Ali (as):
_"Agar main Momin ki naak bhi talwaar se kaatt doo'n ke mujhse adaawat kare to nahi karega aur agar Munafiq par saari duniya unddeyl doo'n ke mujhse mohabbat kar le to nahi karega, is liye ke ye faisla Rasule Akram (saww) ki zabaan se ho chuka hai ke "Aye Ali (as), Momin tumse dushmani nahi kar sakta aur Munafiq tumse mohabbat nahi kar sakta"._
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p142)
😈
Imam Husain (as):
_"Jis feyl (amal) par uzr-khwaahi karna (excuse / bahaane bataana) pade, wo kaam hi na karo is liye ke Momin na bura kaam karta hai na bahaane-baazi karta hai aur munafiq roz bura kaam karta hai aur uzr-khwaahi karta hai."_
(Al Kaafi, v3, p327)
👺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"(Aur farmaya) Momin se riya-kaari karna ek qism ka SHIRK hai magar Munafiq (hypocrite) se uske ghar mein riya-kaari karna ba-manzile IBAADAT hai… (Aur farmaya) khuda us shakhs par Rehmat nazil farmaye jo mukhalefeen ke dilo'n mein hamari Muhabbat paida karta hai aur hamen unki nazro'n mein Dushman nahi banata."_
(Aeteqadaat – Shaikh Sadooq, p112)

        ♦ _*QATL BY MISTAKE*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (554) 🔪🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَا كَانَ لِمُؤْمِنٍ أَنْ يَقْتُلَ مُؤْمِنًا إِلَّا خَطَأً ۚ وَمَنْ قَتَلَ مُؤْمِنًا خَطَأً فَتَحْرِيرُ رَقَبَةٍ مُؤْمِنَةٍ وَدِيَةٌ مُسَلَّمَةٌ إِلَىٰ أَهْلِهِ إِلَّا أَنْ يَصَّدَّقُوا ۚ فَإِنْ كَانَ مِنْ قَوْمٍ عَدُوٍّ لَكُمْ وَهُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ فَتَحْرِيرُ رَقَبَةٍ مُؤْمِنَةٍ ۖ وَإِنْ كَانَ مِنْ قَوْمٍ بَيْنَكُمْ وَبَيْنَهُمْ مِيثَاقٌ فَدِيَةٌ مُسَلَّمَةٌ إِلَىٰ أَهْلِهِ وَتَحْرِيرُ رَقَبَةٍ مُؤْمِنَةٍ ۖ فَمَنْ لَمْ يَجِدْ فَصِيَامُ شَهْرَيْنِ مُتَتَابِعَيْنِ تَوْبَةً مِنَ اللَّهِ ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا*
[Surat An-Nisa' 92]

_" *Kisi Momin ko ye Haq nahi ke woh kisi Momin ka qatl kare magar ghalti se* aur jo Shakhs kisi Momin ko ghalti se qatl kare to iska Kaffarah ye hai ke ek Momin ko ghulami se azad kare aur Maqtool ke Warison ko 'Khoon Baha' de."_
_"Agar woh Maqtool aisi qaum ka fard hai jo tumhara Dushman hai aur Qatl hone wala Momin hai to sirf ek Momin Ghulam azad karna hoga. Agar Maqtool aisi qaum ka fard hai jiska tumse Moaeda (treaty) hai to uske warison ko 'Khoon Baha' dena hoga aur ek Momin ko azad karna hoga. Phir jo Ghulam na paye to pai dar pai do Mahino ke Roza rakhe."_    
_"Yehi Allah ki taraf se Tauba ka raasta hai aur Allah Ilm o Hikmat wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 92)

📚📖 🔪🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta do Ayaton mein Allah ne Munafiq ko Qatl ka Hukm diya. Lekin iska ghalat fayda uthaya ja sakta hai. Allah ne is Ayat mein is par bhi rok lagayi hai.
As a general rule Momin Qatl nahi karta. Lekin agar by mistake kar bhi de to bhi uski saza hai. Is Ayat mein Shak o shubha ya ghalti se kisi ka qatl ho jaye uski saza ke mutalliq hai. Jan boojh kar, amdan, voluntary qatl ke bare mein next Ayat mein ayega.
*Qatle Khata ki Saza:*
(1) Ek Ghulam Azad karna.
--- Ijtemai Nuqsan ki talafi.
(2) Diyat ka ada karna. (Khoon Baha, Monetary Punishment)
--- Economical bharpai.
(3) Do Mahina Roza rakhna.
--- Spiritual bharpai. Akhlaqi wa Roohani Talafi.
Muslim aur Non-Muslim ke liye alag alag qanoon hain.
Islam ne is baat ki ahmiyat di hai ke ghalti se bhi qatl na ho. Qatl ek sangin jurm hai, Gunah e Kabira hai. Isliye bhale hi anjane mein ye jurm ho jaye, saza zaroor milegi.
Lekin ISIS ke liye ye bahut easy hai. Jaise ke Islam ne inhi ko saza e qatl ka theka de rakha hai.  
Tafseeli Ahkam ke liye Tauzeehul Masael refer karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🔪🗡
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khata (Shubh e Amd) (By mistake) ye hai ke tum jaan boojh kar aisi cheez se kisi ko mare jis se koi qatl na hota ho, aur mukammal Qatl e Khata ye hai ke insaan kisi aur cheez ko marna chahta ho aur ittifaq se koi shakhs iski zad mein aa jaye."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🙅‍♂
Imam Musa Kazim (as):
_"Fitrat par paida hone wala shakhs Momin hota hai, jab tak kisi ki tarbiyat mein aa kar doosra Deen ikhtiyar na kar le."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

    ♦ AMDAN QATL عمد قتل♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (555) 🔪🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يَقْتُلْ مُؤْمِنًا مُتَعَمِّدًا فَجَزَاؤُهُ جَهَنَّمُ خَالِدًا فِيهَا وَغَضِبَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهِ وَلَعَنَهُ وَأَعَدَّ لَهُ عَذَابًا عَظِيمًا*

"Aur jo koi kisi Momin ko jaan boojh kar Qatl kare to us ki Saza Jahannum hai. Woh us mein hamesha rahega aur us par Allah ka Ghazab aur Uski La'anat hai aur Allah ne uske liye sakht Azaab tayyar kar rakha hai."
(Surah Nisa: 93)

📚📖 🔪🗡
👉 Tafseer:
Guzishta Ayat mein Qatl jo sahvan, ghalti se ho jaye uski saza ka bayan tha.
Is Ayat mein jo Shakhs kisi Momin ko Jaan boojh kar Qatl kare uski saza ka bayan hai.
Saza:
(1) Hamesha Jahannum mein rahna.
(2) Ghazab e Ilahi.
(3) La'anat (Rehmat e Khuda se Mehroom)
(4) Azaab e Azeem mein mubtela rakhna.

Imam Sadiq (as):
"Is Ayat se woh Shakhs murad hain jo kisi Momin ko uske Imaan ki wajah se qatl kare to uske liye ye sari sazayen hain."
(Kitab Ma'anil Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
Is Ayat mein woh ashkhas nahi hai jo kisi ko badle ke qasd se Qatl karen, jo zaati mafad ke liye qatl karen. Is Ayat mein un Qatil ka zikr hai jinki Tauba qubool nahi hogi. Kiyonki inka Jurm itna sangin hai: Ek Momin, Ba Imaan ka qatl. Iska talluq Aqeede se hai, Nazaryati qatl hai. Isliye is mein woh sab Qatil shumar honge jinhone Anbiya ka qatl kiya, Aimma ka qatl kiya, aur woh Qatil jisne Ummul Aimma, ummul Sadaat, Rasool e Karim (saww) ki beti Fatema Zehra (sa) ko Shaheed kiya. Imam Husain (as) ka qatil.
Rivayaat ke mutabiq inke liye Tauba ki koi jagah nahi, balke Abadi Azaab rakha hai.
Aap ne note kiya hoga Doosre Qatilon ke liye jaisa ke pichhli Ayat mein bataya Dunyavi saza rakhi gayi. Jo Gunahgar/Mujrim jab woh is Duniya mein saza kaat leta hai to saza ke baad uske jurm ki talafi ho jati hai aur woh paak ho jata hai, woh ab Mujrim nahi kahlata lekin in Qatilon ke liye Allah ne koi Dunyavi punishment ke bare mein nahi farmaya balke Akherat ki saza sunai, jo ke unlimited hai. Kiyonki ye jurm itna sangin hai ke unhone Allah ke Mehboob, Mukhlis bandon ka qatl kiya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!
🙇 🔪🗡
Paighambar e Akram (saww):
*لزوال الدنيا اهون على الله من قتل امرء مسلم.*
_"Duniya ka zawal aur khatm ho jana Khuda ke haan ek mard e Musalman ke qatl hone se kamtar hai."_

*لو ان رجلا قتل بالمشرق و آخر رضی بالمغرب لا شرک فی دمه.*
_"Agar ek shakhs East mein qatl ho jaye aur doosra West mein ho aur is par raazi ho to woh bhi uske khoon mein sharik hai."_
(Al Munar, Vol 5, P-361)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

              ♦ _*JIHAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (556) 🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا إِذَا ضَرَبْتُمْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ فَتَبَيَّنُوا وَلَا تَقُولُوا لِمَنْ أَلْقَىٰ إِلَيْكُمُ السَّلَامَ لَسْتَ مُؤْمِنًا تَبْتَغُونَ عَرَضَ الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا فَعِنْدَ اللَّهِ مَغَانِمُ كَثِيرَةٌ ۚ كَذَٰلِكَ كُنْتُمْ مِنْ قَبْلُ فَمَنَّ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكُمْ فَتَبَيَّنُوا ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرًا*

_"Aye Imaan walon! Jab Allah ki raah mein Jihad ke liye niklo to Dost o Dushman mein Tameez karo aur jo tumhari taraf Salam mein taqdeem kare to use fauran ye na kaho ke tum Momin nahi ho. Agar tumhe Dunyawi fawaid matloob hain to Allah ke paas tumhare liye bahut sa Maal e Ghanimat maujood hai. Akhir tum bhi to pahle aise hi the. Phir Allah ne tum par Ehsaan kiya. Lehaza tehqeeq se kaam lo. Khuda ko tumhare Aamaal ki khabar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 94)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Silsilah e bayan Jihad ke mutalliq jari hai.
Rasool e Khuda (sa) ne Osama bin Zaid ko kuchh sawaro ke daste ke sath Fidak ki Yahoodi basti ki taraf ravana kiya. Jab basti walo ko pata chala ke Rasoole Khuda (saww) ka Lashkar aa raha hai woh log zor zor se Kalma e Tayyeba ke naare lagane lage. Osama ko ye sab dhong laga aur ek ko halak kar diya. Iske baad jab Osama Rasool (saww) ki khidmat mein hazir hua to woh naraaz hue aur farma:
_"Tum us shakhs ko qatl kar diya jis ne Tawheed o Risaalat ki gawahi di!"_
Usne farmaya ke main apni difa ke liye kiya. Rasool e Akram (saww) ne farmaya:
_"Kiya tu ne uske dil ka parda hata kar dekha tha, tu ne Kalma sun kar bhi aitbar nahi kiya?"_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)
Isse pahle ham bata chuke hain ke Jihad sirf Dushman se difa ke maqsad ke tahet hota hai. Jihad sirf ek Masoom ke saye mein ho sakta hai, kiyonki ghair Masoom se aisi ghalti ho sakti hai jaise ke is waqae mein bataya.
Aaj ka Musalman balke har zamane mein Jihad Jihad ke nare deta aya hai. Koi bhi khud sakhta leader ban jata hai aur apne mafad ke liye qatl e aam karna shuru karta. Zaroori nahi ke sab Non-Muslim se Jihad kiya jaye. Agar woh amaan chahta hai to use uske haal par chhod dena chahiye.
Lekin Aaj to ham ye dekh rahe hai ke Jihad ke naam par puri Duniya mein Antakwad (Terrorism) phail raha hai. IS, Al Qaeda, Taliban aur unki shakhen sab Jihad ka nara de kar sirf Kalma go ka hi qatl e aam kar rahe hain.
Sab se badi Musibat ye hai jin ko Islam se lena dena nahi wohi Islam ke thekedar bane hai. Is Ayat se ye baten sabit hain. Iski wajah yehi hai inhone Ahle Bait e Athaar ka daman chhod diya hai aur la ilmi ki talwaar Ahle Imaan par chala rahe hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡
Imam Sadiq (as)
se kisi shakhs ne kaha, _"Allah aap ko jazaa e khair ataa farmaye. Kiya Hazrat Ali (as) Deen mein pukhta aur qawi (firm and strong) nahi the?" Aap (as) ne farmaya, "Haa'n, wo qawi the". Usne kaha, "Phir qaum kis tarah un par ghaalib aa gayi aur unhone iska difaa (defend) nahi kiya aur na unko roka"._
To aap (as) ne farmaya: _"Kitaab e Khuda mein ek Ayat hai jisne unko is baat se roka". Us shakhs ne kaha, "Wo kaun si Ayaat hai?"_
_Aap (as) ne farmaya,_
*......لَوْ تَزَيَّلُوا لَعَذَّبْنَا الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا مِنْهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*
[Surat Al-Fath 25]
_"Kyun ki Allah Azz Wa Jall ki Momin Amaanatein Kaafiro'n aur Munafiqo'n ki sulbo'n (loins) mein maujood the to Ali (as) ke liye ye mumkin nahi tha ke unke aaba (purvaj) ko qatl kare de'n ta waqt ye ke Amaanatein paida ho jaayein aur jab Amaanatein nikal aayi'n to Ali (as) unpe hamlawar huwe aur unse muqabila kiya. Isi tarah hamare Ahlebait (as) ke Qaim (atfs) ka us waqt tak zahoor na hoga jab tak Allah ki Amaanatein paida na ho jaayein phir wo apne Mukhaalifeen par galba haasil kar ke unko qatl karenge"._
(Kamaluddin, v2, p608)

              ♦ _*JIHAAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (557) 🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يَسْتَوِي الْقَاعِدُونَ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ غَيْرُ أُولِي الضَّرَرِ وَالْمُجَاهِدُونَ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَنْفُسِهِمْ ۚ فَضَّلَ اللَّهُ الْمُجَاهِدِينَ بِأَمْوَالِهِمْ وَأَنْفُسِهِمْ عَلَى الْقَاعِدِينَ دَرَجَةً ۚ وَكُلًّا وَعَدَ اللَّهُ الْحُسْنَىٰ ۚ وَفَضَّلَ اللَّهُ الْمُجَاهِدِينَ عَلَى الْقَاعِدِينَ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا * دَرَجَاتٍ مِنْهُ وَمَغْفِرَةً وَرَحْمَةً ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Sahebane Imaan mein se jo log kisi mazoori ke baghair ghar baithe rahte hain aur jo Allah ki raah mein Jaan o Maal se Jihad karte hain. Ye dono barabar nahi hain. Allah ne Maal o Jaan se Jihad karne walon ko baithe rahne walon ke Muqabile mein Ajre Azeem ata kiya hai."_
_"Unke liye Allah ki taraf se bade Darje hain aur Maghferat aur Rehmat hai aur Allah Bada Bakhshne wala, Meherban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 95 - 96)

📚📖 🗡
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jihad ke kai aspect is silsile ki Ayaton mein zikr kar chuke hai. Aaj ki Ayat Jihad karne walon ki Fazilat mein hai. Baghair kisi excuse ke jo ghar mein baithe rahte, Jihad karne wale unse bartar hain.
Jihad Aalam e Aab o Gul ka ek General Qanoon hai aur Duniya mein jo cheez hai chahe Nabatat ho ya Haiwanat (Living or Non-living) sab Jihad ke zariye apna raasta saaf karti hain taake apne Matlooba Kamalaat tak pahunch jaye. Misal ke taur par darakht (tree) ki jaden har waqt quwwat wa ghaza hasil karne ke liye active rahti hain, agar ye koshish chhod den to ped sookh jayega. Insaan bhi zinda rahne ke liye Jaddo Jahed karta rahta hai. Isliye apne Deen ko zinda rakhne ke liye bhi Jaddo Jahed ki zaroorat hoti hai. Isliye Allah ne unko bartari di hai.
Jihad ka mafhoom sirf Dushman se hatiyar se ladna hi nahi balke iske maani wasi hai.
Jo ilme Deen hasil karne ki koshish karta hai use Ijtehaad kahte hai. Ek Shakhs apne Ahlo Ayaal ko ba hayat rakhne ki koshish karta hai woh bhi Jihad hai. Deen ki khatir agar koi kisi ki madad kar raha hai woh bhi Jihad hai.... etc.
Is Ayat mein Active Insaano ki madah ki gayi hai aur Kahil, Sust, Lazy logon ki mazammat ki hai. Un logon ko condemn kiya hai jo ghar baithe rahte hai aur kuchh nahi karte.
Malhooz rahe Roze Ashura Imam Husain (as) apne 72 sathiyon ke sath Karbala mein Jihad kar rahe the jabke aksariyat ghar baithe tamasha dekh rahi thi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🗡
Rasool e Khuda (saww)
_"Jihad karo taake Azmat apni Aulad ko wirse mein de jao."_
🗡
Rasool e Khuda (saww)
_"Jo Shakhs Jihad ko tark kar deta hai Khuda use Zillat ka libaas pahna deta hai aur Faqr o Faqa uski Zindagi par aur tareeki wa siyahi uske Deen par manhoos saye ki tarah chha jati hai. Khuda wande Alam meri Ummat ko ghodon ke sumo ke zariye jo Jihad mein aage jaate hain aur nezon ki eno ke wasile se Izzat Bakhshta hai."_
(Wasail, Kitabul Jihad, Ch 1, H-2,16)
🗡
Amirul Momenin Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Jihad Jannat ke Darwazon mein se ek Darwaza hai jise Khuda ne apne makhsoos doston ke liye khol rakha hai. Jihad Taqwa ka pur Fazilat Libaas hai. Jihad Khuda ki na qabil shikast zirah hai. Jihad Parwardigar e Alam ki Sipar aur Dhaal hai. Jo Shakhs Jihad ko tark kar deta hai Khuda uske Jism par Zillat aur Musibat ka Libaas pahna deta hai aur use logon ki nigah mein Zaleel o Khwar kar deta hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba 27)

           ♦ _*MUSTAZ'AFEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (558) 🐪🐫

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ تَوَفَّاهُمُ الْمَلَائِكَةُ ظَالِمِي أَنْفُسِهِمْ قَالُوا فِيمَ كُنْتُمْ ۖ قَالُوا كُنَّا مُسْتَضْعَفِينَ فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ قَالُوا أَلَمْ تَكُنْ أَرْضُ اللَّهِ وَاسِعَةً فَتُهَاجِرُوا فِيهَا ۚ فَأُولَٰئِكَ مَأْوَاهُمْ جَهَنَّمُ ۖ وَسَاءَتْ مَصِيرًا * إِلَّا الْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ مِنَ الرِّجَالِ وَالنِّسَاءِ وَالْوِلْدَانِ لَا يَسْتَطِيعُونَ حِيلَةً وَلَا يَهْتَدُونَ سَبِيلًا * فَأُولَٰئِكَ عَسَى اللَّهُ أَنْ يَعْفُوَ عَنْهُمْ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَفُوًّا غَفُورًا*

_"Jo log apne Nafs par Zulm kar rahe the jab Farishton ne unki Roohen qabz ki to unse kaha ke tum kis haal mein mubtela the? Unhone kaha ke ham Zameen mein kamzor be bas the. Farishton ne kaha ke kiya Khuda ki Zameen wasi (expanded) na thi ke tum us mein hijrat karte? Ye log hain jin ka thikana Jahannam hai aur woh bura thikana hai."_
_"Haan jo Mard, Aurten aur bachche waqai be bas (Muztaz'af) aur Zalemana mahaul se nikalne ka koi raasta aur zariyah nahi paate to qareeb hai ke Allah unhe Maaf kar de, Allah bada Maaf Karnewala aur Bakhshne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 97 - 99)

📚📖 🐪🐫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Jihad ki guftugu ke baad ab un log ke bare mein zikr kiya gaya hai jo Muslim Minority Kafir Majority ke darmiyan mein rahte the. Aisa aaj bhi hota hai ke Minority group mein se kuchh Aksariyat ke sath ho jate hain aur aap ko bachane ke khatir unki haan mein haan karte hain. Aur jo aisa nahi karte woh unke zulm ka shikar hote hain.  Misal ke taur par Saudi ya India mein Minority Community, ya US ya UK etc. Ye Minority Community ya to unke Zulm bardasht karti hai ya phir unka saath dena padta hai, ya Taqayya mein rahna padta hai. Yahan tak ke ye Malakul Maut inki Rooh qabz karta hai. Yahan in Marhoom Minority se sawal hota hai ke kiyon tum zulm sahte sahte mar gaye, kisi aur jagah hijrat kar lete, Duniya itni badi hai. Ye sawal unke liye hai jo itni capacity rakhte the ke woh wahan se migrate ho jayen. Lekin jo log wahi phans gaye, majboor hai, mazoor hain, unhe Allah maaf kar dega.
Yahan Allah logon ko takeed kar raha hai ke aap Islami mahaul mein rahen. Agar aisa mahaul nahi hai to doosri jagah transfer kar len.
Kuchh baten is Ayat mein ayi hain jis ka tafseeli tazkarah baad mein hoga, woh ye hain:
(1) Rooh qabz karne ke liye Malaika muayyan hai, unka chief Malakul Maut 'Izrael' hai.
(2) Muztaz'af:
Imam Ali (as):
_"Woh Shakhs Muztaz'af nahi hai jis par Hujjat tamam ho chuki ho us ne Haq ko suna ho aur uske zahen ne uska idrak kiya ho."_
(Tafseer e Burhan, V-2, P-291)
Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
_"Muztaz'af woh Shakhs hai jis tak Hujjat aur Daleel na pahunchi ho aur woh (Mazahib aur Aqaed ke bare mein) maujood ikhtelaf ko na samajh saka ho aur jo us cheez ko samajh chuka ho woh Muztaz'af nahi hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain, V-1, P-539)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

(Noorus Saqlain)

(Nahjul Balagha)

              ♦ _*HIJRAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (559) 🐪🐫

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يُهَاجِرْ فِي سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ يَجِدْ فِي الْأَرْضِ مُرَاغَمًا كَثِيرًا وَسَعَةً ۚ وَمَنْ يَخْرُجْ مِنْ بَيْتِهِ مُهَاجِرًا إِلَى اللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ ثُمَّ يُدْرِكْهُ الْمَوْتُ فَقَدْ وَقَعَ أَجْرُهُ عَلَى اللَّهِ ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Aur jo bhi Allah ki raah mein HIJRAT karega to woh Zameen mein panah lene ke liye bahut jagah aur basar auqat ke liye badi gunjayish payega aur jo apne ghar se Allah aur Rasool ki taraf Hijrat ke liye nikle. Phir raaste mein use Maut aa jaye to uska Ajr Allah ke zimme Wajib ho gaya aur Allah bahut Bakhshne wala, Meherban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 100)

📚📖 🐪🐫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Hijrat na karne walon se sawal kiya gaya tha. Is Ayat mein Hijrat ki takeed ki gayi hai. Ye Hijrat Deen baqa ke liye hai. Deen ki tableegh mein agar hamare watan mein rahne se agar rukawate paida ho rahi hon to Hijrat behtar hai. Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne Mecca se Medina Hijrat ki jab Kuffare Quraish ka zulm zyada badh gaya tha. Aise Mahaul mein Tableegh karna mushkil ho gaya. Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) ko apne bistar par sulaya aur Hijrat ki.
Islam mein ye Din bahut ahmiyat rakhta hai. Isi liye jab Umar ko khayal aya ke puri Hukumate Islamiya mein ek hi Calender hona chahiye to kuchh uski kuchh samajh mein nahi aya. Tab Hazrat Ali (as) se mashwara liya gaya to unhone yehi Hijrat ka Din bataya. Isliye Islami Hijri Calendar ki shuru'at hui.
Hijrat se Musalmano ko zyada Azaadi mili. Aur zyada taqatwar aur mazboot hue.
Lekin ek Musalman Gunahon ke raaston ko chhod kar Neki ki taraf bhi hijrat karta ha. Ye Roohani Hijrat hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🐪🐫
Paighambar e Akram (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs apne Deen ki hifazat ke liye ek sar zameen se doosri sar zameen ki taraf ek balisht barabar Hijrat kare to woh Jannat ka Mushtheq ho jata hai aur Muhammad o Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ki rafaqat aur ham nashini use naseeb hogi (kiyonki ye dono Azeem Paighambar Alam e hasti mein Hijrat karne walo ke Peshwa aur Rahnuma the.)"_
(Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-541)
🐫🐪
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Baaz kahte hain ke hamne Hijrat ki hai halanke haqiqat mein unhone ne Hijrat nahi ki, Haqeeqi Hijrat karne wale woh hain jo gunahon se Hijrat ikhtiyar karte hain aur unke murtakib nahi hote."_
(Safinatul Bihar (Hijr))

        ♦ _*NAMAZ-E-QASR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (560) 🙌🏻 🚉

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا ضَرَبْتُمْ فِي الْأَرْضِ فَلَيْسَ عَلَيْكُمْ جُنَاحٌ أَنْ تَقْصُرُوا مِنَ الصَّلَاةِ إِنْ خِفْتُمْ أَنْ يَفْتِنَكُمُ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا ۚ إِنَّ الْكَافِرِينَ كَانُوا لَكُمْ عَدُوًّا مُبِينًا*

_"Aur jab tum Zameen mein Safar karo to tumhare liye NAMAZ QASR karne mein koi harj nahi (khusoosan) jabke tumhe andesha ho ke Kafir tumhe satainge. Yaqeenan Kuffar tumhare liye khule hue Dushman hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 101)

📚📖 🕌 🙌🏻🚉
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat me Hijrat ka zikr tha. Jab ek Shakhs Hijrat karta hai to Safar mein usko Namaz Qasr padhni hogi.
Iske mutalliq kuchh Sawal aur Imam ka Jawab:
🕌🙌🏻
*Sawal: Namaz e Maghrib 3 Rakaten kiyon farz hain aur is mein Qasr kiyon nahi?*

Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Ibteda mein Allah ne har Namaz ki do rakaten hi nazil farmayi thi. Rasool e Akram (saww) ne Maghrib ki Namaz padhi to Aap ko Janabe Fatema (sa) ki Wiladat ki khabar mili. Aap (saww) ne Allah ka Shukr ada karne ki gharz se Namaze Maghrib mein ek Rakat ka izafa kar diya. Aap ko Imam Hasan (as) ki Wiladat ki khush khabari mili to Aap (saww) ne 2 Rakat ka izafa kiya aur Aap ko Imam Husain (as) ki Wiladat ki khush khabari mili to Aap (saww) ne 2 Rakat ka izafa kiya. Hazrat Zehra (sa) ki Wiladat par 1 Rakat aur Hasnain (as) ki Wiladat par 2 - 2 Rakat ka izafat kiyonki Meeras ke Qanoon ke mutabiq ladke ko ladki se dugna hai."_
_"...Isha ki 2 izafi Rakaten Masoomeen (as) ki Aamad ki khushi mein badhai thi."_
(Ilalush Sharaye, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌🙌🏻
*Safar mein Namaz Qasr kiyon?*

Imam Ali Reza (as):
_"Ibteda mein 10 Rakat Namaz hi Wajib thi. Baad mein 7 Rakat ka izafa kiya gaya. Safar ki haalat mein thakan aur mashaqqat ki wajah se Allah ne in izafi Raka'at mein se 6 Raka'at maaf kar di albatta Namaz e Maghrib ki ek Rakat baqi rakhi."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌🙌🏻
*Namaz e Qasr ke liye 8 Farsakh ka Safar kiyon zaroori?*

Imam Reza (as):
_"Qafila aam taur par ek Din mein 8 Farsakh ka fasla tai karta hai. Isi liye ek Din ke Safar par Namaz e Qasr ka hukm diya gaya. Agar ek Din ke Safar par Qasr ka hukm na hota to phir ek saal ke Safar mein bhi Namaz Qasr na hoti kiyonki ek Din ke baad jab doosra Din aata to woh bhi to usi jaisa hota. Isi liye agar ek Din ke Safar par Namaz Qasr na hoti to us jaise doosre Din ke Safar mein bhi Namaz Qasr na hoti kiyonki dono ek hi tarah ke Din hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar, Noorus Saqlain)
🕌🙌🏻
*Imam Reza (as) se sawaal huwa ke Namaz e Juma 2 rak'at hai aur agar Imam na ho to 4 rak'at Namaz e Zuhr kyun padhi jaati hai?*

Imam (as) ne kaha ke iski bahut si wajuhaat (reasons) hai:
_(1) Log Namaz e Juma ke liye door daraaz se safar kar ke aate hain. Allah Ta'ala ne chaha ke log thake huwe hain is liye inhe 2 rak'at ki ri'aayat (concession) di jaaye. Is liye Namaz e Juma 2 Rak'at hai._
_(2) Imam kuchh deyr ke liye khutba deta hai aur muqtadi khutba sunte rehte hain aur unhe Namaz ka intezaar hota hai aur jo Namaz ke intezaar mein ho to wo bhi Namaz mein shumaar kiya jaata hai. Isi liye Juma ke 2 khutbe 2 Rak'at qaaem karne ke barabar hai._
_(3) Imam ke saath 2 Rak'at Namaz Khuda ki nazar mein 4 Rak'at hai kyun ki Imam ke Ilm, Fiqh, Adl aur Fazl ki wajah se 2 Rak'at Namaz ko itni bulandi naseeb hoti hai ke wo 4 Rak'at maani jaati hai._
_(4) Juma musalmano'n ki Eid hai aur Namaz e Eid 2 Rak'at hi huwa karti hai aur 2 khutbo'n ki wajah se isme qasr paida nahi hoti."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p232)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌🙌🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Tamaam Namazo'n mein Azaan ko tark na karo. Aur agar tark karna hi chaho to kam az kam Namaz e Subh aur Maghrib mein to ise hargiz tark na karo kyun ki oon dono Namazo'n mein Qasr nahi hai."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v4, p45)

*1st Jamadi us Sani 1438, 1st March 2017, Wednesday,

       ♦ _*NAMAZ-E-KHAUF*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (561) 🕌⚔

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِذَا كُنْتَ فِيهِمْ فَأَقَمْتَ لَهُمُ الصَّلَاةَ فَلْتَقُمْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْهُمْ مَعَكَ وَلْيَأْخُذُوا أَسْلِحَتَهُمْ فَإِذَا سَجَدُوا فَلْيَكُونُوا مِنْ وَرَائِكُمْ وَلْتَأْتِ طَائِفَةٌ أُخْرَىٰ لَمْ يُصَلُّوا فَلْيُصَلُّوا مَعَكَ وَلْيَأْخُذُوا حِذْرَهُمْ وَأَسْلِحَتَهُمْ ۗ وَدَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا لَوْ تَغْفُلُونَ عَنْ أَسْلِحَتِكُمْ وَأَمْتِعَتِكُمْ فَيَمِيلُونَ عَلَيْكُمْ مَيْلَةً وَاحِدَةً ۚ وَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْكُمْ إِنْ كَانَ بِكُمْ أَذًى مِنْ مَطَرٍ أَوْ كُنْتُمْ مَرْضَىٰ أَنْ تَضَعُوا أَسْلِحَتَكُمْ ۖ وَخُذُوا حِذْرَكُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ أَعَدَّ لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابًا مُهِينًا*

_"Aur jab Aap unke darmiyan hon aur unhe Namaz padhane khade hon to un mein se ek giroh ko tumhare saath khada hona chahiye aur unhe chahiye ke apna aslaha (weapons) liye rahen aur jab is giroh ke afraad Sajdah kar len to pichhe chalen jayen aur unki jagah woh giroh aa jaye jis ne Namaz abhi tak nahi padhi. Woh aa kar tumhare saath Namaz padhen aur woh bhi jo chaukanna rahe aur apna aslaha liye rahe. Kuffar chahte hain ke tum apne Aslaha aur samaan se ghaafil ho jao taake woh tum par yakbargi hamla kar den. Haan agar tum Barish ya Beemari ki wajah se Aslaha na utha sako to Aslaha rakh dene mein koi harj nahi hai magar phir bhi chaukanne raho. Yaqeen rakho ke Allah ke Allah ne Kafiron ke liye ruswa kun Azaab muhayya kiya hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 102)

📚📖 🕌⚔
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Maidane Jang mein padhi jane wali ye Namaz *'Namaz e Khauf'* kahlayi jati hai. Iska tareeqa jo ke Ayat mein kulli taur bayan kiya gaya hai lekin detail tareeqa e Sunnat ke mutabiq ye hai:
4 Rakat Namaz 2 Rakat mein change ho jati hai. Ye ba Jamat hoti hai. Pahla giroh Peshnamaz ke sath 1 Rakat padh leta hai aur Peshnamaz 1 Rakat ke baad thoda rukta hai aur woh giroh doosri Rakat ko alaihdgi mein anjam deta hai aur Mahaz e Jang ki taraf palat jata hai aur phir doosra giroh uski jagah le leta hai aur woh apni ek Rakat Peshnamaz ke sath aur doosri farada anjam deta hai.
Ye Namaz har daur mein hoti rahi Rasoole Akram (saww), Hazrat Ali (as) ki Imamat mein. Imam Husain (as) ne Karbala mein yehi Namaz padhai. Iske alawa fauji commander ne jaise Huzaifa Yamani ne bhi padhai.
Jahan Allah ne apni jaan o maal ki hifazat ka khayal rakhne ka hukm diya wahin ye bhi bata diya ke Namaz har haalat mein zaroori hai, ise tark nahi kar sakte. Aur Jamat ki ahmiyat ka bhi pata chalta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ek shakhs ki Jamaat mein padhi huwi ek rakaat Namaz, uski uske ghar mein padhi huwi 40 saal ki Namaz se afzal hai."_
(Wasaail, v 5, p374)
(The Prayer)
🕌
Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa):
_"Allah Namaz ko isliye Wajib kiya taake us mein  Takabbur ko khatm ho jaye."_
(Biharul Anwar, Vol 82, P-209, H-19)

*2th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 2th March 2017, Thursday,

                ♦ _*NAMAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (563) 🕌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَإِذَا قَضَيْتُمُ الصَّلَاةَ فَاذْكُرُوا اللَّهَ قِيَامًا وَقُعُودًا وَعَلَىٰ جُنُوبِكُمْ ۚ فَإِذَا اطْمَأْنَنْتُمْ فَأَقِيمُوا الصَّلَاةَ ۚ إِنَّ الصَّلَاةَ كَانَتْ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ كِتَابًا مَوْقُوتًا*

_"Jab tum Namaz tamam kar lo to khade, baithe aur lete har haal mein Khuda ko yaad karte raho aur jab itminan hasil ho jaye to baqaida Namaz qaem karo. Namaz dar haqiqat aisa fariza hai jo pabandi e waqt ke sath Ahle Imaan par lazim ki gayi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 103)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke mauzu ko jari rakhte hue Allah ne Namaz ko har insaan par har haal mein Wajib qarar diya hai. Isko kisi haalat mein tark nahi kar sakte. Saath hi waqt ki pabandi ki bhi takeed ki hai. Awwale Waqt Namaz padhne ki bhi zyada takeed ki gayi hai. Isse Khuda ki Ibaadat mein nazm o zabt (Discipline) ki ahmiyat ka pata chalta hai. Ye isliye ke insaan kisi bhi waqt Khuda se ghafil na rahe. Kisi bhi successful system (Kamyab Nizam) ke liye Discipline bahut zaroori hai. Ye Discipline sirf Mazhabe Islam mein hi payi jati hai. Baqi Duniya ke sare mazahib mein koi punctual system nahi hai.
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat ka matlab ye hai ke Namaz ek mustaqil Fariza hai. Agar tumne jaldi ki ya kuchh takhir ki to usse tumhe koi nuqsaan nahi pahunchega. Haan tumne Namaz ko zaye (waste) kar diya to ye aur baat hai. Kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ne Namaz zaye karne walon ki mazammat (condemn) karte hue farmaya hai: (Maryam:59)"_
(Al Kafi, Raavi: Dawood bin Farqad)
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Mareez khada hokar Namaz padhe, agar khada hone ki taqat na ho to baith kar Namaz padhe aur agar baith kar na padh sakta ho to let kar Namaz padhe. Takbeer kahe, iske baad qarat kare aur jab Ruku karne ka irada kare to apni ankho ko band kare phir *سبحان الله ربى العظيم و بحمده* kahe. Jab Ruku padh le to apni Aankh khole, uska Aankh kholna Ruku se sar buland karne ke qaem maqam hai. Phir Sajdah ka iraada kare to Aankhen band kare aur zikre Sajdah padhe. Jab dono Sajde lar le to Aankhen khol de aur uski Aankhon ka kholna uske sar Sajde ke uthane ke qaem maqam hai. Phir Tashahud padhe aur Salam padh kar Namaz mukammal kare."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Har Namaz ke liye 2 waqt hote hain: Ek awwal aur ek aakhir. Unme awwal waqt afzal hai, kisi ko ikhtiyaar nahi hai ke wo aakhir waqt ko ikhtiyaar kare siwaaye kisi khaas wajah ke. Aakhri waqt to sirf oon logo'n ke liye hai jo mareez aur beemar hote hain ya kisi uzr ki wajah se Namaz nahi padh sakte. Awwal e waqt Khuda ki raza-mandi hai aur aakhri waqt Khuda ki meherbaani hai."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5, p609)

Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Har Namaz ke waqt ek Farishta logo'n ko awaaz deta hai ke "Uthho aur wo Aag jo tumhare liye roshan ki gayi hai use apni Namazo'n se bujhaao"._
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p461)


Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jisme ye 2 aadatein hongi wo achcha hai, warna door ho, door ho, door ho. Aap se puchha gaya ke wo kaunsi 2 aadatein hain? Aap ne farmaya, *"Namaz ko waqt par ba-qaida adaa karna* aur mohtaajo'n aur qaidiyo'n se hamdardi karna"._
(Khisaal, p48)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi ek lukma Haraam khayega uski 40 raato'n tak Namaz qubool nahi hogi aur 40 subah tak Dua mustajaab nahi hogi."_
(Noori - Dar as Salaam, p213)
(The Prayer)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww)
ki Wasiyyat:
_"Aye Ali, main tumhein hidayat karta hun ke kuchh aadato'n ki hifazat karna… *Namaze Shab padhna, Namaze Shab padhna, Namaze Shab padhna**"_
(40 Hadith)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*4th Jamadi us Sani 1438*
4th March 2017, Saturday,

   ♦ _*DUSMAN SE MUQABILA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (564) 👺💩

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تَهِنُوا فِي ابْتِغَاءِ الْقَوْمِ ۖ إِنْ تَكُونُوا تَأْلَمُونَ فَإِنَّهُمْ يَأْلَمُونَ كَمَا تَأْلَمُونَ ۖ وَتَرْجُونَ مِنَ اللَّهِ مَا لَا يَرْجُونَ ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Un logon ke taqqub mein susti na dikhao. Agar tum takleef utha rahe ho to tumhari tarah woh bhi takleef utha rahe hain aur tum Allah se us cheez ke ummidwar ho jiske woh ummidwar nahi hain aur Allah Jannewala, Hikmatwala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 104)

📚📖 👺💩
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat Musalmano ko is baat se agah kar rahi hai ke unhe chahiye ke Dushman ki kisi bhi techniques se be khabar na hon aur unke jang ke har zariye ke muqabil chahe woh jismani ho ya nafsani usse zyada mazboot aur ghalba pane wala zariya apnayen. Yahan tak inke naare ke muqabile mein zyada zordar nare lagayen.
Lehaza aaj ke zamane mein bhi Musalmano ko jin dardnak hawadis aur wahshatnak mafasid ne gher rakha hai bajai iske ke afsos karte rahen fa'aliyat se kaam len, hamesha active rahen. Ghalat Kitabon aur Print Media ke muqabile mein bhi sahih kutub aur print media faraham karen. Dushmano ke propaganda ke new means mein aaj ke new tablighati wasail ko kaam mein layen aur wrong means ke muqabile tafreeh aur entertainment ke sahih means ko apne youths ke liye faraham karen. Dushman ke muqabile ke liye mazboot planning aur scheme tayyar karen jisse ham unki sazishon, mansoobon, siyasi, iqtesadi aur social lehaz se muqabila kar saken.
Ye Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke Intezar ka falsafa hai. Intezar susti wa kahili ka naam nahi balke aamadgi ka naam hai. Imam ka zahoor tabhi hoga jab ham nusrat ke liye tayyar honge.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👺💩
Imam Ali (as):
_"Apne Dushman se aazmaaish ke liye Mashwera liya karo taaki tumhe uski Dushmani ki miqdaar (limit) maalum ho jaaye."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Adaawat)
👺💩
Riwayat:
_"Salwaat ki barkat se hamesha Dushman o Shaitan zaleel o khwaar hota hai."_
(Fazaael e Salwaat Aur Mushkilaat ka Hal)
👺💩
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Kisi se Dushmani na karo chaahe tumhe ye gumaan ho ke wo tumhe nuqsaan Nahi pahu'nchaega aur kisi se Dosti na chhodo chahe tumhe gumaan ho ke us say koi faayda na hoga."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*7th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 7th March 2017, Tuesday,
