            ♦ _*QAZAWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (565) ⚖ 🔨

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّا أَنْزَلْنَا إِلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ بِالْحَقِّ لِتَحْكُمَ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ بِمَا أَرَاكَ اللَّهُ ۚ وَلَا تَكُنْ لِلْخَائِنِينَ خَصِيمًا*

_"Beshak Hamne Aap (saww) ki taraf Kitab nazil ki  taake jo Raahe Raast Allah ne Aapko dikhai hai, uske mutabiq logon ke darmiyan faisla karo aur Khayanat karon ke liye jhagadne wale na banen."_
(Surah Nisa: 105)

📚📖 ⚖🔨
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Allah ne Rasool e Akram (saww) ko ikhtiyar diya ke logon ke darmiyan Qur'an wa Shariyat ke mutabiq faisla karen. Qazi agar Masoom ho to Mazloom ko uska Haq milega warna woh ghalat faisla bhi kar sakta hai.
Ayat ke Shane Nuzool mein ek chori ka waqea hai jis mein chor apni chori chhupane ke liye ek doosre par tuhmat lagate rahe aur ye pechida maslah Rasool (saww) ke saamne rakha gaya aur Ayat ke mutabiq unhone faisla kiya. Tafseel ki yahan gunjayish nahi hai.
Aaj jab ke koi Masoom zahiri taur par nahi hai isliye jo Muslim Judge faisla dete hain unhe Qur'an aur Rivayaat e Masoomeen (as) ki roshni mein hi apne faisle dene honge. Is mein Hakim e Shara'a bhi shamil hain.
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ne Rasool e Khuda (saww) aur Aimma e Tahereen (as) ke alawa kisi ko Amr tafweez nahi kiya. Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya (4:105) aur yehi umoor Shariyat ki tafweez Ausiya mein bhi jari hai"_
(Al Kafi)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as) ne apne student Abu Hanifa se guftugu ki:
_"Tum apne aap ko "Sahib e Ray" (Self Decision) samajhte ho jabke Ray sirf Rasool e Khuda (saww) ki Sahih thi, baqi logon ki ray ghalat hoti hai. Aapki (saww) Ray bhi Khuda ki taraf se hoti thi aur wo "اراءت الهى" par mushtamil thi. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne apne Paighambar se farmaya: (4:105)."_

In rivayaat se pata chala hamare faisle aur ray ki koi auqat nahi. Ham mein itni salahiyat nahi hai, ham ghalti kar sakte hain. Aur ghalti se ek begunah ko phansi ho sakti hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚒
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Jo ladai jhagde mein had se badh jai woh gunahgar hota hai aur jo us mein kami kare us par zulm dhaye jate hain aur jo ladta jhagadta hai uske liye mushkil hota hai ke Khauf e Khuda qaem rakhe."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
⚖
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
🤝 👀
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Momin Momin ka bhai, uski aa'nkh aur uska Rehbar hai, na uske saath khayaanat karta hai, na Zulm karta hai, na Milaawat karta hai aur na Waada-khilaafi karta hai."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*8th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 8th March 2017, Wednesday,

           ♦ _*ISTEGHFAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (566) 👏🏻🙌🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَاسْتَغْفِرِ اللَّهَ ۖ إِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Aur Allah se Maghferat ki darkhwast karo, Woh Bada Maghferat Karnewala Meherban hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 106)

📚📖 👏🏻🙌🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Aaj Jumerat hai Maghferat ki raat hai. Allah is Ayat mein farmaya raha hai Isteghfar karo, Woh qubool karne wala hai. Mayusi Gunahe Kabira hai. Aaj ki raat Dua-e-Kumail padhna chahiye sath hi uske matalib par bhi ghaur karen ke banda kis tarah Khuda se faryad karta hai:
Hazrat Ali (as) ne ye Dua apne sahabi Kumail bin Ziyad ko taleem farmayi.
Is Dua ke kuchh fiqre mulaheza hon:

*اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَهتِكُ الْعِصَمَ اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ النِّقَمَ اللَّهُمَ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُغيِّرُ النِّعَمَ اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَحْبِسُ الدُّعَاءَ اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تَقْطَعُ الرََّّجَاءَ اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي الذُّنُوبَ الَّتِي تُنْزِلُ البَلاءَ اللَّهُمَّ اغْفِرْ لِي كُلَّ ذَنْبٍ أَذْنَبْتُهُ وَكُلَّ خَطِيئَةٍ أَخْطَأْتُهَا*
_"Aye Allah mere woh Gunah ko bakhsh de jo Izzat mein batta laga dete hain, jo Nuzool e Bala ka baes hote hain, jo Nematon ko badal dete hain, jo Duaon ko darja e Maqbooliyat tak pahunchne se rok dete hain, jo Ummidon ko poora nahi hone dete, jin se Bala nazil hoti hai, jo maine kiye hon aur har us khata ko ma'af kar de jo mujh se sarzad ho gayi ho."_

Is mein hame ye bhi sabaq milta hai ke Gunah ke asaraat/effects kiya hain. Lekin banda is baat ka iqraar karta hai ke Khuda ki Hukumat se bhaag kar nikal jana na mumkin hai. Sirf aur sirf Khuda hi uski Maghferat kar sakta hai. Kiyonki woh janta hai usne apne upar zulm kiya aur apni jihalat ki wajah se itni jura'at karne laga.
*وَلا يُمْكِنُ الْفِرَارُ مِنْ حُكُومَتِكَ اللَّهُمَّ لا أَجِدُ لِذُنُوبِي غَافِراً*
*ظَلَمْتُ نَفْسِي, وَتَجَرَّأْتُ بِجَهْلِي*

Aur ye sab isliye hua ke Duniya ne usko fareb dahi se dhoke mein rakha, uske Nafs ki Khayanat aur tal matol ne dhoka diya.
*وَخَدَعَتْنِي الدُّنْيَا بِغُرُورِهَا وَنَفْسِي بِجِنَايَتِهَا وَمِطَاِلي*

Phir Akhir mein ham Dua karte hai ke is Raat mein khas kar is waqt:

*كُلَّ جُرْمٍ أَجْرَمْتُهُ، وَكُلَّ ذَنْبٍ أَذْنَبْتُهُ، وَكُلَّ قَبِيحٍ أَسْرَرْتُهُ، وَكُلَّ جَهْلٍ عَمِلْتُهُ، كَتَمْتُهُ أَوْ أَعْلَنتُهُ، أَخفَيْتُهُ أَوْ أَظْهَرْتُهُ، وَكُلَّ سَيِّئَةٍ أَمَرْتَ بِإِثْبَاتِهَا الْكِرَامَ الكَاتِبِينَ، الَّذِينَ وَكَّلْتَهُم بِحِفْظِ مَا يَكُونُ مِنِّي*
_"Mere har ek woh jurm jo mujh se ho gaya ho bakhsh de, aur har woh Gunah jo mujh se sarzad ho gaya maaf kar de, aur har woh burai jo meine chhupa ka ki ho, aur har jihalat jisko mein amal mein laya hun, jisko meine chhupaya ho ya zahir kiya ho, ya poshida iska irtikab kiya ho ya khul kar aur har aisi badi jiske inderaj ka Tu ne Kiraman Katibeen ko Hukm diya ho...."_
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v7)
👏🏻🙌🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah ke bare mein ye Bande ka dhoka hai ke Insaan lagatar gunah karta rahe aur is se Maghferat ki ummeed bhi rakkhe."_
(Sharh Dua e Kumail)

          ♦ _*KHAYANAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (567)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تُجَادِلْ عَنِ الَّذِينَ يَخْتَانُونَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ مَنْ كَانَ خَوَّانًا أَثِيمًا*

_"Aur jo log apne Nafs se Khayanat karte hain unki taraf se jhagadne wale mat bano. Allah ko Khayanatkar aur Ma'asiyatkar Shakhs pasand nahi hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 107)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😏
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Logo'n ki Amaanat rakhne se Rozi aati hai aur amaanat mein Khayaanat karne se Faqeeri aati hai."_
(Tuhaful Uqool)
😏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo shakhs hum logo'n ki Muhabbat ki thandak apne dil mein mehsoos kare use chahiye ke wo apni Maa ko bahut bahut Duaein de is liye ke usne uske Baap ki Amaanat mein khayaanat nahi ki."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p108)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*10th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 10th March 2017, Friday,

            ♦ _*KHAYANAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (568) 🤓😎

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَا تُجَادِلْ عَنِ الَّذِينَ يَخْتَانُونَ أَنْفُسَهُمْ ۚ إِنَّ اللَّهَ لَا يُحِبُّ مَنْ كَانَ خَوَّانًا أَثِيمًا * يَسْتَخْفُونَ مِنَ النَّاسِ وَلَا يَسْتَخْفُونَ مِنَ اللَّهِ وَهُوَ مَعَهُمْ إِذْ يُبَيِّتُونَ مَا لَا يَرْضَىٰ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ بِمَا يَعْمَلُونَ مُحِيطًا * هَا أَنْتُمْ هَٰؤُلَاءِ جَادَلْتُمْ عَنْهُمْ فِي الْحَيَاةِ الدُّنْيَا فَمَنْ يُجَادِلُ اللَّهَ عَنْهُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ أَمْ مَنْ يَكُونُ عَلَيْهِمْ وَكِيلًا*

_"Aur jo log apne Nafs se Khayanat karte hain unki taraf se jhagadne wale mat bano. Allah ko Khayanatkar aur Ma'asiyatkar Shakhs pasand nahi hain."_
_"Ye log Insaano se to apni harkaton ko chhupate hain magar woh Khuda se nahi chhupa sakte. Woh to us waqt bhi unke sath hota hai jab ye Raaton ko chhup kar Uski Marzi ke khilaf mashware karte hain. Khuda unke tamam Aamaal ka ahata kiye hue hai."_
_"Haan tumne in Mujrimon ki taraf se Duniya ki Zindagi mein to jhagda kar liya magar Qayamat ke Din unke liye Allah se kaun jhagda karega aur haan unka Vakil aur Tarafdar kaun banega?"_
(Surah Nisa: 107)

📚📖 🤓😎
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayaat Khayanat (Be-imaani) karne walon ke bare mein hai jinhone apne Nafs par zulm kiya. Dhiyan rahe ke is Duniya ke tamam afraad ek Jism ki tarah hain. Agar aap kisi ke sath bura kar rahe hain, yaani ke apne aap par bura kar rahe hain. Ek Shakhs apne hath se apne mooh par thapad marta hai, iska asar poore jism par hoga. Jurm Karnewala ye samjhta hai ke use koi dekh nahi raha. Agar usko maloom ho jaye ke Khuda dekh raha hai to woh ye jurm hi na kare. Isliye Gunah karna yaani Khuda ki Sifat Muheet, Aleem, Baseer ka inkaar karna hai. Khuda unki bhi mazammat karta hai jo in logon ki himayat karte hain.
Haqeeqat mein ye 3 Ayaten pahle to Paighambar e Islam (saww) aur sabhi Qaziyon ko Haq ki Wasiyyat ki gayi hai ke woh mukammal taur par nigrani aur dhiyan rakhen ke kuchh log hila sazi aur jhoote gawahon ke zariye doosron ke Huqooq ko pa'maal na karen phir Khayanat Karnewalon aur baad mein unka difa Karnewalo ko tanbih ki gayi hai ke woh is Jahan aur doosre Jahan mein Aamaal ke bure nataij par nazar rakhen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😎🤓💰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Logo'n ki Amaanat rakhne se Rozi aati hai aur Amaanat mein Khayanat karne se Faqeeri aati hai."_
(Tuhaful Uqool)
🤓😎
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Munafiq ki 3 nishaniyaa'n hain:_
_(1) Jab baat karta hai to jhoot bolta hai,_
_(2) Jab Waada karta hai to Waada khilaafi karta hai,_
_(3) Jab Amaanat rakhi jati hai to Khayanat karta hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p188)
😎🤓😏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"3 logo'n se daro:_
_(1) Khaain (khayaanat-karne wala),_
_(2) Zaalim,_
_(3) Chugal-khor._
_Isliye ke Khayanat karne wala agar aaj tumhare faayde ke liye Khayanat (be-Imaani) kar raha hai to kal tumhare (nuqsaan ke liye) Khayanat karega. Aur jo aaj tumhari khaatir  zulm kar rah hai, kal tum par hi zulm karega. Aur jo tumse doosro'n ki chugli khaata hai, wo doosro'n se tumhari chugli khayega."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*11th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 11th March 2017, Saturday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
       ♦ _*TOHMAT (BLAME)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (569) 😲👉

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ سُوءًا أَوْ يَظْلِمْ نَفْسَهُ ثُمَّ يَسْتَغْفِرِ اللَّهَ يَجِدِ اللَّهَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا * وَمَنْ يَكْسِبْ إِثْمًا فَإِنَّمَا يَكْسِبُهُ عَلَىٰ نَفْسِهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا * وَمَنْ يَكْسِبْ خَطِيئَةً أَوْ إِثْمًا ثُمَّ يَرْمِ بِهِ بَرِيئًا فَقَدِ احْتَمَلَ بُهْتَانًا وَإِثْمًا مُبِينًا*
[Surat An-Nisa' 110 - 112]

_"Jo bhi Bura Amal kare ya apne Nafs par zulm kare uske baad Allah se Maghferat talab kare to woh Allah ko Maghferat Karnewala Meherban payega."_
_"Jo bhi Burai Kamai to woh Kamai uske liye wabal sabit hogi aur Allah Sahib e Ilm aur Sahib e Hikmat hai."_
_"Phir jisne koi Khata ya Gunah kare uska ilzam kisi be Gunah par thop diya to usne bade Bohtan aur sarih (clear) Gunah ka bar samet liya"_
(Surah Nisa: 110 - 112)

📚📖 😲👉
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Insaan bahut se illat o asbaab (Factors) ke tahet Gunah kar baithta hai. Chunke ye Gunah anjane mein ho gaye, to jab woh pasheman hota to woh Allah ko Ghafoor, Rahim pata hai.
Lekin jurm to jurm hai, insaan jab Gunah ka irtekab karta hai to iska asar doosron par to padta hi hai, khud bhi usse asar andaz hota hai. Jaise ye rivayat mulaheza ho:
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi ek luqma Haraam khayega uski 40 raato'n tak Namaz qubool nahi hogi aur 40 subah tak Dua mustajaab nahi hogi.”_
(Noori - Dar as Salaam, p213) (The Prayer)
Isliye bhale woh apne Gunah ki baad mein tauba kar le lekin asar se nahi Bach sakta.
Lekin ek shakhs khud ghalti kare phir usko kisi be Gunah par Tohmat lagai yani woh doosron par teer chala raha hai. Shikar ghayal ya qatl to ho jayega lekin uska Gunah uske sar par hoga. Woh shakhs uske qatil ke manind hoga. Is shakhs ki bakhshish nahi hai.
Isliye insaan ko chahiye ke in sab baton se bache.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😲👉
Imam Sadiq (as):
*البهتان على البرئ اثقل من جبال راسيات.*
_"Begunah par Bohtan bandhna Azeem pahad se bhi zyada sangin hai."_
(Safinatul Bihar, Vol 1, بهت)
😲👉
Imam Sadiq (as):
*اذا اتهم المؤمن اخاه انماث الايمان كما ينماث الملح فى الماء.*
_"Jo shakhs apne Momin bhai par Tohmat lagata hai to Imaan uske dil mein is tarah ghul jata hai jis tarah Namak pani mein ghul jata hai."_
(Usool e Kafi, Vol 2, P-269 باب التهمة و سوء الظن)
😲👉
Paighambar e Islam (saww):
_"Jo Shakhs kisi Momin Mard ya Aurat par Bohtan (blame) bandhe ya unke bare mein koi aisi baat kahe jo un mein na ho to Khuda Wande Alam use Qayamat ke Din Aag ke ek teele par khada kar dega. Yahan tak ke woh is baat se bariuz zimmah ho jaye jo usne kahi hain."_
(Safinatul Bihar, Vol 1, P-111)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*12th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 12th March 2017, Sunday,

     (Madare Hazrate Abbas (as)

       ♦ _*ISMAT E ANBIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (570) 🔄

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَوْلَا فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكَ وَرَحْمَتُهُ لَهَمَّتْ طَائِفَةٌ مِنْهُمْ أَنْ يُضِلُّوكَ وَمَا يُضِلُّونَ إِلَّا أَنْفُسَهُمْ ۖ وَمَا يَضُرُّونَكَ مِنْ شَيْءٍ ۚ وَأَنْزَلَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْكَ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَعَلَّمَكَ مَا لَمْ تَكُنْ تَعْلَمُ ۚ وَكَانَ فَضْلُ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكَ عَظِيمًا*

_"Agar Aap (saww) par Khuda ka Fazl aur Rehmat na hoti to unki ek Jamat ne Aapko (saww) bahkane ka iraada kar hi liya tha halanke woh apne siwa kisi aur ko ghalat fahmi mein nahi dal rahe the aur woh tumhe kuchh bhi nuqsan na pahuncha sakte the. Allah ne Aap (saww) par Kitab o Hikmat nazil ki aur Aap  (saww) ko un tamam baton ka ilm diya jinhe Aap (saww) nahi Jaante the aur Aap (saww) par Khuda ka bahut bada Fazl hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 113)

📚📖 🔄
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ka talluq Anbiya wa Aimma (as) ki Ismat se hai. Hamara Rehbar jab tak Masoom na ho wo hamari Rahbari nahi kar sakta. Kiyonki woh hamara Life Model hota hai. Kiyonki agar woh ghalti ya khata ya mistake kare to ham sahi aur ghalat mein confused ho jayenge. Gunah ki to door ki baat hai. Islami Rahbar paidaish se maut tak Masoom hota hai.
Ye Khuda ka Lutf o Karam hai ke Allah ne unko har shar se mehfooz rakha.  Nabi ya Imam ka Masoom hona ye koi Karamat nahi aur na hi majboor hain. Is Ayat ke mutabiq Allah ne unhe aisa Ilm o Hikmat diya hai jiski wajah se woh apne ikhtiyar se kisi bhi shar se door rahte hain. Misal ke taur par ek Doctor kabhi bhi germs alooda (dirty) paani nahi piyega. Doctor hone ki wajah se woh khud apne ikhtiyar wa knowledge ke mutabiq ehtiyat bartega.
Anbiya wa Aimma (as) ko Allah ki taraf se bhi Rehmat o Fazl rahta hai. Rivayat ke mutabiq Allah ne unki hifazat ke liye ek khas Farishta muayyan kiya hai jisko Roohul Quds kahte hain. 🔄
Imam Reza (as):
_"Allah ne hamko Roohul Quds se support kiya jo ke Farishta nahi hai aur woh kisi Nabi ke pas nahi tha siwae Rasool e Khuda (saww) aur Aimma (as), woh Aimma (as) ki madad karte hain aur woh Allah aur hamare darmiyan Noori Sutoon (pillar) hain."_
(Uyoonul Akhbar Ar Reza)
🔄
Abu Basir ne Abu Abdullah (Imam Sadiq) (as) se is Ayat ke bare mein sawal kiya:
*وَكَذَٰلِكَ أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَيْكَ رُوحًا مِنْ أَمْرِنَا ۚ*
[Surah Shura 52]
Imam (as) ne farmaya:
_"Is Ayat mein Rooh (Roohul Quds) se murad ek Khuda ki Makhlooq hai, jo Jibrael o Mikail se zyada Nemat yafta wa Aala hai, jo Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke pas rahti thi jo unhe inform aur guide karti rahti thi, aur unke baad woh Aimma (as) ke sath rahti hai."_
(Al Kaafi)
🔄
Imam Sadiq (as)
ke saamne Raavi ne Quran ki ye Ayat padhi _'Aur tum par jo bhi musibat aati hai wo tumhari apni paida ki huwi hoti hai'_ (Surah Shura: 30) aur Imam (as) se farmaya:
"Is Ayat ko madde nazar rakh kar jawab de'n ke Hazrat Ali (as) aur unke Khandan par masaaib ke pahad kyun toote the jab ke wo to Masoom the?"
Imam (as) ne farmaya: _"Rasule Khuda (saww) Masoom (be-gunah / infallible) the, uske bawajood Aap (saww) rozana 100 baar Astagfaar kiya karte the. Allah Apne Auliya par masaaib naazil karta hai taaki unhe un masaaib ka ajr (reward) ataa kiya jaaye."_
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v7, p510)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Koi shakhs hamare baare mein sheyr ka ek bait (stanza) kahta hi nahi jab tak use Roohul Quds ke zariye taaid (madad) haasil nahi hoti."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v5)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*13th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 13th March 2017, Monday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

♦ _*RAATON KA SAHI ISTEMAL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (571) 🌃🌌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا خَيْرَ فِي كَثِيرٍ مِنْ نَجْوَاهُمْ إِلَّا مَنْ أَمَرَ بِصَدَقَةٍ أَوْ مَعْرُوفٍ أَوْ إِصْلَاحٍ بَيْنَ النَّاسِ ۚ وَمَنْ يَفْعَلْ ذَٰلِكَ ابْتِغَاءَ مَرْضَاتِ اللَّهِ فَسَوْفَ نُؤْتِيهِ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*
_"Logon ki Khufiya Sargoshiyon (Secret Meetings) mein aksar wa beshtar koi bhalai nahi hoti. Magar jo koi poshida (secretly) taur par Sadaqa wa Khairat aur logon ke darmiyan Islah ki talqeen kare to ye achhi baat hai aur jo koi Allah ki Raza joi ke liye aisa kaam karega to Ham use Bada Ajr ata karenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 114)

📚📖 🌃🌌
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein hamari Raaton ka zikr hai, ke ye Raaten ham kaise guzarten hai. Waise Allah ne Raat Insaan ki rahat ke liye banayi hai jaisa ke doosri Ayat mein zikr hai. Lekin sabhi khufiya (secret) kaam Raaton mein kiye jaate hain. Shaitan sifat log Raaton mein Secret Meetings karte hain aur apne ghalat karnamo ki planning karte hain. No.2 kaamon ki planning bhi raaton ko hoti hai. Chor uchakke ki bhi Raaton mein nikal padte hain.
Allah ne inki mazammat karte hue farmata hai ke kiyon apni Raaten zaya kar rahe ho. In Raaton ka sahi masraf karo jisse Deen o Duniya mein fayda ho. Jo Best Kaam yahan bataya hai woh hai Khufiya Sadaqa wa Khairat aur Logon ke darmiyan Islah. Hazrat Ali (as) ka woh waqea mashoor hai ke kis tarah woh Raaton ko Gharibon ki madad kiya karte ke khud lene wala unko nahi pahchan pata tha. Is tarah baqi Aimmah (as) ke bahut se aise waqeat hain jiski yahan gunjaish nahi hai.
Isliye hamari Raaten, Shabbedari Ibadaat mein guzarni chahiye. Karbala mein bhi Imam Husain (as) ne ek Raat ki muhlat Ibaadat ke liye maangi thi. Jo kaam bhi fi sabilillah kiya jaye woh Ibaadat hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤝
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Kiya tumhe aise Sadqe se aagah karun jise Khuda aur uska Rasool pasand karte hain: (Aur woh ye hai ke) jab log ek doosre ke Dushman ho jayen to un mein Sulah karo aur jab ek doosre se door ho jayen to unhe nazdeek lao."_
(Tafseer Qartabi, Vol 3, P-1955)
🤝🤝
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Guftugu (Conversation) Teen tarah ki hoti hai:_
_(1) Sach (Truth)_
_(2) Jhoot (Lie)_
_(3) Logon ke darmiyan Islah (Reconcile)_
_Islah: Tumne ek Shakhs se doosre ka shikwa suna to tumne doosre fareeq se kaha ke bhi aap to khwah makhwah us par naraaz hain. Wo to aapke mutalliq falan falan qism ki achhi baten kar raha tha aur yun jhoot maslahet aamez ka sahara le kar do afraad ke darmiyan Sulah karate ho to is amal ko "اصلاح بين الناس Islah bainan Nas" kaha jata hai."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🤝🤝
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Teen maqamat par Jhoot bolna jaez hai:_
_(1) Jang ke harbe ke taur par_
_(2) Biwi se Waade ke waqt._
_(3) Logon ke darmiyan Sulah karate waqt."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*14th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 14th March 2017, Tuesday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

♦ _*TARKE RAHE AHLE IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (572) 🛣

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ يُشَاقِقِ الرَّسُولَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا تَبَيَّنَ لَهُ الْهُدَىٰ وَيَتَّبِعْ غَيْرَ سَبِيلِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ نُوَلِّهِ مَا تَوَلَّىٰ وَنُصْلِهِ جَهَنَّمَ ۖ وَسَاءَتْ مَصِيرًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Hidayat wazeh (clear) hone ke baad Rasool (saww) ki mukhalefat kare aur Ahle Imaan ki ravish ko chhod kar Auron ki ravish par chale to jidhar woh phira hoga Ham bhi usko usi taraf pher denge aur ham use Dozakh mein jhonkenge jo bad tareen jagah qarar di gayi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 115)

📚📖 🛣
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Jab insaan ghalti ka murtakib hota hota hai to agaahi ke baad uske saamne do raaste hote hain: (1) Tauba ka raasta jisse nijat mil sakti hai (2) Hatdharmi ka raasta jiske manhoos nataij hote hain.
Is Ayat mein is doosre raaste ka zikr hai. *يُشَاقِقِ*ka  yehi meaning hai yani sochi samjhi mukhalefat.
Rasoole Khuda (saww) ne jab ke wazeh taur par logon ke darmiyan Haq ki Hidayat ki phir bhi log kisi aur raaste par chalen to ye hatdharmi nahi to kiya hai. Ghadeer ki maidan mein jab Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne apne baad sawa lakh ke majme apne Janasheen ka Ailaan kar diya, aur farmaya mein do wazni cheezen chhod kar ja raha hun ek Quran aur Ahle Bait (as), aur jinhone Quran o Ahle Bait (as) ki pairavi ki wohi Ahle Imaan hain, phir Musalmano ne Ahle Imaan ka raasta chhod doosron ke raaste par chale gaye.  Allah Ta'ala farmata hai ke unko jane do jis bhi raaste par jaye, agar unka Rehbar Jannat ya Jahannam mein jayega to woh bhi unke pairavi karenge. Allah ne Hujjat tamam kar di ab koi shikwa nahi kar sakta mujhe maloom nahi tha. Haq to Ashkaar ho gaya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛣
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaa-pan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
🛣
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Jis izzat-daar ne Haq ko chhoda wo zaleel huwa aur jis zaleel ne Haq par amal kiya wo saheb e izzat huwa."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p233)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*15th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 15th March 2017, Wednesday,

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
        ♦ _*AMAAL E KHAIR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (577) 🌟

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَيْسَ بِأَمَانِيِّكُمْ وَلَا أَمَانِيِّ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ ۗ مَنْ يَعْمَلْ سُوءًا يُجْزَ بِهِ وَلَا يَجِدْ لَهُ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَلِيًّا وَلَا نَصِيرًا * وَمَنْ يَعْمَلْ مِنَ الصَّالِحَاتِ مِنْ ذَكَرٍ أَوْ أُنْثَىٰ وَهُوَ مُؤْمِنٌ فَأُولَٰئِكَ يَدْخُلُونَ الْجَنَّةَ وَلَا يُظْلَمُونَ نَقِيرًا*

_"Na tumahari Aarzooun se kaam banega, na Ahle Kitab (Jews & Christians) ki ummeedon se kuchh hasil hoga, jo bhi bura kaam karega use usi ka badla diya jayega aur Allah ke alawa use koi Hami wa Madadgar nahi milega."_
_"Aur jo bhi Nek Amal karega, khwah Mard ho ya Aurat, basharte ke ho woh Momin ho (Shia), to aise hi log Jannat mein dakhil honge aur un par zarrah barabar bhi Haq talfi na hone payegi."_
(Surah Nisa: 123 - 124)

📚📖 🌟
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Tafseer e Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke Musalman aur Ahle Kitab ek doosre par fakhr karte the. Ahle Kitab kahte the ke hamare Nabi pahle aye, Musalman kahte the ke Hamare Nabi Khatemul Anbiya hain. Aur ham Ummat e Khair hain (3:110).
Allah ne un sab ki Aarzooun par pani pher diya. Ek doore se Muqabila karne ki zaroorat nahi, har insaan ko uske Amal ke mutabiq phal milega. Means hamare Action ke mutabiq hi result milega chahe tum Musalman kiyon na ho.
Lekin aaj ham dekhte ke Musalman apni Fazilat ke liye zyada lad raha hai. Musalmano mein 73 firqe hain aur har Firqa apne aap ko ek doosre se bartar samajhta hai. Apne alawa doosre ko Kafir hi Kafir karta rahta hai aur fakhr se kahta hain ham Jannati hain. Ji haan, Janaat kisi ki Miraas nahi. Jannat mein dakhil hone ke liye is Ayat ne do sharte rakhi hain: Pahle Momin hona, phir Nek Amal. Har Musalman Momin nahi hai. Isliye zaroori hai ke aap pahle Momin bane. Rivayat ke mutabiq jiske dil mein Ali (as) ki Vilayat hai woh Momin hai. Uske baad Amaal ki Manzil aati hai.
Hai to mushkil lekin koshish to kar sakte hain. Allah par bharosa rakhen. Woh Adil hai. Tumhari qabiliyat wa hasiyat ko woh achhi tarah Jaanta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌟
_*Sharayte Momin:*_
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaa-pan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
🌟
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali, Khuda ne mujh se ahad (waada) kiya hai ke jo tumhe dost rakhta hai wo Momin hoga aur tumhe dushman jaan-ne wala munafiq hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, Majlis 28, p133)
🌟
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Meri aur mere Ahlebait (as) ki Wilayat Jahannum se amaan ka waseela hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p232)
🌟
Riwayat:
_"Ahlebait (as) ki mawaddat ko apne liye laazim qaraar do, kyun ki jo shakhs Allah ki bargaah mein haazir hoga is haalat mein ke wo hum Ahlebait (as) se mohabbat rakhta hoga, wo hamari shafa'at ki wajah se Jannat mein zaroor daakhil hoga. Aur muhje qasam hai Oos zaat ki jiske qabza e qudrat mein meri jaan hai, hamari maarefat ke baghair kisi bande ka amal usko faayda nahi dega."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)
🌟
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)! Tumhare wo saathi jo tumhari maarefat rakhte hain unse kaho ke oon kaamo'n se parhez karein jo unke dushman karte hain. Phir koi din raat aisi nahi hogi ke Rehmat e Ilaahi unke shaamil e haal na ho. Lihaaza, oon logo'n ko buraaiyo'n se apna daaman bachaana chahiye."_
(Shiane  Ahlebait (as), p38)
🌟
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Momin wo hai jo Fitna o fasaad ke waqt qaabu mein rahe, musibat mein Sabr, khushi mein shukrguzaar, Rizq e Khuda par qaane' (contented / santushtt) ho, dushmano'n par zulm na kare, uska badan qaabu mein rahe, log oos se raahat mein rahein, Ilm uska dost aur hilm (forbearance / sahansheelta) uska vazeer ho, aql ke lashkar ka ameer ho, narmi uska bhai ho, neki uska baap ho."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p191)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*21st Jamadi us Sani 1438*
21st March 2017, Tuesday,

 ♦ _*IBRAHIM KHALILULLAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (578)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَمَنْ أَحْسَنُ دِينًا مِمَّنْ أَسْلَمَ وَجْهَهُ لِلَّهِ وَهُوَ مُحْسِنٌ وَاتَّبَعَ مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا ۗ وَاتَّخَذَ اللَّهُ إِبْرَاهِيمَ خَلِيلًا * وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ مُحِيطًا*

_"Bhala uski ravish se behtar aur kis ka Tarze Zindagi ho sakta hai jisne Khuda ke saamne sar Tasleem kham kar diya ho (Submission to God) aur apna ravayya Nek rakha aur yaksoo ho kar Ibrahim (as) ke tareeqe ki pairavi ki. Allah ne Ibrahim (as) ko apna Dost aur Khaleel banaya."_
_"Aur jo kuchh Aasmaano aur Zameen mein hai woh Khuda ki Milkiyat hai aur Allah har cheez par Ahata Rakhne Wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 125 - 126)

📚📖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Islam hamara behtareen Tarz e Zindagi hai. Yehi hamari Jeevan Shaili hai. Iske 3 wujuhat hain:
1. Total Submission to God. (Mukammal Khuda ke Huzoor mein Supurdgi)
2. Goodness (Nekokari)
3. Deen e Ibrahim (as) ko follow karna.
Khaleel خليل ke do matlab hain: Dost aur Mohtaj.
Yahan Dost ka meaning liya gaya kiyonki Khuda Mohtaj nahi, kiyonki Woh puri Khilqat ka Malik hai.
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda ne Ibrahim (as) ko agar apna Khalil aur Dost banaya hai to uski wajah ye nahi thi ke Woh unki Dosti ka Mohtaj tha balke ye is bena par tha ke Ibrahim (as) Khuda Ta'ala ke Mufeed aur Uski Raah mein koshish karne karne wale Bande the."_
(Majmaul Bayan)
🌱
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Khuda Ta'ala ne Ibrahim (as) ko apna Khalil Isliye banaya kiyonki unhone kabhi kisi sawal aur taqaza karne wale ko mehroom nahi kiya aur kabhi kisi se sawal aur taqaza nahi kiya."_
(Tafseer e Safi, Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-417, Uyoonul Akhbar Ar Raza)
🌱
Hazrat Ibrahim (as) ko ye maqam zyada Sajdah karne, bhookon ko khana khilane aur Raat ki tareeki mein Namaz padhte ya Parwardigar ki ita'at ke liye koshan rahne ki wajah se hasil hua.
Isliye hamare Rasool (saww) Be'sat ke pahle jo Deen raej tha woh Deen e Haneef (as) tha.
Rasool e Akram (saww) aur Yahoodi ke darmiyan e bahes mein Yahoodi ne kaha ke Ibrahim (as) aap se behtar the kiyonki woh Allah ke Khalil the. Aap (saww) ne jawab diya: 🌱
_"Woh Allah ke Khalil the to mein Allah ka Habib Muhammad hun"_
(Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍵🍺🍪
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Jab Farishte Insaani shakl mein Ibrahim (as) ke ghar aye to Ibrahim (as) ne Mehman Nawazi ki taur par khana nosh farmane ke liye kaha to Farishto ne kaha: Ham  us waqt nahi khayenge jab tak Aap hamen iski qeemat nahi batayenge.
Aap ne farmaya:
_" Iski qeemat ye hai ke jab khana shuru karo to us waqt 'Bismillah بسم الله' padho aur jab khana khatm karo to 'Al hamdo lillah الحمد لله' kaho."_  
Hazrat ka ye jawab sun kar Jibrael e Ameen (as) apne sathiyon ki taraf mutawajjah hue:
"Ye Shakhs is baat ka mustahaq hai ke Khuda use apna Khalil banaye."
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌹
Imam Ali Naqi (as):
_"Allah ne Ibrahim (as) ko Apna Khaleel (dost) is liye chuna kyun ki wo Muhammad (saww) aur unke Ahlebait (as) pe bahut zyada Salwaat bhejte the."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p25)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

      ♦ _*YATEEM LADKIYAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (578) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَيَسْتَفْتُونَكَ فِي النِّسَاءِ ۖ قُلِ اللَّهُ يُفْتِيكُمْ فِيهِنَّ وَمَا يُتْلَىٰ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي الْكِتَابِ فِي يَتَامَى النِّسَاءِ اللَّاتِي لَا تُؤْتُونَهُنَّ مَا كُتِبَ لَهُنَّ وَتَرْغَبُونَ أَنْ تَنْكِحُوهُنَّ وَالْمُسْتَضْعَفِينَ مِنَ الْوِلْدَانِ وَأَنْ تَقُومُوا لِلْيَتَامَىٰ بِالْقِسْطِ ۚ وَمَا تَفْعَلُوا مِنْ خَيْرٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِهِ عَلِيمًا*

_"Ye log Aap (saww) se Yateem ladkiyon ke mutalliq Hukm-e-Ilahi poochhte hain. Aap kah den ke Allah tumhe unke mamle mein Fatwa deta hai aur sath hi apne woh Ahkam jinka talluq Yateem ladkiyon se hai, jinke Haq tum ada nahi karte aur jin ke Nikah karne se tum baaz rahte ho (ya lalach ki bena par tum khud unse Nikah kar lena chahte ho).  Woh Ahkam un bachchon ke mutalliq hain jo bechare koi zor nahi rakhte. Allah tumhe Hidayat karta hai ke Yateemon ke sath Insaaf ke sulook par qaem raho aur jo bhi tum bhalai karoge to Allah usko bakhoobi Jannewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 127)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yateem Ladkiyon ke haq ke bare mein pahle bhi zikr kar chuke hain aur jis Ahkam ke bare mein sawal hua hai uska jawab bhi pichhli Ayaton mein aa chuka hai.
Yateem ki jo parwarish karta hai woh use uske Maal se mehroom rakhta hai, unki shaadi nahi karta, ya Maal ki lalach mein shaadi kar leta hai unki mazammat ki hai. Khuda sab ko dekhta rahta hai kaun kis ke sath kaisa sulook karta hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jannat mein ek ghar hai jiska naam 'Daar ul Farah' (Khushi ka ghar) hai. Usme sirf wohi shakhs jayega jo Momeneen ke Yateem bachcho'n ko khush karta hoga."_
(Meezan ul Hikmah, v4, p739)
🕌
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne apne Nabi (saww) ko Yateem is liye banaya taaki unpar kisi ki Ita'at (Obedience) farz na rahe."_
(Elal ush Sharaaye, p99)
🕌
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Baghair Maa-Baap ke Yateem se bada Yateem wo hai jo apne Imam-e-Zamana (atfs) tak na pahunch sake aur Ahkam-e-Deen (rules of religion) aur Wazaaif-e-Ilaahi ke jaan'ne mein hairaan o pareshaan ho. (Hamari Ummat ke Ulema mein se) jo unki hidayat aur taalim o tarbiyat kare, wo roz e Qayamat hamare saath mehshoor honge aur ek khaas buland darje ke maalik honge."_
(Ehtejaaj e Tabrisi, v1, p15)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*23rd Jamadi us Sani 1438, 23rd March 2017, Thursday,

               ♦ _*SULAAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (579) 👰🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنِ امْرَأَةٌ خَافَتْ مِنْ بَعْلِهَا نُشُوزًا أَوْ إِعْرَاضًا فَلَا جُنَاحَ عَلَيْهِمَا أَنْ يُصْلِحَا بَيْنَهُمَا صُلْحًا ۚ وَالصُّلْحُ خَيْرٌ ۗ وَأُحْضِرَتِ الْأَنْفُسُ الشُّحَّ ۚ وَإِنْ تُحْسِنُوا وَتَتَّقُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرًا*

_"Agar kisi Aurat ko apne Shauhar se bad sulooki ya be rukhi ka khatra ho to koi harj nahi Miya Biwi (kuchh Huqooq ki kami beshi par) apas mein SULAH kar len. SULAH beher haal behtar hai. Nafs tang dili ki taraf jald mael ho jate hain lekin agar tum ehsaan se pesh aao aur Khaufe Khuda se kaam lo (Taqwa) to Khuda tumhare Aamaal se Bakhabar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 128)

📚📖 👰🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ki wazahat Imam ne is tarah ki:
👰🏻
Imam Reza (as):
_"Nushuz *نشوز* se ye murad hai ke Shauhar apni Biwi ko Talaq dene ka iraada kare to Aurat us se kahe ke 'mein Haq e Mehr ka bojh teri pusht se kam karti hun aur tujhe itna Maal deti hun aur mein kuchh din teri doosri Biwi ke liye teri wajah se Halal karti hun', agar woh apas mein kuchh le de kar Musalehat kar len to jaez hai."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
👰🏻
Imam Moosa Kazim (as):
_"Jab kubhi Miya Biwi mein nachaaqi waqe ho jae aur Shauhar apni Biwi ko Talaq dene ka iraada kare to Biwi us se ye kahe ke 'mujhe apne paas rahne de, mein apne kuchh Huqooq tumhe ma'af karti hun aur kuchh din doosri Biwi ke liye bhi Halal karti hun. ......"_
(Al Kaafi)
👰🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Is Ayat ka maqsad ye hai ke agar koi Mard apni Biwi ko Talaq par majboor kare. Aur Aurat ye kahe ke mujhe logon ki nafrat ka nishana na banao, tum mujhe Talaq mat do. Albatta meri hisse ki raat tum jise dena chaho de do aur mujhe meri haalat par rahne do...."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Agar 2 Momenin (Miya Biwi) 3 din se zyada ek doosre se naraaz ho'n to main un dono se bezaar hoo'n. Aap se puchha gaya, "Yabn Rasulallah! Agar che wo shakhs (Shauhar) zaalim hi kyun na ho aur mazloom ka kya gunah hoga?"_
Aap (as) ne farmaya, _"Mazloom (Biwi) zaalim ke paas jaa-kar Sulah kyun nahi karti taake unke darmiyaan nafrat khatm ho?"_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p229)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*25th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 25th March 2017, Saturday,

*SHAHADAT IMAN ALI NAQI (as)*

♦ _*BIWIYON KE DARMIYAN ADL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (580) 👰🏻👰🏼

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلَنْ تَسْتَطِيعُوا أَنْ تَعْدِلُوا بَيْنَ النِّسَاءِ وَلَوْ حَرَصْتُمْ ۖ فَلَا تَمِيلُوا كُلَّ الْمَيْلِ فَتَذَرُوهَا كَالْمُعَلَّقَةِ ۚ وَإِنْ تُصْلِحُوا وَتَتَّقُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا * وَإِنْ يَتَفَرَّقَا يُغْنِ اللَّهُ كُلًّا مِنْ سَعَتِهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ وَاسِعًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Tum Biwiyon ke darmiyan Adl ke mukammal taqaze hargiz pura na kar sakoge lehaza aisa na ho ke tum ek Biwi ki taraf mukammal taur par jhuk jao aur doosri ko latakta hua chhod do. Agar tum durust tarze amal apnao aur Khuda se darte raho (Taqwa) to Allah Bakhshne wala Meherban hai."_
_"Agar dono alag hona chahen to Khuda ko apne Khazane ki wus'at se Ghani aur Beniyaz bana dega. Allah Saheb e Wus'at aur Saheb e Hikmat hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 129 - 130)

📚📖 👰🏻👰🏼
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein is baat ka zikr tha ke agar Shauhar do Biwiyan rakhta hai aur ek se zyada Muhabbat rakhne ki wajah se apni pahli Biwi ko Talaq dene par amada ho jata hai to isko rokne ke liye Biwi ki taraf se Sulah ki tajweez pesh ki gayi thi.
Is Ayat mein Allah is baat ko madde nazar rakhte hue Mard ko bata raha hai ke tum sab Biwiyon se barabar Muhabbat nahi kar sakte. Biwiyon ke darmiyan Adalat zaroori hai.
Mashoor Dahariya (Atheist) Ibne Abil Awja ne Hisham bin Hakam (Student of Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya:
"Allah ne Ayat (Nisa:3) mein mein bataya Biwiyon ke darmiyan Adl zaroori hai, jabke (Nisa:129) mein farma raha hai ke ye mumkin nahi hai. Ye tazad (contradiction) kiyon?
Hisham jawab nahi de paye to Imam (as) se ruju kiya.
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya:
_" Pahli Ayat mein Allah ne ye farmaya ke agar tum Adl na kar sakoge to phir ek hi Biwi par qana't karo. Usse nan o nafqa (Biwi ka kharch) ka Adl murad hai aur doosri Ayat mein Allah Ta'ala ne jo ye farmaya hai ke tum Biwiyon ke darmiyan Adl qaem na kar sakoge, lehaza kisi ek Biwi ki taraf mukammal taur par na jhuko ke doosri Biwi muallaqa nazar aye. Isse Muaddat (Muhabbat) murad hai. Yaani Allah ne farmaya ke tum Biwiyon ko barabar ki Muhabbat hargiz na de sakoge."_
(Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-420, Noorus Saqlain, Tafseer e Namoona)
Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya ke "Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Biwiyon ke liye apni Raaten taqseem ki thi jabke Aap (saww) bimar hote to bhi Aap Biwiyon ki bari ka khayal rakhte."
Hazrat Ali (as) ki do Biwiyan thi. Aap (as) bari ka khusoosi khayal rakhte the aur jiski bari na hoti thi uske ghar mein Wuzu bhi nahi karte the.
(Noorus Saqlain)
Chunke log in baaton ka khayal kam rakhte hain jiske natije mein ghar ka mahaul bigadta hai aur sukoon khatm ho jata hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👰🏻👰🏼
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah farmata hai, "Pus jaan lo ke Allah koi amal qubool na karega jab tak qaum Adl (insaaf / justice) ke qaail na hongi"._
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p110)
👰🏻👰🏼
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo bhi Aurat apne Shauhar ko apni zabaan se aziyyat de / dukh pahunchaye …wo Jahannum mein dakhil hone walo'n mein pehli hogi; aur isi tarah wo aadmi jo apni Biwi ke saath na-insaafi kare."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v103, p224) (Family Life Of Islam)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*26th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 26th March 2017, Sunday,

♦ _*ALLAH: SARI KAINAT KA MALIK*_♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (581) 🌏

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَلَقَدْ وَصَّيْنَا الَّذِينَ أُوتُوا الْكِتَابَ مِنْ قَبْلِكُمْ وَإِيَّاكُمْ أَنِ اتَّقُوا اللَّهَ ۚ وَإِنْ تَكْفُرُوا فَإِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَنِيًّا حَمِيدًا * وَلِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلًا * إِنْ يَشَأْ يُذْهِبْكُمْ أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ وَيَأْتِ بِآخَرِينَ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلَىٰ ذَٰلِكَ قَدِيرًا*

_"Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Allah ki Milkiyyat hain. Ham ne tum se pahle Ahle Kitab ko aur ab tum ko ye Wasiyyat ki hai ke Allah se Darte raho (Taqwa). Aur agar tum ne Kufr ka ravayya ikhtiyar kiya to yaad rakho ke Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Khuda ki Milkiyyat hain. Woh Beniyaz aur har Ta'reef ke qabil hai."_
_"Aur Aasmaano aur Zameen ki tamam Ashya Khuda ki Milkiyyat hain aur bataure Karsaaz Khuda Kafi hai."_
_"Agar Chahe to tum logon ko Zameen se hata kar tumhari jagah doosron ko le aaye aur Allah isi par Qadir hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 131 - 133)

📚📖 🌏
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Poori Kainat ka Maalik Allah hai. Shuru se akhir tak Allah ne ek advice di ke Allah se daro means Taqwa o Parhezgari ikhtiyar karo. Jo zaat aise Lamutanahi hai (Unlimited) aur be payan Qudrat rakhti hai woh apne Bando ko Beniyaz karne se Aajiz nahi ho sakti. Taqwa ikhtiyar karna hamare liye fayde mand hai aur Khuda ko iski zaroorat nahi. Khuda ki nafarmani se khud insaan ko hi nuqsaan hoga. Allah ki Milkiyyat ka takraar is baat ki ahmiyat ko bata raha hai ki itni Azeem Zaat ki nafarmani karoge to tumhara kiya hashr hoga. Is liye zaroori hai ke ham Gunahon se parhez karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍂
Imam Askari (as):
_"Taqwa e Ilahi ikhtiyaar karo aur (hamare liye) baais e zeenat bano, baais e buraayi na bano."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p243)
🍃
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda ka matlab rona aur aa'nsu bahana nahi hai, kyun ki jab Taqwa na ho jo usay gunaho'n se roke, ye khauf jhoota hai."_
(Uddatud Daee, ch4)
🌿
Imam Ali (as):
Yaqeenan aksar log 2 khoobiyo'n ki wajah se Jannat mein daakhil honge aur wo 2 khoobiyaa'n hain: Taqwa aur Husn e Khulq."_
(good manners)
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p35)
☘
Rasule Khuda (saww)
se puchha gaya, _"Ya Rasulallah! Islam kya hai? Uski khususiyat bayaan farmayein"._
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Islam uryiaa'n hai yaani baghair libaas hai uska libaas Taqwa hai, uski zeenat Hayaa aur Parhezgaari uska maalik aur uska kamaal hai. Uska phal (fruit) nek aamal hain aur har cheez ki ek buniyaad hai aur Islam ki buniyaad hum Ahlebait (as) ki mohabbat hai"._
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p221)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*27th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 27th March 2017, Monday,

                 ♦ _*DUNIYA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (582) 🌏

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَنْ كَانَ يُرِيدُ ثَوَابَ الدُّنْيَا فَعِنْدَ اللَّهِ ثَوَابُ الدُّنْيَا وَالْآخِرَةِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ سَمِيعًا بَصِيرًا*

_"Jo Shakhs Duniyavi badla ka khwahish mand ho to use maloom hona chahiye ke Allah ke paas Duniya ka Sawab bhi aur Akherat ka Sawab bhi hai aur Allah Sunnewala aur Dekhnewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 134)

📚📖 🌏 _*Tafseer:*_
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌏
*Q: Duniya ko Duniya kiyon kahte hai?*
Amirul Momenin Ali (as) ne ek Yahoodi sawal ka Jawab diya:
_"Ye lafz ' *دنو*' se derived hai jiske maani hain 'Qareeb' aur chunke Duniya qareeb hai isi liye use Duniya kaha jata hai jabke Aamaal ki jaza wa saza ka Din takhir se aata hai isi liye is Din ko 'Yaum e Akherat *يوم آخرت*' kaha jata hai."_
(Ilalus Sharai, Noorus Saqlain)
🌏
Rasoole Akram (as):
_"Ye lafz ' *دناءت*' se derived (mushtaq) hai aur Duniya ka ghar chunke intihai ghatiya hai, isi liye isko 'Duniya' kaha jata hai. Agar Duniya ko Akherat ke sath paida kiya jata to Ahle Duniya bhi Ahle Akherat ki tarah se fana hote. ' *آخرت*' ki wajah tasmiyyah ye hai ke woh Duniya ke baad takhir se qaem hogi. Iske saalon ki kaifiyat bayan nahi ki ja sakti aur iske dino ko shumar nahi kiya ja sakta aur Ahle Akherat par Maut taari na hogi."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌏
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Duniya baik waqt 'Talib' bhi hai, 'Matloob' bhi hai. Jo Duniya ko Talab karta hai to Maut us Talibe Duniya ko Talab karti hai, yahan tak ke use Duniya se bahar nikal leti hai aur jo Akherat ko talab karta hai to Duniya bhi use talab karti hai aur woh Duniya mein rah kar apne hisse ka rizq khata hai."_
(Man La Yahzarul Faqih, Chap Nawadir)
🌏
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Jo Shakhs apne dil ko Duniya se lagayega to us ke evaz woh 3 baaton mein mubtela ho jayega:_
_(1) Kabhi na khatam hone._
_(2) Poori na hone wali Aarzoo._
_(3) Kabhi hasil na hone wali khwahish."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------
*28th Jamadi us Sani 1438, 28th March 2017, Tuesday,

               ♦ _*ADAALAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (583) ⚖

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا كُونُوا قَوَّامِينَ بِالْقِسْطِ شُهَدَاءَ لِلَّهِ وَلَوْ عَلَىٰ أَنْفُسِكُمْ أَوِ الْوَالِدَيْنِ وَالْأَقْرَبِينَ ۚ إِنْ يَكُنْ غَنِيًّا أَوْ فَقِيرًا فَاللَّهُ أَوْلَىٰ بِهِمَا ۖ فَلَا تَتَّبِعُوا الْهَوَىٰ أَنْ تَعْدِلُوا ۚ وَإِنْ تَلْوُوا أَوْ تُعْرِضُوا فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ بِمَا تَعْمَلُونَ خَبِيرًا*

_"Aye Imaan Walo! Insaaf ke Alambardar bano. Allah ke liye Gawah bano agarche tumhare Gawahi khud tumhare liye ya tumhare Waledain ke liye ya tumhare Rishtedaron ke liye nuqsan deh hi kiyon na ho. Fareeq e Maamla khwah Maldaar ho ya Ghareeb, Allah tum se zyada unka Khairkhwah hai. Lehaza Khwaheshat ki pairavi na karo taake Insaaf kar sakoge. Agar tum ne lagi lipti baat kahi ya Sachchai se pahlu bachaya to jaan lo ke tumhare Aamaal ki Allah ko sab Khabar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 135)

📚📖 ⚖
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Agar aap Allah ko Haazir o Naazir jaante hain to Allah ka hukm hai ke Insaaf qaem karo. Adaalat ke maamle mein yahan apno ki paasdari se door rahne ki nasihat ki gayi hai. Agar Adaalat mein tarafdari barti gayi to Insaaf barqaraar nahi rakha ja sakta. Hazrat Ali (as) ne Adaalat ki bahut si misalen pesh ki: Jaise do Auraten is baat par lad rahi thi ke ye bachha unka hai. Ali (as) ne faisla sunaya ke bachche ko kaat kar adha adha dono de diya jaye. Ek Aurat ne kaha ke bachcha doosri Aurat ko de diya jaye lekin kaata na jaye. Ali (as) ne farmaya ke yehi iski Maa hai. Is tarah ke bahut waqeat kitabo mein darj hain refer karen.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚖
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Qayamat ke Din 3 qism ke afraad tamam makhlooq mein se Khuda ke zyada qareeb honge yahan tak ke Allah Hisaab se farigh ho jaye.: Woh Shakhs hai jo:_
_(1) Qudrat rakhte hue bhi apne se kamzor par zulm na kare._
_(2) Do Afraad ke darmiyan chale magar woh kisi ek ki taraf joo barabar bhi mael (incline) na ho._
_(3) Har haal mein Haq baat kahe khwah usse uska fayda hota ya nuqsan._"
(Kitabul Khisaal)
⚖
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jhooti gawaahi dene wala Dozakh ke alawa kahi'n aur nahi jayega."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Sadooq, p450)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*29th Jamadi us Sani 1438*
29th March 2017, Wednesday,

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
               ♦ _*IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (584) 💐

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا آمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرَسُولِهِ وَالْكِتَابِ الَّذِي نَزَّلَ عَلَىٰ رَسُولِهِ وَالْكِتَابِ الَّذِي أَنْزَلَ مِنْ قَبْلُ ۚ وَمَنْ يَكْفُرْ بِاللَّهِ وَمَلَائِكَتِهِ وَكُتُبِهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ فَقَدْ ضَلَّ ضَلَالًا بَعِيدًا*

_"Aye Imaan walo! (Waqai) Imaan le aao Khuda par, Uske Paighambar par, Uski Kitab par jo us par nazil hui aur un (Aasmani) Kutub par jo isse pahle bheji gayi hain aur jo Shakhs Khuda, Uske Malaeka (Angels), Uski Kutub, Uske Rusul aur Roze Akherat ka inkar kare woh bahut door ki Gumrahi mein mubtela hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 136)

📚📖  _*Tafseer:*_
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍀
Imam Ali (as):
_"Imaan zabaan se iqraar aur dil se maarefat aur aa'za se amal karne ke majmu'e ka naam hai."_
(Uyoon Akhbaar ar Reza, v2, p77)
🌻
Imam Reza (as):
_"Imaan Islam se ek darja afzal hai, aur TAQWA Imaan se, aur YAQEEN Imaan se, aur Adam ki Aulad ko Yaqeen se afzal koi cheez nahi di gayi."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar v78, p338)
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
🌼
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Imaan ke hote huwe koi amal nuqsaan nahi pahu'nchata aur kufr ke hote huwe koi amal fayda nahi pahu'nchata."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p82)
🌺
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Ali (as) ki mohabbat Imaan hai aur Ali (as) ka bugz kufr hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p123)
🌷
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Kisi shakhs ke dil mein Imaan us waqt tak daakhil nahi ho sakta jab tak wo mere Ahlebait (as) ke saath Allah aur uske Rasul (saww) ki khaatir mohabbat na rakhta ho."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Toosi, v1, p133)
🌹
*Imam Mohd Baqir (as):*
_"Jo shakhs har *Jumeraat* ko apne Naakhun kaate to uski Aulad ki bhi aa'nkh nahi aayegi (even his children will not suffer from eye pain / conjunctivitis)."_
(Wasaail ush Shia, v5, p 61)

              ♦ _*MURTAD*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (585)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا ثُمَّ كَفَرُوا ثُمَّ آمَنُوا ثُمَّ كَفَرُوا ثُمَّ ازْدَادُوا كُفْرًا لَمْ يَكُنِ اللَّهُ لِيَغْفِرَ لَهُمْ وَلَا لِيَهْدِيَهُمْ سَبِيلًا * بَشِّرِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*

_"Yaqeenan woh log jo Imaan laye phir Kufr ikhtiyar kiys, phir Imaan laye, phir Khufr ikhtiyar kiya, phir Kufr mein badhte chale gaye, to Allah unko hargiz Ma'af mahi karega aur na kabhi unko seedhi raah dikhayega. Aap Munafeqeen ko dardnak Azaab ki Basharat de den."_
(Surah Nisa: 137 - 138)

📚📖
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Tarz o Ravish ka taghayyur (change), har rang o roop ki ye tabdeeli aur taloon mizaji ka ye aalam dar asal Islami Usoolon ki sahih taur par tehqeeq na karne ka nateeja hai aur ya Munafeqeen aur Ahle Kitab mein se mutassib Kuffar ki sazish hai taake haqeeqi Momenin ko mutazalzal (shaky) kiya ja sake kiyonki unke za'am mein unki aamad o raft haqeeqi Momenin ke Imaan ko davan dol kar degi. Isliye inke liye dardnak Azaab hai. Haqeeqat mein woh kaun hain, Rivayato mein mulaheza farmayen.
🍀
Usoole Kafi mein hai ke ye Ayat Hazrat Ali (as) ke un siyasi hareefon ke mutalliq nazil hui jo ibteda mein Nabi e Akram (saww) par Imaan laye aur jab unke saamne Vilayet e Ali (as) pesh ki gayi to unhone inkar kar diya. Phir jab Maqam e Ghadeer mein Rasool e Akram (saww) ne "Man kunto Maula...." Ka Ailan kiya to woh Imaan le aye. Phir jab Rasool e Khuda (saww) ki Aankhen band hui to unhone inkaar kar diya. Iske baad woh gumrahi mein badhte hi gaye aur yun unke dil Imaan se khaali ho gaye.'
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌷
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah ne Apni makhlooq ko paida nahi kiya jab tak ke us se Apni Wahdaniyat aur is Zurriyat e Zakiya ki Wilayat aur unke Dushmano se bara'at ka Ahad (promise) nahi le liye. Aur Arsh qaem nahi huwa jab tak ke uspar Noor se *La Ilaha Illallah Muhammadan Rasulallah Aliyyun Waliyullah* na likha gaya."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p232)

                 ♦ _*DOSTI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (586) 👬

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*بَشِّرِ الْمُنَافِقِينَ بِأَنَّ لَهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا * الَّذِينَ يَتَّخِذُونَ الْكَافِرِينَ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ أَيَبْتَغُونَ عِنْدَهُمُ الْعِزَّةَ فَإِنَّ الْعِزَّةَ لِلَّهِ جَمِيعًا*

_"Aap (saww) Munafeqeen ko dardnak Azaab ki basharat de den."_
_"Jo Ahle Imaan ko chhod kar Kafiron ko apna Sarparast banate hain. Kiya ye Munafiq izzat ki talab mein unke paas jaate hain jabke tamam tar Izzat to Allah ke liye hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 138 - 139)

📚📖 👬
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat tamam Musalmano ko tanbeeh karti hai ke woh apni izzat o aabroo ke liye chahe woh iqtesadi (financial) ya saqafati (cultural) pehloo ko ho ya siyaasi hawale se Dushmanan e Islam ki dosti talash na karen balke woh Zaate Ilahi par Bharosa karen jo tamam Izzaton ka sarchashma hai. Dushmanan e Islam ki apni bhi koi izzat nahi to woh doosron ko kiya denge aur agar unki ba zahir kuchh izzat ho bhi to woh qabil e etemad nahi hain kiyonki jab bhi inke mafad ka taqaza hua woh fauran apne Mukhlis tareen ittehadiyon ko bhi chhod kar apni rah len ge aur unki ye haalat hogi jise kabhi shanasai hi na thi.
Daur hazir ki tareekh bhi aise waqeaat se bhari padi hai. Aur aaj kal bhi aisa hi ho raha hai India mein haal hi election mein ye zyada dekha gaya. Jab Musalmano ke aise haalat ho jate hain ke Kafiron se dosti karne lagte hain aur gunah badh jate hain to Allah un par ek zalim badshah muayyan kar deta hai.
(Tafseer e Namoona)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👬
Imam Askari (as):
_"Tumhara behtareen Dost wo hai jo tumhari galtiyo'n ko bhool jaaye aur tumhare ehsaanaat ko yaad rakkhe."_
(Insaan ke Kamaal mein Akhlaaq ka Kirdaar)
👬
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Dosti aur dushmani wiraasat mein muntaqil (transfer) hoti hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p11)
👬
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Logo'n mein nek Dost 3 tarah ke tajrube se banao:_
_(1) Gaiz o gazab mein dekho ke wo haqq se khaarij to nahi hota hai,_
_(2) Daulat ke zariye se aazmao,_
_(3) Safar saath kar ke dekho."_
(Imam Jafar Sadiq (as) - Almustashaar Abdul Haleem Jundi (Misri), p208)

  ♦ _*MEHFIL-E-GUNAH (CLUB)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (587) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَقَدْ نَزَّلَ عَلَيْكُمْ فِي الْكِتَابِ أَنْ إِذَا سَمِعْتُمْ آيَاتِ اللَّهِ يُكْفَرُ بِهَا وَيُسْتَهْزَأُ بِهَا فَلَا تَقْعُدُوا مَعَهُمْ حَتَّىٰ يَخُوضُوا فِي حَدِيثٍ غَيْرِهِ ۚ إِنَّكُمْ إِذًا مِثْلُهُمْ ۗ إِنَّ اللَّهَ جَامِعُ الْمُنَافِقِينَ وَالْكَافِرِينَ فِي جَهَنَّمَ جَمِيعًا*

_"Allah tum ko is Kitab mein pahle hi Hukm de chuka hai ke jab tum suno ke Allah ki Ayaat ke khilaf Kufr baka ja raha hai aur unka Mazaq udaya ja raha hai to unke sath mat baitho, yahan tak ke woh doosri baaton mein masroof na ho jayen warna tum bhi un jaise qarar paoge. Yaqeen jano ke Allah Kuffar aur Munafiqon ko Jahannam mein ek jagah jama karne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 140)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Yahan Quran ka Mazaq means Deen ka mazaq, Shariyat ka mazaq hai. Aisi Majlis ya Club mein sharik hona jaez nahi.
(1) Majlis e Gunah (Club) mein shirkat irtekabe gunah ke manind hai, chahe sharik hone wala khamosh baithta rahe, Burai par razamandi yaani gunah ko support karna hai.
(2) Nahi Munkir agarche nahi anjaam de sakte lekin aisi Majlison se door rahna behtar hai.
(3) Gunah ki Mehfilon mein shirkat karne wale ka Gunah bhi Gunah karne wale ke barabar hai.
(4) Lekin agar Tauheen e Deen na ho to Non-Muslim ki Majlis mein sharik hone mein koi harj nahi, Mubah kam hai.
(5) Gunehgaron ki Mehfil mein ek Musalman sharik ho aur Gunah par aitraz na kare to ye Munafiqat hai. Kam se kam use na pasandgi ka to izhaar karna hi chahiye.
Saqeefa ke bare mein kuchh aise information milte hain ke jahan kuchh badkar Arab jama hote the. Deen ke Khilaf wahan sazishen hui jiska natija Musalman aaj tak bhugat raha hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Bani Adam ke aa'za (parts) par Imaan farz kiya aur har hisse ke liye Imaan ka alaihda taqaza muqarrar kiya. Allah ne Kaan par ye farz kiya ke jis cheez ke sunne se Allah ne mana kiya hai woh use na sune aur unki taraf tawajjah na kare. Isi liye Allah Ta'ala ne is Ayat mein farmaya (4:140)."_
(Usoole Kaafi)
🤓
Imam Reza (as):
_"Jab dekho ke koi shakhs Haq ka inkaar kar raha hai aur usko jhutla raha hai aur Ahle Haq par aitraz kar raha hai to tum uske paas se uth kar chale jao. Uske saath na baitho."_
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*4th Rajab 1438, 2nd April 2017, Sunday,

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (588) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*الَّذِينَ يَتَرَبَّصُونَ بِكُمْ فَإِنْ كَانَ لَكُمْ فَتْحٌ مِنَ اللَّهِ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَكُنْ مَعَكُمْ وَإِنْ كَانَ لِلْكَافِرِينَ نَصِيبٌ قَالُوا أَلَمْ نَسْتَحْوِذْ عَلَيْكُمْ وَنَمْنَعْكُمْ مِنَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ فَاللَّهُ يَحْكُمُ بَيْنَكُمْ يَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ ۗ وَلَنْ يَجْعَلَ اللَّهُ لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَلَى الْمُؤْمِنِينَ سَبِيلًا*

_"Yaqeen Jano ke Allah Kuffar aur Munafiqon ko Jahannam mein ek jagah jama karne wala hai."_
_"Ye Munafiq tumhare halaat ka intezar kar rahe hain. (Dekh rahe hain ke tumhara anjam kiya hota hai). Agar tumhe Allah ki tarah se fatah (Victory) naseeb hui to woh aa kar kahenge ke kiya ham tumhare sath na the? Aur agar Kuffar ka pallah bhari raha ke kiya ham tumhare khilaf ladne par qadir na the. Phir bhi ham ne tum ko Musalmano se bachaya? Allah tumhare aur unke darmiyan Qayamat ke Din Faisla karega. Allah Kafiron ke liye Musalmano par ghalib aane ki hargiz sabeel nahi rakhega."_
(Surah Nisa: 141)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein Islam Mukhalif Majlis mein shamil hone ke liye mana kiya tha. Phir hame Shaqeefa ki Majlis yaad aa gayi, kiya woh anti thi ya pro-Islam thi. Agar Pro-Islam hoti to Rasool e Akram (saww) ke hukm se hoti aur sabhi Sahaba us mein sharik hote lekin doosre sabhi sahaba Rasoole Akram (saww) ke Dafn o Kafan mein mashghool the.
Pas agar Musalman koi Anti-Islamic Activities karen to unhe Munafiq (Hypocrite) kaha jayega. Yahan is Ayat mein Allah ne Munafiqon ki kartooton ka zikr karna shuru kiya hai. Inhe is Ayat mein thali ka Baigan bataya hai. Agar Musalman jeete to unke sath aur agar Kuffar jeete to unke sath. Allah Qayamat ke Din sab ki poll khol dega. Munafeqeen ki kuchh aur sifat agli Ayat mein zikr hoga.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Reza (as):
_"Allah Kafiron ke liye Musalmano par ghalib aane ki hargiz sabeel nahi rakhega.": is Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke Allah Kafiron ko Daleel o Hujjat ke zariye se Anbiya par kabhi ghalba nahi dega."_
🤓
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Aye Ali (as)!...Khuda ki qasam! Aap se mohabbat wo rakkhega jo Momin hoga aur bugz wo rakkhega jo Munafiq (hypocrite) hoga."_
(Amaali - Shaikh Mufeed, p33)
🤓
Imam Kazim (as):
_"Kitna bura wo shakhs hai jo 2 chehre aur 2 zabaan waala ho - yaani Munafiq ho; saamne apne biradar e Momin ki taarif kare aur peethh pichhe geebat kare."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*5th Rajab 1438, 3rd April 2017, Monday,

           ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (589) 🤓

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ يُخَادِعُونَ اللَّهَ وَهُوَ خَادِعُهُمْ وَإِذَا قَامُوا إِلَى الصَّلَاةِ قَامُوا كُسَالَىٰ يُرَاءُونَ النَّاسَ وَلَا يَذْكُرُونَ اللَّهَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا * مُذَبْذَبِينَ بَيْنَ ذَٰلِكَ لَا إِلَىٰ هَٰؤُلَاءِ وَلَا إِلَىٰ هَٰؤُلَاءِ ۚ وَمَنْ يُضْلِلِ اللَّهُ فَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُ سَبِيلًا*

_"Munafeqeen Khuda ko dhoka dena chahte hain jabke Khuda unko Dhoke mein rakhne wala hai aur jab Munafiq Namaz ke liye uthte hain to nihayat susti ke sath uthte hain. Ye log Namaz mehez logon ke dikhawe ke liye padhte hain aur Khuda ko bahut kam yaad karte hain."_
_"Ye Munafiq Islam aur Kufr ke darmiyan hairan o sargardan hain, na poore is taraf hain na poore us taraf hain aur jisko Khuda Gumrahi mein chhod de uske liye aap ko koi raasta na milega."_
(Surah Nisa: 142 - 143)

📚📖 🤓
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein Munafeqeen ki kuchh aur sifat bayan ki gayi hain:
(1) Woh apni chaal mein khud phans jate hain. Woh dhoka dena chahte hain jabke khud hi dhoka kha jate hain.
(2) Chunke woh Khuda aur Uske Azeem Waadon par Imaan nahi rakhte isliye sab Ibadaat dikhawe ke liye karte hain.
(3) Chunke woh Khuda se door ho jaate hain isliye Khuda se attachment toot jata hai, isliye unki ibadaat, Namaz sab ek formalities hoti hain. Namaz zyada padhte hain par khuloos nahi rahta.
(4) Agar Khuda ka koi zikr karen to woh dil se nahi balke adatan hota hain.
(5) Ye log dhobi ke gadhe ke tarah hain na ghar ka na ghat ka. Na to Musalman ka kirdar rakhte na hi khul kar kufr ka ailan karte hain. Ye Muallaq insaan hain.
Isliye Khuda ne unhe chhod diya hai unhe kabhi nijaat nahi milegi. Kiyonki woh Ahle Bait (as) ke Dushman hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Hazrat Luqman ne apne bete se farmaya:_
_Munafiq ki 3 Nishaniyan hain:_
_(1) Uski zaban uske dil ki mukhalif hoti hai._
_(2)  Uska fe'l (act) uske qaul (saying) ka mukhalif hona._
_(3) Uska batin uska zahir ka mukhalif hota hai."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🎷🤓
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Susti karne wale (Lazy) ki 3 Nishaniyan:_
_(1) Jab akela hoga to Masti karega._
_(2) Jab log uske paas maujood honge to wo chusti karega._
_(3) Har kaam mein chahega ke log uski ta'reef karen."_
(Kitabul Khisal)
🕌🤓
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Kasmasate hue, ungte hue aur bojhalpan ikhtiyar karke Namaz ke liye khada na hona kiyonki ye Munafiqat ki Alamat hai."_
(Ilalush Sharaye)

      ♦ _*SARPARAST, WALI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (590) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا لَا تَتَّخِذُوا الْكَافِرِينَ أَوْلِيَاءَ مِنْ دُونِ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۚ أَتُرِيدُونَ أَنْ تَجْعَلُوا لِلَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ سُلْطَانًا مُبِينًا*

_"Imaan Walo! Momenin ko chhod kar Kuffar ko apna Wali aur Sarparast (ya sahara) na banao. Kiya tum chahte ho (aisa karke) apne khilaf Bargahe Ilahi mein ek wazeh Daleel qaem kar lo."_
(Surah Nisa: 144)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Munafeqeen ki kuchh khusoosiyat bayan ki gayin, ab Allah hame nasihat kar raha hai ke in logon se door rahen, inko na apna dost banayen, na Wali ya Sarparast. Na inko apna Sahara banaye, na Madadgar. Kiyon ham idhar udhar jaye jabke ham Allah ne hame Ahle Bait (as) jaise Sarparast se nawaza. 14 Masoomeen (as) ke alawa hamara kaun hajat rawa ho sakta hai. Aur Hazrat Abbas (as) Babul Hawaij ko hamare liye shafe qarar diya. Ham Babul Hawaij ke samne sawali bante hai. Beshak Hamara Maula Mushkil kusha, jiska farzand Bawaij, yehi hamari zindagi ke sahare hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷
*اَلسَّلاَمُ عَلَیْکَ یَابْنَ اَمِیْرِ الْمُؤْمِنِیْن اَلسَّلاَمُ عَلَیْکَ اَیُّہَا الْعَبْدُ الصَّالِحُ الْمُطِیْعُ لِلّٰہِ وَ لِرَسُوْلِہٖ اَشْہَدُ اَنَّکَ قَدْ جَاہَدْتَ وَ نَصَحْتَ وَ صَبَرْتَ حَتّٰی اَتٰیکَ الْیَقِیْن*
*لَعْنَ اﷲُ الظَّالِمِیِن لَکُمْ مِنَ الْاَوَّلِیْنَ وَالْآخِرِیْنَ وَ اَلْحِقْہُمْ بِدَرَکِ الْجَحِیْمِ.*

_"Salam ho yabna Ameerul Momenin, Salam ho aye Abde Saleh (Nek Bande), Allah o Rasool (saww) ke Mutee wa farmabardar, Mein gawahi deta hun ke Aap ne Jihad aur Sabr kiya yahan tak ke Yaqeen (Maut) ke aa gayi."_
_"Allah ki Laanat ho jisne Aapko qatl kiya Awwl o Akhir, Jaheem unka mustaqil thikana ho."_
🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷🌷
Hazrat Abbas (as) ki is Ziyarat mein Aap ko in Alqaab se nawaza gaya hai:
Abdus Saleh, Allah o Rasool ke Mutee, jaise ke Aap ne Imam Husain (as) ke sath apne wafadari nibhai. Sabr: Kisi Shuja ko Imam ki ita'at mein Dushman par war na karna Sabr ki inteha thi.
Hazrat Khizr (as) ko Quran mein Abd e Saleh se khitab kiya, jinka Ilm Musa (as) ki Ilm se zyada tha, na H. Musa (as) unke Ilm ke saamne Sabr kar paye, har baat mein kiyon.....ye 2 Nabi the. Hazrat Abbas ko bhi usi Alfaz se khitab kiya gaya aur Hazrat Khizr ki woh sifaat payi jaati hain. Agar Hazrat Abbas (as) ki mulaqat H. Khizr se hoti to unhe kahna nahi padta
( *قَالَ إِنَّكَ لَنْ تَسْتَطِيع مَعِيَ صَبْرًا* ) [Surat Al-Kahf 67]
Hazrat Abbas Ilm o Shuja'at ke markaz the.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*7th Rajab 1438, 5th April 2017, Wednesday,

             ♦ _*MUNAFEQEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (591)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الْمُنَافِقِينَ فِي الدَّرْكِ الْأَسْفَلِ مِنَ النَّارِ وَلَنْ تَجِدَ لَهُمْ نَصِيرًا * إِلَّا الَّذِينَ تَابُوا وَأَصْلَحُوا وَاعْتَصَمُوا بِاللَّهِ وَأَخْلَصُوا دِينَهُمْ لِلَّهِ فَأُولَٰئِكَ مَعَ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ ۖ وَسَوْفَ يُؤْتِ اللَّهُ الْمُؤْمِنِينَ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Yaqeenan Munafiq Dozakh ke sab se past tabqe mein honge aur tum unka koi Madadgar na paoge."_
_"Albatta un mein se jo Tauba kar len aur apni Islah kar len aur Khuda se poori tarah wabasta ho jayen air apne Deen ko Allah ke liye khalis kar den to aise afraad Momin ke saath honge aur anqareeb Allah Ahle Imaan ko Ajre Azeem ata karega."_
(Surah Nisa: 145 - 146)

📚📖 👽
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Munafeqeen ki khusisiyat ka bayan hua. Aaj ki Ayat mein zikr hai ke unko iska kiya badla milega. Musalman ya to Momin hoga ya Munafiq. Momin ke liye Ajre Azeem hai jabke Munafiq ke liye Jahannam ka sab se nichla tabqa hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 👽
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Aye girohe Mardum! Mere baad aise Rahnuma honge jo Dozakh ki dawat denge aur Qayamat ke Din unki Madad na ki jayegi."_
_"Aye Girohe Mardum! Unse Allah bhi bari hai aur mein bhi unse la talluq hun."_
_"Aye Girohe Mardum! Woh aur unke Madadgar aur unke Pairokar aur unke itteba karne wale (followers) Dozakh ke nichle tabqe mein honge aur Takabbur karne walon ke liye intihai bura tikhana hain."_
(Ehtejaj e Tabarsi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*8th Rajab 1438, 6th April 2017, Thursday,

♦ _*SHUKR-E-NEMATE ILAHI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (592) 🙏🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*مَا يَفْعَلُ اللَّهُ بِعَذَابِكُمْ إِنْ شَكَرْتُمْ وَآمَنْتُمْ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ شَاكِرًا عَلِيمًا*

_"Khuda tumhe Azaab de kar kiya karega agar tum Uska Shukr karo aur Imaan ki Raah par chalne lag jao. Khuda bada Qadardan aur sab ke haal se Waqif hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 147)

📚📖 🙏🏻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaat mein Khuda ke Azaab ka zikr hua. Ye Dardnak Azaab inteqami nahi taake Woh Gunehgar Bando se inteqam le balke ye insaan ke Imaan o Aamal ka natija hai. Agar ham Uski Nematon ka Shukr karen aur Khuda par Imaan le ayen to Khuda ko Azaab ki zaroorat hi kiyon pade.
Is Ayat mein 'Shukr' ko 'Imaan' par muqaddam rakha hai. Ye isliye ke jab tak Insaan Uski Nematon ko pahchan na le aur Shukr Guzari ke maqam tak na pahunch jaye us waqt tak khud Use nahi pahchan sakta. Kiyonki Uski Nematen Ma'arefat ka zariya hain. Wujoob e Ma'arefat e Ilahi ke liye Wujoob Shukre Mun'im (منعم) zaroori hai aur Shukr Guzari Insaani Fitrat hai, Nemat Bakhshne wale ka Shukr ada karna Wajib hai, lehaza is Nematen ata karne wale ki Ma'arefat bhi Wajib hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙏🏻
Imam Sajjad (as):
_"Wo gunah jo nemato'n ko badal dete hain wo ye hain: Logo'n par zyadati karna, Khairaat karne aur neki karne ki aadat chhor dena, Kufraane Ne'mat karna, Shukr e Khuda na bajaa laana."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p86)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Ne'mat ka Shukr ye hai ke moharramaat se (haraam cheezo'n se aur haraam kaamo'n se) bacha jaaye aur poora shukriya ye kehna hai AL HAMDU LILLAHI RABBIL AALAMIN."_
(Al Kaafi, v3, p347)
🙏🏻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Agar Allah ne tujhe khush-haal (prosperous) banaya hai to Uska Shukr adaa karo, aur agar bad-haal (destitute) ho to Astagfaar karo."_
(Rizq)
🙏🏻
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Allah ki sabse mehboob makhlooq wo hai jo kisi bhi Ne'mat ke ataa hone par Shukr kare aur Musibat ke waqt Sabr kare."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*9th Rajab 1438, 7th April 2017, Friday,

   ♦ _*MAZLOOM KI AWAAZ*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (593) 🤷🏻‍♂🙋🏻‍♂

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَا يُحِبُّ اللَّهُ الْجَهْرَ بِالسُّوءِ مِنَ الْقَوْلِ إِلَّا مَنْ ظُلِمَ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ سَمِيعًا عَلِيمًا * إِنْ تُبْدُوا خَيْرًا أَوْ تُخْفُوهُ أَوْ تَعْفُوا عَنْ سُوءٍ فَإِنَّ اللَّهَ كَانَ عَفُوًّا قَدِيرًا*

_"Allah buland awaaz se kisi ki badgoi pasand nahi karta magar jab koi Mazloom ho to use uski ijaazat hai aur Allah Sunnewala aur sab kuchh Jannewala hai."_
_"Agar tum kisi khair ko zahir karo ya use makhfi (hidden) rakho ya kisi Burai se darguzar (ignore) karo to Allah Gunahon ka Ma'af Karnewala aur Sahibe Ikhtiyar hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 148 - 149)

📚📖 🙋🏻‍♂🤷🏻‍♂
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Khuda ko pasand nahi ke koi kisi ki badgoi kare ya logon ke oyoob (defects) bayan kiye jayen kiyonki Khuda Sattarul Oyoob (Aibo ko Chhupanewala) hai, logon ki izzat o aabru ka khayal rakhna hamara farz hai. Lekin jo zalim hai uske aibon ko chhupana nahi chahiye.
Tafseer e Ali ibne Ibrahim ke mutabiq Ayat ka mafhoom ye hai ke Mazloom ko Zaalim ka shikwa karne ki ijaazat hai kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ko ya pasand nahi ke Insaan Zulm o Burai ka Shikwa kare albatta Mazloom ko aisa karne ki ijaazat hai. Use Zaalim ke khilaf buland Awaaz se wa waila karne ka Haq hai.
Ek aur Hadis mein hai ke agar tumhare paas koi Shakhs aaye aur tumhare saamne khushamad karte hue tumhari taarifen kare jo tum mein maujood nahi hain to uski baat ko qubool na karna aur use jhutlana, usne tum par zulm kiya hai.
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🙋🏻‍♂🤷🏻‍♂
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Madad hasil karne ke liye Mazloom ko ijaazat hai ke woh Zaalim par Sab o Shitam (gaali ya bura bhala kahna) kar sakta hai lekin iske liye shart ye hai ke woh aise maamle ke liye madad hasil karne ka khwahishmand ho jiski madad Deeni aitbar se bhi jaaez ho."_
(Majmaul Bayan, Noorus Saqlain)
🤷🏻‍♂
Imam Jafar Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi shakhs kisi ka Mehmaan ho aur Mezbaan achchi Mehmaan nawazi na kare to us Mehmaan ko ye Haq hasil hai ke woh uski Bukhilana (Kanjoos) Mezbaani ko bayan kare."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻🌻
*Imam Muhammad Taqi (as):*
_"Agar Ulema apni nasihat ko chhupa le'n, yaani sargardaa'n (bhattakte / aawara) aur gumraah insaan ki hidayat na karein ya (ma'anvi / spiritually) murda insaan ko dekh kar usay zinda na karein to unhone apne saath khayaanat ki."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p207)
🌻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"4 baatein insaan ko amal par ubhaarti hai: Sehet, Maaldaari, Ilm, Taufeeq."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p205)
🌻
Imam Taqi (as):
_"Jis ne'mat ka shukriya adaa na kiya jaaye wo oos gunah ke misl hai jo baksha na jaaye."_
(Aqwaal 14 Masumeen (as), p207)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*10th Rajab 1438, 8th April 2017, Saturday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

♦ _*KUCHH PAR IMAAN, KUCHH SE INKAAR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (594) 🚩

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ يَكْفُرُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَيُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يُفَرِّقُوا بَيْنَ اللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَيَقُولُونَ نُؤْمِنُ بِبَعْضٍ وَنَكْفُرُ بِبَعْضٍ وَيُرِيدُونَ أَنْ يَتَّخِذُوا بَيْنَ ذَٰلِكَ سَبِيلًا * أُولَٰئِكَ هُمُ الْكَافِرُونَ حَقًّا ۚ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لِلْكَافِرِينَ عَذَابًا مُهِينًا*

_"Beshak jo log Allah aur uske Rasoolon ka inkaar karte hain aur woh Allah aur Uske Rasoolon ke darmiyan tafreeq (difference) paida karna chahte hain aur kahte hain ke ham baaz par Imaan rakhte hain aur baaz ka inkaar karte hain aur woh chahte hain ke Imaan o Kufr ke darmiyan mein ek raah nikal len."_
_"Ye log pakke Kafir hain aur Ham ne Kafiron ke liye ruswa karnewala Azaab tayyar kar rakha hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 150 - 151)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Ye Ayat dar asal Yahoodi aur Esaiyon ki haalat bayan kar rahi hai. Yahoodi Hazrat Esa (as) ko nahi maante the jabke Esaayi Rasoole Khuda (saww) ko nahi maante. Jabke Allah ka Hukm hai 1,2400 Paighambar par Imaan rakhna aur unke Ausiya par bhi. In mein koi farq nahi. Musalman ka matlab hi ye hai ke jo kuchh Allah ne hukm kiya hai sab ke aage apna sar kham karna, Allah ke saamne tasleem ho jana. Yahan common minimum program se kaam nahi chalega. Kisi ek ka bhi inkaar Kufr hai. Aur inkaar karne walon ke liye ruswa kun Azaab hai.
Tafseer e Ali bin Ibrahim mein is Ayat ke zimn mein likha hai ke isse woh log murad hain jo kuchh Anbiya ko manne ka daawa karte the aur kuchh Anbiya par Imaan nahi rakhte the aur is Ummat mein jo log Rasoole Khuda par Imaan rakhen aur Amirul Momenin (as) ki Imamat ka inkar karen to woh bhi ma'anavi taur par unke hi bhai hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
Imam Ali (as):
_"Momin aur kaafir ke darmiyaan sirf Namaz ka farq hai. Lihaaza, jo Namaz ko chhor kar Imaan ka daawa kare, uska amal usay jhootlayega aur khud uske khilaaf gawaahi dega."_
(Tajalliyat e Hikmat, ch Namaz)
🚩
Imam Ali (as):
_"(Khud ko) Astagfaar / Tauba se muattar (khushbudaar) kar lo, tumhe gunaho'n ki badbu ruswaa (badnaam) nahi karegi."_
(Kashkool, Book 2, p88)
🚩
Imam Askari (as):
_"Momin ke liye kitni buri baat hai ke aisi cheez ki taraf raghbat (khwaish) rakhe jo uski zillat o ruswaayi ka sabab ho."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p237)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*11th Rajab 1438, 9th April 2017, Sunday,

🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

              ♦ _*MOMENIN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (595) 🌻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَالَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ وَلَمْ يُفَرِّقُوا بَيْنَ أَحَدٍ مِنْهُمْ أُولَٰئِكَ سَوْفَ يُؤْتِيهِمْ أُجُورَهُمْ ۗ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ غَفُورًا رَحِيمًا*

_"Aur jo log Allah aur Uske Rasoolon par Imaan laye aur Rasoolon ke darmiyan tafarraqa paida nahi kiya, unko Khuda anqareeb unka Ajr dega. Woh Bahut Zyada Bakhshne wala aur Meherbani Karnewala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 152)

📚📖 🌻
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein pakke Kafiron ka bayan tha, iske baad Momenin ki kaifiyat aur Anjam ka zikr hai.
Guzishta Ayaat mein Anbiya mein tab'eez o tafreeq ke qael logon ko Haqeeqi Kuffar qarar diya gaya hai lekin jo sab par Imaan laye hain unhen Haqeeqi Momin nahi kaha gaya balke sirf Momin kaha gaya hai shayad ye farq is bina par ho ke Haqeeqi Momin woh hain jo Imaan ke alawa Amal ke lehaz se bhi bilkul Paak o Saleh hon.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌻
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Momin ke saaye ke alawa Qayamat ki zameen Aag hai. Beshak uska Sadqa hi uska saayebaa'n (shade) hoga."_
(Sawaabul Aamaal o Iqaabul Aamaal)
🌻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Wo gunah jiska tumhe ranj / dukh ho, Allah ke nazdeek us Neki se behtar hai jis se tum mein guroor (pride) paida ho jaaye."_
(Nahjul Balagha)
🌻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Khauf e Khuda se Momin ka rona uske aa'nkho'n ki thandak hai."_
(Hadiyat ush Shia, p44)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
*12th Rajab 1438, 10th April 2017, Monday,
🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸🔸

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
      ♦ _*MO'JEZA KA DEMAND*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (596) 📚

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَسْأَلُكَ أَهْلُ الْكِتَابِ أَنْ تُنَزِّلَ عَلَيْهِمْ كِتَابًا مِنَ السَّمَاءِ ۚ فَقَدْ سَأَلُوا مُوسَىٰ أَكْبَرَ مِنْ ذَٰلِكَ فَقَالُوا أَرِنَا اللَّهَ جَهْرَةً فَأَخَذَتْهُمُ الصَّاعِقَةُ بِظُلْمِهِمْ ۚ ثُمَّ اتَّخَذُوا الْعِجْلَ مِنْ بَعْدِ مَا جَاءَتْهُمُ الْبَيِّنَاتُ فَعَفَوْنَا عَنْ ذَٰلِكَ ۚ وَآتَيْنَا مُوسَىٰ سُلْطَانًا مُبِينًا*

_"Aye Nabi! Ye Ahle Kitab agar aaj Aap se ye mutaleba kar rahe hain ke Aap Aasmaan se un par koi Kitab naazil karayen. Isse badh chadh kar unhone Moosa se mujremana mutaleba kiya tha aur unhone kaha tha ke hamen Khuda ko ailaniya (openly) dikha do. Isi sarkashi ki wajah se Bijli ne unhen apni giraft mein le liya tha. Phir unhone hamari wazeh (clear) Nishaniyon ke aa jane ke baad Gausala (Calf) ko Ma'bood (Deity) bana liya tha. Hamne isse bhi darguzar (Ma'af) kiya tha aur Hamne Moosa (as) ko khuli hui Daleel ataa ki thi."_
(Surah Nisa: 153)

📚📖 📕
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodiyon ka mutaleba nek niyyati nahi tha. Kabhi kabhi sawal ka maqsad jawab nahi, balke tanz hota hai. Unhe ne demand kiya ke kiyon ek poori Kitab ek sath nazil ho jaye. Jabke Tauret unko ek sath hi di ja chuki hai. Allah ne to unka ek mutaleba pahle hi poora kar chuka tha, lekin woh sahi raah par to kiya aate, ek Gausala ki pooja karne lage. Unka mutaleba tha ke ham Khuda ko direct apni Aankh se dekhna chahte hain. Allah ne unki ye maang poori ki. Sawal ye hain ke kiya Allah ne apne Aap ko dikhaya. Allah ke Jism/Body se mubarrah hai. Sirf Matter/Maddah ko hi ham dekh sakte hai. Allah Matter nahi hai, na koi Body rakhta hai. To phir unhone kiya dekha? Rivayaton se pata chalta hai ke woh Noor ki tajalli Hazrat Ali (as) ki thi. Jab woh is tajalli ko Khuda samajh kar bardasht nahi kar paye to Haqiqat ko kaise bardasht karte. Lekin is ke baad bhi unhone ne ek bachhre ki pooja ki.
Isi tarah aaj kal ye bhi sawal kiya jata hai ke Ahle Bait (as) ke bare mein Qur'an mein zikr kahan hai? Jab hamare Nabi (saww) ne khud unke bare mein clear Ayaten bata di phir bhi samajh mein nahi ayen to koi kare.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚🏞
Imam Ali (as)
se puchha gaya ke Suraj ki raushni mein jo intehaai baareek baareek zarraat (kann / particles) dikhayi dete hain wo kya hain? Aap ne farmaya:
_"H. Musa (as) ne Allah se deedaar ki darkhwaast ki thi. Allah ne farmaya ke tum pahaad par nazrein jamaao, agar pahaad apni jagah qaem raha to tum Mujhe dekh loge aur agar pahaad apni jagah par qaem na raha to tum Mujhe nahi dekh sakoge kyun ki tumhari nigaah kamzor hai, tum Mere deedaar ki taab (tolerance) nahi laa sakte. Iske baad Allah ne pahaad par jalwa giraya. Pahaad ke 3 hisse ho gaye, ek hissa uddkar aasmaan ki taraf gaya, doosra hissa zameen ke nichhe dha'ns gaya, aur tumhein ghar ke kamro'n mein jo bareek zarraat dikhayi dete hain ye oosi pahaad ka gubaar (dhuul / dust) hai"._
(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v3, p445)
📚
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo koi bhi ye chahta hai ke Ilm e Adam (as) aur parhezgaari e Nuh (as) aur burdbaari (forbearance / sahahsheelta) e Ibrahim (as) aur azmat e Musa (as) aur Ibadat e Isa (as) par nazar kare to wo Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) par nigaah kare."_
(Maula Ali Ki Shaan Mein 1000 Ahadees, h270, p188)

♦ _*AHD O PAIMAN (COVENANT)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (597) 📜✍🏻

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَرَفَعْنَا فَوْقَهُمُ الطُّورَ بِمِيثَاقِهِمْ وَقُلْنَا لَهُمُ ادْخُلُوا الْبَابَ سُجَّدًا وَقُلْنَا لَهُمْ لَا تَعْدُوا فِي السَّبْتِ وَأَخَذْنَا مِنْهُمْ مِيثَاقًا غَلِيظًا*

_"Aur Hamne un logon par Toor ko utha kar un se Ita'at ka Ahd liya tha aur Hamne unse kaha tha ke Sajdah rez ho kar Darwaze mein dakhil ho jao aur Hamne unse kaha tha ke Hafte ke roz (Saturday) zyadti na karna aur Hamne unse pukhta Ahd (Covenant) liya tha."_
(Surah Nisa: 154)

📚📖 📜✍🏻
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodiyon se Kohe Toor ke saye mein Ahd liya gaya. Ye same zikr Ayat (Baqarah: 63) mein ho chuka hai. Tafseer e Majmaul Bayan aur Al Manar mein hai Toor ka pahad apni jagah se ukhad gaya aur unke sar par musallat ho gaya. Jabke doosri Tafseer hai ke pahad mein zalzalah aya. Aur ye pahad ka tukda unke sar par ruka raha jab tak unhon Ahd na le liya. Is tarah Allah ne itni sakhti ke sath Ahd liya. Is Ayat ke zel mein ham detail zikr kar chuke hain.
Mufassir Tabarsi, Ibne Zaid ka qaul bayan karte hain.
"Jis waqt Hazrat Moosa (as) kohe Toor se wapas aye aur apne sath Tauret laye to apni Qaum ko bataya ke mein Aasmaani Kitab le kar aya hun jo Deeni Ahkam aur Halal o Haram par mushtamil hai. Ye woh Ahkam hai jinhen Khuda ne tumhare liye Amali Program qarar diya hai. Ye unke liye mushkil Ahkam the. Yahoodi nafarmani aur sarkashi par tul gaye. Khuda ne bhi Farishton ko ma'moor kiya ke woh Kohe Toor ka ek bahut bada tukda unke saron par la kar khada kar den. Isi asna mein Hazrat Moosa (as) ne unhe khabar di ke Ahd o Paiman (Covenant) baandh lo, Ahkam e Khuda par amal karo, sarkashi o baghawat se Tauba karo, tum se ye Azaab tal jayega warna sab halak ho jayege. Is par unhone sar tasleem kham kar diya. Tauret ko qubool kiya aur Khuda ke huzoor mein Sajdah kiya. Jab har lamha woh Kohe Toor ke apne saron par girne ke muntazir the lekin bil Akhir unki Tauba ki wajah se Azaab e Ilahi tal gaya."
Yahi mazmoon Sura Baqarah: 93, Aaraaf: 171 mein bhi aya hai.
Khuda ne Hukm diya tha ke Saturday ko Holiday karen. Chunke woh darya kinare rahte the, us din Machhli (fish) ka shikar ki manadi ki.
Lekin Yahoodiyon ne baad mein ye Ahd tod diya, aur Azaab ke mustaheq hue.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜✍🏻
Imam Ali (as):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Musa (as) ko 4 baato'n ki Wasiyyat ki:_
_(1) Jab tak tere gunah maaf na ho, doosro'n ke aib talaashne mein mashgool na hona,_
_(2) Jab tak Mere Khazane khatm na ho, apni Rozi ki fikr mat karna,_
_(3) Meri Haakimiyat (rule) ke hote huwe kisi gair ki haakimiyat ko tasleem na karna aur_
_(4) Jab tak Shaitan mar na jaaye uske Makr o Fareb se ghaafil na rahna."_
(Khisaal, p118)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*15th Rajab 1438, 13th April 2017, Thursday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*
