                ♦ _*AHD SHIKNI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (598) 📜🗡

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِمَا نَقْضِهِمْ مِيثَاقَهُمْ وَكُفْرِهِمْ بِآيَاتِ اللَّهِ وَقَتْلِهِمُ الْأَنْبِيَاءَ بِغَيْرِ حَقٍّ وَقَوْلِهِمْ قُلُوبُنَا غُلْفٌ ۚ بَلْ طَبَعَ اللَّهُ عَلَيْهَا بِكُفْرِهِمْ فَلَا يُؤْمِنُونَ إِلَّا قَلِيلًا*

_"Akhirkar unki Ahd Shikni (Covenant Breaking) ki wajah se aur is wajah se ke unhone Allah ki Ayat ka inkaar kiya aur bahut se Anbiya ko Na-Haq qatl kiya, aur ye kaha ke hamare dilon par parde pade hue hain, halanke dar haqiqat unke Kufr ki wajah se Allah ne unke dilon par Mohr laga di hai, lehaza un mein se bahut kam afraad Imaan late hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 155)

📚📖 📜🗡
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Kal ham ne Ayat ke zel mein bayan kiya tha ke Hazrat Moosa (as) ke zariye Allah ne Yahoodiyon se Ahd liya ke woh Ahkam Ilahi par amal karenge. Lekin baad mein woh palat gaye aur is Ahd par amal na karke isko ko tod diya jiska Natija ye hua ke unke Kufr ki wajah se Rehnooma e Deen ko qatl kiya. Allah ne Azaab ke taur par unke dilon par Mohr laga di. Ye Yahoodiyon ka zikr hai, lekin dekha jaye to Rasoole Akram (saww) ki rehlat ke baad khud Musalmano ne bhi yehi tarikh dohrai. Is Ayat ke misdaq woh log bhi hain jinhone Rahnuma e Islam ko Shaheed kiya. Isliye Duniya mein Momin kam hi nazar aate hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📜🗡
*رسول الله (ص): لا دين لمن لا عهد له .*
_"Jo Shakhs Ahd qaem nahi rakh sakta uska koi Deen nahi."_
[Nawadir al-R`awandi, p. 5]
📜🗡
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Jab woh Ahd Shikni karte hain Allah apne Dushman ko un par musallat kar deta hai."_
[Bihar al-Anwar, v. 100, p. 46, no. 3]
📜🗡
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Beshak, Jo apne muaede mein wafa nahi karta ya Ahd Shikni karta hai, ya aisa waada karta hai jo uski salahiyat ke bahar ho, ya us mein se kuchh baghair nek niyyat ke ghatata hai, to phir mein Roze Qayamat unka gareban pakdunga."_
[Kanz al-`Ummal, no. 10924]
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*16th Rajab 1438, 14th April 2017, Friday,

BAZM-E-ADAB WELCOMES YOU*

✝ _*SALEEB (CRUCIFICATION)*_ ✝

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (599)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَبِكُفْرِهِمْ وَقَوْلِهِمْ عَلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ بُهْتَانًا عَظِيمًا * وَقَوْلِهِمْ إِنَّا قَتَلْنَا الْمَسِيحَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ وَمَا صَلَبُوهُ وَلَٰكِنْ شُبِّهَ لَهُمْ ۚ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ لَفِي شَكٍّ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ إِلَّا اتِّبَاعَ الظَّنِّ ۚ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا * بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aur unke Kufr aur Maryam (sa) par Azeem buhtaan lagane ki wajah se."_
_"Aur unke is qaul ki wajah se ke ham ne Maseeh Esa bin Maryam Rasoolullah ko qatl kar diya hai. Halanke unhone fil waqae use qatl nahi kiya aur na Saleeb par chadhaya gaya (Crucified) balke Maamla un par Mushtaba kar diya gaya jin logon ne Esa (as) ke mutalliq ikhtelaf kiya woh dar asl Shak mein mubtela hain inke pas is ke mutalliq koi Ilm nahi hai. Unhone mehez guman hi ki pairavi ki hai. Unhone Yaqeenan Maseeh ko qatl nahi kiya tha ."_
_"Balke Khuda ne use apne taraf utha liya. Allah Zabardast Taqat Rakhne wala aur Hakeem hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 156 - 158)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayaton Ahd Shikni ka zikr hua tha. Ahd Shikni ke wajah Ahle Kitab ne Anbiya ka qatl kiya. Lekin is Ayat mein zikr ye hai ke unhone Hazrat Esa (as) ko qatl karne ki koshish ki lekin Allah ne H. Esa (as) ko utha liya. Ahadis mulaheza ho:
✝
Imam Baqir (as):
"Jis Raat Allah Ta'ala ne Hazrat Esa (as) ko uthana tha us Raat Aap (as) ne apne Hawariyun (Disciples) ko jama hone ka hukm diya. Isha ke waqt woh jama hue aur unki tadaad 12 thi. Aap (as) ne unhe ghar mein dakhil kiya. Kuchh der ke liye Aap chale gaye aur baad mein us ghar ke kone ke chashme se Aap baramad hue aurAap ke sar se paani ke qataraat tapak rahe the.
Aap (as) ne Hawariyun se farmaya:
" Allah ne meri taraf Wahi ki hai ke Woh mujhe is waqt apni taraf utha raha hai aur Woh mujhe Yahoodiyon se Paak karne wala hai. Tum mein ek shakhs ko meri shabeeh bana diya jayega. Woh qatl ho jayega aur use Saleeb par chadha diya jayega. Woh mere sath Jannat mein mere darje mein hoga."
"Tum mein se ek Subah hone se pahle 12 martaba mera inkaar karega."
"..... Mere baad tumhare 3 giroh banenge. Un mein se 2 giroh Khuda par iftera karne wale (Buhtaan) honge aur unka thikana Dozakh mein hoga aur ek giroh Sham'oon ki pairavi karega aur woh Khuda ke mutalliq sachchi baten karega aur woh giroh Jannat mein jayega."
"Iske baad Allah ne unko us ghar ke ek kone se apni jaanib utha liya. Hawariyun ne Aap ko Aasmaan ki taraf jate hue dekha."
✝
Rasool e Akram (saww):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) Baitul Muqaddas aye aur unhone is shaher mein rah kar 33 baras tak Tableegh e Deen karte rahe......"_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✝
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hawaariyo'n ne H. Isa (as) se puchhha, "Hum kin logo'n ke saath baithhein?" Aap (as) ne farmaya, "Jinki soorat se zikr e Khuda yaad aaye, jinki guftagu se tumhara Ilm zyada ho, jinke Ilm se Akherat ki taraf raghbat ho"._
(Al Kaafi, v1, p85)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

🙇 ✝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Jis Raat Ameerul Momin (as) ki Shahadat hui to Imam Hasan (as) ne khutba diya: 'Isi Raat Musa (as) ke Wasi Yoosha bin Noon ki wafat hui thi aur isi Raat Esa bin Maryam (as) ko uthaya gaya tha aur Quran Majeed bhi is Raat nazil hua tha."_
(Usoole Kaafi)

✝ _*SALEEB (CRUCIFICATION)*_ ✝

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (600) ✝

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَبِكُفْرِهِمْ وَقَوْلِهِمْ عَلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ بُهْتَانًا عَظِيمًا * وَقَوْلِهِمْ إِنَّا قَتَلْنَا الْمَسِيحَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ وَمَا صَلَبُوهُ وَلَٰكِنْ شُبِّهَ لَهُمْ ۚ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ لَفِي شَكٍّ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ إِلَّا اتِّبَاعَ الظَّنِّ ۚ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا * بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aur unke Kufr aur Maryam (sa) par Azeem buhtaan lagane ki wajah se."_
_"Aur unke is qaul ki wajah se ke ham ne Maseeh Esa bin Maryam Rasoolullah ko qatl kar diya hai. Halanke unhone fil waqae use qatl nahi kiya aur na Saleeb par chadhaya gaya (Crucified) balke Maamla un par Mushtaba kar diya gaya jin logon ne Esa (as) ke mutalliq ikhtelaf kiya woh dar asl Shak mein mubtela hain inke pas is ke mutalliq koi Ilm nahi hai. Unhone mehez guman hi ki pairavi ki hai. Unhone Yaqeenan Maseeh ko qatl nahi kiya tha ."_
_"Balke Khuda ne use apne taraf utha liya. Allah Zabardast Taqat Rakhne wala aur Hakeem hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 156 - 158)

📚📖 ✝
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Guzishta post is Ayat ke zel mein Ahadees post ki thi.
Christian ye maante hai ke Good Friday ke Din Hazrat Esa (as) (Jesus Christ) is Duniya se gaye aur Easter ke Din (Sunday) phir zahir ho gaye. Unka Aqeeda hai ke H. Esa (as) qatl hue, unhone ne logon Gunah ke evaz qurbani di, aur puri Duniye ke insano ko gunahon se pak kar diya. Is kaam ke liye Khuda ko Jesus ke roop mein zameen par aana pada. 3 God ka Aqeeda un mein paya jata hai jise Trinity kahte hain.
Islam unke Aqaed ko radd karta hai. Khuda itna Majboor nahi ke usko logon ki hidayat ya Kaffare ke liye bhes badalna pade.
Woh kahte hain:
God is One, The God, The Son of God (Jesus Christ) The Holy Spirit.
Trinity Hindu Aqeede mein payi jati jise kahte hain Trimurty. Ye sab batil Aqaed hain.
Aql is baat ko tasleem nahi kar sakti ke Jo Ek hai woh 3 kaise ho sakta hai. Is Topic ko doosri Ayat ke zel mein discuss karenge.
Aaj ki Ayat mein Quran jawab de raha hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) ka qatl nahi hua balke woh zinda hain. Khuda ka koi beta nahi (Sura Tauheed). Agar Hazrat Esa (as) logon ke liye fidya (atonement) ban gaye to iska matlab ye hua ke ab sab Christian azadi ke saath gunah kar sakte hain, ya phir ghadi ghadi Hazrat Esa (as) ko fidya dena hoga. Bible jis mein ye Aqaed ka zikr hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) qatl hue,  woh baad mein Hawariyon ne likhi. Asl Injeel to Christian ke pas hai hi nahi, jo hai woh bhi English translation hai. In kitabon mein tehreef mumkin hai. Jin mein se ek Injeel Barnabas hai jo Bible mein shamil nahi.
Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim mein marqoom hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) ki Rahme Maadar mein tasveer kashi ki gayi. Woh Baap ke Sulb mein nahi rahe the aur jab unhe zameen se uthaya gaya to inhone oon (wool) ka Jubba pahna hua tha.
(Noorus Saqlain)
Islam ka jo Aqeeda hai wohi Hazrat Esa (as) ka hai. Woh ek Nabi the, jinko Allah ne logon ki Hidayat ke liye maboos kiya tha.  Woh Chauthe Aasmaan par abhi tak zinda hain aur Imam Mahdi (atfs) ke zahoor ke baad Hazrat Esa (as) bhi zahir honge.
(To be cont'd.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Yahoodi Hazrat Esa (as) ki talaash mein wahan aye. Unhone us jawan ko jo shabeeh Esa (as) ban chuka tha wahan se giraftar kar liya aur jis ke mutalliq Aap (as) ne farmaya tha ke woh Subah hone se pahle 12 martaba unka inkaar karega usne bhi Aapka 12 martaba inkaar kiya aur yun Aapki dono peshingoiyan (forecast) sahih sabit hui."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✝
Imam Husain (as):

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p86)

   ✝ _*HAZRAT ESA (as)*_ ✝

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (600) ✝

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَبِكُفْرِهِمْ وَقَوْلِهِمْ عَلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ بُهْتَانًا عَظِيمًا * وَقَوْلِهِمْ إِنَّا قَتَلْنَا الْمَسِيحَ عِيسَى ابْنَ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولَ اللَّهِ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ وَمَا صَلَبُوهُ وَلَٰكِنْ شُبِّهَ لَهُمْ ۚ وَإِنَّ الَّذِينَ اخْتَلَفُوا فِيهِ لَفِي شَكٍّ مِنْهُ ۚ مَا لَهُمْ بِهِ مِنْ عِلْمٍ إِلَّا اتِّبَاعَ الظَّنِّ ۚ وَمَا قَتَلُوهُ يَقِينًا * بَلْ رَفَعَهُ اللَّهُ إِلَيْهِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*
(Surah Nisa: 156 - 158)
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ✝
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Mahdi (atfs) zahoor karenge to Khuda Esa (as) ko naazil karega aur ye dono ek jagah jama ho jayenge aur jab Wajib Namaz ka waqt hoga to Mahdi (atfs) Esa (as) se kahenge, “Aye Rooh e Khuda, aage badhiye (yaani Jamaat padhaiye)”. Isa (as) farmayenge, “Aap Ahlebait (as) par koi bhi sabqat (lead) nahi kar sakta hai”. Phir Mahdi (atfs) aage badhenge aur Esa (as) Aap ke pichhe Namaz padhenge."_
(Jamaal e Muntazar, p489)
✝
Hazrat Esa (as):
_"Duniya aur Akherat ki misaal (ek shakhs ki) 2 biwi jaisi hai. Wo agar ek ko raazi karega to doosri uspe gussa ho jayegi."_
(Miskhat ul Anwaar)
✝
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) ne apne hawaariyo'n se kaha, "Aise shakhs ki hum-nashini (dosti) ikhtiyaar karo jiska deedar tumko Khuda ki yaad mein mubtela kar de, aur jiski guftaar (baatein) tumhare Ilm aur daanish (knowledge) mein izafa kare, aur jiska kirdaar tum ko Akherat ka mushtaaq (eager / utsuk) bana de."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p23)
✝
Hazrat Esa (as):
_"Logo'n mein sabse zaleel (wretched) wo shakhs hai jo apne Ilm ke liye mash'hoor ho, apne amal ke liye nahi."_
(Lantern of the Path, p11)

     ♦ _*MAUT KE WAQT IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (601) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ إِلَّا لَيُؤْمِنَنَّ بِهِ قَبْلَ مَوْتِهِ ۖ وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَكُونُ عَلَيْهِمْ شَهِيدًا*

_"Ahle Kitab (Jews & Christians) mein se koi aisa na hoga jo uski Maut se pahle un par Imaan na le ayenga. Qayamat ke Din woh un par Gawah honge."_
(Surah Nisa: 159)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat ka doosri tarah se bhi tarjuma kiya ja sakta hai: _"Har Ahle Kitab apni Maut se pahle Hazrat Esa (as) (Islami taur par) Imaan lata hai."_ Lekin ye sahi tarjuma nahi hai. Hajjaj bhi is hi ghalat fahmi mubtela hua aur kitne Ahle Kitab ko qatl kiya lekin koi bhi marne se pahle Imaan nahi laya. Shahr bin Hooshan ne Imam Mohd Baqir (as) se rivayat ki aur is Ayat ka real meaning bataya:
_"Qayamat se pahle Esa bin Maryam (as) Duniya mein nazil honge. Us waqt jitne bhi Yahoodi aur doosre Ahle Kitab hon woh Hazrat Esa (as) ki Maut se qabl un par Imaan layenge aur Esa (as) Hazrat Imam Mahdi (as) ki iqteda mein Namaz padhenge."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✨
Abu Huraira se riwayat:
_"Rasool e Khuda (saww) ne farmaya, " Tumhara kiya hoga jab Ibne Maryam (Esa as) tumhare darniyan nazil honge aur logon ka Qur'ani Ahkam  se faisla denge Bible ke Ahkam se nahi."_
(Fateh-ul Bari page 304 and 305 Vol 7)
(Source: Android App Sahih Al Bukhari, Vol 4, Book 55, Hadis 658)
✨
Majmaul Bayan mein hai ke Ahle Kitab Maut ke waqt Hazrat Rasoole Khuda (saww) par Imaan layenge.
✨
Is Ayat se pata chalta ke har Kafir ehtezar ke waqt (near Death) Imaan qubool kar leta hai lekin ye qabil e qubool nahi hota. Firaun bhi akhiri waqt mein Imaan le aya tha lekin qubool nahi hua.
Ye Isliye ke Maut ke waqt uske upar pade parde hat jate hai aur ab uski Ankhen khul jati hain woh apni Aankhon se haqiqat ko dekhta hai.
Ayat ke doosre matalib se ye baat wazeh hai Imam Mahdi (as) ke Zahoor ke baad sab log ek hi Deen yani Islam par  lmaan le ayenge.
Aur ajkal ke ye research news bhi kuchh isi tarah bayan kar rahi hai.
_"Islam is fastest growing religion, Pew study says."_ - aleteia.org:  
http://aleteia.org/2017/03/28/islam-is-fastest-growing-religion-pew-study-says/
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⚰
Hazrat Ali (as):
*ياحار حمدان من يمت يرنى*
*من مؤمن او منافق قبلا*
*يعرضى طرفه و اعرفه*
*بعينه و اسمه و ما فعلا*
_"Haris Hamdani! Jo bhi marta hai mujhe chahe woh Momin ho ya Munafiq ho. Uski nigahen mujhe pahchanti hain aur meri nazar use pahchati hain. Aur mujhe uska naam bhi maaloom hota hai aur mujhe uske afa'al ka bhi ilm hota hai."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
✨
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Tamam Ahle Adyaan (people of Religions) marte waqt Rasoole Khuda (saww) Ameerul Momenin (as) ki Ziyarat karke marte hain."_
(Noorus Saqlain)

     ♦ _*MAUT KE WAQT IMAAN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (601) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَإِنْ مِنْ أَهْلِ الْكِتَابِ إِلَّا لَيُؤْمِنَنَّ بِهِ قَبْلَ مَوْتِهِ ۖ وَيَوْمَ الْقِيَامَةِ يَكُونُ عَلَيْهِمْ شَهِيدًا*

_"Ahle Kitab (Jews & Christians) mein se koi aisa na hoga jo uski Maut se pahle un par Imaan na le ayenga. Qayamat ke Din woh un par Gawah honge."_
(Surah Nisa: 159)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🚩
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Hazrat Ali (as) ka dost-daar (chahne-wala) Hazrat Ali (as) ki 3 maqaamat par Ziyarat karega aur khush hoga:_
_(1) Maut ke waqt,_
_(2) Siraat par aur_
_(3) Hauz e Kausar par."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p101)
🚩
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Momin ki nishaani ye hai ke jab uski Maut ka waqt aata hai to uske chehre ka rang jitna sufaid tha oos se zyada sufaid aur raushan ho jaata hai, pehsaani par paseena aane lagta hai, uski aa'nkho’n se aansuo’n ki tarah rutubat behne lagti hai; to yehi uski Ruuh nikalne ki nishaani hai…"_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p100)
🚩

(Shiane Ahlebait (as), p17)

         ♦ _*HARAM GHAZA*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (602) 🍪🍨

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَبِظُلْمٍ مِنَ الَّذِينَ هَادُوا حَرَّمْنَا عَلَيْهِمْ طَيِّبَاتٍ أُحِلَّتْ لَهُمْ وَبِصَدِّهِمْ عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ كَثِيرًا*

_"Un Yahoodiyon ke isi zalemana ravayye ki wajah se Ham ne un par woh pakeeza cheezen Haram kar din jo ke unke liye Halal qarar di gayi thi aur is bena par bhi ke woh logon ko bakasrat Khuda ki Rah se rokte hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 160)

📚📖 🍪🍨
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Shariyat mein khane ke mutalliq Ahkam hain kuchh Haram to kuchh Halal hain. Jo hame khane se mana kiya gaya hai uska matlab ye nahi ke woh cheez gandi hai, kharab hai jaisa ke ham samajhte hain. Allah ne jo hame Hukm diya hai bas us par amal karna hai.
Is ayat ke mutabiq Allah ne un cheezon ko khaane se roka jo ke haqeeqat mein paak thi. Allah ne Yahoodiyon ko unke zulm ki saza is tarah di. Surah An'am:146 mein bhi isi mauzoo par tazkarah hai. Ayat:
_"Hamne Yahoodiyon ke Zulm o Sitam ki wajah se har janwar jiska sum phata na ho un par Haram qarar de diya. Nez Gay (Cow) aur Bhed Bakri ki charbi bhi ke jis se unhe lagao tha un par Haram kar di magar iska woh hissa jo janwar ki pusht ya Aanton ke atraaf mein ho ya haddi ke sath mila hua ho."_
(An'am:146)
🍪🍨
Imam Sadiq (as):
(Ayat (An'am:146) ke zel mein)
_"Bani Israel ke Hukkam aur Raoosa (Chiefs) Faqeer aur Nadaar logon ko Parindo ke gosht aur janwaron ki charbi khane se rokte the. Khuda ne unke is Zulm o Sitam ki wajah se un cheezon ko khud un par Haram qarar de diya."_
(Tafseer e Burhan, Vol 1, P-559)
Maujooda Tauret 11th chapter of Leviticus mein ye Haram ghaza ki list di gayi hai.
Ye pababdiyan unke Zulm ki saza thi.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍪🍨
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Agar koi Shakhs apni Zameen mein Gehun (Wheat) kasht kare aur Gehun ki paidawar achchhi na ho ya us mein Jau (Barely) ya Jaee (Oat) zyada paida ho jaye to uski wajah bhi uska koi zulm hota hai. Us shakhs ne ya to zameen ke area ke mutalliq koi zulm kiya hoga ya phir usne kaashtkaron aur mazdooron par zulm kiya hoga kiyonki Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya: (4:160)"_
(Al Kaafi, Noorus Saqlain)
🍨🍪
_"Hazrat Yaqoob (as) ko عرق النساء Arthritis or Sciatic Pain dard mahsoos hua to Aap (as) ne Ahd kiya ke agar Allah Ta'ala ne unhe shifa ata ki to woh apni pasandeeda ghaza (favorite dish) istemal nahi karenge. Allah Ta'ala ne shifa di to unhone apne upar Oont (Camel) ka gosht Haram kar diya tha, jabke ye gosht unhe bahut pasand tha. Unhone Tauret ke nuzool se pahle Oont ke gosht ko apne liye Haram qarar diya tha aur jab Tauret nazil hui to Tauret mein Khuda ne ise Haram nahi kiya tha. Baad mein Aulad e Yaqoob (as) (Bani Israel) ne Oont ka gosht khana chhod diya."_
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim, Noorus Saqlain)
🍪🍨
_*KOONDE KI NAZR:*_
Nazre Imam Sadiq (as) ek tarah ki mannat ka poora hona hai ke agar meri hajat poori hogi to mein Nazr doonga aur logon ko khilaonga.
Lekin ho sakta hai Sab ki ek hi mannat ho ke agar Muawiya mar gaya to Nazr karonga aur is khushi mein logon ko khana khilaonga. Is General mannat ko sab hi poora karte hain. Ye bhi ek Khushi manane ka ek tareeqa hai.
(Jo Lakadhare ki kahani sunayi jati hai uska koi reference nahi hai. Ye silsila kab se shuru hua iski bhi koi pukhta tarikh nahi hai. Lekin jo Momenin Nazr kar rahe hain woh jaez hai.)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

*22nd Rajab 1438, 20th April 2017, Thursday,

      ♦ _*SOOD (INTEREST)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (603) 💰

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَأَخْذِهِمُ الرِّبَا وَقَدْ نُهُوا عَنْهُ وَأَكْلِهِمْ أَمْوَالَ النَّاسِ بِالْبَاطِلِ ۚ وَأَعْتَدْنَا لِلْكَافِرِينَ مِنْهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا*

_"Aur is bena par ke woh Sood (Interest) lete hain jabke unhe Sood se mana kiya gaya hai aur woh logon ke Maal najaez zarae se khate hain. Jo log un mein se Kafir hain unke liye Ham ne Dardnak Azaab tayyar kar rakha hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 161)

📚📖 💰
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Cont'd ....
Yahoodiyon par Azaab ki ek wajah ye bhi thi ke woh Sood khate the that means logo se najaez Maal lete the. Means Sood (Interest) us zamane se hi haram hai. Aur is wajah se Allah ne unke liye Dardnak Azaab tayyar kiya hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Jo shakhs len-den karna chahta hai usay 5 cheezo'n se bachna chaahiye:_
_(1) Sood (interest / vyaaj),_
_(2) Qasam khana,_
_(3) Maal ka aib chhupana,_
_(4) Jo cheez doosro'n ko bechni ho uski taarif karna aur_
_(5) Jo cheez auro'n se kharidnaho uski buraai karna."_
(Tehzibul Islam)
💰
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Sood-khor (byaaj lene wala) duniya se paagal aur diwaana ho kar marta hai."_
(Aasmani Nasihatein, v2, p149)
💰
Imam Reza (as):
_"Sood (interest) ka khana gunah e kabeera hai aur is hukm ko maamuli samajhna Kufr mein daakhil kar deta hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p56)
💰
Imam Ali (as):
_"Rasule Khuda (saww) ne uspar la'nat bheji hai jo Sood (interest) leta hai,deta hai…jo Sood ka contract likhta hai aur jo is len den mein gawaah hota hai."_
(Greater Sins I)

♦ _*RASEKHOONA FIL ILM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (604) 📚

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَٰكِنِ الرَّاسِخُونَ فِي الْعِلْمِ مِنْهُمْ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ يُؤْمِنُونَ بِمَا أُنْزِلَ إِلَيْكَ وَمَا أُنْزِلَ مِنْ قَبْلِكَ ۚ وَالْمُقِيمِينَ الصَّلَاةَ ۚ وَالْمُؤْتُونَ الزَّكَاةَ وَالْمُؤْمِنُونَ بِاللَّهِ وَالْيَوْمِ الْآخِرِ أُولَٰئِكَ سَنُؤْتِيهِمْ أَجْرًا عَظِيمًا*

_"Lekin un mein se jo Ilm mein pukhta hain aur Imaan laane wale hain woh un tamam baton par Imaan rakhte hain jo tum par nazil ki gayi hain aur jo kuchh Aap se pahle nazil kiya gaya hai, is tarah ke Imaan laane wale aur Namaz o Zakat ki pabandi karne wale aur Allah aur Roz e Akhir par Kamil Aqeeda rakhne wale logon ko Ham anqareeb Ajre Azeem ata karenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 162)

📚📖 📕📗
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Yahoodiyon ka bayaan ho raha tha ke unke Zulm ki wajah se unke liye shakht Shariyat nazil hui. Lekin woh Yahoodi jo apne ilm o research ki wajah se Momin ho gaye aur Namaz o Zakat ko pabandi karne lage unke liye Azeem Ajr hai.
Rasekhoona fil Ilm ka tazkarah ham Surah Ale Imran ki Ayat no.7 ke zel mein kar chuke hain.
Kaynat mein koi Rasekhoona fil Ilm nahi siwai uske jo Mimber se Salooni kahe (poochho jo poochhna hai) aur woh hain Ameerul Momenin Hazrat Ali ibne Abi Talib (as). Is bare mein Aap farmate hain:
Imam Ali (as):
_"Aur jaan lo 'Rasekhoona fil Ilm' (Staunch in Knowledge) woh hai jo Asraar e ghaibi (Hidden Secrets) ke Muqabile mein etraaf e ijz karte hain aur un asraar ki tafseer se aajiz hain. Isi ijz ne unhe is silsile mein kavish o koshish se beniyaz kar diya hai."_
(Nahjul Balagha, Khutba e Ashbah no. 90)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 📚
Rasule Khuda (saww):
_"Main sheher e Ilm hoo'n aur Ali (as) uske darwaza hain. Pus jo shakhs Ilm haasil karna chahta hai, usko darwaze se aana chahiye."_
(Guftaar e Dil Nasheen, p21)
📚
Imam Baqir (as):
_"Tamaam Ambiya (as) ka Ilm J. Paigambar e Akram (saww) mein jamaa kiya gaya tha jinhone Ameerul Momeneen Ali ibne Abi Taalib (as) ko taalim kiya. Phir hum uske waaris huwe. Koi Imam is duniya se nahi jaata jab tak oos jaisa ya jaisa Allah chaahe uski jagah par qaaem na ho jaaye."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p125)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

*24th Rajab 1438, 22nd April 2017, Saturday,

BAZM-E-ADAB COMMEMORATE SHAHADAT OF IMAM MUSA KAZIM (as)*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
  ♦ _*WAḤY وحى REVELATION*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (605) 💫

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّا أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَيْكَ كَمَا أَوْحَيْنَا إِلَىٰ نُوحٍ وَالنَّبِيِّينَ مِنْ بَعْدِهِ ۚ وَأَوْحَيْنَا إِلَىٰ إِبْرَاهِيمَ وَإِسْمَاعِيلَ وَإِسْحَاقَ وَيَعْقُوبَ وَالْأَسْبَاطِ وَعِيسَىٰ وَأَيُّوبَ وَيُونُسَ وَهَارُونَ وَسُلَيْمَانَ ۚ وَآتَيْنَا دَاوُودَ زَبُورًا*

_"Ham ne Aap ki taraf usi tarah se Waḥy nazil ki hai jis tarah Nooh (as) aur unke baad ke Paighambaron ki taraf bheji thi aur Ham ne Ibrahim (as), Ismael (as), Ishaq (as), Yaqoob (as), Aulade Yaqoob (Bani Israel), Esa (as), Ayyub (as), Yunus (as), Haroon (as) aur Sulaiman (as) ki taraf bheji aur Ham ne Dawood (as) ko Zuboor ata ki hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 163)

📚📖 💫
👉 _* Tafseer:*_
Ab ham Nabuwwat ke Topic par tazkara shuru karte hain. Aaj ki Ayat Waḥy وحى ke mutalliq hai. Har Nabi ya Rasool ko Waḥy ke zariye Khuda ke Ahkamat o qawanin nazil hote the. Poora Quran Rasoole Akram (saww) par Waḥy ke zariye nazil hua. Jaisa ke Ayat 42:51 mein hai Nabi (saww) koi kalam nahi karte the siwai Waḥy ke. Waḥy Allah ka Kalam hai. Ye Allah aur Nabi ke darmiyan messaging service hain. Waḥy ke 3 tareeqe bataye gaye hain:
(1) Nabi par jaagte ya khwab mein ilham hona.
(2) Koi makhfi Awaaz sunai dena.
(3) H. Jibrael (as) ke zariye.

_*Ilham الهام*_ means inspiration jo aam insaan ko bhi ho sakta hai.
Lekin _*Waḥy وحى*_ sirf Anbiya ke liye makhsoos hai.
Yahan tak ke Imam ko Ilham hota tha Waḥy nahi.
Nayi Shariyat sirf Rasool le kar aate hain. Imam sirf us Shariyat ka nifaz karte hain. Bahut se Anbiya ne Pichhli Shariyat ka nifaz (execute) kiya, nayi Shariyat Ulool Azm Rasool le kar aye.
🌫💨
Waḥy ke mutalliq rivayaat mulaheza farmayen:
Imam Sadiq (as):
"Ek martaba Jibrael e Amin (as) Rasool e Khuda (saww) ke pas baithe hue the achanak woh Aasmaan ki taraf dekhne lage phir unhone kaha:
_" Ya Rasoolallah! Ye Rabbe Ta'ala ka hajib hai aur poori Makhlooq mein se ye Khuda ke zyada qareeb hai. Iske saamne surkh Yaqoot ki Takhti maujood hoti hai. Jab Allah Ta'ala koi Waḥy nazil karta hai to takhti mein larzish (vibration) paida hoti hai. Ye Takhti ko dekhta hai to is mein Waḥy likhi hoti hai. Ye wahan se Hukm e Ilahi hasil karke hamare pas sipurd karta hai. Ham is Paigham (Msg) ko Aasmanon aur Zameen par pahunchate hain."_
(Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim)
🌪
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Hazrat Esa (as) ke baad Muhammad (saww) tak Farishton ne Waḥy ki koi sada nahi suni thi. Jab Allah Ta'ala ne Muhammad Mustafa (saww) par Waḥy nazil ki to Ahle Aasmaan ko Waḥy ki awaz chattan par lohe ki awaz jaisi mehsoos hui. Is awaz ko sun kar Ahle Aasman behosh ho gaye aur jab unke dilon se Waḥy ki ghabrahat door ho gayi to Jibrael (as) Waḥy le kar Rasoole Akram (saww) par nazil hue."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
💫
_"Muhammad Mustafa (saww) ko sirf Nooh (as) ki Waḥy ka nahi balke jumla Anbiya (as) ki tarah ka Khazinadar banaya"_
(Tafaeer e Ayyashi)
📕
Nabi e Akram (saww):
_"Zuboor Mahe Ramazan ki 8 tarikh ko nazil hui."
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌳🌿
*Imam Musa Kazim (as):*
(Aaj unki Shahadat ka din hai)
_"Bani Israel ne Hazrat Musa (as) se khwahish ki ke woh unhe Khuda ka Kalam sunayen."_
_"Musa (as) unhe Kohe Toor par le gaye aur unhone Allah se request ki. Allah ne ek darakht (tree) mein Kalam paida kiya, phir use phaila diya. Bani Israel ko woh Awaaz 6 direction se yani North, South, East aur West aur upar niche se aati hui mehsoos hui."_
(Kitabut Tauheed, Noorus Saqlain)

SHIA CHANNEL COMMEMORATE WAFAT of MOHSIN E ISLAM JANABE ABU TALIB (as)*

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
♦ _*NUBUWWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (606) 🕌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*وَرُسُلًا قَدْ قَصَصْنَاهُمْ عَلَيْكَ مِنْ قَبْلُ وَرُسُلًا لَمْ نَقْصُصْهُمْ عَلَيْكَ ۚ وَكَلَّمَ اللَّهُ مُوسَىٰ تَكْلِيمًا*

_"Kuchh Rasool aise hain jin ke waqeat Ham se bayan kar chuke hain aur kuchh Rasool woh hain jinke waqeat Ham ne Aap se bayan nahi kiye aur Allah ne Musa (as) se Kalam ka Haq ada kar diya."_
(Surah Nisa: 164)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein zikr hua ke Allah ne sab Anbiya ka zikr nahi kiya hai. Sirf 25 Anbiya ke naam hi Qur'an mein darj hain. Baqi information Ahadis wa rivayaat se pata chalta hai.
🕌
Imam Mohd Baqir (as):
_"Hazrat Nooh (as) aur Hazrat Adam (as) ke darmiyan bahut se gumnam Nabi (as) guzre hain isliye Allah ne bhi Qur'an Karim mein unka zikr makhfi rakha hai. Kuchh mashhoor Anbiya ke waqeat Allah ne bayan kiye hain jabke zyada tar Anbiya ke waqeat ka Qur'an Karim mein tazkarah maujood nahi hai jaisa ke Allah Ta'ala ne farmaya (4:164)"_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun
Ne'mah)

Kal Waḥy ka tazarah hua tha, yani Allah Anbiya se Kalam karta hai, iski ek misal Hazrat Musa (as) ka Khuda se Kalam hai. Isliye kahte hain Musa Kalimullah (as).
🌳🌿
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Allah Ta'ala ne Musa (as) se 1,24,000 Kalamat Irshad farmaye aur ye Kalam musalsal 3 dino tak jari rahe. Is dauran Musa (as) ne na kuchh khaya aur na piya. Aur jab Bani Israel ke pas wapas aye aur unki guftugu suni to unhe in logon ki guftugu achhi na lagi kiyonki unke Kaano mein Allah ke Kalam ka ras ghula hua tha."_
(Kitabul Khisaal)
🌳🌿
Hazrat Ali (as):
_"Allah ne Musa (as) se Kalam kiya lekin kisi aaza wa jawareh (body parts) se madad nahi li, Allah in Sifat se kahi Buland hai."_
_"Khuda ke Kalam karne ke kai tariqe hain:_
_(1) Usne Rasoolon se direct guftugu ki._
_(2) Kuchh kalam woh bhi hai jise usne Anbiya ke dilon mein dala._
_(3) Kuchh Kalam Anbiya ko Khwab mein sunaya gaya._
_(4) Kuchh Kalam Waḥy wa Tanzeel ke zariye bheja."_
(Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😭😭
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jab Hazrat Abu Talib (as) ki wafaat huwi to J. Jibreel (as) naazil huwe aur kaha, "Ya Muhammad (saww), ab Makke se Hijrat kijiye kyun ki ab Makke mein aap ka koi nasir o madadgaar nahi raha.."_
(Hayaatul Quloob, v2, p494), (Kamaluddin, v1, p207)
🌴☘🌱🌿
Riwayat:
_"Jab Rasule Khuda (saww) ka chand Musalmano'n ke saath Sheb e Abu Talib mein muhasira (blockade) kiya gaya to unhe 4 saal tak wahi'n rehna pada, na khaane ke liye koi cheez thi na peene ke liye paani maujood tha. Lekin jab bhi bhook ya pyaas ghaalib aa jaati to Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (as) par Salwaat bhejte jis se bhook aur pyaas khatm ho jaati kyun ki aasmaan se unke liye khoraak aur paani naazil hota. Jab bhi unke libaas gande aur maile ho jaate to kapde haath mein lekar Muhammad (saww) aur Aal e Muhammad (saww) par Salwaat bhejte to barf ki tarah sufaid aur saaf shaffaf ho jaate. Salwaat ki barkat se wo itne aasuda haal (aaraam se) the ke muhaasira kham hone ke baad bhi wahaa'n se nikalna nahi chahte the."_
(Durood O Salaam Ki Barkatein, p48)

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (618) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رُسُلًا مُبَشِّرِينَ وَمُنْذِرِينَ لِئَلَّا يَكُونَ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَى اللَّهِ حُجَّةٌ بَعْدَ الرُّسُلِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Ye sare Rasool basharat dene wale aur daranewale the aur unhe is liye bheja gaya ke Rasoolon ke aane ke  baad insaanon ki Khuda ke muqabile mein koi Hujjat baqi na rahe aur Allah Ghalib aur Hikmat wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 165)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Nubuwwat ke topic jari rakhte hue is Ayat ko phir se repeat kar rahe hain. Jaisa ke Sura Juma mein bhi padhte hain
*هُوَ الَّذِي بَعَثَ فِي الْأُمِّيِّينَ رَسُولًا مِنْهُمْ يَتْلُو عَلَيْهِمْ آيَاتِهِ وَيُزَكِّيهِمْ وَيُعَلِّمُهُمُ الْكِتَابَ وَالْحِكْمَةَ وَإِنْ كَانُوا مِنْ قَبْلُ لَفِي ضَلَالٍ مُبِينٍ*

_"Us Khuda ne Makke Walon mein ek Rasool bheja jo unhi mein se tha taake unke saamne Aayaat ki tilawat kare aur unke Nufoos ko Pakeezah banaye aur Kitab o Hikmat ki taleem de agarche ye log badi khuli hui gumrahi mein mubtila the."_
(Surah Jumu'ah 2)

Ye Ayaten Nubuwwat ka hadaf o maqsad bata rahi hain. Islam hi aisa mazhab hai jahan ye Aqeeda paya jata hai.
Kuchh din pahle hamne pahle Imam Hazrat Ali (as) ki Rivayaat pesh ki thi, aaj Imam Mahdi (as) ke Wiladat ke mauqe par unki Rivayaat pesh karte hai:
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌷
*قال الإمام المهدي (عج):*
*"إن الله تعالى لم يخلق الخلق عبثا.  و لا اهملهم سدى، بل خلقهم بقدرته، و جعل لهم اسماعا و ابصارا و قلوبا و البابا، ثم بعث إليهم النبيين (عليهم السلام) مبشرين و منذرين، يأمرونهم بطاعته و ينهونهم عن معصية، و يعرفونهم ما جهلوه من أمر خالقهم و دينهم، و أنزل عليهم كتابا ....."*

_"Beshak Khuda Wande Aalam ne logon ko behooda paida nahi farmaya hai, aur bekaar nahi chhoda diya hai, balke unko apni Qudrat se khalq farmaya hai au unko Aankh, Kaan, Dil aur Aql di hai, iske baad unki taraf Basharat bene wale aur darane wale Anbiya ko bheja taake log Khuda ki ita'at karen aur Uski nafarmani se parhez karen, aur apne Khuda wa Deen ki nisbat jin cheezon se jahil hain unko seekh saken, aur unke liye Kitab Nazil ki hai......"_

(Al Ghaiba e Toosi, P-288, H-246, Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-280, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-194, H-21)

♦ _*NUBAWWAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (608) 🕌

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*رُسُلًا مُبَشِّرِينَ وَمُنْذِرِينَ لِئَلَّا يَكُونَ لِلنَّاسِ عَلَى اللَّهِ حُجَّةٌ بَعْدَ الرُّسُلِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَزِيزًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Ye sare Rasool basharat dene wale aur daranewale the aur unhe is liye bheja gaya ke Rasoolon ke aane ke baad insaanon ki Khuda ke muqabile mein koi Hujjat baqi na rahe aur Allah Ghalib aur Hikmat wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 165)

📚📖 🕌
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Ameerul Momenin Hazrat Ali (as) Nubuwwat ki is tarah wazahat karte hain:
_"Allah ne apne Rasool mab'oos kiye aur lagatar Anbiya bheje *taake un se Fitrat ke Ahd o Paiman poore karayen. Uski bhooli hui Ne'maten yaad dilayen. Paigham e Rabbani pahunch kar Hujjat tamam karen, Aql ke dafinon ko ubharen aur unhe qudrat ko Nishaniyan dikhayen.* Ye saron par buland baam Aasmaan, unke niche bichha hua farsh e Zameen, zinda rakhne wala samaane maeeshat (Financial assets), Fana kar dene wali ujlen, buddha kar dene wali bimariyan, pai dar pai aane wale haadse, Allah apni Makhlooq ko baghair kisi irsal kardah Paighambar ya Aasmaani Kitab ya Daleel e qata'ee ya tareeqe roshan ke baghair yun hi nahi chhoda. Aise Rasool jinhe ta'daad ki kami aur jhutlane walon ki kasrat darmandah wa aajiz nahi karti thi. Un mein koi sabiq tha jis mein aane wale ka naam o nishan bataya. Koi baad mein aya jise pahla pahchanwa chuka tha. Isi tarah muddaten guzar gayin. Zamane beet gaye. Baap dadaon ki jagah unki Auladen bas gayin yahan tak ke Allah ne eefa e Ahd (fulfilment of Covenant) aur Itmam e Hujjat ke liye Muhammad (saww) ko mab'oos kiya."_
(Nahjul Balagha)

♦ _*ALLAH GAWAH*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (609)

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَٰكِنِ اللَّهُ يَشْهَدُ بِمَا أَنْزَلَ إِلَيْكَ ۖ أَنْزَلَهُ بِعِلْمِهِ ۖ وَالْمَلَائِكَةُ يَشْهَدُونَ ۚ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ شَهِيدًا*

_"(Log mane ya na mane) magar Allah Gawahi deta hai ke jo kuchh Usne tum par Nazil kiya hai use apne Ilm se Nazil kiya hai aur Malaeka bhi Gawah hain aur Allah bataur Gawah Kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 166)

📚📖 📙
👉 _*�Tafseer:*_
Allah ne jo kuchh Rasoole Akram (saww) par Nazil uske liye Allah aur ke Malaika Gawah hain. Agar ham Allah par Aqeeda rakhte hain to Uski Gawahi hamare liye Kafi hai, phir shak ki koi gunjaish nahi rah jati.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 😳
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Main Ali (as) par ta'jjub karta hoo'n. Hazaaro'n gawaah hone ke bawajood unhe apna Haq nahi mila, jab ke apna Haq paane ke liye sirf 2 gawah zaruri hai."_
(Bihaar ul Anwaar, v37, p140, 40 Hadith – Ghadeer)
💧💦
Imam Sadiq (as):
_"Jo qatra (boond / drop) bhi aasmaan se naazil hota hai uske saath ek Farishta bhi naazil hota hai aur wo oos qatre ko wahaa'n rakh deta hai jahaa'n uske liye jagah muqarrar hai."_
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v1, p334)

(Surah Al-Fath: 1)

🌷 *WILADAT MUBAARAK* 🌷
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
              ♦ _*KUFR*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (610) 🌷

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَصَدُّوا عَنْ سَبِيلِ اللَّهِ قَدْ ضَلُّوا ضَلَالًا بَعِيدًا * إِنَّ الَّذِينَ كَفَرُوا وَظَلَمُوا لَمْ يَكُنِ اللَّهُ لِيَغْفِرَ لَهُمْ وَلَا لِيَهْدِيَهُمْ طَرِيقًا * إِلَّا طَرِيقَ جَهَنَّمَ خَالِدِينَ فِيهَا أَبَدًا ۚ وَكَانَ ذَٰلِكَ عَلَى اللَّهِ يَسِيرًا*
[Surat An-Nisa' 167 - 169]

_"Beshak jin logon ne Kufr kiya aur Rahe Khuda se (logon ko) mana kiya woh gumrahi mein babut door tak chale gaye hain."_
_"Beshak jin logon ne Kufr kiya aur Zulm kiya Khuda unhe hargiz ma'af nahi karega aur na hi inhe (Apne) Raaste ki Hidayat dega."_
_"Siwai Jahannam ke raaste ke (inhe aur koi Rahnumai nahi karega) jahan unko hamesha rahna hai aur ye Khuda ke liye bahut hi Aasaan hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 167 - 169)

📚📖 🌷
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Is Ayat mein un Kafiron ko condemn kiya hai jinhone:
(1) Kufr ikhtiyar kiya,
(2) Doosron ko Rahe Khuda ze roka,
(3) Apne upar Zulm kiya (Gunah ka irtekab) aur doosron par bhi Zulm kiya,
Ye log Hidayat ke qabil nahi. Ye log gumrahi mein bahut door chale gaye hain. Inko Allah nahi Bakhshnewala, inka permanent thikana Jahannam hai.
Is Ayat ke zail mein Imam Mohd Baqir wa Jafar Sadia (as) farmate hain:
"Agarche ye Ayat tamam Kafireen o Zalemeen ke liye nazil hui hai magar jin logon ne Ale Muhammad (as) par Zulm karke unke Huqooq ghazb kiye ye unhe bataur e khas mushtamil (included) hain."
(Tafseer Ali bin Ibrahim, Usoole Kafi, Noorus Saqlain)

Rahe Khuda Rahe Ahle Bait (as) hai, inse adawat Kufr hai. Aur Kufr ka thikana Jahannam hai.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_H. Jaabir ibne Abullah Ansari Madine ki galiyo’n mein gasht lagaate aur kaha karte ke Ali (as) behtareen bashar hain. Jo oos se inkaar kare wo kaafir hai. Aye giroh e Ansaar! Tum apni aulaad ko Ali (as) ki mohabbat sikhao, jo oos se inkaar kare to to uski Maa ke haal par nazar daalo._
(Man La Yahzarahul Faqih, v3, p307)

(Kamaluddin, v1, p279)
(Sahih Bukhari aur Muslim (Kitabul Amarah)  mein bhi 12 Khulufa Ki Hadis hai.)

                 ♦ _*RASOOL*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (611) 🚩

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ قَدْ جَاءَكُمُ الرَّسُولُ بِالْحَقِّ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ فَآمِنُوا خَيْرًا لَكُمْ ۚ وَإِنْ تَكْفُرُوا فَإِنَّ لِلَّهِ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَالْأَرْضِ ۚ وَكَانَ اللَّهُ عَلِيمًا حَكِيمًا*

_"Aye logo! Ye Rasool tumhare pas tumhare Rab ki taraf se Haq le kar aya hai. Imaan lao yahi tumhare lite behtar hai. Agar tumne Kufr kiya to Zameen wa Aasmaan ki tamam cheezen Khuda ki Milkiyat hain aur Allah Ilm o Hikmat wala hai. "_
(Surah Nisa: 170)

📚📖 🚩
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat mein ghair Momin afraad ka anjaam bayan kiya gaya hai. Ab is Ayat mein Imaan ki Dawat di gayi hai aur iske Natije ka zikr kiya gaya hai. Rasool par Alif Laam bata raha hai ke log is Rasool ke pahle muntazir the jiska pichhli Aasmaani Kitabon mein nishandahi ki ja chuki thi na ke Yahood o Nasaara balki Mushrekin bhi. Turuqe Ahle Bait (as) se manqool baaz rivayaat mein Haq ki tafseer "Vilayat e Hazrat Ali (as)" se ki gayi Hai. Kiyonki Ayat ke woh misdaq hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

🙇 🚩

_"Momin ka chiraag hamare Haq ki maarefat hai aur badtareen andhaa-pan hamare fazl se aa'nkhein band kar lena hai."_
(Aqwaal e Masoomeen (as), p167)
🚩

ne kaha hai ke _"300 Ayatein Hazrat Ali (as) ki shaan mein naazil huwi hai aur Nizamuddin Auliya ke mutaabiq pura Quran Hazrat Ali (as) ki madah mein hai."_
(Haqeeqat e Tabarra by Allamah Farogh Kazmi, p40)

            ♦ _*HAZRAT ESA (as)*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (612) ⛪

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لَا تَغْلُوا فِي دِينِكُمْ وَلَا تَقُولُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ إِلَّا الْحَقَّ ۚ إِنَّمَا الْمَسِيحُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ وَكَلِمَتُهُ أَلْقَاهَا إِلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ وَرُوحٌ مِنْهُ ۖ فَآمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ ۖ وَلَا تَقُولُوا ثَلَاثَةٌ ۚ انْتَهُوا خَيْرًا لَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّمَا اللَّهُ إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ ۖ سُبْحَانَهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ وَلَدٌ ۘ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلًا*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab (Christians​) apne Deen mein Ghuloo (Extremism) na karo aur Allah ki taraf Haq ke alawa koi baat mansoob na karo. Maseeh Esa bin Maryam bas Allah ke Rasool hain aur uska Kalma hai (Jesus is Word of God) jiska ilqa' (cast, throw) Maryam ki taraf kiya gaya hai aur Allah ki taraf se ek Rooh hain. Tum Allah aur Uske Rasoolon par Imaan Lao aur teen (3) (Trinity) ka naam bhi na lo. Isse baaz aa jao, is mein tumhari bhalai hai. Allah to bas ek hi Ma'bood (Diety) hai. Woh Pak o Munazzah hai ke uska koi  beta ho. Asmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Uski Milkiyat mein hain. Bataur Karsaz, Vakil Allah Kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 171)

📚📖 ⛪
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Kal hamne Walidat o Nasl ka tazkara kiya tha aur bataya tha ke hamare character mein Nasl ka ahm role hai.
Nubuwwat ke topic jari rakhte hue aaj ki Ayat mein Hazrat Esa (as) ka tazkara hai. Unko Maseeh مسیح kahte hain. Iski wajah ye hai ke unka wujood har tarah ki paleedi aur gunahon se مسح Masah Shuda (Wipe out) tha.
(Hadis e Rasool, Tafseer Majmaul Bayan)
Hazrat Esa (as) ki tasveer kashi sirf Rahme Madar (Womb) (Janabe Maryam) mein hui. Woh kabhi Walid ki Sulb (Loin) mein nahi rahe the agarche Hazrat Maryam (as) ke Aaba o Ajdad (Forefathers) Aslaab (Loins) e Anbiya mein rahe the.
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)
Hazrat Esa (as) ko Khuda ka Kalma aur Roohullah se khitab kiya jata hai. Is Ayat mein bhi khitab wohi hua aur Bible mein bhi Word of God and Holy Spirit naam diya gaya hai.
Hazrat Esa (as) ki Rooh ke bare mein Imam Sadiq (as) se sawal kiya gaya to farmaya:
_"Woh Allah ki paida karda Rooh hain jise Allah ne Adam wa Esa (as) mein wad'eeyat (entrusted) kiya tha."_ (Usoole Kafi)
Qur'an mein Esa (as) ka naam unki waledah ke sath 16 martaba aya hai. Is ka maqsad ye hai ke Hazrat Esa (as) Khuda ke bete nahi hain. Jesus is not son of God. Unki Wiladat hui, doodh piya aur aaghose Madar mein parvarish pai, yani tamam bashari sifat un mein maujood thi. To ek bashar, insaan Khuda kaise ho sakta hai. Is topic par mazeed guftgu ainda post mein hogi.
(To be cont'd ......)

✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 ⛪
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
Hawaariyo'n ne H. Isa (as) se puchha, _"Hum kin logo'n ke saath baithhein?"_ Aap (as) ne farmaya, _"Jinki soorat se zikr e Khuda yaad aaye, jinki guftagu se tumhara Ilm zyada ho, jinke Ilm se Akherat ki taraf raghbat ho"._
(Al Kaafi, v1, p85)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
----------------------------------------------
📌 *Note:*
*Wiladat Ali Ibnul Husain (as)*
Wiladat ki tarikhon mein  ikhtelaf ki wajah mukhtalif raviyon ko khabaren hain. Tarikh mein Wiladat​ Ali ibnul Husain (as) diya gaya hai. Imam Husain (as) ki 3 farzandon ka naam Ali tha. Bade bete ko Ali Akbar, chhote ko Ali Asghar aur beech mein Ali Ausat. Ahadees mein alag rivayaat hain ke bade bete Ali Akbar the ya Imam Sajjad (as). Janabe Ali Asghar (as) ka naam Abdullah bhi bataya jata hai. Isliye kuchh jagah Janabe Ali Akbar (as) to kuchh jagah Imam Sajjad ki Wiladat manai jati hai. Jabke 11 Shabaan bhi Viladat e Janabe Ali Akbar bhi zyada maaroof hai. Lekin isse hamare Aqeede par koi asar nahi padta. Jiske ke liye jo bhi tareekh sabit ho wo waise mana sakta hai. Pahle logon mein in tarikhon ki kam maloomat hoti thi, kab konsi important tarikh chali gayi pata nahi chalta tha. Lekin aajkal Social Media ka zyada phailao ki wajah se Duniya bhar ki maloomat hath par rahti hai. Sahih Ilm to Imam e Asr (atfs) ki Zahoor ke baad hi pata hoga.
Wallaho Aalam.

         *3rd May 2017, Wednesday,*
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
               ♦ _*TRINITY*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (612) 💒

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَهْلَ الْكِتَابِ لَا تَغْلُوا فِي دِينِكُمْ وَلَا تَقُولُوا عَلَى اللَّهِ إِلَّا الْحَقَّ ۚ إِنَّمَا الْمَسِيحُ عِيسَى ابْنُ مَرْيَمَ رَسُولُ اللَّهِ وَكَلِمَتُهُ أَلْقَاهَا إِلَىٰ مَرْيَمَ وَرُوحٌ مِنْهُ ۖ فَآمِنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَرُسُلِهِ ۖ وَلَا تَقُولُوا ثَلَاثَةٌ ۚ انْتَهُوا خَيْرًا لَكُمْ ۚ إِنَّمَا اللَّهُ إِلَٰهٌ وَاحِدٌ ۖ سُبْحَانَهُ أَنْ يَكُونَ لَهُ وَلَدٌ ۘ لَهُ مَا فِي السَّمَاوَاتِ وَمَا فِي الْأَرْضِ ۗ وَكَفَىٰ بِاللَّهِ وَكِيلًا*

_"Aye Ahle Kitab (Christians​) apne Deen mein Ghuloo (Extremism) na karo aur Allah ki taraf Haq ke alawa koi baat mansoob na karo. Maseeh Esa bin Maryam bas Allah ke Rasool hain aur uska Kalma hai (Jesus is Word of God) jiska ilqa' (cast, throw) Maryam ki taraf kiya gaya hai aur Allah ki taraf se ek Rooh hain. *Tum Allah aur Uske Rasoolon par Imaan Lao aur teen (3) (Trinity) ka naam bhi na lo.* Isse baaz aa jao, is mein tumhari bhalai hai. Allah to bas ek hi Ma'bood (Diety) hai. Woh Pak o Munazzah hai ke uska koi  beta ho. Asmaano aur Zameen ki tamam cheezen Uski Milkiyat mein hain. Bataur Karsaz, Vakil Allah Kafi hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 171)

📚📖 💒
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Hazrat Esa (as) ka bayan jari hai. Christians mein Jesus Christ se maroof hain. Woh Trinity ka Aqeeda rakhte hain. Trinity means One God The Father, The Son of God (Jesus), The Holy Spirit (Roohul Qudus). Iska matlab 3 Khuda: Khuda , Khuda ka beta, Rooh equal to One God. Ek Khuda jisne Zameen mein aa kar Hazrat Esa ka Roop liya aur in do ke Medium hai Rooh. Aql ye samajhne se qasir hai ke 1 = 3 kaise ho sakta hai. Aisa hi milta julta Aqeeda Hinduism mein bhi hai jise Trimurti kahte hain. Teen Buton ki pooja karte hain. Parsi (Zoroastrian) 2 Khuda ki parastish karte hain.
Allah ne is Ayat mein is sab Aqeedon ko batil qarar diya hai. Hazrat Esa (as) Khuda ke bheje hue Paighambar the na khud Khuda. Hazrat Esa (as) ko Allah ki Rooh aur Kalam bataya. Allah Ta'ala is sab se Paak hai.
Trinity (1 = 3) ko dekh kar to ek bachcha bhi hansega.
American writer Mr. Hawks kahta hai:
_"Lekin Masla e Taslees (Trinity) Old aur New Testaments mein makhfi (hidden) aur ghair waazeh hai."_
(Qamoos e Muqaddas, P-345)
Problem of Trinity taqreeban 3rd Century ke baad Christians mein paida hua. Ye ek bidat hui. Kuchh ka kahna hai ke iska source Trimurti hai (Brahma, Vishnu, Shiva).
Trinity mein ek defect ye hai ke ye Khuda ko Limit karti hai jabke Allah Unlimited hai, Compound nahi hai. Woh kis cheez ka Mohtaj nahi. Khuda Insaani libaas mein Majboor nazar ayenge.
Woh explain karte hain ke jaise Suraj aur uski Roshni dono light hain. Doosri misal dete hain ke ek hi admi kai aine (Mirror) mein alag alag nazar aata hai. Ya jaise ek Traingle ke 3 corners ko reduce karke ek point bana diya jaye. Aur bhi bahut se explanation diye jaate hain. Unki misalon par ghaur karen to pata chalega ke Suraj aur Roshni do alag shay hain. Roshni ya mirror image aks/Shadow hain haqeeqat nahi. Ek Shakhs ek waqt mein Khuda ho aur ek aur usi waqt doosra Khuda bhi Hukoomat kar raha ho, is mein contradiction hoga. Sufism ka Aqeeda jo ke woh bhi batil hai, Christians iski misal dete hain ke aap bhi ye Aqeeda rakhte hain. Yani Wahdat mein Kasrat aur Kasrat mein Wahdat. Wahdatul Wujood ka Aqeeda khud batil hai iska Islam se koi rabt nahi. Yani Sufi Hazrat kahte hain Hasti bas ek hai jo mukhtalif chehron mein nazar aati hai. Means kiya Kutte mein bhi Khuda nazar ayega!!
Doosri misal Christians ye dete hain ke jaise aap Imam Husain (as) ko ثار الله Sarallah (Khuda ka khoon) se tashbih dete ho. Hamara jawab ye hai ثار means خون بہا yani Khoon ka badla sirf Allah hi lega. Phir kahte hai jaise Ali (as) يد الله (Allah ke haath). Ham ye majazi taur par mante hai (Metaphor) jismani haqeeqat nahi. Allah koi jismani haath nahi rakhta. Yadullah means Power of Allah (Allah ki Qudrat). Lekin Christians H. Esa (as) ko haqeeqat mein Khuda ka beta maante hain. (Qamoos e Muqaddas, P-345).
Khulasa ye Trinity Tauheed ke khilaf hai. Agar Allah ek hai to Haqeeqat mein ek hai, yahan tak ke Uski Sifat bhi Uski Zaat se alag hain. Woh Wajibul Wujood se bhi kahi Bala wa Aala hai.
Ham Uske Saamne Walah وله (Perplexity - Hairani wa pareshani ki manzil mein hain). Woh Kiya hai - hamare Quwwat e Fahem ke bahar hai. Isiliye ham ne kaha 'الله' Allah.
(Barivayat e Imam Sadiq as)
Detail studies ke liye is topic ki Books refer karen.

(To be Cont'd ........)

(Maula Ali Ki Shaan Mein 1000 Ahadees, h270, p188)

⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
              ♦ _*BANDAGI*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (613) ⛪

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفَ الْمَسِيحُ أَنْ يَكُونَ عَبْدًا لِلَّهِ وَلَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ الْمُقَرَّبُونَ ۚ وَمَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفْ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ وَيَسْتَكْبِرْ فَسَيَحْشُرُهُمْ إِلَيْهِ جَمِيعًا * فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ فَيُوَفِّيهِمْ أُجُورَهُمْ وَيَزِيدُهُمْ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ ۖ وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ اسْتَنْكَفُوا وَاسْتَكْبَرُوا فَيُعَذِّبُهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا وَلَا يَجِدُونَ لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَلِيًّا وَلَا نَصِيرًا*

_"Maseeh (Massiah) ne kabhi bhi Banda e Khuda hone ko apne liye aar nahi samjha,_ (He was not ashamed to be servant of God. - Khuda ke banda hona unke ke liye koi hajo ki baat nahi thi.)
_aur na hi Muqarrab Farishte Khuda ke Bande hone ko apne liye aar عار mehsoos karte hain aur jin logon ne bhi Uski Bandagi ko aar samjha aur Takabbur kiya to aise tamam logon ko Allah apne pas jama karega."_
_"Beharhal woh log jo Imaan laye honge aur jinhone Nek amal kiye honge to Khuda unhe unka mukammal Ajr ataa karega aur Apne Fazl se unke Ajr mein izaafa karega aur woh log jinhone Khuda ki Bandagi ko aar samjha hoga aur Takabbur kiya hoga to Allah unhe dardnaak Azaab dega aur Khuda ke alawa woh apne liye koi Sarparast aur Madadgaar nahi payenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 172 - 173)

📚📖 ⛪
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ka Topic is Ayat se muttasil hai. Guzishta Ayat mein Christians ke Trinity Concept ko batil qarar diya tha. Allah Ta'ala ne bataya ke Hazrat Esa (as) Khuda nahi balke Paighambar the, na ke woh Trinity ka juz the. Is Ayat mein bhi isi baat ka zikr hai ke kabhi bhi Hazrat Esa (as) aur Farishton ne Bandagi ko neecha tasawwur nahi kiya. Balke Allah ke nazdeek sab se badi Fazilat Allah ki Bandagi hai. Tashahood mein bhi ham padhte hai:
*اشهد ان محمدا عبده و رسوله.*
"Muhammad (saww) (pahle) Allah ke Bande hain​, (phir) Uske Rasool hain."
Pas Bandagi ki manzilat Risalat se bala hai.
Yahan Ayat se ye sabit hai hai ke khud Hazrat Esa (as) ne kabhi Khuda ke beta hone ka dawa nahi kiya.
Ek Christian Jasaleeq Imam Reza (as) ke pas aya aur bola ke aap Jesus Christ ki tauheen karte hain Khuda ka Banda kah kar!!
Imam (as) ne farmaya ke Hazrat Esa (as) ki baqi baten to achhi thi lekin woh zyada Ibadat nahi karte the. Christian jhunjhla gaya - _'kitni ghalat baat kar rahe hain, sab jaante hain ke woh sab se zyada Ibadat Guzar the.'_
Imam (as) ne farmaya ke _'woh kis ki Ibadat karte the? Kiya Khuda ke alawa kisi aur ki Ibadat karte the. Abhi tu ne iqrar kiya​ ke woh Khuda ke Bande, Makhlooq, Uske Ibadat Guzar the na ke Ma'bood.'_
Christian khamosh ho gaya!!!
(Manaqib ibne Shahre Ashoob, Vol 4, P-352)
Ayat ka doosra pahlu ye hai ke Farishton ke bare mein bhi yehi baat bayan ki gayi hai. Iski wajah ye ke Trinity ka jab zikr hota hai, Roohul Qudus (Holy Spirit) bhi iska ek juz hai, jo ek Farishte ka naam hai. Woh bhi Allah ki ibadat karta hai na ke woh Khuda hai. Doosri baat ye ke bahut se mazhab hain jo Farishton ki pooja karte hain. Islam ke pahle Arab mein Farishton aur Jino ki ibadat hoti thi.
Aaj ke daur mein bhi kuchh Mazahib aise hain jo Farishton ya Jinn ki pooja karte hain aur unhe apna Daata (Deity) tasawwur karte hain. Woh ye hain:
Iraq mein Yazidi Malak Taloos ki pooja karte hain.
Angelici ek firqa hai​ hai jiska Philosopher Augustine  ke Aqeeda ki roo se Angels ki pooja karte the, unka kahna tha ke Khuda in Farishton ke zariye Duniya khalq ki.
Doosra mazhab hai - Gnosticism jo Aeon Farishte ki Ibadat karte hain.
Aur bhi bahut hain lekin misal ke taur par itna kafi hai.
Farishton ke bare mein mazeed guftgu next post mein hogi, inshallah.

(To be continued .....)

(Meezan ul Hikmah, v6, p32)

(Tafseer Noor us Saqlain, v2, p508)

    ♦ _*MALAIKA-E-MUQARRAB*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (614) 🌅

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*لَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفَ الْمَسِيحُ أَنْ يَكُونَ عَبْدًا لِلَّهِ وَلَا الْمَلَائِكَةُ الْمُقَرَّبُونَ ۚ وَمَنْ يَسْتَنْكِفْ عَنْ عِبَادَتِهِ وَيَسْتَكْبِرْ فَسَيَحْشُرُهُمْ إِلَيْهِ جَمِيعًا * فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا وَعَمِلُوا الصَّالِحَاتِ فَيُوَفِّيهِمْ أُجُورَهُمْ وَيَزِيدُهُمْ مِنْ فَضْلِهِ ۖ وَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ اسْتَنْكَفُوا وَاسْتَكْبَرُوا فَيُعَذِّبُهُمْ عَذَابًا أَلِيمًا وَلَا يَجِدُونَ لَهُمْ مِنْ دُونِ اللَّهِ وَلِيًّا وَلَا نَصِيرًا*

_"Maseeh (Massiah) ne kabhi bhi Banda e Khuda hone ko apne liye aar nahi samjha,_ (He was not ashamed to be servant of God. - Khuda ke banda hona unke ke liye koi hajo ki baat nahi thi.)
_*aur na hi Muqarrab Farishte Khuda ke Bande hone ko apne liye aar عار mehsoos karte hain* aur jin logon ne bhi Uski Bandagi ko aar samjha aur Takabbur kiya to aise tamam logon ko Allah apne pas jama karega."_
_"Beharhal woh log jo Imaan laye honge aur jinhone Nek amal kiye honge to Khuda unhe unka mukammal Ajr ataa karega aur Apne Fazl se unke Ajr mein izaafa karega aur woh log jinhone Khuda ki Bandagi ko aar samjha hoga aur Takabbur kiya hoga to Allah unhe dardnaak Azaab dega aur Khuda ke alawa woh apne liye koi Sarparast aur Madadgaar nahi payenge."_
(Surah Nisa: 172 - 173)

📚📖 🌅
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta post mein ham ne is Ayat ke is point ki taraf ishaara ke kiya ke Hazrat Esa (as) & Malaika Muqarrab Khuda ki Bandagi karte the. In mein se kisi ne Uloohiyat (Divinity) ka dawa nahi kiya.
Aaj Rivayat ke zariye Malaika Muqarrab ka ta'arruf karate hain:
🍁
Hazrat Rasoole Akram (saww) ne Hazrat Ali (as) se farmaya: _"Dahne haath mein Angoothi pahno taake Muqarrab ban jao."_
Hazrat Ali (as) ne arz kiya: _"Ya Rasoolallah! Muqarrabin kaun hain?"_
Aap (saww) ne farmaya: _"Jibrael wa Mikael."_
(Ilalush Sharay, Raavi Salman Farsi)
🍀
Jibrael e Ameen (as) ne Rasoolallah (saww) se arz kiya:
_"Khuda aur uski Makhlooq ke darmiyan 70 Hazaar parde hael hain aur tamam Makhlooq mein se Mein aur Israfeel Khuda ke zyada qareeb hain. Hamare aur Khuda ke darmiyan Noor, Zulmat, Badal aur Paani ke chaar parde hael hain."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim)
🌻
Rasoole Khuda (saww) se sawal kiya gaya Ali (as) afzal hain ya Malaika e Muqarrab?
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Malaika e Muqarrab ko sharaf mila hi Muhammad (saww) aur Ali (as) ki Muhabbat ki wajah se hai kiyonki unhone ham dono ko Vilayat qubool ki thi. Ali (as) ka jo bhi Shia apne dil ko dhoke aur Gunahon ki nijasat se paak rakhta hai woh Malaika se Afzal hai."_
(Ehtejaaj e Tabarasi, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🍂🌾
'Jab Janabe Fatema Zehra (sa) Mehrab e Ibadat mein khadi hoti thi to unhe 70 Hazaar Muqarrab Farishte Salam karte the aur Bibi se guftgu karte the jo unhone Hazrat Maryam (sa) se ki thi.'
(Imaali e Sudooq)

         ♦ _*NOOR-E-MUBEEN*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (615) 🌟

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَا أَيُّهَا النَّاسُ قَدْ جَاءَكُمْ بُرْهَانٌ مِنْ رَبِّكُمْ وَأَنْزَلْنَا إِلَيْكُمْ نُورًا مُبِينًا*

_"Aye logo! Tumhare Rab ki taraf se tumhare pas Roshan Daleel aa chuki hai aur tumhari taraf waazeh Noor bhi nazil kar chuke hain."_
(Surah Nisa: 174)

📚📖 🌟
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Guzishta Ayat ke zel mein bayan kiya tha ke Farishton ko Muqarrab hone ka sharaf Muhammad (saww) aur Ali (as) ki Muhabbat ki wajah se mila. Aaj ki Ayat mein dono ko 'Burhan' aur 'Noor' se khitab kiya hai.

Imam Sadiq (as) ne farmaya Noor نور se Ali ibne Abi Talib (as) ki Vilayat murad hai. (Majmaul Bayan) Tafseer Ali Ibne Ibrahim mein Noor se Ameerul Momin ki Imamat murad hai. Imam Sadiq (as) ne is Ayat ke zail mein farmaya برهان 'Burhan' se Rasoole Khuda (saww) aur نور 'Noor' se Hazrat Ali (as) murad hain. Ek sawal ke jawab mein farmaya صراط مستقيم (Sirate Mustaqeem) Ali (as) hain.
(Tafseer e Ayyashi)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🌟
Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Shabe Me'raj mere Rab ne mujhe ye Waḥy farmayi:_
_"Muhammad (saww)! Meine Zameen par nigah dali to Meine tera intekhab kiya aur tujhe Nabi banaya. Meine apne Naam se tera naam mushtaq (derived) kiya. Mein محمود Mehmood hun aur tu محمد Muhammad (saww) hai. Phir Meine Zameen par dubara nigah dali to Meine Ali (as) ka intekhab kiya. Meine use tera Wasi, tera Khalifa, tera Damaad aur teri nasl ka Walid banaya aur Meine apne Namon mein se us naam mushtaq kiya. Mein  على الاعلى Aliyul Aala hun aur woh على Ali (as) hai. Meine فاطمه Fatema (sa), حسن Hasan (as) aur حسين Husain (as) ko tum dono ke Anwaar se paida kiya. Phir Meine unki Vilayat ko Farishton ke samne pesh kiya. Jisne unki Vilayat ko qubool kiya woh mere pas Muqarrab bane."_
(Kamaluddin wa Tamamun Ne'ma, Noorus Saqlain)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜

       ♦ _*SIRAATE MUSTAQEEM*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (616) 🛣

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*فَأَمَّا الَّذِينَ آمَنُوا بِاللَّهِ وَاعْتَصَمُوا بِهِ فَسَيُدْخِلُهُمْ فِي رَحْمَةٍ مِنْهُ وَفَضْلٍ وَيَهْدِيهِمْ إِلَيْهِ صِرَاطًا مُسْتَقِيمًا*

_*Woh log jo Khuda par Imaan laye hain (Momin) aur jo Usse wabasta ho chuke hain (touch mein hain), Khuda aise logon ko apni Rehmat aur Fazl mein dakhil karega unhe apni taraf se aane ka Seedha Raasta dikhayega."_
(Surah Nisa: 175)

📚📖 🛣
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
'Noor-e-Mubeen' ka tazkara jari hai. Is Ayat ke zail mein Imam Sadiq (as) farmate hain:
_"Rehmat-e-Ilahi aur Fazle Parwardigaar mein wohi log dakhil honge jo Ameerul Mo'meneen aur Aimma ki Vilayat se mutamassik honge. Aur Hazrat Ali (as) Siraate Mustaqeem hai."_
(Tafseer Ali ibne Ibrahim & Ayyashi)
🕌
Sura Al Hamd mein har Namazi Dua mangta hai hame hame aise Raaste ki Hidayat kar jin par Tu ne Ne'maten nazil na ke Bhatke huwon ka raasta jin par tera ghazab nazil hua.
Ab dekhte hain ke صراط المستقيم Siratul Mustaqeem (Seedha Raasta) kiya hai?
Siraate Mustaqeem Quran mein kai jagah par aya jaise:

*قُلْ إِنَّنِي هَدَانِي رَبِّي إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ دِينًا قِيَمًا مِلَّةَ إِبْرَاهِيمَ حَنِيفًا ۚ وَمَا كَانَ مِنَ الْمُشْرِكِينَ*
[Surat Al-An'am 161]

*وَأَنِ اعْبُدُونِي ۚ هَٰذَا صِرَاطٌ مُسْتَقِيمٌ*
[Surat Ya-Seen 61]

*وَمَنْ يَعْتَصِمْ بِاللَّهِ فَقَدْ هُدِيَ إِلَىٰ صِرَاطٍ مُسْتَقِيمٍ*
[Surat Aal-E-Imran 101]

*وَاعْتَصِمُوا بِحَبْلِ اللَّهِ جَمِيعًا وَلَا تَفَرَّقُوا ۚ وَاذْكُرُوا نِعْمَتَ اللَّهِ عَلَيْكُمْ .......*
[Surat Aal-E-Imran 103]
(Tarjuma Quran se refer karen)
In Ayaton se pata chalta hai ke Deen e Ibrahim (as) jo ke Deen e Hanif hai wohi Seedha Raasta hai. Allah ki Ibadaat bhi Allah ka Seedha Raasta hai. Jo Allah ki Rassi ko thame rahe, touch mein rahe, ye bhi Seedha Raasta hai.
Rivayaat ko refer karte hain:

Rasoole Khuda (saww):
_"Siraate Mustaqeem Anbiya ka Raasta hai aur Anbiya woh Hastiyan hain jin par Allah ne Ne'maten nazil ki."_

Imam Sadiq (as):
_*Isse murad Imam ka Raasta aur uski Ma'arefat hai."_

*والله نحن الصراط المستقيم*
_"Bakhuda ham hi Siraate Mustaqeem hain"_

_"Siraate Mustaqeem Ameerul Mo'meneen Ali (as) hain."_
(Noorus Saqlain, Vol 1, P-20, 21)

Ye baat musallam hai ke jo Deen e Hanif Hazrat Ibrahim (as) laye wohi Rasoole Khuda (as) ka Raasta tha aur wohi Raasta Aimma e Ahle Bait (as) ka tha.
Pas Ayat wa Rivayaat ka khulasa ye hai ke Anbiya ka Raasta, Rasoole Khuda wa unke Ausiya wa Ahle Bait (as) ka Raasta hi Siraate Mustaqeem hai.
Isliye Darood Muhammad (saww) wa Ale Muhammad (as) par bheji jati hai. Agar Namaz mein​ Darood nahi bhejen to Namaz bhi batil hai. Kiyonki ye Hastiyan Noor e Mubeen hai. Inke Dushmanan ka Raasta الضالين ka Raasta hai jin par Allah ka ghazab nazil hua. Ujela ka Raasta chhod kar doosri raah ikhtiyar karenge to andhera hi nazar ayega. Kiyon na ham Roshan wa Seedha Raasta ikhtiyar karen. Agar ye raasta sab ko mil gaya hota to har Namaz mein har Namazi ye dua nahi karta.
Aur Aaj ke Ayat ke mutabik jo in hastiyon se mutamassik (touch mein) ho jayega to Allah hi Seedhe Raaste ki taraf Hidayat karega.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 🛣
Imam Sadiq (as):
_" 'Siraat e Mustaqeem' H. Ali (as) aur unki Imamat ka eteqaad karna hai."_
(Irshadaat e Masumeen (as), p46)

             ♦ _*WIRASAT*_ ♦

As-salamu alaikum wa Rahmatullahi wa Barakatohu

Start your Day by reading Quran: (621) 👫

*بِسْمِ اللَّهِ الرَّحْمَٰنِ الرَّحِيمِ*

*يَسْتَفْتُونَكَ قُلِ اللَّهُ يُفْتِيكُمْ فِي الْكَلَالَةِ ۚ إِنِ امْرُؤٌ هَلَكَ لَيْسَ لَهُ وَلَدٌ وَلَهُ أُخْتٌ فَلَهَا نِصْفُ مَا تَرَكَ ۚ وَهُوَ يَرِثُهَا إِنْ لَمْ يَكُنْ لَهَا وَلَدٌ ۚ فَإِنْ كَانَتَا اثْنَتَيْنِ فَلَهُمَا الثُّلُثَانِ مِمَّا تَرَكَ ۚ وَإِنْ كَانُوا إِخْوَةً رِجَالًا وَنِسَاءً فَلِلذَّكَرِ مِثْلُ حَظِّ الْأُنْثَيَيْنِ ۗ يُبَيِّنُ اللَّهُ لَكُمْ أَنْ تَضِلُّوا ۗ وَاللَّهُ بِكُلِّ شَيْءٍ عَلِيمٌ*

_"Ay Nabi! Ye log Aap se Fatwa daryaft karte hain. Aap kah dijiye ke Kalalah كلاله (Bhai Bahen) ke bare mein Khuda tumko ye Fatwa deta hai: Agar koi shakhs be Aulad mar jaye aur sirf Bahen (sister) waris ho to use Tarke (inheritance) mein se nisf (half) milega. Isi tarah se agar Bahen mar jaye aur uski Aulad na ho to Bhai uska Waris hoga. Phir agar Waris do Bahnen hain to unhe Tarke ka do tihai (2/3 rd) milega. Agar Bahen Bhai dono hain to mard ke liye Mard ke liye Aurat ka Dohra (double) hissa hoga. Khuda ye sab waazeh kar raha hai taake bahekne na pao aur Khuda har cheez ko achchi tarah se Janne wala hai."_
(Surah Nisa: 176)

📚📖 👫
👉 _*Tafseer:*_
Sura Nisa ki Tafseer ke Silsilah ki ye Akhiri Ayat hai. Wirasat ke bare mein kuchh Ahkam Ayat no.12 mein aa chuke hain. Ek fatwe ka yahan bayan hai. كلاله means Brother & Sister. Unke bare mein Ahkam bayan kiye gaye hain. Is Ayat ki Tafseer ki yaha gunjaish nahi hai. Bahut Ahadis hain. Is Topic par ham Tauzeehul Masael Ay. Sistani Maslah no. 2737 se refer kar sakte hain.
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
✍🏻___Syed Shoeb Raza Abdi
----------------------------------------------

_*MORAL OF THE DAY ....!!!!!!!!*_
🙇 💰
_*Haram Maal:*_
*قال الامام المهدى (عج):*
*فلا يحل لأحد أن يتصرف من مال بغير إذنه.*
Imam Mahdi (as):
_"Kisi insaan ke liye ye jaez nahi hai ke malik ki ijazat ke bagair uske maal ko istemal kare."_
(Kamaluddin, P-521, H-49, Ehtejaaj, Vol 2, P-299, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-183, H-11, Wasaelus Shia, Vol 9, P-540, H-12670)

_*Waqf:*_💰📜
Imam Mahdi (as):
_"Tumne hamse us shakhs ke bare mein sawal kiya jisne kisi cheez ko hamare liye Waqf kar diya ho lekin baad mein woh khud us cheez ka mohtaj ho gaya ho? Aise shakhs ka Hukm yehi hai ke agar us ne jo cheez hamare liye Waqf ki hai lekin abhi tak usko diya nahi hai, to woh mukhtar hai aur Waqf se sarfe nazar kar (phir) sakta hai, lekin agar usko de diya hai to uska Waqf qatai (Absolutely) ho chuka hai, jis ke baad woh usko wapas nahi le sakta, chahe woh uska mohtaj ho ya na ho."_
(Kamaluddin, Vol 2, P-520, H-49, Biharul Anwaar, Vol 53, P-182, H-11)
⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜⚜
